“CHHI3-A2-LAI7 E5 PEK-HAP8-HOE.”
(Nga2-ko 2:2)
1
“Pa-pah, ma-mah, kin2 pi7-pan7 oh!  Pai3-tng5 e5 cheng-siaN teh tan5-lah-ne7!  Hui7-bi2 e5 sim chin hoaN-hi2: in-ui7 kin-mi5 si7 Kiu3-chu2-tan3.  I kap in hiaN-ko Teng-liong5(登龍) chu7 kui2-na7 tiam2-cheng cheng5, chiu7 saN-khou3 oaN7 pian7-pian7, tak8-hang7 chun2-pi7 cheng2-che5 beh khi3 hu3.  Hui7-bi2 kin-ni5 19 hoe3 tu2 ti7 Ko-tiong 3 lian5, koh chit8 hak8-ki5 e7 pit8-giap8.  SeN choe3 siu3-khi3, oah8-tang7, leng2-li7.  I e5 tek8-tiong5 chiu7-si7 im-gak8, gau5 toaN5 kng3-khim5, siaN ia7 chin sui2, chhiuN3 khi2-lai5 oan2-jin5 gim5-leng5(銀鈴).  Ji5-chhiaN2 oan2-choan2 chheng-chhui3.  Si7 thian-seng e5 chu-chit, chiong-lai5 iu2-bong7 e5 im-gak8-ka.  Teng-liong5 si7 thak8 Tai7-hak8 siong-kho, ia7-si7 chit8 e5 siu3-chai5, Kin-ni5 24 hoe3, chhu3-bi7 im-gak8 kap phau2-be2.  Koh chit8-ki5 ia7 e7 pit8-giap8.  In-tau si7 li7 Chiang-chiu koan7-siaN5 jip8-soaN iok 5, 6 phou3-lou7 e5 soaN-kha, si7 chit8 e5 sio2-sio2 e5 ke-chhi7.  Jin5-khau2 iok-liok8 3, 4 chheng lang5.  Chian5-chheng si5-tai7 bat tui3 hia chhut kui2-na7 e5 ki2-jin5, siu3-chai5 ia7 be7 chio2, sou2-i2 lang5 chheng hit e5 ke-a2 kio3 choe3 Su7-liong5-ke(士隆街).  Ke sui-jian5 se3-se3 khiok u7 chit8 choa7 ke-a2-lou7, u7 che7-che7 tiam3, be7 hi5 bah long2 u7.  Lan2 e5 pai3-tng5 si7 ti7 ke-a2-thau5, kui-bou5 put-chi2 toa7, si7 chit8 keng tong5-hong5 e5 iuN5-koan2(洋館).  Ti7 lau5-teng2 le2-pai3, lau5-e7 choe3 Chu2-jit8-oh8.  Bok8-su-koan2 khi2-tit chin-sui2, ti7 chit e5 soaN-kha na2-chun2 chin bo5 su3-phoe3 e5 khoan2.  M7-ku2 ki5-sit8 chit keng kau3-hoe7 si7 chin heng.  Mui2-le2-pai3 chit8-pou iok 300 goa7 lang5 le2-pai3.  Chia si7 chit8 e5 soaN-hoe3 e5 chhut-jip8-khau2.  Che7-che7 hiaN-ti7 si7 tui3 soaN-lai7 chhut-lai5 le2-pai3.  Chia thiN-khi3 liang5, keng2-ti3 ho2, joah8-thiN se-iuN5 soan-kau3-su siong5-siong5 lai5 chia hioh-khun3, kau3-hoe7 ia7 u7 hu7-siat chit8 keng pin5-bin5 e5 chin2-liau5-sou2, hoan7-chia2 ia7 chin-che7.  Ong5 Bok8-su e5 thoan5-to7-li2, Li2 i-seng e5 i-piN7 long2 chin chhut-mia5.
Hui7-bi2(惠美) e5 lau7-pe7 ia7-si7 chit8 e5 lau7 siu3-chai5, i e5 kong bat pai3-beng7 koe3 Chiang-chiu koan7-tiuN2.  Sng3 si7 chit8 e5 bun5-bek8 e5 se3-ka.  Kho2-sioh lau7 siu3-chai5 cha2 bat chiah8 a-phian3, ji5-chhiaN2 koh hoN3 phiau5, tou2, im2.  Sou2-i2 ke-hoe2 ui7 i phoa3 khi3 chin-che7.  Tng oa2 40 hoe3 peN7 chit8 e7 hiam2-si2, khi3 jip8 koan7-siaN5 lan2 kau3-hoe7 e5 i-koan2, tui3 an2-ni m7-na7 peN7 ho2, soa3 koe2 a-phian3.  Siang7 hoaN-hi2 e5 chiu7-si7 tit-tioh8 to7-li2 sin3 Ia5-sou.  Hit-si5 Hui7-bi2 iok 7, 8 hoe3, Teng-liong5 iok 12 hoe3.  Au7-lai5 na2 jiat8-sim chiu7 siu7 keng2 choe3 TiuN2-lo2.  Kau3-taN lian5-lian5 tiong5-jim7.  Ti7 chit e5 se3-se3 e5 te7-hng siu3-chai5 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 tai7-ke to bat--i.  
Tui3 seN chit tui3 kiaN2 liau2-au7 long2 bo5 koh u7 se3-kiaN2, sou2-i2 nng7-lau7 thiaN3 mia7-mia7.  I bo5 choe3 seng-li2, i keng-eng5 long5-giap8, chiong sou2 u7 kui2-kah chui2-chhan5 chhiaN3 tng5-kang lai5 choh.  I sui-jian5 si7 bun5-sin iau2-ku2 chin u7 gian2-kiu3 sim, i e5 tiu7-a2, a2-si7 beh8-a2 long2 bat siu7 seng2 long5-hoe7 siuN2.  M7-na7 keng-long5 tui3 chhi7 gu5, iuN5, ti to chin u7 gian2-kiu3, koh ia7 ka-ti7 khui hi5-ti5 pang3-hi5.  Ti7 au7-bin7 oa2 soaN e5 koe2-chi2 theh8 sou2 cheng3 e5 kam-a2 ia7 chin sui2.  I chai han-chu5 keng toa7-ti.  Koh chhi7 gu5 khioh tui-pui5, put-lun7 tui-pui5-sia3 e5 kian3-cho7, tak8-hang7 chin hap8-li2.  I e5 pui5 chhiong-chiok, tui3 thou2-te7 chhim keng, si-pui5 sek-hap8.  I e5 gou7-kak tak8-ni5 to pi2 lang5 khah ho2 siu.  Chhek siok8 e5 si5 chhi7 che7-che7 ke, ah seN nng7.  Go5, ah ti7 hi5-ti5 pang3-sai2, khut u7 pui5 hi5 gau5 toa7.  Bo5-lun7 peN5-bin7, lip8-the2 e5 long5-giap8 i to siuN7 e7 kau3.  Ti7 i au7-piah ia7 u7 chap8 goa7 kah e5 soaN cheng3 siuN-si sio hoe2-thoaN3, ia7 u7 cheng3 che7-che7 e7 choe3-tit liau7 e5 chhiu7, si7 chit8 e5 gau5 phah-sng3 e5 lang5.  Siong7-te3 toa7-toa7 siuN2-su3 i, kau3-hoe7 e5 keng-che3 i ia7 kek8-lek8 chi-chhi5 chin-chiaN3 si7 Siong7-te3 ho2 e5 koan2-ke.
TaN Teng-liong5 kap sio-moai7 Hui7-bi2 tng ti7 hioh ni5 to3--lai5 e7 tit choe3-hoe2 khi3 hu3 Seng3-tan3 iu5-ge7-hoe7 si7 12 hun e5 hoaN-hi2.  Kin-mi5 nng7 hiaN-moai7 beh piau2-ian2 kng3-khim5 tok8-chau3, kap hiaN-ko e5 sio2-the5-khim5 tok8-chau3, kap hap8-chau3.  Tek8-piat8 Hui7-bi2 e5 tok8-chhiuN3 Ong5 Bok8-su e5 leng7-ai3 Soat-mui5(雪梅) sio2-chia2 e5 phoaN7-chau3 si7 choe3 te7-it siu7 chu3-bak8 e5 chhut-bok8.  Nng7 hiaN-moai7 phok-phok-thiau3 tit8-tit8 teh tan2 pa-pa, ma-ma m7 khah-kin2 thang lai5 khi3.  In-ui7 pa-pa, ma-ma lau7-lah, kiaN5-lou7 tah8-tham7 su-iau3 in choe3 phoaN7.  Koh bo5-loa7-ku2 chiu7 choe3 hoe2 khi3 pai3-tng5.  Hit me5-hng lang5-kheh, hoe7-iu2 boan2-tng5, ti7 chit e5 soaN-kha se3-se3 e5 ke-a2 u7 chit khoan2 e5 chu2-chhui si7 chin hi-han2.  Na7 m7-si7 lan2 e5 kau3-hoe7, thang kong2 bo5 tang3 khoaN3 e5 seng7-hoe7.  In nng7 hiaN-moai7 e5 piau2-ian2 kap Soat-mui5 sio2-chia2 e5 piau2-ian2 chin-chiaN3 si7 hit am3 siang7 ho2, hou7 lang5 toa7 o-lo2 e5 chiat-bok8.  Soat-mui5 sio2-chia2 pi2 Hui7-bi2 ke nng7 hoe3, kin-ni5 21 hoe3, cha2 chit8-ni5 Ko-tiong i2-keng pit8-giap8, iau2 boe7 choe3 chhin, ti7 chhu3-nih pang-chan7 pe7-bu2.  Le2-pai3-jit8 Chu2-jit8-oh8 iu3-ti7 kho, kap le2-pai3-sek e5 toaN5-khim5 long2 si7 i hu7-tam, chin-chiaN3 si7 ho2 lu2-tek e5 sio2-chia2.  Ti7 iu5-ge7-hoe7 tiong u7 chit8-chhut kio3-cho3 “Chhoe7 po2-chu” (si7 Ia5-sou e5 phi3-ju7) choe3 khi2 chin pek-chin, chin kam2-kek lang5.  Teng-liong5 khoaN3 liau2 chhim-chhim in3-siong7 ti7 nau2-lai7.  Soa3 lian5-siong2 i e5 ho2 peng5-iu2 Khun-hong, chiu7-si7 cha2 i 2 ni5 tui3 in e5 bo2-hau7 pit8-giap8--e5.  Hian7-chai7 si7 choe3 chu-po2 e5 chin3-chhut khau2 siong(珠寶進出口商).  KiaN5 kui2 na7 pai2 In3-tou7, Bian2-tian7, Siam7-lo5 put-chi2 ho2 than3, ke-hoe2 i2-keng seng5.  I soa3 chu-chu siuN7 na7 toa7-oh8 pit8-giap8 tek-khah beh ka7 i choe3 chhi3 khoaN3-mai7.  Iu5-ge7-hoe7 soah to3-lai5 chiong chit e5 su7 kong2 hou7 lau7-pe7 thiaN, lau7-pe7 bo5 chan3-seng5 chong2-si7 tiam7-tiam7 bo5 in3.  Lau7-bo2 koh khah bo5 chan3-seng5 tit8-tit8 phoa3 chhui3-cham5.  M7-ku2 Hui7-bi2 chin chan3-seng5.  I kong2 chheng-lian5-lang5 eng-kai ai3 u7 mou7-hiam2 e5 cheng-sin5, eng-kai lo5-lek8 hun3-tou3, chiong-lai5 chiah u7 seng5-kong e5 ng3-bang7.
Nng7-lau7 khoaN3 kiaN2 long2 khi3 koh jip8-oh8, hut-jian5 kam2-kak chin bo5 lam7, ia7 siuN7 kong2 Teng-liong5 tioh8 liong7-cha2 ka7 i chhoa7, ng3-bang7 thang chou2-chi2 i khi3 hng7-hng7 keng-siong e5 liam7-thau5.  Nng7-lang5 chham-siong5 liau2 chiu7 tang5-i3.  SiuN7-lai5 siuN7-khi3 chiu7 siuN7 kong2 lai5 choe3 Ong5 Bok8-su e5 leng7-chhian-kim Soat-mui5 sio2-chia2.  Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 chit8 e7 kong2, tiuN2-lo2-niu5 bo5 te7 2 ku3 chiu7 chan3-seng5.  Tui3 an2-ni chiu7 iang-lang5 khi3 ka7 Bok8-su kong2.  Ko2-jian5 si7 thian-chok chi-hap8, ia7 sia2-phoe hou7 Teng-liong5, ia7 tham3 Hui7-bi2 e5 i3-kian3.  Tai7-ke long2 chan3-seng5.  Soat-mui5 ia7 chin boan2-chiok chit e5 hun-su7.  Tui3 an2-ni chiu7 chhiang3 le2-pai3 koaN7-tiaN7, ng3-bang7 koh kui2 goeh8-jit8 ku2 pit8-giap8 thang kiat-hun.
Si5-jit8 chin khoai3-koe3 koh bo5 ku2 Teng-liong5 kap Hui7-bi2 long2 pit8-giap8 to3-lai5 lah.  Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 in chit8-ke m7-bian7 kong2, Ong5 Bok8-su in ia7-si7 chin hoaN-hi2.  Soat-mui5 sio2-chia2 pi7-pan7 ke3-chng chin-chiaN3 bo5-eng5.
Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 in nng7-lau7 hoaN-hi2 kin2 ai3 khoaN3-kiN3 sun-a2, chiu7 koaN2 Teng-liong5 tioh8 kin2 kiat-hun, na7-si7 Teng-liong5 sim chu-chu siuN7 beh kap lang5 khi3 goa7-kok choe3 seng-li2, chin ai3 ka-jip8 tui7-siong(隊商).  Sim long2 bo5 sim-chiaN5 ti7 kin2 kiat-hun e5 su7.  Na7-si7 be7 jim2-tit ni5-lau7 e5 pe7-bo2 pek-chhiat iau3-kiu5 chiu7 chin7 hau3-to7 ti7 pit8-giap8 e5 chit8 goeh8-jit8 au7 chiu7 kiat-hun.  Hit-jit8 e5 kiat-hun-sek chin-chiaN3 si7 seng7-tai7.
Sin-hun au7 bit8-goeh8 tiong e5 hu-hu7 chin-chiaN3 si7 tiN-bit8.  Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 in nng7-lau7 ia7 chin-chiaN3 boan2-chiok.  Chit8 ke chhiong-moa2 gim5-si, chhiuN3-koa kam2-sia7 e5 chhio3 siaN.  U7 chit8-jit8 hut-jian5 u7 tian7-po3 lai5, chiu7-si7 Teng-liong5 sia2-phoe hou7 i e5 ho2 peng5-iu2 Khun-hong(昆芳) tham3 mng7 in chhut-kok e5 si5-jit8.  In si7 chou2-chit chit8-tui7 7 e5, to-sou3 si7 chheng-lian5, ia7 kui2 na7 e5 si7 chin lau2-lian7 e5 chong3-lian5 lang5, in koan3-si3 khia5-be2 poaN5-soaN koe3-nia2 ian7-lou7 tui3 hoa3-hoan(化蕃) a2-si7 sim2-mih8 soaN-lai7 e5 lang5 be2 ia2-siu3 e5 phoe5, a2-si7 chhiuN7-ge5, lok8-jiong5 tui3 soaN-nih tit8-tit8 koe3 kau3 In3-tou7 e5 toa7 tou-chhi7, u7-si5 kau3 Bian2-tian7, a2-si7 Siam7-lo5 lai5 choe3 seng-li2.  Jian5-au7 chiu7 koh be2 hoe3 to3-lai5 pun2-kok chit pai2 si7 beh khi3 In3-tou7.  In koat-teng7 ti7 8 goeh8 beh chhut-hoat, kau3 8 goeh8 15 beh ti7 Hun5-lam5 seng2-siaN5 hoe5-hap8.  Chit-si5 u7 kong3-tian7 lai5 hou7 Teng-liong5.  Teng-liong5 chiap tioh8 chit tiuN tian7 chin-chiaN3 chit8-si5 sam-sim liong2-i3.  Na7 beh khi3 ia7 tng ti7 bit8-goeh8-tiong.  Na7 m7-khi3 sit8-chai7 sit-loh8 ho2 ki-hoe7.  I e5 pe7-bu2 si7 kek8-lek8 hoan2-tui3.  Soat-mui5 chit8-sim m7-kam tiong7-hu liam-piN beh chhut-goa7 koh si7 beh khi3 hiah-hng7, chit8-sim iu7 chhiat-bong7 hu-kun seng5-kong.  Hui7-bi2 thau5 kau3 boe2 si7 chan3-seng5 a-ko e5 chian5-chin3.  Kau3-boe2 siuN7 kong2 m7-thang kap lang5 sit-iok, chiu7 hun3-jian5 koat-sim chhut-hoat.  In chit8-tui7 7 e5, chit pai2 lian5 Teng-liong5 hap8-kiong7 u7 8 e5.  Siang7 che7 hoe3 32 hoe3, choe3 tui7-tiuN2.  Teng-liong5 25 hoe3 siang7 chio2-hoe3, peng5-iu2 Khun-hong 27 hoe3, tai7-ke long2 si7 chin gau5 khia5-be2 u7 lek8-liong7 e5 chheng-lian5.
8 goeh8 chhe 1 Teng-liong5 thau3-cha2 khi2-lai5, pi7-pan7 cheng2-che5 chiu7 beh chhut-hoat.  Lau7 pe7-bu2 oa2 toa7-mng5 lau5 bak8-sai2 lai5 sang3.  Ma-mah khan Teng-liong5 e5 chhiu2 chap8 teng-leng5 peh hoan-hu3 kio3 i tioh8 se3-ji7.  Pe7-bo2 sang3 kau3 toa7-mng5 chiu7 theng5-pou7.  HiaN-so2 sio2-kou tit8-tit8 toe3 Teng-liong5 kiaN5 kau3 chin hng7.  Teng-liong5 chit8-chhiu2 khan-be2, chit8-chhiu2 khan Soat-mui5, nng7-lang5 loan5-loan5 put-sia2 m7-kam pun-khui.  Au7-lai5 Hui7-bi2 theng5 kha, niu7 in 2 e5 ka-ti7 kiaN5, kau3 khah khi3 Teng-liong5 chim Soat-mui5, sim-lai7 na2-chun2 u7 kong2 be7 chhut e5 m7-kam, m7-ku2 i2-keng kap lang5 iok, koh ia7 phau7 bu5-han7 e5 kng-beng5, ng3-bang7 thang siong7-chin3 seng5-kong.  Chiu7 koat-jian5 kap ai3-chhe pun-khui, phau7 chheng-lian5 lip8-chi3 chhut hiong-koan, lip8-se3 su7-giap8 put-seng5 su2 put-soan5 e5 sim-chi3, chiu7 chiuN7-be2 hui-pian tit8-tit8 phau2 chin3-cheng5 bo5 koh oat8-thau5.  Soat-mui5 sim chhin-chhiuN7 beh piak-lih8, in-ui7 i bat thiaN hit tiau5 lou7 e5 gui5-hiam2, m7-na7 lou7 phaiN2 u7 toan7-gai5 choat8-phek, ji5-chhiaN2 koh u7 tok8-choa5 beng2-siu3, ia7 u7 chheN-hoan e5 chhut-chhau2.  ChiN5 sui-jian5 ho2 than3, na7-si7 seN3-mia7 si7 12 hun e5 gui5-hiam2.  Na2-chun2 kiat-hiong bi7-lai5 sian iu2-tiau7 e5 khoan2, sou2-i2 chit8-si5 Soat-mui5 e5 sim chhin-chhiuN7 beh piak-lih8 e5 kan-khou2, koh khoaN3 Teng-liong5 chit8 e7 chiuN7 be2, bi2-piN chit8 phah be2 tit8 phau2 bo5 oat8-thau5, soa3 khui siaN khau3, sio2-kou Hui7-bi2 kin2 chau2-lai5 ka7 i an-ui3.  Nng7 e5 sim bun7-bun7 saN khan to3-tng2--lai5.  Hui7-bi2 khoaN3 so2-so2 e5 iu-bun7 sim ia7 soa3 seN-khi2 bu5-han7 e5 tong5-cheng5.  Tauh-ti2 ko-ko m7-chai e7 peng5-an seng5-kong kau3 chhu3 a2-be7?  Na7 be7, i tui3 so2-so2 kak-tek u7 chap8-ji7-ban7-hun e5 be7-tit koe3-sim, in-ui7 chit e5 su7 si7 i chit8 lang5 toa7 chan3-seng5.  Sou2-i2 soa3 siuN7 bo5 oe7 thang kong2, 2 lang5 khan-chhiu2 cheng7-cheng7 kiaN5, na7-si7 Soat-mui5 na2 kiaN5 bo5 theng5 e5 chhit bak8-sai2 sim chin sim-bun7!  Khoa3-sim tiong7-hu......chian5-tou5......m7-chai......?  
2
Teng-liong5 kau3 Hun5-lam5 e5 si5 chiu7 sia2-phoe to3--lai5, chit8-tiuN hou7 pe7-bo2, chit8-tiuN hou7 Soat-mui5.  Hou7 Soat-mui5 hit-tiuN tai7 khai3 si7 sia2 an2-ni.
Goa2 sou2 thiaN3 e5 Mui5.  Tng li7-piat8 e5 si5 goa2 khoaN3 li2 e5 khoan2-sit, sit8-chai7 kau3-giah8 hou7 goa2 e7 chhui3 sim toan7 tng5.  Ah3!  Sou2 thiaN3--e5, na7-si7 ui7-tioh8 chiong-lai5 goa2 ng3-bang7 li2 chhim-chhim chu7-ui3.  Goa2 goan7 seN, si2 ui7-tioh8 li2 lai5 tioh8-boa5.  Na7-si7 chit-pang e5 chhut-goa7 lou7-tou5 si7 12 hun e5 hiam2-iau3, goa2 ng3-bang7 li2 me5-jit8 ui7-tioh8 goa2 ki5-to2, ng3-bang7 e7-tit koh peng5-an kiN3-bin7.  Ti7 hit-si5 thang oan5-seng5 thiaN3-thang3 tiN-bit8 bi2-moa2 e5 ka-teng5.
Li2 sou2 thiaN3 e5 Liong5 sia2.
A.D.  1930.8.15.  sia2 ti7 Hun5-lam5 li2-sia3.
Soat-mui5 chih tioh8 chit-tiuN phoe, chit8-sim hoaN-hi2 na2-chun2 koh kiN3 tioh8 sou2 siau3-liam7 hu-kun e5 bin7.  Chiu7 chhun-chhiu2 theh8 kiaN3-tai5 teng2 kiat-hun nng7-lang5 khia7 saN pai5 sio kau-chhiu2 e5 siong7 lai5 khoaN3.  Chit8-bin7 na2-chun2 sim beh piah-lih8 e5 kan-khou2, put-ti put-kak soa3 hau2 chhut--lai5.  Hui7-bi2 ti7 keh-piah choe3 saN, thiaN pang5-nih u7 lang5 teh hau2 e5 siaN, koaN2-kin2 pang3 chhiu2 ka7 i tham3 khoaN3-mai7, chiu7-chai si7 in A-so2 chit8-chhiu2 theh8 a-hiaN e5 phoe, chit8-chhiu2 theh8 kap a-hiaN kiat-hun e5 siong7 teh hau2.  I koaN2-kin2 chau2 jip8-khi3 kio3 A-so2......  Soat-mui5 chai sio2-kou jip8--lai5, ia7 chiu7 kin2 pang3 siong7 ti7 kiaN3-tai5, theh8 chhiu2-kin chhit bak8-sai2.  Hui7-bi2 chit8-si5 ia7 siuN7 bo5 sim2-mih8 oe7 thang an-ui3 so2-so2.  Chit8-bin7 ia7 chu7-chek, beh chai oe7 hou7 so2-so2 chiah-nih siong-sim lan5 koe3, chiu7 mai3 hiah-nih chek-kek8 lai5 kou2-le7 ko-ko chhut-goa7.  Soa3 siuN7 kong2 ban7-it na7 u7-iaN2 u7 sim2-mih8 put-chhek e tai7-chi3 chek-seng5 long2 i e5.  In-ui7 pe7-bo2 long2 bo5 chan3-seng5, thong ke chi2-u7 i chit8 e5 kek8-lek8 chan3-seng5.  Hui7-bi2 bak8-sai2 ia7 soa3 lau5 chhut--lai5, chio so2-so2 kui7-loh8 ki5-to2.  Put-ti put-kak nng7 e5 hiaN-so2 sio2-kou soa3 lam2-teh hau2.  Hut-jian5 thiaN u7 kha-pou7-siaN teh lai5, chu3-i3 thiaN si7 A-pa e5 siaN, nng7 lang5 chiu7 kin2 tiam7 khi3 chhit bak8-sai2 kap A-pa chheng2-an.  Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 chai in nng7-e5 tha-tu2-a2 tek-khak si7 ui7 in A-ko teh ki5-to2 lau5-bak8-sai2, in-ui7 khoaN3 in nng7-e5 bak8-chiu-phoe5 ham-ham, bak8-chiu ang5-ang5, moa2-bin7 long2 si7 lau5 bak8-sai2 e5 hun5-jiah, koh kun5 u7 kui7 loh8 thou5-kha e5 kiaN-lang5.  Lau7 tiuN2-lo2 chu7-jian5 sim-lai5 ia7-si7 chin sim-bun7 khoa3-sim, chong2-si7 chit8-bin7 kho3 Siong7-te3, koh khoaN3 in nng7 hiaN-so2 sio2-kou hiah sio-thiaN3 ia7 chin siu7 an-ui3, chhui3 chiu7 teN3 chhio3-chhio3 khui-siaN an-ui3 in kong2 “Mih-sai2 hiah-nih koe3-thau5 iu-bun7, ban7-su7 chong2-si7 tioh8 oa2-kho3 Siong7-te3, ng3-bang7 Siong7-te pang-chan7”.  Kong2-liau2 chiu7 khi3.  Hui7-bi2 ia7 eng7 ho2-oe7 an-ui3 so2-so2.  Tui3 hit-am3 khi2 Hui7-bi2 koe3 lai5 kap A-so2 choe3 phoaN7, siong5-siong5 thak8 Seng3-keng saN an-ui3.
Kong2-kau3 Teng-liong5 kap peng5-iu2 hoe7 che5 liau2-au7 chiu7 tui3 Hun5-lam5 chhut-hoat tit8-tit8 ng3 lam5 kiaN5.  Bian2 loa7 ku2 chiu7 kau3 kok-keng2 e5 pian-kai3.  Keng-koe3 it-chhe3 e5 chhiu2-siok8 ho2-se3 chiu7 koe3 kok-keng2 jip8 Bian2-tian7 e5 pak-pou7 pian-kai3, koe3 Pa-ki-su-tan3 jip8 In3-tou7 e5 pak-peng5.  Kau3 jip8 In3-tou7 e5 pak-peng5 e5 si5, lou7-chhau2 i3-goa7 e5 phaiN2, thiaN kong2 si7 ui7-tioh8 kin-ni5 e5 toa7 soat-pheng (Koan5 soaN e5 seh pang loh8--lai5) sou2 choe3 e5 toa7 chui2, kap kui2-na7 pai2 e5 te7-tang7 chhu7 soaN, ti3-kau3 eng2-koe3 u7 lou7 e5 sou2-chai7 soa3 piN3-choe3 bo5 lou7, ke chin hui-siong5 e5 phaiN2 kiaN5.  Jit8-si5 kiaN5 am3-si5 hioh, siong5-siong5 koaN2 be7 kau3 sou2 ai3 kau3 e5 sou2-chai7, in chiu7 tah pou3-piN5 ti7 toa7 chhiu7 kha, a2-si7 kho3 toa7 chioh8-gam5 lai5 tah.  Khiok ia7 che7, chio2 i2-keng u7 tui3 kui-hoa3 e5 hoan-a2 lai5 be2 tam7-poh8 siu3-phoe5.  Kho2-sioh chit8-hang7 chiu7-si7 Teng-liong5 tauh-ti2 si7 thau5 chit8 hoe5, lou7 bo5-sek8, tak8-hang7 chheN-sou, ti7 peN5-lou7 chin gau5 phau2 be2, kau3 chia kam2-kak tak8-hang7 to bo5 li7-pian7, bo5 koan3-si3.  Sou2-i2 tiaN7-tiaN7 kiaN5 choe3 au7-bin7.  U7-si5 choe3 lok8-ngou2-chia2 toe3 be7 tioh8 tin7.  Kai-chai3 Khun-hong-hiaN tai3-liam7 tioh8 tang5 bo2-hau7 chhut-sin e5 hau7-iu2, chiu7 siong5-siong5 tan2--i, u7 si5 tai7-ke hioh-khun3 khoaN3 bo5 Teng-liong5 e5 si5, i chiu7 koh hoe5-thau5 khi3 chhoe7.  Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni m7-na7 chit8-pai2, Teng-liong5 ka-ti7 ia7 kam2-kak tui3 pat8 e5 tui7-oan5 chin put-chu7.  Na7-si7 tai7-ke khiok long2 hian2-chhut tang5-kiaN5 chiu7-si7 tang5-mia7 e5 ho2-i3 bo5 lang5 koe3-chek--i, na7-si7 i ka-ti7 sim-lai7 chin lan5-koe3.  U7 chit8-me5 ti7 tou5-tiong tu2-tioh8 toa7-hou7, hou7 chhin-chhiuN7 kheng-phun5 (kui-phun5 e5 chui2 teh piaN3 loh8-lai5) e5 se3-bin7.  Ji5-chhiaN2 bo5 goeh8 bo5 chheN, lou7 iu7 kut8, chin-chiaN3 si7 chhun3-pou7 lan5 heng5.  Sui-jian5 iau2-boe7 kau3 u5-teng7 e5 lou7-cham7, kou-put-chiong chiu7 koat-teng7 ti7 lou7-tiong chhoe7 sek-tong3 e5 sou2-chai7 lai5 hioh-khun3.  Tai7-ke chham-siong5 chiu7 tah pou3-piN5 ti7 toa7 chioh8-gam5 e5 e7-bin7.  Cha2 bat thiaN hit kak-si3 bat u7 chheN-hoan chhut-chhau2 sou2-i2 tai7-ke chin keng2-kak (keng2-chheN2 cheng-sin5) tiuN-ti5.  Tan3-si7 hit mi5 si7 bo5 goeh8 bo5 chheN hong-kak bo5 beng5(tang-sai lam5-pak jin7 be7 chin).  Sit8-chai7 si7 chit8 e5 chin bo5 peng5-an e5 me5-hng.  Che7-che7 lang5 long2 cheng-sin5 cheng-sin5 m7-kaN2 khun3.  Na7-si7 Teng-liong5 m7-bat tu2-tioh8 chit-khoan2 e5 khun3-khou2, kak-tek chap8-ji7-hun e5 ia3-sian7.  Koh ui7-tioh8 ak-hou7 u7 lioh8-a2 leng2-tioh8 e5 khoan2, thau5-khak hin5-hin5 tang7-tang7, to2-loh8-khi3 put-ti put-kak soa3 khun3 loh8-bin5.  Hut-jian5 khoaN3 tioh8 phok-phok-thiau3 chhin-chhiuN7 se3-chiah chiau2-a2 kho2-ai3 e5 sio2-moai7 ti7 hng7-hng7 chau2 oa2 lai5 chiap-i, kio3 A-ko e5 khoan2-sit.  Chong2-si7 i e5 bak8-chiu e5 si7-soaN3 si7 tit8-tit8 khoaN3 koe3 sio2-moai7 e5 au7-bin7, khia7 ti7 toa7-mng5 piN teh tan2--i e5 ai3-chhe Soat-mui5.  Ah!  Soat-mui5 li2 e5 bi5-chhio3 chaiN2-iuN7 sui2 kau3 an2-ni, oan2-ju5 chit8-lui2 kek8 kho2-ai3, kek8 kiau-hong (kiau-sek koh siu2) bi2-le7 e5 mui5-kui3.  Tu2-tu2 khui hiong3 hu-kun hong3-chhut i choe3-ho2 e5 phang-bi7, kap hou7 lang5 khoaN3 liau2 sim ui7-tioh8 i lai5 to5-chui3 e5 kiau-thai3.  Teng-liong5 siam2-koe3 sio2-moai7, bo5 kap sio2-moai7 chheng2-an tit8-tit8 chau2 kau3 toa7 mng5-piN lai5 chiap i e5 ai3-kheng Soat-mui5, Soat-mui5 siang-chhiu2 chhun khui-khui lai5 chiap i e5 tiong7-hu.  Teng-liong5 chau2-oa2 pho7 Soat-mui5 ti7 heng-cheng5, be7 ki3-tit ti7 au7-bin7 u7 sio2-moai7, ti7 thiaN-mng5 khau2 u7 pe7-bo2 teh khoaN3, chiu7 pho7 Soat-mui5 chhim-chhim e5 jiat8-bun2 (chhim[chhin]-jiat8 e5 saN-chim).  Tu2 kak-tek chap8-ji7-ban7-hun e5 chhin-bit8 an-ui3 e5 si5, hut-jian5 u7 chhin-chhiuN7 chheng-thiN lok8-lui5 siam2-tian7 phek-lek8 e5 siaN, toa7 hoah “chheN-hoan chhut-chhau2, choan5-oan5 chian3-tou3 chun2-pi7”.  M7-chai si7 hoah khah-kin2, a2-si7 chheng3-siaN khah kin2, tui7-tiuN2 thau5 mng5 e5 chheng3 i2-keng tan5.  Teng-liong5 tui3 tiN-bit8 e5 bin5-bang7 kiaN chheN2, sim phok8-phok8-chheng2, chit8-sim chin kiaN, chit8-chun7 e5 leng2-hong chhoe--lai5 kat-tit thong seng-khu e5 ke-bo2-phoe5 long2 gia5 khi2--lai5.  Soa3 lau5 chit8-sin e5 leng2-koaN7.  Kam2-kak thau5-khak phoe5 soa3 phong3 khi2--lai5, kha soa3 phu5-phu5 m7-chai tioh8 choe3 sim2-mih8.  Na7-si7 chit8-sim iau2 teh to5-chui3 i e5 bin5-bang7, oan2-jian5 chhin-chhiuN7 chin, teh siuN7 i kho2-ai3 e5 Mui5 chhin-chhiuN7 mui5-kui3 e5 sui2 koh phang, hit e5 kiau-thau3 e5 kho2-ai3.  Hit e5 khi3-bi7 na2-chun2 iau2 tiau5 ti7 i e5 phiN7, kam2-kak ai3-kheng chu-tun5 e5 ian-chi hek8-chia2 u7 bak ti7 i e5 bin7, jiok8-chhiN2 jiok8-chui3 poaN3 chheN2 poaN3 bo5-chheN2 e5 sun3-kan, tui7-tiuN2 toa7-siaN hoah tioh8 bih-loh8 u3, kheN-a2 tui3-bin7 hit-peng5 e5 chheng3-siaN kin2 lai5, chit-peng5 e5 chheng3 ia7 phah, ti7 am3-me5 bo5 khoaN3 lang5-bin7, chu7-jian5 chhiu7-bak8 chioh8-thau5 long2 bo5 khoaN3 kiN3.  Chi2 u7 khoaN3 khong-tiong chheng3-chi2 e5 hoe2-kng, tui3 an2-ni lai5 chhai-chhek tui3-tek8 e5 hong-kak kap hng7 kin7.  Teng-liong5 chiah tui3 be5-bang7 kiaN-chheN2, chheN-kong5 sa chit8 ki-chheng3 ng3 tui3-tek8 e5 hong-kak ia7 phah khi3.  Chit8-si5 chheng3-chi2 hiu-hiu kio3 e5 siaN thoan5 ti7 kheN-a2 kap soaN-piah e5 tiong-kan, ia7 tui3 hit e5 chheng3-chi2 e5 hoe2-kng sio2-khoa2 u7 khoaN3-tioh8 but8-the2 e5 chun5-chai7.  Hoan-a2 chit-pai2 si7 chin u7 ke3-oe7-tek8 e5 chhut-chhau2, bok8-tek8 si7 ai3 chhiuN2 be2, in-ui7 in u7 8 chiah chin sui2 e5 be2.  Ti7 kheN-a2 hit-bin7 teh phah-chheng3 e5 hoan si7 hi-tiong seng-se3 ke-iaN3 hoah-hiam3 chng-choe3 che7-che7 lang5) , chheng3 tan5 e5 si5 siong5-siong5 thiaN in chhut toa7-siaN kui tin7 hoah-hiu, hit e5 hiu-hiu kio3 e5 siaN in7 moa2 soaN-kheN, put-ti put-kak sit8-chai7 hou7 lang5 kam2-kak sit-taN2, ki-tiong Teng-liong5 si7 siang7-kiaN.  Sim-lai7 seN-khi2 hou7-hoe2 e5 sim.  Hoan-a2 ki5-sit8 iau2 u7 chit8-tin7 kho3 in e5 te7-se3, lou7-chhau2 sek8, tui3 au7-bin7 eng7 pe5--e5, tiam7-tiam7 pau-ui5--lai5, chhiu2 giah8 hoan-a2 pio, io ha5 hoan-to, bi oa2 lai5 kau3 chin pek-sin in long2 m7 chai, kou3 ng3 kheN-a2 hit-peng5, ng3 thau5-cheng5 phah-chheng3.  Chit8 e5 hoan-a2 sun7 Teng-liong5 phah-chheng3 e5 hoe2-kng tui3 au7-bin7 eng7 pio-a2 choh8 khi3, pat8-lang5 e7-hiau2 bih ti7 u3-nih bo5 hiah khoai3 khoaN3 tioh8.  Teng-liong5 be7 hiau2, bih bo5 ho2-se3, khut bo5 loh8 khi3, poaN3 sin lou7-chhut ti7 goa7 bin7.  Sou2-i2 pio-a2 tui3 au7-bin7 chhak8--lai5 tui3-tui3 tioh8 kha-chiah phiaN sim, aih8 chit8-e5 thiaN-kiN3 u7 lang5 to2-loh8-khi3 e5 siaN.  Koh u7 chit8 e5 ou-iaN2 thiau3-oa2 lang5 to2-loh8-khi3 e5 sou2-chai7.  Li7 Teng-liong5 iok 20 pou7 cho2-iu7 si7 Khun-hong bih ti7 chit8 te3 gam5-chioh8 e5 piN-ah, i te7-lak8-kam2 e5 tit8-kak si7 kong2 chham2-lah, chhut-su7 lah.  Hoan-a2 pek-oa2, tong5-su7 sun2-sit lah.  Sou2-i2 kin2-chiong i seng pi7-pan7 ti7 sin-piN e5 chhiu2-liu5-tan5 chhut-lat8 tim3 tui3 lang5 to2-loh8-khi3, kap ou-iaN2 thiau3 oa2-khi3 e5 sou2-chai7.  Hut-jian5 pok8-chou3 e5 siaN chin kiong5-liat8, toe3 hit e5 pok8-cha3 ia7 hoat-chhut hoe2-kng, khoaN3-kiN3 toe3 siaN chit8 e5 ou-toa7-han3 chhiu2 giah8 chit8-ki peh8 ki3-ki3 e5 hoan-to, ai-chit8-siaN chin toa7 siaN chu7 an2-ni ia7 to2 loh khi3, tu2-tu2 siang3 tui3 tai7-seng to2 loh8-khi3 Teng-liong5 e5 sin-piN, chiau3-khoaN3 hit e5 hoan-a2 si7 beh lai5 cham7 Teng-liong5 e5 thau5-khak, soa3 poeh8 i e5 pio-a2 e5 khoan2, koh sun7 chhiu2-liu5-tan5 pok8-cha3 e5 hoe2-kng chiah khoaN3 tioh8 iau2-u7 kui2-na7-e5 hoan-a2 ku-ku teh chau2 ti7 au7-bin7, Khun-hong hoan-sin eng7 te2-chheng3 koh phah-si2 chit8 e5.  Tui7-tiuN2 eng7 tng5-chheng3 ia7 phah si2 chit8 e5.  Tui3 an2-ni hoan-a2 hoah the3-chui2, thiN i2-keng phah-phu2 kng lah, chit e5 hiam2-tiuN5 chiah koe3.
Sit8-chai7 si7 chit8-tiuN5 e5 khou2-chian3.  ThiN kng kiam2-tiam2 jin5, be2, hoe3-mih8 chiah chai Teng-liong5 chha-put-to bo5 ng3-bang7 lah.  In-ui7 hit ki hoan-a2-pio si7 tui3 khah-chiah-phiaN-sim tuh8 jip8 kau3 sim-chong7, ji5-chhiaN2 pio-a2-boe2 u7 boah tok8-ioh8.  Hoeh lau5 chin-che7, bin7 long2 pian3-sek, gan2-sin5 ia7 long2 pian3 lah, kong2-oe7 long2 sit-siaN lah.  Tai7-ke chin iu-bun7, m7-ku2 ia7 be7-tit ui7 i chit8 e5 choan5-tui7 lai5 ti7 chia tam-ian5 siuN ku2 (tam-gou7 ian5-oan7).  Khun-hong chin chhin-chhiat phak loh8-khi3 thou5-nih lai5 thiaN i kong2-oe7.
SiaN toan7-toan7 siok8-siok8, bak8-sai2 si3-lam5-sui5.  Hit e5 oe7 tai7-khai3 si7 kong2 an2-ni, “Ah!  tui3……tui3 tai7-ke… chin put…put-chu7……” theng5 chin ku2 long2 bo5 koh chhut-siaN, Khun-hong ka7 i an-ui3 io5-chhiu2 kong2 “be7-be7.” Ia7 theh8 chhiu2-kin-a2 ka7 i chhit bak8-sai2.  Kau3-boe2 bak8-chiu koh thi2-kim kong2 “Chiong…chiong goa2 e5 thau5……thau5-mng5 koah chit8-chit8 sut-sut-a2……theh8 to3 khi3 hou7……”, soa3 hau2 chhut-lai5 chu7 an2-ni be7 koh kong2, Khun-hong ka7 i kong2 “Li2 si7 kio3-goa2 koah li2 e5 thau5-mng5 theh8 to3-khi3 hou7 li2 e5 po7-bo2 kap hu7-jin5-lang5 khoaN3 a2 m7-si7.” Hit-si5 i2-keng be7 hiau2 in3, kan-ta tim3-thau5 chu7 an2-ni thau5-khak kau loh8-khi3 khui3-tng7.  Khun-hong chiau3 i e5 i3-su3 chiu7 ka7 i koah tam7-poh8 thau5-mng5 khi2-lai5, koh tui3 saN ka7 i koah nng7-liap8 liu2-a2 si7 tang5-e5 sui2-sui2 ka7 i pau choe3-hoe2.  Koh kiam2-tiam2 pat8-mih8, chiu7 chai chit8-chiah be2 sio2-khoa2 tioh8-siong ki5-u5 bo5 sit-loh8.  Tui3 an2-ni m7-kaN2 koh chhian5-oan7, kin2-kin2 chiong Teng-liong5 e5 sin-si ka7 i khng3 ti7 chit8 e5 toa7-chioh8 khang, teng2-bin7 koh kng kui2-na7 te3 chioh8 ka7 i teh-leh, eng7 to ka-i khek chit8 e5 sip8-ji7-ke e5 ki3-ho7, jian5-au7 chiu7 kin2 li7-khui hit sou2-chai7, in-ui7 kiaN-liau2 hoan-a2 khi3 tho2 kiu3-peng, beh po3 oan-siu5 chiu7 ka-poe7 e5 jin5-sou3 lai5 pau-ui5.  Hit-si5 koaN2 put-tek8-chiong chiu7 toa7 li7-hai7, sou2-i2 me5-jit8 kiam-heng5 long2 m7-kaN2 koh theng5 kha.  Hoan-a2 chin-chiaN3 m7-goan7 koh tui--lai5.    
3
Si5-kan chin khoai3-koe3 liam-piN keh 3, 4 goeh8-jit8.  Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 chit8 ke lau7 siau3-lian5 long2 me5-jit8 niau-niau bang7, bang7 khoaN3 u7 siau-sit a2-bo5?  In-ui7 ti7 oa2 goeh8-goa7 jit8 cheng5, siang7 chit8-me5 thong-ke long2 bin5-bang7 phaiN2-bang7.  Tek8-piat8 Soat-mui5 bin5-bang7 Teng-liong5 to3--lai5 kap i saN-si5, hit e5 bin7-iong5 chin phaiN2-khoaN3, Soat-mui5 chhun-chhiu2 beh khan--i e5 si5 hut-jian5 soa3 bo5 khi3, hit-me5 thong-me5 long2 bo5 khun3, kio3 sio2-kou khi2-lai5, tian7-hoe2 choan7-toh8 nng7 lang5 che7 teh sio khoaN3 kau3 thiN-kng.  Sim-tiong kam2-kak chap8-ji7-ban7-hun e5 thong3-khou2.  Tai7-khai3 hit-am3 chiu7-si7 Teng-liong5 sit-su7 hit-me5.  Tui3 hit-si5 khi2 in put-si5 giau-gi5 lun7 Teng-liong5 e5 su7 si7 hiong che7, kiat chio2.  Sou2-i2 bang7 khoaN3 u7 sim2-mih8 siau-sit e5 sim it-hoat chhiat.  Nng7-lau7 bak8-chiu hoe-hoe na7 khoaN3 chit8 e5 lang5 tui3 mng5-khau2 khoe3, a2-si7 lang5-kheh lai5, siong5-siong5 gou7-jin7 choe3 theh8 iu5-pian7--e5 lai5 kap lang5 saN-chioh mng7.  KiN3 lang5 kiN3 mng7 Teng-liong5 e5 siau-sit.  Che ia7-si7 bok8-koai3 chi2-u7 chit e5 hau7-siN, koh tai7-hak8 tu2 pit8-giap8, ia7 tu2 kiat-hun.  Koh khah hou7 lang5 siong-sim--e5, chiu7-si7 chin ho2 kha-chhiu2, Soat-mui5 chiaN3-chiaN3 si7 jip8-mng5-hi2.  I2-keng u7 sin iok 4 goeh8 jit8 lah.  Pak-tou2 tek8-piat8 toa7 e5, u7 lang5 kong2 poh-kaN2 e7 siang-seN, na7 bo5 4 goeh8-jit8 an2-choaN2 pak-tou2 e7 hiah toa7.  KhoaN3 an2-ni na7 ban7-it u7 iaN2 sit-su7 khoaN3 beh chaiN2-iuN7?  Soat-mui5 pak-tou2-lai7 e5 eN-a2 na7 chhut-si3 soa3 m7-bat khoaN3 lau7-pe7, ia7 chit e5 tng siau3-lian5 e5 ma-ma beh an2-choaN2 lai5 chiuN2 chit e5 chhut-si3 chiu7 m7-chai lau7-pe7 e5 kiaN2.  Sit8-chai7 siuN7-liau2 hou7 lang5 be7 kim3-tit e7 sim-sng.  M7-na7 lau7 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 in hu-hu7, chiu7 lian5 Ong5 Bok8-su in nng7 hu-hu7 to ia7-si7 be7 kong2-tit e5 khoa3-sim, sou2-i2 saN-oan si3-oat to-si7 tiaN7 khi3 ka7 i khoaN3-khoaN3 leh.  Soat-mui5 chu7 tui3 chai ka-ti7 u7 sin liau2-au7 chit8-bin7 si7 it-hoat ke-thiN i e5 su-liam7 tiong7-hu.  San2-ki5 na2-kin7 su-liam7 tiong7-hu e5 sim na2-chhiat.  Chit8-sim siuN7 lim5-phun5 e5 si5, si7 thau5 chhiuN7-a2-kiaN2, kau3-si5 hu-kun bo5 ti7 sin-piN m7-chai beh chaiN2-iuN7?  Na7 ban7-it, in-ui7 seN iaN5 ke-chiu2 phang, seN su si3-phiN3 pang.  Koh pak-tou2 hui-siong5 toa7 e5, seng-san2 e5 si5, chit8-tiau5 seN3-mia7 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 hong chian5 e5 teng-hoe2.  Siat-su2……!  Hu-kun bo5 ti7 sin-piN kau3-si5, m7 chai7 beh chaiN2-iuN7?  Na7 seN iaN5, tiong7-hu ti7 sin-piN m7-chai goa7 hoaN-hi2.  Ia7 hit-si5 m7-chai beh ka7 eN-a2 ho7 choe3 sim2-mih8 mia5?  Hu-kun beh chhut-hoat e5 si5 m7-chai i u7 sin, in-ui7 koh kui2-jit8-a2 chiah u7 moa2 chit8 goeh8-jit8.  Hit-si5 m7-chai, kau3 i chhut-hoat liau2 chiah tiaN7 siuN7 beh thou3, chhui3 chhin3 be7 chiah8.  Ka-ki7 bo5 hit e5 keng-giam7 m7-bat, ia7 m7-kaN2 kong2.  Sio2-kou choe3-hoe2 tiam3, si7 cha-bou2 gin2-na2-lang5 ia7 m7-bat, long2 si7 ka7 i ke2-soeh choe3 a-so2 hoan5-lo2 be7 chiah8.  Si7 kau3 chin ku2 lah Ong5 Bok8-su-niu5 lai5 khoaN3 tioh8, chiah ka7 ta-ke (chheN-m2) kong2, au7-lai5 chiah thiah chap8-saN-bi7, an-thai-im2 lai5 hou7 i chiah8.  Sio2-kou chai in so2-so2 ai3 chiah8 sng, sou2-i2 na7 khi3 le2-pai3 e5 si5 tui3 ke-nih koe3 chiu7 kio3 chhe-eng7 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 Sou3-lan5-ah be2 sim2-mih8 li2-a2-kiam5 lah, a2-si7 boe5-a2-koaN to3-lai5 pun in so2-so2 chiah8.  Na7 khoaN3 in so2-so2 sim iu-bun7 teh lau5 bak8-sai2, i chiu7 khi3 kheh-thiaN toaN5 kng3-khim5, toaN5 io-kiaN2-koa.  U7-si5 soa3 chhiuN3, in so2-so2 put-ti7 put-kak u7 si5 bak8-sai2 kam5 ti7 bak8-kin5, chhui3 soa3 chhio3 chhut--lai5.  Koh Soat-mui5 ia7 kui2-hun chai thai-kau3 e5 eng2-hiong2 chiu7 chin7 sou2 e7 m7-ai3 hoan5-lo2, siong5-siong5 kap sio2-kou toaN5-khim5 chhiuN3-koa, gim5-si, u7 si5 khi3 au7-piah kam-a2-hng5 san3-pou7.  U7-si5 tau3 chhi7 ke, ah, tau3 khoan2 ti-chhai3 lai5 be7 ki3-tit iu-bun7 e5 su7.
Kong2 Teng-liong5 si2, Khun-hong eng7 to ka7 i khek e5 ki3-ho7 kek8-ki5 kan2-tan, chiu7-si7 sip8-ji7-ke3 e5 ki3-ho7.  In-ui7 Khun-hong chai Teng-liong5 si7 Ki-tok-tou5.  Ti7 toa7-oh8 choe3-hoe2 chit8-ni5, tai7-ke kam2-cheng5 chin ho2, ia7 bat hou7 Teng-liong5 chio i khi3 hu3 Ki-tok-kau3 e5 chheng-lian5-hoe7.  Sou2-i2 sui-jian5 m7-si7 Ki-tok-tou5 na7-si7 tui3 Ki-tok-kau3 e5 su7 to-siau2 u7 li2-kai2 sou2-i2 chiah e7 eng7 to ka7 i khek sip8-ji7-ke3 e5 ki3-ho7.  Liau2-au7 in chiu7 koh chhut-hoat, in-ui7 me5-jit8 kiam heng5, chiu7 hou7 hoan-a2 jiok boe7 tioh8.  Tui3 hit-si5 in m7-kaN2 koh ti7 soaN-lai7 be2-hoe3 tit8-tit8 kau3 ti7 tou-chhi7.  Au7-lai5 kau3 chit8 e5 siaN5 kio3-choe3 Ka-ni2-kok-tap (?????), chiu7 chiong in e5 be2-phit long2 be7 tiau7, kap ti7 soaN-lai7 sou2 be2 e5 siu3-phoe5 ia7 it-chin7 be7.  Ti7 hia pan7-hoe3, chiu7 che7-chun5 lai5 Giong2-kong, Pin5-nng5-su7, hui-tui3, Sin-ka-pho, tui3 Hiong-kang2 lai5 chiuN7-liok8.  M7-kaN2 koh tui3 goan5-lou7 to3-khi3.  Ia7 tui3 hit pai2 liau2-au7 in hit tui7 chiu7 kai2-san3 m7-kaN2 koh choe3 hit ho7 seng-li2.  Khun-hong chiN5 ia7 i2-keng than3 koe3 chhiu2.  U7 chit8-jit8 toa3 tam7-poh8 le2-mih8, theh8 Teng-liong5 e5 thau5-mng5 kap i ka7 i ka khi2--lai5 e5 nng7 liap8 tang5 liu2-a2, eng7 tiu5-a2-pou3 ka7 i pau ho2 se3, soa3 eng7 chit8 e5 kheh-a2 ka7 i te2-leh beh theh8 lai5 hou7 in e5 pe7-bo2.  Ia7 i thoe3 Teng-liong5 be7 hit-chiah be2, kap ka7 i khoan2 choe3-hoe2, kap iau2 ti7 heng5-li2 pau-ko2-lai7 iau2-boe7 eng7 khi3 e5 chiN5, long2 khui chheng-toaN khoan2 ho2-se3, it-gou7 it-chap8 chin beng5-pek8 beh lai5 sng3 hou7 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2.
Tu2 jip8-mng5 e5 si5 goa7-bin7 e5 kou3-mng5 e5 tng5 kang-a2 kin2 chau2 lai5 po3.  Kong2 u7 chit8 e5 lang5-kheh seN choe3 chin chheng-siu3, u7 le2-mau7 e5 chheng-lian5 beh lai5 chhoe7 lau7 thau5-ke.  Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 chiu7 chhut-lai5, chit8--e5 khoaN3 na2-chun2 chin bin7-sek8, ki5-sit8 long2 m7-bat saN-kiN3-bin7, na7 si7 in-ui7 Khun-hong e5 bin7 chhau3-tu2-kham2 kui2-hun u7 kap Teng-liong5 siang7-khoan2 e5 sou2-chai7, tek8-piat8 e7-kok chiam-chiam, bak8-chiu toa7-toa7 lui2, bak8-bai5 chin toa7-choa7, sin-the2 chin-iong2, ke Teng-liong5 nng7 hoe3, sou2-i2 hong2-hut chin sio-siang7.  Tai7-ke ak-chhiu2 sio mng7 seN3-mia5 chiu7 che7-loh8.  Khun-hong chiu7 kio3 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 choe3 Lim5 siok-hu7, i ia7 ka-ti7 kai3-siau7 si7 seN3 Tan5 mia5 Khun-hong.  Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 chiu7 mng7 i kin-a2-jit8 lai5 e5 iau3-su7.  I chiu7 kong2 i si7 leng7-long5 Teng-liong5 e5 hak8-iu2, Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 chit8 e7 thiaN-kiN3 an2-ni hian2-beng5 10 hun e5 chhin-bit8, kin2 kio3 Hui7-bi2 phang5-te5 lai5 chhiaN2 ko-ko e5 hak8-heng.  Hui7-bi2 kap so2-so2 bih ti7 kheh-thiaN e5 pin5-au7 teh thau-thiaN oe7, tui3 pin5-phang7 khoaN3 chit e5 chheng-lian5 hong2-hut kap A-ko beh siang7-bin7, sou2-i2 kak-tek hui-siong5 e5 ai3-bou7.  Hui7-bi2 kin2 chau2 jip8 khi3 ka7 A-bu2 kong2 “Ma-mah, ti7 kheh-thiaN chit8 e5 chheng-lian5 lai5 tham3 pa-pah.  Hit e5 lang5 e5 bin7 chiok-seng5 goan2 ko-ko, koh kong2 si7 goan2 ko-ko e5 hak8-iu2, ia7 pa-pah kio3-goa2 lai5 phau3-te5.” Lim5 tiuN2-lo2-niu5 chit8 e7 thiaN-kiN3 an2-ni ti7 chau3-kha teh peh thou5-tau7, si7-kin2 pang3-leh, saN-pou7 choe3 nng7-pou7 lap chau2-lai5 kau3 thiaN-nih, chit8 e7 chiu7 chau2 oa2-khi3, mng7 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 kong2 chit ui7 sian-siN bat lan2 Teng-liong5 si7 bo5?  TiuN2-lo2 in3 si7.  TiuN2-lo2-niu5 taN-thau5 siong5-se3 khoaN3 Khun-hong, chin-chiaN3 u7 iaN2 na2 Hui7-bi2 sou2 kong2 chiok-seng5 Teng-liong5 e5 bin7, put-ko3 hi7-a2 pi2 Teng-liong5 khah toa7 tui3, ia7 khah chhau3-lau7 tam7-poh8.  Tu2 teh kong2 e5 si5 Hui7-bi2 phang5-te5 lai5, chiu7 siang-chhiu2 phang5 hou7 Khun-hong, Khun-hong chin kheh-khi3 khia7 khi2-lai5 ia7 eng7 siang-chhiu2 chiap te5.  Sim-lai7 am3-am3 teh siuN7, sit8-chai7 si7 chin sui2, leng2-li7, koh hoat8-phoat, le2-gi5 toan-chong, tai7-toan7 e5 lu2-chu2.  Chit8-si5 khia7 leh soa3 be7 ki3-tit koh che7 loh8 khi3, bak8-chiu khoaN3 Hui7-bi2 bo5-nih.  Hui7-bi2 khoaN3 Khun-hong hiah-nih chu3-bak8 teh khoaN3 i, soa3 kak-tek chin phaiN2-se3 bin7 soa3 chhih loh8-khi3.  M7-ku2 koh chit8-bin7 ia7 si7 chin ai3 khoaN3 chit e5 chheng-lian5 e5 bin7, in-ui7 an2-choaN2 hiah seng5 A-ko e5 bin7, sou2-i2 ho2 taN2 koh giah8-thau5 eng7 bak8-boe2 ka7 i khoaN3-mai7, bo5 phah-sng3 hit e5 chheng-lian5 iau2 si7 bak8-chiu bo5 nih-bak8 bo5 tng2-lun5 e5 teh khoaN3 i, hit-si5 Hui7-bi2 soa3 kian3-siau3 bin7 ang5, bin7 hoat-chhut sio-hong7 chhui3 bun2-chhio3, chiu7 an2-ni oat tui3 pin5-au7 jip8-khi3, koh kap in A-so2 khia7 ti7 hia thiaN oe7.  Khun-hong khoaN3 Hui7-bi2 bin7 ang5 bun2-chhio3 hit-si5 e5 sim-cheng5 chin-chiaN3 u7 bi5-biau7 be7 hiau2 kong2 e5 in3-siong7.  Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 chiu7 koh mng7 kong2 Teng-liong5 e5 kin7-hong2 m7-chai i chai a2-bo5?  Khun-hong chiah lau2-sit8 ka7 i kong2, i chiu7-si7 kap Teng-liong5 choe3-hoe2 khi3 choe3 tui7-siong e5 peng5-iu2.  Boe7 chhut-hoat-cheng5 kong3-tian7 lai5 hou7 Teng-liong5 e5 chiu7-si7 i.
Pin5-au7 nng7 hiaN-so2 sio2-kou chit8 e7 thiaN an2-ni long2 be7 ki3-tit it-chhe3, chiu7 an2-ni chong5 chhut-lai5 khia7 ti7 ma-ma e5 au7-bin7, eng7 bak8-chiu kim-kim siong3 Khun-hong e5 bin7.  Au7-lai5 tiuN2-lo2 chiu7 mng7 kong2 li2 to3--lai5 na7-si7 Teng-liong5 thai2 bo5 to3--lai5?  Khun-hong chit8-si5 soa3 be7-hiau2 in3 in-ui7 khoaN3 tong5-siong7 nng7-ui7 pe7-bo2 chiah lau7, ia7 Teng-liong5 e5 thai3-thai3 pak-tou2 hiah toa7 e5, chiu7 aN3-thau5 thou2 chit8 e7 toa7-khui3.  Se3-se3 siaN kong2 “Teng-liong5 kun i2-keng koe3-sin lah,” hit e5 siaN-im chin se3, siaN boe2 e7 chhoah.  Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 thiaN chit8 e7 pang3-siaN toa7 khau3.  TiuN2-lo2-niu5 chu7 an2-ni khau3 chit8 ku3 “Goa2 khou2-ah,” chiu7 tiam7-tiam7 lek loh8-khi3.  Hui7-bi2 ia7 khau3 kau3 be7 tng2-siaN, Soat-mui5 chu7 an2-ni un ti7 thou5-kha bin7 phak ti7 piah-nih, siaN-siaN ku3-ku3 “A-hu-ah!  Goa2 taN beh chaiN2-iuN7 ah?  A-hu-ah!  Goa2 taN beh chaiN2-iuN7 ah!!” Khah liam7 ia7-si7 chit ku3, in-ui7 i i3-sek chian5-tou5 ban7-su7 hiu-i3.  It-chhe3 e5 kng-beng5, heng7-hok, tiN-bit8, bi2-moa2, li2-siong2 e5 ka-teng5 i2-keng hun2-chhui3 khi3 lah.  Ah!  I pak-tou2 te2 e5 kiaN2 bo5 pe7 lah.  M7-bat lau7-pe7 e5 kiaN2 li2 si7 ho5-teng2 e5 kho2-lin5 ah?  Ah!  Chhan3-lan7 e5 chheng-chhun bo5 khi3 lah, it-chhe3 e5 it-chhe3 ou-am3 lah.  Goa2 e5 kiaN3-tai5, goa2 e5 sin-niu5-saN, kap sou2 pi7-pan7 e5 hoa3-chong-phin2 bo5 lou7-eng7 lah.  Bo5 sou2 thiaN3 e5 thang khoaN3-kou3 goa2 lah.  “Ah!  A-hu ah!  TaN beh chaiN2-iuN7 ah!!” Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 khoaN3 tiuN2-lo2-niu5 hun7-khi3 kin2-kin2 chiong tiuN2-lo2-niu5 ka7 i pho7 ti7 sa-hoat tng5 phong3-i2 hou7 i to2 tit8-tit8 an-cheng7.  Khun-hong koaN2-kin2 chau2 tui3 au7-boe2 khi3 chhiuN7 chit8 poah8 leng2-chui2 un3 bin7-kin lai5 tau3-u3.  Hui7-bi2 ia7 peh khi2--lai5 kin2 chau2-khi3 lau5-teng2 thin5 chit8-poe pho-to5-chiu2 lai5, chiu7 eng7 se3 te5-si5 ka7 i koan3.  Theng5 chit8-e7-a2 chiu7 cheng-sin5, khoaN3 tiong7-hu, Hui7-bi2, Khun-hong long2 ti7 sin-piN, Soat-mui5 khoaN3 ta-ke an2-ni ia7 peh khi2--lai5 chhit bak8-sai2 lai5 an-ui3 ta-ke.  Chit8-si5 soa3 na2 kak-tek chit8-ke thoan5-iN5 e5 khoan2-sit.  Chhit-chhian5 peh-chhian5 soa3 hong7-hun am3, Khun-hong ia7 chiu7 saN-si5 beh to3-khi3.  Na7-si7 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 kap tiuN2-lo2-niu5 long2 kek8-lek8 ka7 i ban2-liu5.  Hit-me5-hng chiu7 tiam3 ti7 in hia hou7 in chhiaN2.  Chiah8 pa2 in chiu7 ka-teng5 le2-pai3.  Tai7-ke chin iu-bun7, Ong5 Bok8-su in hu-hu7 thiaN chit e5 siau-sit ia7 lai5, koh ke-a2-lai7 kui2-na7 e5 tng-chit hoe7-iu2 ia7 lai5 saN an-ui3.  Soa3 na2 khui tui-to7 hoe7.  Ti7 hit e5 sek tiong Khun-hong chin siong5-se3 kong2-khi2 hit e5 keng-koe3, soa3 chiong thau5-mng5 kap liu2-a2, kap sou2 u7 e5 chiN5, i2-kip8 chheng-toaN long2 theh8 chhut-lai5 hou7 in khoaN3.  Tai7-ke chin iu-bun7, chong2-si7 Ong5 Bok8-su khou2-khng3 tai7-ke tioh8 ti7 Chu2 lai5 siu7 an-ui3.  Tai7-ke sui-bong2 iu-bun7 iau2-ku2 bo5 koe3-thau5, chiu7 gim5-si ki5-to2 soaN3-hoe7.
Na7 [Tan7]-si7 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2, kap tiuN2-lo2-niu5 chhim-chhim kam2-kek Khun-hong e5 ho2-i3, koh choe3 lang5 tiong-hou7, sou2-i2 soa3 u7 chit e5 ian5, na2-chun2 ai3 jin7 i choe3 gi7-chu2 e5 khoan2, chong2-si7 m7-kaN2 sui5-pian7 khui-chhui3, chiu7 tit8-tit8 ka7 i lau5, na7-si7 Hui7-bi2 khoaN3 pe7-bo2 e5 ho2-i3, koh khoaN3 Khun-hong e5 khoan2 chu7-jian5 ia7 seN-khi2 ai3-bou7 e5 sim, sou2-i2 tng-ti7 Khun-hong tiam3 ti7 in tau e5 si5, u7 na2 chhin-chhiuN7 hiaN-moai7 e5 chhin-bit8.  Chong2-si7 su7-su7 se3-ji7, m7-kaN2 hih-hiauh, tek8-piat8 lan2 si7 sin3 Chu2 e5 lang5, sou2-i2 chin tai7-hong, sin7-tiong7, u7 le2-mau7 e5 saN kau-poe5, na7-si7 nng7 e5 chheng-lian5 tai7-ke sim-lai7 u7 chit8 e5 kong2 be7 chhut e5 ho2-kam2 che si7 su7-sit8.  
4
Khun-hong ti7 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 in tau bak8-chit-nih soa3 toa3 5, 6 jit8, in-ui7 in chin hoaN-hi2 i tiam3 leh.  Khun-hong tiam3 liau2 ia7 chin u7 chhu3-bi7, in-ui7 u7 Hui7-bi2 thang choe3 phoaN7 kong2 oe7.  In ia7 chin sin3-iong7 i, sou2-i2 in nng7 e5 chheng-lian5 tiaN7 chhoa7-chhut chhoa7-jip8.  U7 si5 khi3 soaN-nih ban2 pek-hap8-hoe.  U7-si5 khi3 khe-a2 tio3-hi5, oan2-ju5 hiaN moai7 e5 chhin-bit8.  Tan3-si7 in nng7-lang5 e5 sim-keng2 bo5 tu2-tu2 siang7-khoan2.  Chit8 e5 si7 teh siuN7 khah-hng7 khah-chhim e5 tai7-chi3, si7 iu2-i3-tek e5 kau-poe5.  Chit8 e5 si7 ui7 su-liam7 ko-ko, si7 sun5-kiat e5 iu2-gi5 na7-tiaN7.  Pai3 6 lah, Khun-hong chiu7 siuN7 beh to3-khi3 chiu7 kap in saN-si5.  Bo5 phah-sng3 Lim5 TiuN2-lo2-niu5 soa3 koh siuN7 khi2 Teng-liong5 lai5 pi-siong, ui7-tioh8 an2-ni tai7-ke soa3 koh kiong5 lau5 i bin5-a2-jit8 tai7-ke thang choe3-hoe2 khi3 le2-pai3.  Khun-hong khoaN3 in e5 chhin-chhiat, chiu7 koh tiam3 leh.  Bin5-a2-jit8 tai7-ke chiu7 chhoa7-chhoa7 khi3 le2-pai3.  Nng7 hiaN-so2 sio2-kou hu7-tam ka3 Iu3-ti7-kho.  A-so2 toaN5 khim5, Hui7-bi2 chhoa7 hak8-seng iu5-hi3 chhiuN3-koa.  Bo5 chit8-hang7 bo5 m7 chhim-chhim in2-khi2 Khun-hong to-tai7 e5 chu3-i3 kap su-liam7.  Le2-pai3 soah tai7-ke ui5 oa2 lai5 ka7 tiuN2-lo2-niu5 ai-siong an-ui3.  Ki5-sit8 chiah e5 su7 si7 ke-thiN choe3 lau7-bu2 e5 lang5 e5 siong-sim, chit8-si5 tiuN2-lo2-niu5 sim-chong7 soa3 koh bo5 lat8 beh to2 loh8-khi3.  Tai7-khai3 si7 lang5 ui5 siuN-che7, ia7 kong2 siuN-che7 oe7, koh chin siong-sim.  Soat-mui5 kap Hui7-bi2 khoaN3 ma-mah bin7 tng2-sek tit8-tit8 beh be7-kou3-tit, kin2 ka7 i chhah jip8-khi3 Bok8-su e5 pang5 hioh-khun3.  Au7-lai5 put-chi2 khah song2-khoai3 chiah hou7 Hui7-bi2 kap Khun-hong chit8 lang5 thiaN7 chit8 peng5, un-un-a2 kiaN5 to3-khi3.  Pai3-tng5 ti7 ke-a2-thau5, Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 in chhu3 khah ti7 ke-a2-boe2, chiam2-jian5 u7 kui2-na7 pah-pou7 e5 hng7.  Chit8 lang5 thiaN7 chit8-peng5 soa3 chhin-chhiuN7 chin-chiaN3 e5 hiaN-moai7 e5 kam2-kak.  Lau7 tiuN2-lo2 kap sim-pu7 Soat-mui5 toe3 ti7 sin-piN ban7-ban7 kiaN5 kau3 chhu3.  Tai7-ke chin siu7 an-ui3.  Tui3 an2-ni Khun-hong iu7-koh ke tiam3 hia kui2-na7-jit8.
U7 chit8-jit8 koat-teng7 bin5-a2-jit8 beh to3-khi3, chiu7 koh choe3-hoe2 khi3 ban2 pek-hap8-hoe, kau3 ti7 soaN-nih e5 toa7 chhiu7 kha, u7 chit8-te3 toa7 chioh8 chheng-khi3 chheng-khi3, Khun-hong chiu7 chiong i ka-ti7 e5 chhiu2-kin-a2 thi2-khui chhu ti7 chioh8-thau5 teng2, khan Hui7-bi2 e5 chhiu2 chhiaN2 i che7.  Hui7-bi2 chiu7 che7, i ka-ti7 ia7 che7 ti7 Hui7-bi2 e5 sin-piN.  Hian2-chhut ban7-hun e5 chhin-chhiat chhio3-iong5 e5 bin7 tui3 Hui7-bi2 kong2 “Hui7-bi2 sio2-chia2, goa2 tui3 li2 chin sit-le2, goa2 siuN7 beh tui3 li2 kong2 chit8-ku3 oe7, na7-si7 chin tiu-tu5 kong2 long2 be7 chhut--lai5, m7-chai m-chai…?” Hui7-bi2 khoaN3 i thun-thun thou3-thou3 i-ni ng3-nngh8, chiu7 ho2-i3 ka7 i kong2 “Beh thai2 u7 sim2-mih8 sit-le2, li2 lai5, goan2 chin siu7 an-ui3, chin hoaN-hi2 li2 e5 pang-bang5, goan2 eng-kai ka7 li2 seh-sia7, na2-li2 u7 sit-le2 e5 sou2-chai7.” “M7-si7 an2-ni lah, si7 goa2 chit-si5 beh ka7 li2 kong2 chit8 ku3 oe7, tui3 li2 khah sit-le2, goa2 si7 ng3-bang7 li2 m7-thang siu7-khi3.” “Be7-be7, chhiaN2 li2 kong2, bo5-lun7 li2 kong2 sim2-mih8 goa2 to be7 siu7-khi3, chhiaN2 li2 an-sim.” Tui3 an2-ni Khun-hong chiu7 chin an-sim, khan Hui7-bi2 e5 chhiu2 khi2-lai5 chim, ia7 ka7 i kong2 “Hui7 moai7-moai7 goa2 sit8-chai7 chin thiaN3 li2, goa2 ng3-bang7 e7-tit eng2-oan2 thiaN3--li2…….” Hui7-bi2 thiaN chit kau3 oe7 sim hut-jian5 kam2-kak chin kin2-tiong, tan3-si7 bo5 chek-si5 in3--i, chiu7 aN3-io eng7 cheng2-thau5-a2 oe7 ti7 thou5-kha e5 thou5-soa teng2, oe7 chit8 boe2 hi5, Khun-hong khoaN3 hit e5 hi5 e5 tou5, sim chin hoaN-hi2, i e5 i3-su3 si7 kong2 Hui7-bi2 in2--i, piau2-si7 nng7-lang5 saN tek-i3 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 hi5 tit-tioh8 chui2 e5 hoaN-hi2.  Ki5-sit8 m7-si7, na7-si7 Khun-hong bo5 beng5 hit e5 i3-su3, chiu7 koh tit8-tit8 kong2 chin che7 ho2-i3 e5 oe7.  Ti3-kau3 Hui7-bi2 put-tek-i2 chiu7 koh aN3-io eng7 cheng2-thau5-a2 oe7 sip8-ji7-ke3 e5 ki3-ho7.  Hit-si5 i chiah hut-jian5 hiau2-ngou7, chai Hui7-bi2 oe7 “Hi5,” oe7 “Sip8-ji7-ke3” long2 si7 piau2-hian7 i si7 Ki-tok-tou5.  Bo5 sui-pian7 beh kap bi7-sin3-chia2 kiat-hun.  Na7-si7 Khun-hong e5 sim si7 chin-chhiat e5 kiu5-ai3.  Kou-put-chiong Hui7-bi2 chiu7 theng5-sin khi2--lai5 eng7 chin giam5-siok tai7-hong e5 khoan2-sit, lau2-lau2 sit8-sit8 ka7 i kong2.
“Khun-hong-ko, chin to-sia7 li2 e5 ho2-i3.  Na7-si7 li2, goa2 e5 kau-poe5, goa2 si7 chun-keng3 li2 choe3 goa2 e5 ko-ko e5 hak8-heng, kam2-sia7 li2 koe3-khi3 tui3 goan2 A-ko e5 ho2-i3.  Na7-si7 khah chhim e5 su7, chit si5 goa2 bo5 teh siuN7.
1.  Goa2 si7 chit8 e5 soaN-lai7 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2, goa2 m7-kaN2 siuN7 sim2-mih8, goa2 chai goa2 be7 kham-tit.
2.  Lun7 khah chhim e5 su7, goa2 tioh8 chun-tiong7 pe7-bo2.  Goa2 e5 pe7-bo2 boe7 tang5-i3 e5 i2-cheng5, goa2 be7-tit seng kap li2 iok-sok sim2-mih8.
3.  U7 chit8-hang7 ui5-lan5 e5 su7, chiu7-si7 goan2 si7 Ki-tok-tou5.  Li2, goa2 sin3-giong2 pou7-tiau bo5 it-ti3, chiong-lai5 ui7 chit e5 su7 un2-tang3 u7 kan-khou2.
Sou2-i2 goa2 chhiaN2 Khun-hong-ko chhim-siuN7.  Goa2 siuN7 lan2 e5 chhin-bit8, kau3 ti7 iu2-gi5 e5 theng5-tou7 chiu7 ho2.  Goa2 ia7 hoaN-hi2 li2 an-ui3 goa2 e5 pe7-bo2, sou2-i2 chhim-chhim ka7 li2 seh-sia7.
Khun-hong khoaN3 tioh8 Hui7-bi2 e5 tai7-hong, cheng-kiat it-hoat kam2-hok8.  Soa3 kam2-kak beh ban2 sui2 e5 mui5-kai3 m7-si7 sui-pian7 kho2-khi, u7 i lai7-lai7 e5 chhi3.  M7-na7 m7-kaN2 siu7-khi3 soa3 it-hoat hian2-beng5 i e5 un-khun5, ho2-i3 lai5 kou-chiaN5 Hui7-bi2.  Ti7 bu5-i3 e5 tiong-kan, hut-jian5 pho7 Hui7-bi2 lai5 chim--i.  Hui7-bi2 chin siu7-khi3 chiu7 an2-ni khia7 khi2--lai5, tiam7-tiam7 oat to3-khi3.  To3-khi3 kau3-chhu3 jip8-khi3 pang5-nih mng5 koaiN-leh, phak ti7 i peng5-si5 teh thak8-chheh sia2-ji7 e5 toh-a2 lau5 bak8-sai2.  I e5 sim chin kan-khou2, ka-ti7 kiam2-tiam2 i e5 heng5-ui5, tai7-khai3 si7 tui3 siuN7 su-liam7 ko-ko, sim bo5-liau5 khang-hi, hut-jian5 tit-tioh8 iN7-seng3 lam5 peng5-iu2, chhin-chhiuN7 hiaN-ko e5 khoan2-sit, chiu7 soa3 sit-loh8 kin2-sin7, bo5 kheh-khi3 e5 heng5-tong7, phah-sng3 si7 tui3 an2-ni e5 siu7 gou7-hoe7.  Kin-ni5 Hui7-bi2 si7 21 hoe3, Khun-hong si7 27 hoe3, tai7-ke boe7 chhoa7, boe7 ke3.  Nng7 e5 chheng-lian5 choe3-hoe2, bo5 siu7 koan2-sok, hong2-hut bo5 gi5-gou7 e5 si5, chiu7 an3-cheng5 chhin-chhiuN7 thiau-phi5 e5 chok-giat8 gin2-na2 thau chau2-jip8 khi3 sim-pang5-nih, ki3-jian5 hou7 i thau-chau2-jip8--khi3, chin-chiaN3 si7 oh-tit koaN2 chhut-khi3.  Hui7-bi2 chhim-chhim thong3-hoe2 i ka-ti7 choe3 sin3 Chu2 e5 lu2-chu2, bo5 kau3-giah8 kin2-sin7 lai5 siu7 lam5 peng5-iu2 e5 gou7-hoe7.  I ka-ti7 chin7-chek, ia7 kam2-kak siu7 chin toa7 e5 bu2-jiok8.
Khun-hong siu7 si-ai3 (施愛 ai3-cheng5 beh hou7--lang5) e5 ku7-choat8, chit8-si5 kam2-kak bu5-beng5-hoe2 toa7-toh8.  M7-chai siu7-khi3 an2-choaN2, soa3 chu7-po7 chu7-khi3 e5 khoan2-sit, khia7 tiam3 hia gang7-gang7 khoaN3 Hui7-bi2 chau2 loh8 soaN bo5 saN-si5 choe3 i khi3 e5 poe7-iaN2, hou7-chu.  Ti7 thiaN3-e5 lai7-bin7 khoaN3 sim2-mih8, thiaN sim2-mih8 to sui2.  Chit8-sim khi3 Hui7-bi2 choe3 i khi3, chit8-sim soa3 kam2-poe7 Hui7-bi2 e5 jin5-keh e5 ko-kiat, u7 chi3-khi3.  Tui3 pe7-bu2 iu2-hau3, tui3 chong-kau3 tiong-sit8.  Tui3 iu2-gi5-ai3, kap loan5-ai3 u7 hun-beng5, sin5-seng3 put-kho2 chhim-hoan7.  SiuN7-lai5 siuN7-khi3, koh si7 lai5 lang5-tau choe3 lang5-kheh, soa3 m7-kaN2 siu7-khi3.  Chong2-si7 chin pai7-heng3, chin sit-i3, ka-ti7 chit8 e5 bo5-liau5 bo5-liau5 tui3 soaN-teng2 un-un-a2 tong7 loh8--lai5.  Soa3 bo5 ban2 hoe, pun2 si7 siuN7 ban2 tam7-poh8 to3-khi3 thang sang3 peng5-iu2, taN lian7 tha-tu2-a2 ti7 lou7-nih beh lai5 kap Hui7-bi2 choe3-hoe2 ban2 e5 kui2-lui2-a2 ia7 thiah-thiah phaiN2 hiat-kak8 tiam3 lou7-piN.  To3-khi3 kau3 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 tau chin bo5-i3.  So5-khi3 kheh-thiaN ka-ti7 chit8 e5 tiam7-tiam7 che7, chin phaiN2-se3 theh8 sin-bun5 om-bin7, na2-chun2 khun3-khi3 e5 khoan2-sit.
Hit-am3 chiah8-png7 Hui7-bi2 ia7 kak-tek chin phaiN2-se3, in-ui7 tui3 lai5 lan2-tau e5 lang5-kheh, hiah ho2-i3 ka7 lang5 lau5, ku7-choat e5 si5 m7 chai piau2-ian2 liau2 e7 siuN koe3 hoe2 a2-be7?  M7-ku2 si7 chhut tui3 bu5-sia5 thian-chin e5 pun2-sim.  Sim ka-ti7 chu7-sin3 si7 tioh8.  In-ui7 sun5-kiat, cheng3-keng tek-khak m7-thang kap siok8-hoa3, chha-put-to, ma2-ma2 hu-hu saN hun7-chap8.  Chong2-si7 lang5-kheh iau2 ti7 lan2 tau, ia7-si7 ai3 piau2-si7 ho2-i3.  Khun-hong khoaN3 Hui7-bi2 ti7 chiah8 am3-tng3 peng5-jian5 piau2-si7 ho2-i3, chiu7 chin siu7 an-ui3.  Keh chai2-khi2 chiu7 saN-si5 to3-khi3.  An2-ni thau5-boe2 tiam3 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2-tau oa2 chiaN5-chap8-jit8.  Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 chit8 ke ia7 ko2-jian5 toa7-toa5 siu7 an-ui3.
Kong2 Khun-hong to-si7 toa7-oh8 pit8-giap8, koh siong-tong e5 ka-teng5.  Ka-ti7 su7-giap8 ia7 seng5-kong, an2-choaN2 e7 kau3 27 hoe3 iau2-boe7 chhoa7, che si7 chit8 e5 chin-chhim e5 goan5-in, bo5 kong2 lin2 long2 m7-chai.  Goan5-in si7 Khun-hong e5 lau7-pe7 cha2-si5 choe3 koaN se3-ka-te2, na7-si7 kho2-sioh cha2-si2.  Lau7-bu2 si7 chit8 e5 bu2-koaN chin u7 se3-lek8 e5 chiong-kun thoan5-tiuN2 e5 sio2-moai7.  Tiong7-hu si2 liau2 chiu7 chiuN2 chheng-koaN2, chi2-u7 chiuN2 chit-e5 Khun-hong, si7 kim--e5, gin5--e5, po2-poe3 ni-ni, na2-chun2 ou7-hioh8 phang5 chin-chu lai5 chiuN2 chit e5 kiaN2.  Ia7 chu7-se3 ui7 Khun-hong io chit8 e5 sim [sin]-pu7-a2.  M7-si7 ui7 bo5 chiN5 lai5 io, si7 ui7 ai3 u7 phoaN7, ai3 chit8 tui3 kiaN2 khah nau7-jiat8.  Chit e5 sim-pu7-a2 ia7-si7 siong-tong e5 mng5-hong e5 chhian-kim, tai7-ke si7 se3-kau e5 peng5-iu2.  Kau3 toa7-han3 ia7 u7 khi3 thak8 lu2-chu2 ko-tiong.  SeN-choe3 ia7-si7 chin sui2, chin u7 ta-ke-ian5.  Chhut-si3 chiu7-si7 pai3-put8-a2 lang5, ta-ke si7 jiat8-sim e5 chhai3-kou, sou2-i2 kin-sui5 ta-ke sio-hiuN liam7-keng, pai3-put8 tak8-hang7 to chin koan3-si3.  Chhai3-iu2 lai5-ong2 ia7 e7-chu2 chhai3-toh.  Siong5-siong5 kin ta-ke khi3 sui5-hiuN.  Ni5-cheh chhoe-koe2 pak8-chang3, hau3 mng5-khau2, pan7 seng-le2, tian7-chiu2, poah8-poe ku3 li2 kong2 kiaN7-kiaN7 to e7.  It-hoat tit ta-ke thiaN3.  Kin-ni5 26 hoe3 lah, chu7 kui2-na7-ni5 cheng5 in ta-ke chiu7 beh ka7 i choe3 toa7-lang5, ka7 i thiah8 ji7-sou2 kong2 “Li2,” Li2 si7 li2-a2, tho5-li2 put-gian5 ha7 chu7 seng5 ke(桃李不言下自成畦) , i3-su3 si7 kong2 tho5-a2, li2-a2 kau3 si5 na7 sek8 m7-bian2 hou-kio3, lang5 chu7-jian5 e7 lai5 chhin-kin7, e7-bin7 bo5 lou7 ia7 e7 piN3 u7 lou7.  “Siu3” si7 siu3-khi3, chhut-lui7 poat8-chui7, tok8-chhut bo5 lang5 e7-tit kap i pi2 ui5-chi “Siu3.” “Chhun” si7 chhun-thiN, ban7-but8 to hian2-chhut eng5-hian2, puh-ge5 thou3-iN2 bou7-seng7, chhun ni5-ni5 chhun, ban7-lian5 to-si7 chhun.  Sou2-i2 Li2 Siu3-chhun(李秀春) chit e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 si7 chiok ho2 mia7.  Chai7 ka im3 pe7-bo2, chhut-mng5 im3 ang-sai3, lian7 kiaN2-sun.  Tan5-ka3 e7 hoat-chai5 tou si7 tui3 chit e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 e5 sou2-ti3.  Koh si7 kap ta-ke tang5-sim liam7-keng, le2-hut8 chiah u7 kin-a2-jit8 Tan5--ka3 e5 ang5-un7(紅運).  Ta-ke it-hoat thiaN3--i, eng7 chhian-hong pek-ke3 ka3 i tioh8 an2-choaN2 lai5 tho2-ho2 Khun-hong.  Na7-si7 bo5-lun7 an2-choaN2 choe3 Khun-hong to bo5 sim-sek, lang5 na7 lai5 po3 chhin-chiaN5 in lau7-bu2 tak8-e5 to ka7-lang5 si5, u7 e5 hou7 i hian7 siau-tok8, sou2-i2 soa3 bo5 lang5 kaN2 khi3 kong2 chhin-chiaN5, chit8-ni5 koe3 chit8-ni5, Khun-hong e7 khi3 goa7-kok choe3 tui7-siong goan5-in ia7 si7 ui7-tioh8 an2-ni, to bo5 ai3 tiam3 chhu3-nih kap Siu3-chhun saN kiN3-bin7.  Chit-chan5-su7 si7 chit e5 ka-teng5 chin toa7 e5 gam5.  Chit-pai2 Khun-hong ka-ti7 hoat-kian3 tioh8 i sim-ai3 e5 lu2 peng5-iu2, sit8-chai7 si7 pang3 be7-li7.  Na7-si7 Hui7-bi2 kian-chhi5 sin3-giong2, chiau3 khoaN3 chit e5 chhin-chiaN5 si7 u7 siong-tong e5 khun3-lan5.  Khun-hong to3-khi3 chek-si5 sia2 phoe lai5 kiu5-chhin. 
5
Khun-hong to3-khi3 me5-jit8 tiaN7-tiaN7 siau3-liam7 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 in e5 ho2 khoan2-thai7.  Chiong-tiong me5-jit8 bo5-lang3 e5 su-liam7 Hui7-bi2.  Ti7 thiaN-nih, ti7 pang5-nih, ti7 goa7-bin7 a2-si7 ti7 lai7-bin7 teh khoaN3 chheh, bo5-m7 tiaN7-tiaN7 u7 Hui7-bi2 e5 chhio3-siaN, kap i e5 bin7-iong5, tek8-piat8 ba-bun2-chhio3 sou2 hian2-chhut chhui3-phoe2 siang-peng5 e5 chiu2-khut-a2, kap hit-tui3 beng5-bun2 e5 bak8-sin5, sit8-chai7 bo5 hoat-hou7 thang tui3 i e5 sim-te2 chhit-khi2--lai5.  Kau3 au7-lai5 i chiu7 koat-sim sia2-phoe khi3 kiu5-chhin.  Ia7 soa3 ka7 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 in seh to-sia7.  Seh to-sia7 e5 phoe kap kiu5-hun e5 phoe tit8-chiap sia2 hou7 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2.  Hit e5 oe7 kiong-keng3 sin7-tiong7 u7 le2-mau7, hian2-beng5 chap8-ji7-hun e5 un-khun5 e5 kiu5-chhin.  Na7-si7 leng7-goa7 sia2 chit8-tiuN hou7 Hui7-bi2, soa3 sia2 chit8 te3 su7-cheng5-si ti7 lai7-bin7.
Hit tiuN phoe chin kan2, na7-si7 i3-gi7 chin chhim-tiong5.  Tai7-khai3 si7 sia2 an2-ni:
“Chhin-ai3 e5 Hui7 moai7.  Tui3 li7-khui li2 liau2-au7 to3--lai5, chit8-lou7 kau3-chhu3 put-lun7 ti7 sim2-mih8 sou2-chai7, bo5-si5 bo5-khek bo5 m7 siau3-liam7 li2.  Bak8-chiu na7 pang3-kheh chiu7 khoaN3 li2 e5 bin7 ti7 bak8-cheng5.  Ti7 sui5 [sui7]-bin5 tiong tiaN7-tiaN7 hou7 li2 e5 chhio3-siaN kiaN-chhiN2.  Goa2 chin-chiaN3 ng3-bang7 e7-tit it-seng siong5-siong5 khoaN3 li2 e5 chhio3-iong5 ti7 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  Goa2 i2-keng u7 chiong chit e5 kiu5-chhin e5 su7 tit8-chiap sia2 phoe hou7 leng7-chun, kau3-si5 leng7-chun na7 teng-kiu5 li2 e5 i3-kian3 e5 si5 ng3-bang7 li2 hoaN-hi2 eng3-seng5.  Chhian-ban7 lang2 e5 saN-thiaN3 kau3 eng2-oan2.
Ia7 goa2 soa3 gu7-kam2 cho3 chit8 siu2 si.
“Chhou-bun2”（初吻).
(Siau3-liam7 ti7 soaN-teng2 choe3-hoe2 ban2 pek-hap8-hoe e5 chhiu7-kha) 
1.  Goa2 e5 sim chin thiong3-khoai3, koh kek8-tong7, kim3 be7-tiau5 chiah chim--li2, Goa2 kak-tek li2 nng2-loan2 sio-lo7 e5 chu-tun5 u7 bo5 pi2 e5 sin5-ki5, Goa2 sui-jian5 bo5 tai7-seng kiu5, lai5 tit li2 un2-chun2 hoaN-hi2, Na7-si7 tui3 chit8-e5 lu2-chu2 chim-chhui3, goa2 si7 thau5 chit8-pai2 choe3 an2-ni.  
Ho5
M7-thang kan-ta bin7 ang5 chhui3 tu7-tu7, chhui3-tun5 iu7 khiau3 khi2-khi2, Ka7 goa2 kong2 lah!  Li2 kiam2 bo5 kap goa2 tong5-kam2 siang7-khoan2 thiaN3-cheng5 e5 tiN?  
2.  ChhiaN2 li2 boh-tit chhim-chhim gin5 goa2, au7-lai5 koh ka7 goa2 chek-pi7, Goa2 che cheng5-put-chu7-kim3 e5 heng5-tong7, chin-chiaN3 si7 chhut tui3 thiaN3-thang3 li2, Goa2 tui3 li2 sou2 phau7 e5 sim-cheng5, sit8-chai7 si7 sun5-chin bo5 pi2, Goa2 sou2 thiaN3--e5!  Li2 e5 sui2 hou7 goa2 moa2-sim su7-su7 to long2 moa2-i3.
3.  Goa2 khoaN3 li2 kau3 jip8-sin5 hit-si5, li2 e5 thau5 mai3 tiaN7-tiaN7 chhih-chhih, ChhiaN2 li2 giah8-thau5 khi2-lai5, koh hou7 goa2 chim chit8--e5, sui2 ah!  Iu3 mi7-mi7, Kong2 chit8--ku3, chhio3 chit8--e5, chhiaN2 li2 m7-bian2 ui3-siau2-le2, kheh-khi3, Ui7 sim2-mih8?  Li2 thai2 kan-ta bin7-ang5, siu7-khi3, soa3 choe3 li2 chau2-khi3 nih8?
Hui7-moai7 li2 chai-kioh ti7 soaN-teng2 choe3 li2 chau2-khi3 hit-si5, khoaN3 li2 e5 poe3[poe7]-eng2 tit8-tit8 chau2 loh8 soaN, goa2 e5 sim sit8-chai7 chhin-chhiuN7 beh piak-lih8 e5 kan-khou2, hit e5 sit-i3 sit8-chai7 oh-tit heng5-iong5.  Na7-si7 siuN7 to3-tng2 soa3 it-hoat khim poe7 li2 e5 iu2-hau3, li2 e5 tui3 sin3-giong2 e5 kian-chhi5, tui3 iu2-gi5-ai3, kap loan5-ai3 e5 hun-beng5, cheng-hiat, it-koat hou7 goa2 su-bou7.  Chong2 kong2 goa2 e5 sim chin oh-tit li7-khui li2.  Na7 u7 pit-iau3, goa2 ui7-tioh8 li2 kap li2 loh8-kau3 ia7 kam-goan7.
Li2 e5 ho2 peng5-iu2 Khun-hong sia2.  Se-ki2 1930. 11. 18.
Hui7-bi2 chih tioh8 chit tiuN phoe kap si, koh chit8-pai2 chhim-chhim thong3-hoe2 chit8-si5 e5 bo5 kin2-sin7.  Ui7-tioh8 hiaN-ko si2, sim-sin5 e5 khang-hi, tui3 ho2-i3 e5 lang5 bo5 the5-hong5, ti3-kau3 thai3-tou7 siu7 gou7-hoe7.  Thak8 kau3 soa3 boe2 hit-ku3 siang7 thong3-sim.  Chiu7-si7 kong2
“Na7 u7 pit-iau3 goa2 ui7-tioh8 li2 kap li2 loh8-kau3 ia7 kam-goan7.” Chit-ku3 oe7 sui-jian5 bo5 i3-su3.  KhoaN3 sin3 Ia5-sou choe3 chit8-khoan2 kiu5-hun e5 chhiu2-toaN7.  “Na7 u7 pit-iau3,” chit-ku3 thak8 liau2 chin liau2-jian5.  Sin3 Chu2 siu7 siok8-hoe5, tit sia3-choe7, teng5-thau5-siN, koh siu7 chiap-lap8 chiaN5-choe3 Siong7-te3 e5 kiaN2, che si7 ho5-teng2 e5 pit-iau3, si7 ho5-teng2 e5 eng5-kng.  Sim2-mih8 kong2 “Na7 u7 pit-iau3,” an2-ni kho2-leng5 kau3 u7 chit8-jit8, chiu7-si7 na7 koai2 koe3-chhiu2 chiu7 piN3-choe3 “Na7 bo5 pit-iau3 chiu7 m7 kap li2 loh8-kau3.  Chiong sin3-giong2 khoaN3-choe3…….
Khun-hong sia2 hit-ku3 si7 beh hian2-beng5 i e5 un-khin5, kam-goan7 khut-hok8 pai3 ti7 Hui7-bi2 e5 chioh8-liu5-kun5 e5 e7-bin7.  Che si7 siok8-jin5 ui7 kiu5-ai3 bo5 keng2 chhiu2-toaN7 e5 leng5-su7(能事).  Na7-si7 Hui7-bi2 thak8 liau2 kam2-kak kho2-thi2, kho2-lian5, kho2-nau2.  Chek-si5 ka7 i thiah choe3 nng7-peng5, hiat ti7 ji7-choa2-lang2.  Au7-lai5 siuN7 kong2 an2-ni bo5 kau3-giah8, chiu7 koh ka7 i khioh khi2--lai5, liam5 hou7 i choe3-hoe2.  Theh8 hou7 pa-pa khoaN3, soa3 kong2 i e5 sim-cheng5.  Lau7 tiuN2-lo2 chin kam2-kek cha-bou2-kiaN2 e5 sin3-sim kian-kou3, chin tong5-cheng5 Hui7-bi2 e5 chu2-tiuN.  Chiu7 ka7 i hoe5-phoe ku7-choat8 chit e5 kiu5-chhin.
Khun-hong sui-jian5 chiap tioh8 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 e5 the-si5, koh chit8-bin7 ia7 bo5 chiap tioh8 Hui7-bi2 e5 hoe5-phoe, chai chit pai2 e5 chiap-hiap8 si7 sit-pai7.  Chong2-si7 i long2 bo5 loe2-chi3, bo5 si2-sim, tit8-tit8 teh tan2 ki-hoe7.  Au7-lai5 i u7 khi3 hong-chit ti7 Bi2-kok chu2-pan7 e5 chui2-iu5 kong-si.  Ti7 keh-ni5 chhun-thiN chin tu2-ho2 siu7 beng7 kong-chhut (ui7 kong-bu7 chhut-chhai) lai5 Su7-liong5 tiau-cha iau3-bu7.  Chiu7-si7 thiaN kong2 ti7 hit hu7-kin7 e5 soaN-kha u7 e7-chhut chioh8-iu5 e5 hi-bong7.  Hek8-chia2 e7-tit ti7 hia kut8 iu5-chiN2 ia7 bo5 tek-khak.  Khun-hong kap ki5-u5 kui2-na7 e5 ki-sut8-chia2 chin iong2-iok8 lai5 Su7-liong5, beh khai-si2 tiau-cha.  Tak8-lang5 long2 khi3 tiam3 lu2-sia7, chi2-u7 i chit8 lang5 chin bo5 kheh-khi3, tit8-tit8 lai5 kau3 tiuN2-lo2 e5 tau.  Put-lun7 thiaN, pang5 long2 chin sek8, ka-ti7 chiu7 jip8-lai5, kio3 chit8-siaN chheng2-an e5 siaN, chiu7 chiong heng5-li2 ka-ti7 poaN-poaN jip8-lai5 i2-cheng5 choe3 lang5-kheh ka-ti7 tiam3 hit-keng lang5-kheh pang5.  Theh8 chin che7 le2-mih8 lai5.  Chin un-sun5 ho2-le2, chhin-su7 e5 tai7-chi3 long2 bo5 koh kong2-khi2.  Na2-chun2 ke-lai7 e5 lang5, tu5-khi3 siong7-pan pan7-su7 i2-goa7 ti7 chhu3-nih long2 kui-kui ki2-ki2, kheh-kheh khi3-khi3.  Mui2 cha2-khi2 e7-hng ka-teng5 le2-pai3, ki5-to2-hoe7, le2-pai3-jit8 e5 le2-pai3 tu5 12 hun bo5-eng5 i2-goa7 i m7-bat bo5 hu3.  Sit8-chai7 giam2-jian5 si7 Ki-tok-tou5.  Cheng5 u7 chiah8-hun taN hun ia7 ke2 khi2--lai5.  Ti7 tiuN2-lo2 e5 ka-teng5 chu7-jian5 bo5 ki-hoe7 thang lim chiu2.  Sit8-chai7 si7 chit8 e5 ho2 chheng-lian5.  Sim-lai7 siuN7 an2-choaN2 lan2 si7 m7-chai.
Bo5 phah-sng3 u7 chit8-jit8 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 tui3 bo5 chu3-i3 kam2-tioh8 soa3 khi2 hi3-iam7.  Lau7-lang5 lah chit8-si5 peN7-se3 soa3 piN3 chin m7-ho2.  Chin tu2-ho2 m7-kin2, m7-ban7 Soat-mui5 lim5-phun5 e5 ki5 kau3-lah.  Kai-chai3 Chu2 in-tian2 chin khoai3-pian7 chiu7 seN chit8 e5 ta-pou eN-a2 chin kou-chui, chu7 8 goeh8-jit8 khi3 hou7 choan-bun5 san2-kho khoaN3, kong2 khoaN3 i e5 pak-tou2 hiah toa7-e5, kho2-leng5 e7 siang-siN ia7 bo5 tek-khak, koh siaN3-tu2-siaN3 theng5 oa2 poaN3 tiam2-cheng, pak-tou2 koh chhui-chun7-thiaN3 koh seN chit8 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 chhut--lai5 hui-siong5 sui2, chin seng5 lau7-bu2 e5 bin7, chit8 e5 seng5 lau7-pe7 e5 bin7.  Tai7-ke toa7 hoaN-hi2, chhin-ke, chheN-m2 ia7 toa7 hoaN-hi2.  Chiu7 ka7 i ho7 mia5 ta-pou eN-a2 ka7 i ho7 mia5 “Ju5-liong5”（如龍） , cha-bou2--e5 chiu7 ka7 i ho7 choe3 “Ju5-mui5”（如梅）.  Siau3-liam7 pe7-bu2, choan5-ke nau7-jiat8 kun2-kun2.  M7-ku2 koh chit8-bin7 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 chin tim5-tang7 to2 ti7 chhng5-nih khah8-chhng5.  Khun-hong chai-iaN2 i e5 ki-hoe7 kau3-lah, chiu7 piaN3 siN3-mia7 e5 un-khun5 tau3 kou3 piN7-lang5.  In-ui7 siang7 chit8-si5 ti7 ke-lai7 u7 nng7-hang7 su7 chiok bo5 eng5.  Lim5 tiuN2-lo2-niu5 ni5-lau7 lah be7 kham-tit, kou3 kau3 boe2-ah am3-si5 bo5 hoat-tit, Soat-mui5 ka-ti7 si7 goeh8-lai7.  Hui7-bi2 kou3 liau2 ia7 kam2-kak chin ia3-sian7, sou2-i2 lai7-goa7 chhiaN2 i-seng, a2-si7 am3-si5 saN lun5 chiau3-kou3, Khun-hong bo5 m7 chin7-lat8.  Ui7-tioh8 thiaN3 Hui7-bi2 siong5-siong5 choe3-hoe2 kou3, a2-si7 hou7 Hui7-bi2 khi3 hioh-khun3, i ka-ti7 chit8 e5 ka-ti7 kou3, kou3 kui-mi5 chin-chiaN3 chhin-chhiuN7 kiaN2-ji5 e5 chhin-chhiat, bu5-bi5 put-chi3 e5 chiu-to3 ho2-i3.
3 jit8 au7 chiu7 pho7 eN-a2 lai5 hou7 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 khoaN3, ta-pou-sun, cha-bou2-sun chin-chiaN3 chin sui2 chin kou2-chui.  TiuN2-lo2 khoaN3 liau2 chin moa2-i3, sim toa7 siu7 an-ui3.  Chai Siong7-te3 po2-sioh thiaN3 i e5 lang5, sui-jian5 tioh8-tak bo5 ti3-kau3 poah8-to2, sui-jian5 poah8-to2 bo5 ti3-kau3 peh be7 khi2--lai5 soa3 choat8-bang7.  TaN Ia5-ho5-hoa bo5 choat8 i e5 hou7-su5, iu5-goan5 su3 i chit8-lam5 chit8-lu2 e5 sun-a2, chiu7 hoaN7-chhiu2 ka7 sun-a2 chiok-hok.  Liau2-au7 bo5 phah-sng3 ti7 hit e7-pou koh khi2 toa7 kan-khou2 chiu7 koe3-sin khi3.
Tng i beh tng7-khui3 e5 si5 ui5-gian5 nng7-ku3 oe7.
1.  Tioh8 chiong Ju5-liong5 hian3-choe3 Chu2 e5 kang-lang5.
2.  Hui7-bi2 choat8-tui3 m7-thang ke3 hou7 bo5 sin3 Chu2 e5 lang5.
TiuN2-lo2-niu5, kap Hui7-bi2 long2 kui7 ti7 chhng5-nih, chit8-lang5 ka7 i khan chit8-chhiu2, kui7 loh8 thoe3 i ki5-to2 an-ui3--i.  Ka7 i kong2 an-sim, tek-khak chiau3 i e5 oe7 khi3 kiaN5.  Tui3 an2-ni tiuN2-lo2 chiu7 an-sim bak8-chiu pang3-kheh to3-khi3 ThiN Pe7 tau.  Hit-si5 Khun-hong tu2 bo5 ti7 sin-piN, to3--lai5 khoaN3 tiuN2-lo2 koe3-sin ia7-si7 chap8-hun e5 ai-siong.  Chiu7 pang-bang5 le2 chong3-sek, chiu7 sun7-su7 an-chong3.
Keh bo5 loa7-ku2 Khun-hong soa3 siu7 tiau3-tong7 khi3 pat8 sou2-chai7.  Soat-mui5 ia7 moa2-goeh8 lah, an2-ni chit8-ke siu-jian5 u7 iu-bun7, m7-ku2 chit8-bin7 ia7 u7 an-ui3.  Kam2-sia7 Chu2 e5 chiok-hok chit8-ke koh chiam7-chiam7 beng5-long2-hoa3.  Ka-chai3 ia7 u7 chit8 e5 chin7-tiong e5 tng5-kang Siu2-jin5(守仁) teh liau7-li2 choe3-sit e5 su7.
Khun-hong to3-khi3 ia7-si7 eng7 chhian-hong pek-ke3 ai3 beh chhoa7 Hui7-bi2.  Au7-lai5 siuN7 tioh8 khi3 chhoe7 in bo2-ku7.  In bo2-ku7 si7 chit8 e5 siau2-chiong3, bou2 kun-thoan5 e5 Thoan5-tiuN2, chhiu2-e7 u7 kui-ban7-peng.  Cha2-si5 lek8-lim5 (choe3 soaN-chhat8-thau5) chhut-sin--e5, sim-seng3 chin thou2, chin hiong5-ok.  Bo2-ku7 chit8-e7 chiu7 in2-i3, choe3-hoe2 khia5-be2 lai5, kong2 si7 beh lai5 mai7-song.  Ki5-sit8 si7 beh lai5 thau-khoaN3 sin-niu5.  Kau3-ui7 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2-niu5 in chu7-jian5 chin ho2-i3 geng5-chiap.  Tui3 siau7-kai3 chiu7 chai si7 Khun-hong e5 bo2-ku7, si7 pun2-koan7 bou2 peng-thoan5 e5 thoan5-tiuN2 TiuN chiong-kun, sou2-i2 chin ho2-le2 saN khoan2-thai7.  Lai5 e5 si7 ia7 long2 bo5 kong2 khi3 chhin-chiaN5 e5 su7, sou2-i2 TiuN2-lo2-niu5 ia7 long2 put-kai2 ki [ki5]-i3.  SaN-si5 to3-khi3, ti7 lou7-nih Khun-hong chiu7 mng7 in bo2-ku7 e5 i3-kian3 khoaN3 liau2 an2-choaN2?  In bo2-ku7 chit8-chhui3 chiu7 in3 i “Chin-ho2!  Ko2-jian5 si7 chit8 e5 ho2 e5 ka-teng5 sou2-chhut e5 siok-lu2, put-lun7 bin7-mau7, le2-gi5, tai7-hong, iu-nga2 long2 bo5 thang hiam5.  Kho2-sioh u7 nng7-hang7 khun3-lan5.” In bo2-ku7 kong2 liau2 soa3 haiN3-thau5 thou3 chit8--e5 toa7-khui3.  Khun-hong sim tui3 hoaN-hi2 e5 soaN-chiam, hut-jian5 siu7 hiat-loh8 kau3 ou-am3 e5 chhim-khiN.  Sui5-si5 mng7 in bo2-ku7 u7 sim2-mih8 ui5-lan5.  In bo2-ku7 in3 kong2, “Te7 1.  Chong-kau3 bo5 siang5, goa2 siuN7 in un2-tang3 m7-kheng2.  2.  Lin2 lau7-bu2 chu7-se3 chiu7 ka7 li2 io Siu3-chhun, che beng5-beng5 si7 beh tui3--li2 e5.  Beh kio3 lin2 lau7-bu2 pang3 Siu3-chhun che ia7-si7 chap8-ji7-hun khun3-lan5.”
Khun-hong thiaN-liau2 soa3 thau5-khak chhih-chhih bak8-sai2 lau5 chhut--lai5.  Sim-te2 siuN7 kong2 bo2-ku7 kah bo5 hoat-tit an2-ni bo5 pan7-hoat lah.  Chu7 an2-ni ka7 in bo2-ku7 kong2.  “A-ku7 na7 kah si7 an2-ni, goa2 ia7 bo5 i3-su3 ai3 koh tiam3 chhu3-nih.  Beh chu7 an2-ni lai5 khi3 liu5 lah.” In bo2-ku7 thiaN tioh8 an2-ni sim-ki it-tong7, tong5-cheng5 chit e5 goe7-seng, chek-si5 in3 i kong2, “Ho2, goa2 u7 pan7-hoat.  Ti7 chit e5 gou7-goeh8-cheh cheng5-au7 tek-khak hou7 li2 oan5-hun.”  Khun-hong bak8-sai2 iau2 khoa3 ti7 bak8-kiN5, chek-si5 chhio3 chhut--lai5.  “Sia7-sia7 bo2-ku2 e5 ho2-i3, li2 beh eng7 sim2-mih8 pan7-hoat?” “Chit si5 ban7-chiah hoat-piau2, goa2 ju5-chhu2, ju5-chhu2 chu7-jian5 chiu7 u7 lang5 thang kau li2 e5 chhiu2 lai5 chiaN5 li2 bi2-ho2 e5 sim-goan7.” 

6
Na7-si7 Hui7-bi2 tui3 chit e5 chhin-su7 i kian-koat khia7 ti7 sin3-giong2 e5 lip8-tiuN5 lai5 ku7-choat8.  Hit e5 goan5-in chiu7-si7 tui3 peng5-si5 e5 sin3-giong2 kap koe3-khi3 khi3 hu3 Chheng-lian5 thoan5-khe3 kan3-pou7 chhun-leng7-hoe7 thiaN J.S.  Bok8-su e5 kang2-ian2 chiu7 it-hoat kian-koat.  Chit-si5 i hoe5-ek tioh8 tang-si5 Bok8-su e5 kang2-ian2.  Hit e5 te5-bak8 si7 “TiN-bit8 e5 ka-teng5”.
I.  Sim2-mih8 kio3-choe3 ka-teng5?
A.  Ti7 hoat-lut8-siong7 e5 teng7-gi7 chiu7-si7: “It-seng kiong7-tong5 seng-oah8, saN-kap tang5 toa3 ti7 chit8 e5 sou2-chai7 e5 chhin-siok8 koan-he7, kio3-choe3 ka-teng5.”
B.  Ka-teng5 e5 hun-lui7:
(1) Chiau3 lang5 e5 che7, chio2, kap se3-tai7 lai7 hun-choe3 toa7, se3 e5 ka-teng5.
(2) Chiau3 keng-che3 e5 chong7-hong2, kap seng-oah8 e5 theng5-tou7 lai5 hun-choe3 ho2-giah8, san3-hiong e5 ka-teng5.
(3) Tui3 Chong-kau3 e5 koan-he7 thang hun choe3 Ki-tok kau3-tou5, a2-si7 Hut8, Ju5, Hoe5-kau3 tou5 e5 ka-teng5.
II.  Kian3-siat ka-teng5 e5 bok8-tek chai7 ti7 to2-ui7?
Chiu7-si7 beh kiong7-tong5 cho7-seng5 keng3-khah heng7-hok e5 seng-oah8.
1.  SaN pang-chan7.
Chhong3-se3-ki3 2:18.  “Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 kong2, lang5 toaN-sin ka-ti7 toa3 m7-ho2; goa2 beh ka7 i cho7 chit8 e5 pang-chan7--e5, lai5 phit-phoe3 i.”

Chhong-se3-ki3 24:67.  “I2-sat chiu7 khan Li7-pek-ka jip8 i e5 lau7-bu2 Sat-lah8 e5 pou3-piN5, chhoa7 i choe3 bou2; koh chin thiaN3 i.  I2-sat tui3 lau7-bu2 si2-au7, kau3 chit-tiap8 chiah tit-tioh8 an-ui3.”
Thoan5-to7 4:11.  “Koh, nng7 lang5 saN-kap khun3, chiu7 oe7 sio-lou7; na7 ka-ti7 chit8-lang5 thai2-tho2 oe7 sio a3?”
Chiau3 i2-siong7 saN chat Seng3-keng lai5 khoaN3 lam5 lu2 saN-kap kian3-cho7 ka-teng5, thnag ti7 bo5-phoaN7 khun3-lan5 Jin5-seng e5 lu2-theng5 tiong, thang saN-pang-chan7, saN an-ui3, saN-kap tit-tioh8 sio-lo7 un-ai3 e5 seng-oah8.  Tui3 an2-ni ng3-bang7 e7-tit saN-kap cho7-seng5 keng3-khah heng7-hok e5 jin5-seng.
2.  Thang seN-thoaN3.
Ka-teng5 e5 chhut-hoat-tiam2 si7 tui3 chit8-tui3, chheng-khi3 e5 lam5-lu2 chheng-lian5 e5 kiat-hap8 choe3 tan-ui7.
Hu-hu7 choe3-chhou e5 phit-phoe3, hit e5 moai5-lang5, si7 Siong7-te3.  Cheng3-hun, chu2-hun-jin5 ia7-si7 Siong7-te3.  Kong2 chiok-su5 e5 ia7-si7 Siong7-te3.  The3 in pi7-pan7 sek8-tiuN5, pan7 chhiN-chhau, choe3 in e5 lang5-kheh saN-kap ka7 in hoaN-hi2 e5 ia7-si7 Siong7-te3. (Chhong3 1:2:).
Tui3 ang-bou2, chiu7-u7 pe7-kiaN2, bo2-kiaN2 chiu7-u7 hiaN-ti7, chiu7-u7 peng5-iu2, sia7-hoe7, kok-ka, kok-che3, se3-kan tui3 an2-ni hoan5-eng5.  Bun5-hoa3, kho-hak8, lek8-su2 e5 ian2-pian3 hoat-tat8, heng-soe tui3 an2-ni lai5.
3.  Cho7 seng5 heng7-hok ka-teng5 e5 iau3-sou3.
A.  Te7-it “ChiN5” chiu7-si7 u7 hong-hu3 e5 i-sit8-chu7.

B.  M7-si7, “Khong-lok8” pi2 chiN5 khah iau3-kin2, chiu7-si7 iong2-kiaN7 e5 sin-the2, tang5-sim ho5-lok8 che pi2 chiN5 khah iau3-kin2.
C.  Pi2 khong-lok8 e5 tai7-seng, tioh8 seng chhoe7 tioh8 “Lang5”.  Chiu7-si7 sim-sim siang-in3(心心相印) tang5-sim, tang5-sin3, chin-chiaN3 saN-thiaN3, saN chun-keng3 e5 lang5.  Sun5-kiat e5 thiaN3 si7 tui3 Sin5 Siong7-te3 chhut-hoat (1.  Iok-han7 4:7, 16) 
Bo5 sin3 Siong7-te3 e5 lang5, sim bo5 tit-tioh8 teng5-thau5-siN, bo5 teng5-thau5-siN e5 lang5 chiu7-si7 hoai5-khng3 Mou5-kui2 e5 ku7-sim, ti7 hit bo5 kng, bo5 thiaN3.  Siat-su2 u7, he si7 siok8-cheng5 e5 thiaN3.  M7-si7 chhut-tui3 chin-li2 e5 sin5 sou2 khe2-si7, m7-si7 chhut-tui3 Siong7-te7 hia lai5 e5 thiaN3.  Na7-si7 siok8-cheng5 e5 thiaN3 si7 tui3 li7-hai7 e5 sio koan-he7, u7 tiau5-kiaN7 e5 thiaN3.  Khia7 ti7 chit-khoan2 siok8-tek(俗的) e5 thiaN3, m7-si7 chhut tui3 Sin3, ng3-bang7 lai5 seN-chhut e5 thiaN3 lai5 kiat-hun u7 gui5-hiam2.  Ji5-chhiaN2 chit nng7 khoan2 bo5 siang7-khoan2 e5 thiaN3, kok-lang5 phau7 i e5 kian3-kai3, chi3-hiong3, sin3-sim, bok8-phiau bo5 tang5 e5 lang5, ui7-tioh8 chit8-si5 siok8-tek8 e5 pian7-gi5 lai5 kiat-hap8, chiong-lai5 e7 seN-chhut piak-lih8, pheng-hoai7, si7 chu7-jian5--e5.  Sou2-i2 Tioh8 seng-chhoe7 lang5.
Seng chhoe7 tang5 sin3, tang5 sim, tang5 chi3-bong7, m7-na7 saN-thiaN3, tioh8 soa3 saN chun-keng3 e5 lang5.  U7 lang5 chiu7 u7 chiN5, u7 chiN5 chiu7 u7 mih8.  Na7-si7 seng keng2 u7 chiN5, u7 mih8 che si7 chin pi-phi2 kian3-siau3 e5 gong7-lang5.  
1.  Seng keng2 ai3-cheng5 it-ti3 e5 lang5.
Nga2-ko ki3 “Ai3-cheng5” 11 pai2.  Ki3 “Sou2-thiaN3”--e5 18 pai2.  Ki3 “Goa2 sou2 loan5-ai3--e5” 32 pai2.
Poe5-kin kong2 “Sia7-kau tek e5 thiaN3 e7 bi2-hoa3 sia7-hoe7.

Jiok8-iok8-tek e5 sia5-loan5 e7 hu2-hoa3 sia7-hoe7.  Cheng-kiat hu-hu7 e5 loan5-ai3 e7 kian3-siat sia7-hoe7”.
Hu-hu7 e5 thiaN3-cheng5 kiam2-chhai2 khi2-thau5 si7 tui3 chu7-su, tok8-chiam3, chona-it khi2, au7-lai5 eng-kai tioh8 chin3 kau3 hou7-siong hong7-su7, kau3-boe2 si7 ui7 ai3 lai5 si2, lai5 hi-seng it-chhe3.  Sou2-i2 thiaN3 m7-si7 chu7-su e5 kam2-cheng5, si7 hi-seng e5 heng5-ui5.
Nga2-ko 2:7.  3:5.  8:4.
“Boh8-tit phah-chhiN2 i, boh8-tit kiau2-jiau2 goa2 sou2-thiaN3 e5, theng3-hau7 i ka-ki7 cheng5-goan7”.
“Phah-chhiN2 i” i3-su3 si7 m7-bian2 pek--i, ai3-cheng5 si7 “cheng5-goan7--e5”.  Si7 chu7-tong7-tek--e5.  Ia7-si7 eng2-oan2 be7 kai2-pian3--e5. (Nga2-ko 8:6-7) Na7 tui7-tioh8 jin5-cheng5, khoan5-keng2, but8-chit lai5 kai2-pian3 si7 chin kian3-siau3.
2.  Tioh8 keng2 ng3-bang7 it-ti3 e5 lang5.
Lan2 si7 Thian-kok bin5 (Hui-lip8-pi2 3:20).  Lan2 si7 ng3 thau5-cheng5 e5 pio, tui3 teng2-bin7 tiau3 lan2 e5 siuN2 teh chau2 e5 lang5 (Hui 3:12-14).  Lan2 si7 chu3-sin5 khoaN3 la5-sou lai5 chau2 e5 lang5 (Hi-pek-lai5 12:2).  Si7 bang7 thiN-siaN5 e5 lang5 (Hi 11:13-16).
3.  Choe3-au7 tioh8 keng2 Sin3-giong2 it-ti3 e5 lang5.
Sin3-giong2 na7 bo5 it-ti3, ng3-bang7 chiu7 bo5 hoat-tou7 it-ti3, thiaN3 sim ia7 bo5 hoat-tou7 thang it-ti3.
Sim2-mih8 kio3-choe3 tiN-bit8 e5 ka-teng5?

A.  Ti7 bo5-cheng5, peh8-bak8-chiu, kio3-me7, kong-kek, teng2-phak8 e7-chian e5 soa-bou5 lu2-theng5 tiong, ka-teng5 si7 lek8-im3 e5 kam-choaN5.
B.  Ti7 chan5-khok, leng2-gan2, kheng-bu2, hiat-kak8, leng2 peng-peng e5 peng-goan5 tiong, ka-teng5 si7 un-sek e5 lou5-piN.
C.  Ti7 chham2-thong3, pi-ai, soe5-thau5 tam3-chi3, khou2-hai2 kong5-hong e5 toa7-long7-tiong, ka-teng5 si7 Ho2 kang2-oan e5 be2-thau5.
Chong2-kong2 ka-teng5 si7 sim2-mih8?  Ka-teng5 chiu7-si7 jin5-seng lu2-theng5-tiong jiok8-the2 an-hioh, cheng-sin5 an-ui3 e5 sou2-chai7.
Ti7 Nga2-ko heng5-iong5 kong2:
“Goa2 si7 Sa-lun5 e5 mui5-kui3-hoe”=Bo5-cheng5 pek-hai7 tiong e5 an-ui3. (Nga2-ko 2:1) 
“Goa2 si7 SoaN-kok tiong e5 pek-hap8-hoe”=Pi-chham2 lau5 bak8-sai2 tiong e5 an-ui3. (Nga2-ko 2:1) 
“Si7 hng5-tiong e5 Hong7-sian-hoa”=Tioh8-boa5 ia3-sian7 tiong e5 an-ui3. (Ngo2-ko 1:14) 

Hu7-jin5-lang5 si7 na2 chun2 sim2-mih8?
“Chhi3-a2-lai7 e5 pek-hap8-hoe”=It-seng tou si7 khou2, chu7 u7 kian-jim2, kiat-pek8. (Nga2-ko 2:2) (kian-jim2) 
“Chioh8-phang7 lai7 e5 kap”=Heng5-chong7 un-sun5, bak8-chiu, siaN-im kho2-ai3. (Nga2-ko 1:14) (hian5-hui7) 

“Goa2 e5 sio2-moai7, goa2 e5 sin-niu5, chiu7-si7 koaiN-so2 e5 hng5; kham3-bat8 e5 chiN2, hong-bat8 e5 chui2-choaN5”=Sun5-kiat cheng-chiat. (Nga2-ko 4:12) (cheng-kiat) 
Teng2-bin7 e5 tiong-hu, hu7-jin5-lang5 si7 Nga2-ko sou2 bio5-sia2 li2-siong2 e5 hu-hu7.
(Ti7 chia am3-chi2 kiaN2-sai2 tiong7-hu si7 Chu2 Ia5-sou sin-niu5 si7 sin3-tou5) 
III.  Beh an-choaN2 keng2 ho2 e5 teng2-tui3?
1.  Keng2 e5 hong-hoat.
A.  Tioh8 seng ki5-to2. (Chhong3 24:12.  21.  26-27) Beh ke3 ia7-si7 pin5 Sin5 e5 chi2-i3. (Chhong3 24:50-51) 
B.  Ho2-bou2 si7 Siong7-te3 siuN2-su3--e5. (Chim-gian5 12: 4.  18:22.  19:13-14) 
2.  Soan2-tek8 e5 phiau-chun2.
A.  Lam5--e5 m7-thang be5 ti7 lu2-seng3 e5 sui2, Chham-sun, Tai7-pit8, So3-lo5-bun5 long2 sit-pai7 ti7 bi2-lu2.
B.  Lu2--e5 m7-thang be5 ti7 cha-pou e5 chiN5, but8-chit.
C.  Tioh8 keng2 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni e5 lu2-chu2.
(Chhong3 24:11.  17-20.  22-27) =Khin5-lo5, hong7-su7, chhin-chhiat, le2-gi5 toan-chong, chun5-chhun5 pe7-bo2, u7 sin3-sim, u7 cham2-cheh8 e5 chai7-sek-lu2. (Chhong3 24:) 

D.  Tioh8 keng2 an2-ni e5 ta-pou-lang5 choe3 ang.
(Chhong3 29:18.  20.  30) =Chiu7-si7 koat-sim thiaN3-li2.  Goan7 ui7 li2 tioh8-boa5, hi-seng, kian7-khong, kian-chi5, u7 li2-ti3, un-chhun5 gau5 the2-thiap e5 lang5.
3.  Sim2-mih8 si7 “bi2” e5 phiau-chun2.
Chhong3-se3-ki3 24:6 “極其俊美還是處女”.
俊=U7 ti3-hui7, iong2-kam2, ho5-kiat, kian7-khong.
處女=Boe7-bat u7 lang5 chhin-kin7 i. (Nga2-ko 4:7.  12.  II Lim5 11:2-3.  Ho5-se-a 3:1) Lai7 sim e5 sui2 te7-it iau3-kin2. (1.  Pi2-tek 3:3-5) 
Sui2 si7 Siong7-te3 tek8-piat8 siuN2-su3--e5, be7 tit ka-ti7 kiau-ngou7. (I2-se-kiat 16:14) 
Lu2-seng3 e5 sui2 si7 kian7-khong, lai7-sim sui2, chhu3-lu2 chit 3 hang7 te7-it sui2.  Ta-pou lang5 sou2 iau3-kiu5 e5 bi2-lu2 si7 cheng-kiat, un-sun5, the2-thiap.  M7-si7 khiok-soaN3-bi2, phoe5-hu e5 iu3-ji7, iau-kiau e5 mi7-thai3.  Na7 kan-ta iau3-kiu5 jiok8-hiong(肉香) jiok8-iok8 e5 boan2-chiok, he si7 chhai2-hoe-phang e5 lam5-seng3, chiong lu2-seng3 tong3 choe3 thit-tho5-mih8 khoan2-thai7 e5.  M7-si7 cheng3-keng hu-hu7 e5 to7-li2.
4.  Siang7-ho2 e5 teng2-tui3 toa3 ti7 to2-ui7?
Ti7 li2 e5 keh-piah, ti7 li2 e5 tang5 kau3-hoe7, tang5-oh8, tang5 hiuN-li2, chiu7-si7 chu7-se3 chiu7 saN chai seng3-cheng5, choe3-hoe2 kau-poe5, goan7 tang5-tiN tang5-khou2 e5 lam5 peng5-iu2, lu2 peng5-iu2 si7 te7-it ho2.

M7-bian2 tham-sim, m7-bian2 hoN3-ki5, te7-it kam2 e5 in3-siong7 thai3 gui5-hiam2.  M7-bian2 li2-siong2 koe3-hun7 siuN-koan5, au7-lai5 si5-ki siuN-ban7 chiah tit8-tit8 loh8-chiat.  Beh ke3 tioh8 than3-chhiN, 18-22 hoe3 choe3 tong-si5.  M7-bian2 siuN gau5-keng2, ti-a2 koe3 cho5-phang.  Ai3 khi3 chhoe7 sin-ki5 e5 khoaN3-mai7.  Kau3-si5 be7 loh8-ngauh li2 chiu7 chai-tai7.  Se3-kan bo5 hit-ho7 lak8-kha tng5-chhiu e5 lang5, m7-bian2 siuN gau5 keng2 “peng7-hoan7”（平凡) , chhou, peN5, tit8-a2--e5 chiu7 ho2.
5.  Sio2-chia2 li2 ia7 tioh8 choe3 chu2-tong7 lai5-keng2.
Sio2-chia2 li2 m7-thang tiaN7 choe3 pi7-tong7 si2-si2, tiaN7 tan2 lang5 lai5 khoaN3 sin-niu5.  Soan2-tek8 loan5-jin5 m7-si7 phin7 jiok8-gan2 lai5 khoaN3, si7 phin7 sim-gan2 lai5 chhoe7.  Tioh8 liong7-cha2, m7-thang koe3 si7 chiah thou2-khui3 poh8-mia7.  Thai3-tou7 tioh8 tai7-hong, tai7-tai7 toan7-toan7, m7-thang hou7 lang5 keng-the2 “bo5 tai7 bo5 chai5”.  Tong7 tiong tai3 cheng7, cheng7-tiong tai3 tong7 tu2-tu2 ho2(中庸) chin oh tioh8 siu-iong2, ku2-tong7 bun5-nga2.  M7-thang siok8-be7 li2 e5 ai3-cheng5.  Lan5-seng3 na2 kong5-phang(狂蜂) , chit8 e7 chio chiu7 lai5.  Ia7 m7-thang khin-khin seng5-siu7 lang5 e5 thiaN3-cheng5.  Tioh8 kin2-sin7, chhim-siuN7, tioh8 ki5-to2.  Tioh8 ka7 pe7-bo2 kong2, m7-thang am3-am3-a2 kap lang5 kau-poe5.  Theng3-hau7 kau3 beh lau3-khui3 lah chiah chhut phoa3 chiu7 chin chhau3-mia5.  

7
IV.  Loan5-ai3 kap kiat-hun.
1.  Sim2-mih8 kio3-choe3 “Loan5-ai3”?
Hun-in si7 Siong7-te3 sou2 phoe3-hap8, lam5 toa7 ai3 chhoa7, lu2 toa7 ai3-ke3, tui3 an2-ni chiah e7 chiaN5-ke chiaN5-sek.（成家，成室） Lam5 lu2 kiat-hun ki3-jian5 si7 jin5-seng pit-jian5 e5 su7, tak8-lang5 khoaN3 choe3 eng-kai chin7 e5 jin5-lun5, (tu5 sin-the2 phoa3-siuN3, kap tek8-piat8 iu2-sou2-kam2, m7-ke3 m7-chhoa7 e5 lang5 i2-goa7).  Na7-si7 an2-ni loan5-ai3 chiu7 chaiN2-iuN7?
“Loan5-ai3” chit ku3 oe7 hong-kian3 su-siuN2 e5 lang5 thiaN liau2 chin ai3-chhio3, chin khoaN3-khin, sim-chi3 u7 lang5 siuN7 choe3 chin kian3-siau3, u7 e5 soa3 siuN7 choe3 put-eng-kai kong2, si7 choe7-ok.  Sit8-chai7 si7 toa7 chho3-gou7.  Tai7-khai3 si7 in-ui7 lang5 bo5 beng5-pek8 loan5-ai3 si7 sim2-mih8 chiah an2-ni.  Ki5-sit8 loan5-ai3 che-si7 hu-hu7 iN7-seng3(夫婦異性) e5 tiong-kan pit-jian5 tioh8 u7 e5 su7, na7 bo5, hu-hu7 e5 koan-he7 si7 be7-tit thang seng5-lip8.
Lan2 na7 thak8 Chhong3-se3-ki3 te7 2 chiuN, lan2 u7 thak8 tioh8 hu7-jin-lang5 si7 tui3 ta-pou-lang5 chhut.  A-tong kong2 “Chit e5 si7 goa2 kut-lai7 e5 kut, bah-lai7 e5 bah, beh chheng choe3 cha-bou2-lang5, in-ui7 i si7 tui3 ta-pou-lang5 theh8 chhut.”  Chong2-si7 au7-tai7 e5 ta-pou-lang5 si7 tui3 cha-bou2-lang5 chhut.  An2-ni hu-hu7 pun2 si7 chit8-the2, lu2 tui3 lam5 chhut, lam5 tui3 lu2 chhut, si7 put-kho2 hun-li7 e5 chit8-the2.  An2-ni li2 kio3 i be7 saN-loan5 be7 saN-ai3, a2-si7 kong2 m7-thang saN-loan5 m7-thang saN-ai3 che si7 tian-to3 gek8-seng3.  Na7 chhin-chhiuN7 khip thih li2 kio3 i mai3 khip thih, che si7 put-kho2-leng5, a2-si7 kio3 chi2-lam5-chiam m7-thang pi2 lam5-peng5, che ia7-si7 chin ui5-lan5 e5 su7.  Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni li2 kio3 lu2 m7-thang loan5 lam5, lam5 m7-thang ai3 lu2, che ia7-si7 chin gek8 chu7-jian5 e5 thian-seng3.  Chiau3 Bi2-kok seng3 e5 hak8-chia2(性學) e5 gian2-kiu3 eN-a2 chiu7 u7 seng3 e5 i3-sek, chha-put-to tui3 2, 3 hoe3 khi2 chiu7 chin beng5-hian2.  Sek(色) kap chiap8(食) che si7 lang5 e5 chu7-jian5 thian-seng3.  Tui3 seng3 e5 bun7-te5 lam5--e5 tai7-seng hoat-tat8, ╳ ╳ ╳, kau3 40 goa7 hoe3 e5 si5 ╳ ╳ ╳.  Khiok ia7 u7 chhi5-siok8 ╳ ╳ ╳.  Lu2--e5 ╳ ╳ ╳, chong2-si7 beh ╳ ╳ ╳.  Au7-lai5 kau3 ╳ ╳ ╳ chiu7 ia3-sian7 khi3.  Lu2--e5 tui3 seng3-iok8 e5 iau3-kiu5 u7 chiu-ki5-seng3 （週期性） chiu7-si7 ╳ ╳ ╳ e5 si5.  Chiu7-si7 ui7-tioh8 thoan5-cheng2 lai5 ╳ ╳ ╳ .  Lam5--e5 m7-si7, lam5--e5 si7 chin hong3-su3, sui-sui pian7-pian7 khoaN3 tioh8 sim2-mih8, thiaN-kiN3, ╳ ╳ ╳ chiu7 tong7-khi2 iok8-cheng3.  Lu2--e5 thiaN3 tiong7-hu si7 chin khoah, chiu7-si7 tui3 che7-che7 hong-bin7 lai5 thiaN3 tiong7-hu.  Lam5--e5 thiaN3 lu2--e5, si7 chiong ╳ ╳  iau3-kiu5 choe3 tiong-sim, ╳ ╳ ╳ na7 be7 ho5, bo5 chheng3-i3, tak8-hang7 to loan7 liau2-liau2.  Lu2--e5 tui3 chit-hang7 khah u7 thun-lun2, na7 chu7-thau5 bo5 ke3, mai3 phah-chhiN2--i, it-seng kho2-i2 choe3 kou-niu5, khiok u7 si5 sim-seng3 e7 piN3 khah kip, tui3 sin-the2 bo5 sim2-mih8 kau3 goa7 toa7 e5 eng2-hiong2.  Lam5--e5 khah oh-lun2, in-ui7 tui3 lam5-seng3 ╳ ╳ ╳, chu7-jian5 e7 iau3-kiu5 ╳ ╳, na7 m7-si7 chin sin7-tiong7, chu7-che3, chiu7 ai3 poah8-to2, jin5-keh e5 siu-iong2 chiu7-si7 chai7 ti7 chia.
Tui3 an2-ni ka7 i khoaN3, tui3 seng-li2-hak8(生理學) siong7 e5 lip8-tiuN5 lam5-lu2 nng7-e5 iN7-seng3, siong kiu5-ai3, kiu5-hap8 che ia7-si7 chin chu7-jian5, tui3 an2-ni bi2-moa2 e5 jin5-seng, liong5-ho2 e5 ka-teng5 seng5-lip8, cheng2-chok8 tit-tioh8 liu5-thoan5.  Sou2-i2 Seng3-keng kong2:
“Li2 beh kan-khou2 siN-kiaN2, li2 beh loan5-bou7 li2 e5 tiong7-hu, i beh koan2-hat li2. (Chhong3 3:16) 
“An2-ni tiong7-hu tioh8 thiaN3 i e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chhin-chhiuN7 ka-ki7 e5 sin-the2.  ThiaN3 ka-ki7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7-si7 thiaN3 ka-ki7.”(I2-hut-sou2 5:28) 
Tioh8 saN-thiaN3 kau3 sim2-mih8 theng5-tou7?  Tioh8 thiaN3 kau3 hou7-siong7 hian3-chhut ka-ti7 e5 siN3-mia7 lai5 kiat-hap8 chiaN5-choe3 chit8-the2 chin7 it-seng.  Na7-si7 lam5 tioh8 tiong7-gi7(義) , lu2 tioh8 tiong7-chiat(節).  ChaiN2-iuN7 an2-ni kong2?  Lan2 lai5 seng kong2 “Loan5-ai3” si7 sim2-mih8?
“Loan5” si7 loan5-bou7, “Ai3” si7 thiaN3-sioh, chiu7-si7 hu7-jin5-lang5 loan5-bou7 i e5 tiong7-hu, ta-pou-lang5 thiaN3-sioh i e5 hu7-jin5-lang5.  An2-ni kio3-choe3 loan5-ai3.  Loan5-ai3 tioh8 u7 nng7 e5 lam5-lu2 iN7-seng3 chiah e7 seng5-lip8.  Kan-ta chit8 e5 be7 seng5-lip8, ia7 nng7 e5 na7 long2 tong5-seng3 chiu7-si7 peN5-peN5 cha-pou--e5, peN5-peN5 cha-bou2--e5, an2-ni si7 tong5-seng3-ai3, si7 pian3-thai3 e5 ai3, m7-si7 loan5-ai3.
Koh loan5-ai3 m7-na7 si7 tioh8 u7 lam5, lu2 nng7-e5 iN7-seng3 chiah e7 seng5-lip8, koh tioh8 u7 leng5, jiok8 (靈肉) e5 it-ti3 chiah e5 seng5-lip8.

Kho2-pi2 chia u7 nng7 e5 lam5, lu2 iN7-seng3 choe3 chin ho2 e5 peng5-iu2 lai5 kau-poe5, hit e5 chhin-bit8 u7 poaN5-koe3 peng5-siong5 e5 chhin-bit8.  Chong2-si7 m7-bat u7 jiok8-the2 e5 koan-he7, kau3 boe2 kiam2-chhai2 jin7 choe3 hiaN, moai7, an2-ni ia7-si7 iu-goan5 si7 iu2-gi5-tek e5 kau-poe5, iu2-gi5-tek e5 saN-thiaN3.  Be7 thang kong2 in nng7-lang5 u7 loan5-ai3.
Koh kho2-pi2 chia u7 nng7 e5 lam5, lu2 iN7-seng3, in u7 tang5-chhng5, chong2-si7 in e5 sim m7-si7 chhut tui3 saN-thiaN3, ╳ ╳ ╳ ╳, a2-si7 ti7 hoa-ke liu2-hang7 e5 boe7 chhio3.  Sui-jian5 u7 jiok8-the2 e5 it-ti3, cheng-sin5 thiaN3-sim bo5 it-ti3, an2-ni ia7 m7-si7 loan5-ai3.
Chin e5 loan5-ai3 si7 cheng-sin5, jiok8-the2 long2-chong2 it-ti3, choe3 ho2 chiu7-si7 leng5-beng7, chiu7-si7 sin3-giong2 ia7 it-ti3.  Che si7 lan2 sin3-chia2, kap se3-siok8 lang5 e5 hun-piat.  Chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 e5 kim-lou5 u7 saN-ki kha tu2-leh.  M7-na7 lang5 kap lang5 koh tiam3 ti7 Sin5, Sin5 e5 thiaN3 koan3-chhoan3 ti7 lang5 kap leng5 e5 tiong-kan lai5 seng5-lip8.  Chit-khoan2 e5 hu-hu7-ai3 chiu7 chin-chiaN3 e7 eng2-oan2 kian-kou3.
TaN loan5-ai3 ki3-jian5 si7 an2-ni, “M7-si7 hu-hu7 e5 tiong-kan chiu7 bo5 loan5-ai3 thang kong2 a2 m7-si7?” “Si7.” Chheng-lian5-lang5 boe7-chhoa7, boe7-ke3 chiu7 sio loan5-ai3, che si7 chho3-gou7 a2 m7-si7?  Si7.  Kiam2-chhai2 si7 poaN5-koe3 iu2-gi5-ai3, lai5 jip8 ti7 iN7-seng3 e5 kiu5-ai3 kai-toaN7.  Chong2-si7 m7-thang kong2 si7 loan5-ai3.  Hit e5 kau-poe5 tek-khak tioh8 chi2 i5 le2, bu5-sia5 （止於禮，無邪).  Na7-si7 kau3 chit e5 theng5-tou7 tioh8 chu3-i3.  
Lam5-lu2 iN7-seng3 khi2-thau5 saN-bat.  
Chiap8-chiap8 chiap-chhiok chiu7 tui3 saN-bat seN-khi2 kam2-cheng5 iu2-ai3(友愛).  
Tui3 iu2-ai3 chiu7 seN-chhut saN pang-chan7, saN hong7-su7.  
Kau3 chia si7 iu2-cheng5, iu2-gi5 e5 kau-poe5.  

Au7-lai5 seN-khi2 chit8-khoan2 put-khou2 su-gi7 e5 ai3 e5 khip-in2-lat8, na2 chiap kin7 chiu7 piN3 choe3 cheng5-tau5 i3-hap8.
Na7 saN-kiN3 chin hoaN-hi2, khah-ku2 bo5 saN-kiN3 chin sim-bun7.  Chin him-bou7 kin2 ai3 koh saN-kiN3, chhoe7 ki-hoe7, cho3 ki-hoe7, saN-oan nng7-tng2 ai3 saN-kiN3.  KiN3 tioh8 chin hoaN-hi2, m7-kam pun-khui, hin7 saN-kiN3 siuN-ban7, hin7 pun-khui siuN-kin2.  SaN-kiN3 e5 si5 sim hoaN-hi2, sim chhiang2, bin7 ang5, sim7-chi3 e7 na2-chun2 hoat-jiat8, beh pun-khui soa3 iu-bun7 soa3 hau2.  Na7 kau3 chit e5 theng5-tou7 i2-keng m7-si7 kan2-tan e5 iu2-gi5-ai3.  Chiu7-si7 thong-siok8 kio3-choe3 “Loan5-ai3”.  Kau3 chia tioh8 chu3-i3.  Tioh8 kian-koat, tioh8 chhim-siuN7, tioh8 ki5-to2.  Na7 chhim-chhim siuN7 liau2 tioh8 ka7 pe7-bo2 kong2, hek8-chia2 tui3 tiong2-poe3 e5 ti-ki2 lai5 chham-siong5.  Na7 chai chit e5 su7 bo5 hap8, chiu7 tioh8 kin2 tiong.  Ia7 m7-thang bo5 kong2, bo5 kong2 chiu7 kiaN-liau2 e7 pian3-choe3 su-thong, kan-im5.
Lang5 eng-kai tioh8 u7 chhu3-su7, bo5 chhu3-su7 loan7-lai5, an2-ni si7 “loan7-ai3”（亂愛) loan7-loan7 ai3, m7-si7 loan5-ai3.  U7-si5 tui3 ti3 bo5 teng7-seng3 soa3 piN3 choe3 saN-kak loan5-ai3 （三角，多角戀愛).  Chiu7-si7 chit8 e5 lu2 siang7 chit8-si5 ai3 nng7 e5 lam5, a2-si7 chit8 e5 lam5 siang7 chit8 si5 ai3 nng7 e5 lu2, a2-si7 loan7-loan7 chhap.  Che long2 si7 tui3 ai3-cheng5 e5 bo5 kin2-sin7 siok8-be7 e5 sou2-ti3.  Thou2-oe7 kong2 in2-khi2 “Kau5 ka7-kau5,” a2-si7 saN-chhoa7 khi3 si2, che long2 si7 chin toa7 e5 chho3-gou7.  Choe3 chheng-lian5 tek-khak m7-thang ham7-loh8 ti7 bo5 chhu3-su7 e5 sou2 ui7-chi “sia5-loan5.” Choe3 pe7-bo2 e5 m7-si7 kim3-chi2 lam5-lu2 e5 kau-gi5, si7 ai3 ka7 i sian7-to7.  Thoe3 in chhoe7 ho2 e5 tang5-phoaN7, lan2 tioh8 choe3 si7-se3 e5 leng2-to7-chia2, in si7 chhin-chhiuN7 chai7-tiuN5 teh keng3-ki e5 lang5, lan2 tiam3 piN-a2 khoaN3, thoe3 in tau3 siuN7, an2-choaN2 chiah e7 chau2 ti7 si3-chiaN3 e5 lou7.
Iu-seng3 loat-pai7, keng2 thau5-tui3 che ia7-si7 chit8 hang7 iu-seng3 loat-pai7 e5 keng3-cheng.  CheN iaN5--e5 chiu7 seng ke3, keng3-cheng iaN5--e5 chiu7 seng chhoa7.
