U7 e5 loh8 tiuN5 loan7 chong5, tek8-piat8 ang-bou2 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 nng7-lang5 pak8 saN-kha e5 tau3-chau2, it-tan3 keng2 m7-tioh8 kaN5, chau2 liau2 kha-pou7 be7 ho5, chau2-chau2 phak-phak loh8-khi3, u7 e5 soa3 phui3-bin7 chau2 bo5 kau3-boe2 chiu7 thau2-khui, chit8 lang5 liu chit8 lou7.  Che si7 chin sit-pai7 thang kian3-kiau3 e5 un7-tong7-oan5.  PoaN3-lou7 li5-hun ia7-si7 an2-ni.
Chhin-ai3 e5 chheng-lian5 hiaN-ti7, lin2 tui3 lu2-seng3 na7 m7-si7 u7 an3-sng3 beh chhoa7 i choe3 bou2.  M7-thang siuN chhin-bit8, tioh8 ti7 iu2-gi5 e5 sou2-chai7 theng5 pou7.  Chhin-ai3 e5 chheng-lian5 chi2-moai7 sio2-chia2.  Lin2 na7 bo5 an3-sng3 beh chiong bou2-kun(某君) choe3 li2 e5 tiong7-hu, li2 m7-thang kap lam5-seng3 siuN chhin-bit8.  Tioh8 ti7 iu2-gi5 e5 ui7 theng5-pou7, koh chin3-khi3 li2 chiu7 toa7 khek-khui.
Sio2-chia2 li2 si7 khia7 ti7 “Seng5-siu7” e5 lip8-tiuN5, lam5--e5 thau-chiah8, liau2-au7 chhui3 chhit-chhit-leh, teN3 m7-chai.  Li2--neh, li2 po2-kui3 e5 le2-choa2, chhu3-lu2 e5 chun-kui3, eng5-kng, khoa-khau2, thang hian3 hou7 li2 e5 tiong7-hu choe3 po2-kui3 eng5-u7 e5 le2-mih8 sit-loh8 lah.  Kiam2-chhai2 ui7-tioh8 an2-ni li2 e5 heng7-un7 long2-chong2 sit8-loh8.  Bo5 tiuN-ti5-a2 chu-thai am3-kiat, giat8-cheng2 puh-ge5, li2 chiu7 chin kai-si2.
Sou2-i2 chheng-lian5 hiaN-ti7, chheng-lian5 chi2-moai7 tioh8 ti7 sin3-giong2-nih toa7-toa7 chiat-che3, kin2-sin7 lan2 e5 phin2-tek.  M7-si7 hu, hu7 m7-thang kong2 loan5-ai3.  Na7 kau-poe5 kau3 ti7 poaN5-koe3 iu2-gi5 tioh8 chu3-i3, tioh8 ka7 pe7-bo2 kong2, m7-thang am3-chiN7, bo5 tiat8-su7.（異性之愛，發乎感情，應止於禮，禮者敬也，互相尊重人格，不亂為是).
ChaiN2-iuN7 kong2 lam5 tiong7 gi7, lu2 tiong7 chiat.（義， 節).  Ia5-sou chai7-se3 e5 si5, u7 lang5 chiong hian7-tiuN5 kiaN5 kan-im5 e5 lang5 liah8 lai5 kiN3 Ia5-sou, khoaN3 tioh8 chaiN2-iuN7 pan7?  Ia5-sou khi2-thau5 m7-chhap, tiam7-tiam7, bin5-chiong3 tit8-tit8 mng7, put-tek-i2 I chiu7 eng7 chhiu2-cheng2-thau5-a2 sia2-ji7 ti7 thou5-kha, koh tit8-tit8 mng7 kou-put-chiong Ia5-sou chiah khui-chhui3 lai5 in3.  ChaiN2-iuN7 Ia5-sou thai2 bo5 chin iong2-iok8 lai5 chhap chit chan5 tai7-chi3?  In-ui7 chit chan5 su7 thang kong2 si7 tui7-loh8 e5 lang5 e5 chu7-jian5-seng3.  Na7 m7-si7 teng5-thau5-siN, chu7-kak tioh8 siu2-ki2, keng3-jian5 seng3-kiat.  Li2 tui3 im5-loan7 e5 lang5 lai5 kong2 si7 ong2-jian5.  Koh kong2 khi2--lai5 ia7-si7 kian3-siau3 su7.  Koh si7 bo5 kong-to7, in-ui7 im5-loan7 m7-si7 chit8 e5 e7 seng5-lip8, tek-khak ai3 nng7 e5.  Kan-ta liah8 lu2--e5 lai5, lam5--e5 pang3 i khi3, che-si7 tiong7 lam5 kheng lu2.  Sou2-i2 Ia5-sou tiam7-tiam7.  Ia5-sou e5 i3-su3 lu2--e5 tioh8 tiong7 chiat.
Cheng-chiat si7 hu7-lu2 e5 seN3-mia7 sio-siang7, na7 u7 cheng-chiat, put-lun7 i si7 ho2-giah8, san3, gau5, han-ban7, lau7, siau3-lian5, sui2, bai2, chai7-sek-lu2, boe7-ke3, ke3-liau2 choe3 lang5 e5 bou2, a2-si7 lau7-bu2, chiu2-koaN2, lau7-po5 lah to si7 chin po2-poe3.  In-ui7 i u7 siu2 cheng-chiat.  Na7 bo5 cheng-chiat i si7 sui2 kau3 na2-chun2 goat8-li2-siong5-ngou5, gau5 kau3 e7 poe-thiN to si7 hou7 lang5 iam3-chian7, chhau3-mih8.  I e7 hou7 pe7-bo2 iu-bun7, e7 hou7 peng5-iu2 khoaN3-khin, e7 hou7 tiong7-hu hiat-kak8, e7 hou7 kiaN2-ji5 put-hau3--i, e7 hou7-sia7-hoe7 e5 lang5 ku7-choat8, phui3-noa7.  Chi2-moai7-ah!  Li2 tioh8 ki3-tit li2 e5 po2-poe3 chiu7-si7 siu2 cheng-chiat.  Na7 sit-loh8 cheng-chiat li2 chiu7 bo5 tat8-chiN5.
HiaN-ti7 ah!  Lam5--e5 tioh8 siu2 cheng5-gi7(情義).  M7-thang bo5 cheng5 bo5 gi7.  Lu2-seng3 chiong i te7-it po2-kui3 e5 thiaN3 hian3 hou7 li2, li2 chiah poe7--i, bo5 cheng5 poe7 gi7, li2 sit8-chai7 pi2 khim5-siu3 khah si2. (KhoaN3 hun2-chiau2 e5 ai3-cheng5).  I te7-it po2-poe3 e5 jiok8-the2, sim-sin5 seN3-mia7 long2 hian3 hou7 li2.  It-seng it-si3 beh kau-tai3 li2, li2 chiah koh poe7--i, hou7 lu2-seng3 sit-loh8 i e5 sim, sin ti7 li2, hou7 i chian5-tou5 ou-am3, chau2-thau5 bo5 lou7.  Hou7 i e5 sin-the2 sim-sin5 siu7 tang7 e5 siong-hun5, hek8-chia2 ti3-kau3 chu7 an2-ni tui7-loh8, a2-si7 chu7-po7, chu7-khi3, li2 sit8-chai7 chek-tek kai-si2.
Ia5-sou chaiN2-iuN7 chu2-tiuN im5-loan7 chiu7 thang li5-hun.  In-ui7 kan-im5 chiu7-si7 hu-hu7 thiaN3 e5 cheng5-hun7, thiaN3 e5 ian5, liu2-toa3 (紐帶) i2-keng tng7-khi3 lah.  Hu-hu7 e5 saN-thiaN3 si7 ka-teng5 e5 tiong-sim, liu2-toa3.  Tiong-sim i2-keng pheng-hoai7, liu2-toa3 i2-keng tng7, sit8-chai7 bo5 tat8-chiN5.  Hu-hu7 e5 kiat-hap8 si7 chu3-tiong7 ti7 sun5-kiat, chiu7-si7 lu2 cheng-chiat, lam5 cheng5-gi7 e5 seng-oah8.  Sou2-i2 bi2-moa2 e5 hu-hu7 seng-oah8 si7 lam5-lu2 ai3 kiong7-tong5 hu7-chek.  Be7 eng7-tit kok-lang5 ka-ti7 hong3-su3.  Lu2--e5 si7 tiong7-hu e5, lam5--e5 si7 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5.  Tai7-ke u7 hou7-siong7 koan2-sok e5 koan5-li7.  Khah-siong5 lang5 si7 siuN7 lu2 e5 kap lang5 su-thong, ang5-heng7 chhut-chiuN5（紅杏出墻） tioh8 ai3 siu7 li5-ian5.  Lam5--e5 khi3 chhoe7 sin e5 hoaN-hi2, ia7 bo5 siu7 chek-pi7.  Che-si7 tiong7-lam5 kheng-lu2, pian3-thai3 e5 lam5-lu2 che3-tou7.  Lam5, lu2 si7 peng5-teng2, kiong7-tong5 hu7-chek, kiong7-tong5 koan2-sok.  Lai5 saN-kap po2-siu2, cheng-chin3 hu-hu7-kan seng3-kiat, saN-thiaN3 e5 seng-oah8.  Na7 pho3-hoai7 chit e5 kui-chun2 long2 si7 im5-loan7.  Siong7-te3 eng2 bo5 chiok-hok.  

8
B.  Lam5-lu2 seng3 e5 chhiong2-tong7.
Lam5-lu2 seng3 e5 chhiong2-tong7, che-si7 kian7-khong-the2 e5 lam5 lu2 jiok8-the2 seng-li2-tek seng5-sek8(kau3-sek8 na2 koe2-chi2 pa2-chui2 kau3-hun) e5 chu7-jian5 hian7-siong7.  Lam5 chiong-cheng5 (鍾情) , lu2 su-chhun (思春).  Lam5-lu2 kau3 hit si5 put-lun7 jiok8-the2, siaN-im, su-siuN2 long2 e7 keng-koe3 tong-jian5 e5 it-tai7 pian3-hoa3.  Che m7-si7 choe7-ok, ia7 m7-si7 pian3-thai3, ia7 m7-si7 thang kian3-siau3 e5 su7.  Chu7-jian5 m7-thang che3-chi2, chong2-si7 tioh8 sian7-to7.  Hou7 i hoat-tat8 ti7 cheng3-kui e5 lou7, lai5 kiat ho2 e5 seng5-ko2.
Lam5 chiong-cheng5, lu2 su-chhun, put-ti put-kak e7 ai3 saN chiap-kin7.  Tui3 sek8-sai7 chiu7 chin3-jip8 iu2-gi5, tui3 iu2-gi5 chiu7 chin3-kau3 tong5-cheng5.  Tui3 tong5-cheng5 chiu7 chin3-kau3 ai3-bou7, kiu5-ai3.  Tui3 ai3-bou7 chiu7 seN-chhut saN pang-chan7, saN po2-hou7.  Kau3-boe2 chiu7 seN-khi2 kam-goan7 ui7 i hi-seng, chun-keng3 e5 sim, ai3 choe3-hoe2, thiaN3 e5 tok8-chiam3, kiat-hun.
Cha-pou--e5 u7 cha-pou e5 iong2-kam2, khong2-khai3 e5 khi3-khai3.  Lu2--e5 u7 lu2 e5 ui3-siau2-le2, sai-nai, iu2-bi2 e5 piau2-cheng5.  Tui3 chia ai3-cheng5 chiu7 puh-iN2, chiu7 seN-chhut kiu5-ai3, kiat-hun e5 su7-sit8.  Tui3 kiat-hun chiu7 chiaN5-choe3 ka-teng5, u7 pe7 kiaN2, bo2 kiaN2 e5 thiaN3 seN-chhut.  Chiu7 u7 ka-teng5 seng-oah8, ka-teng5 kau3-iok8 e5 pit-iau3, ti7 hia seN-khi2 hiaN-ti7, chi2-moai7 e5 ho5-bok8, kiaN2-ji5 hau3-sun7 e5 lun5-li2 (倫理).  Au7-lai5 chiu7 seN-chhut peng5-iu2 sia7-hoe7 e5 to7-tek, chiu7 heng5-seng5 kok-ka u7 kun-sin5 e5 gi7-bu7 koan5-li7.  Kau3 boe2 chiu7 seN-chhut kok-che3 e5 kau-gi5, seN chhut se3-kai3 tai7-tong5 e5 lian5-beng5.  Tui3 an2-ni jin5-lui7 e5 bun5-hoa3, san2-giap8, si-koa, lek8-su2 tit8-tit8 ian2-pian3 chhoan-liu5 put-sek (川流不息) e5 chiap-soa3 loh8 khi3.
Ju5-ko2 kong2 “Loan5-ai3” be7 eng7-tit.  Chiu7 ai3 tai7-seng choat8-tng7 lam5-lu2 e5 tong7-cheng5.  Ki3-jian5 lam5-lu2 tiong2-seng5, jiok8-the2 seng-li2-tek seng5-sek8 chu7-jian5 e7 tong7-cheng5, ki3-jian5 e7 tong7-cheng5 chu7-jian5 iN7-seng3 lam5-lu2 e7 tam7-khi2 ai3-cheng5.  Che thong-siok8 chiu7-si7 kio3 choe3 loan5-ai3.  Na7-si7 an2-ni loan5-ai3 si7 lam5-lu2-kan pit-jian5 e7 hian7-siong7.  Na7-bo5 loan5-ai3 chiu7 kiat-hun put-leng5 seng5-lip8.  Tui3 an2-ni lang5 kap lang5 e5 tiong-kan chiu7 piN3 choe3 kou-so3, bo5 liau5, na2 ki-khi3, bo5 chhio, bo5 khau3, bo5 bak8-sai2, bo5 si-koa, bo5 seN-thoaN3.  Na7 an2-ni “Loan5-ai3” si7 chi3-siong7(戀愛至上) a2-m7-si7?  Ti7 chia lang5-lang5 tioh8 chun2-chat, tioh8 siu-iong2, tioh8 u7 chiam5-siu chu7-che3(潛修自制).  M7-si7 lam7-sam2 chiong chit e5 sin5-seng3, iau3-kin2 e5 to7-tek khoaN3 choe3 peng5-siong5, chhou-siok8 loan7-lai5 chiu7 chin kian3-siau3.  Ai3-cheng5 siok8-be7, eng7 chit e5 sun7-seng3 ho2 e5 phin2-tek lai5 eng7 ti7 gek8-seng3, thang, kian3-siau3 e5 heng5-ui5, chiu7 pi2 sim2-mih8 to7 khah chhau3.
ThiaN lang5 kong2 Loan5-ai3 si7 chi3-siong7, chiu7 kiaN5 bu5-thi2 e5 su7 che-si7 chin kai-si2.  Lam5-lu2 e5 kau-poe5 choe3 iu2-gi5 si7-thang.  Sui-jian5 si7 tiaN7-hun liau2 e5 bi7-hun-hu, bi7-hun-chhe to7 m7-thang.
1.  Kiam2-chhai2 ui7-tioh8 m7 eng3 chit e5 iau-kiu5 chiu7 ti-kau2 hun-in phoa3-lih8.  Bo5 iau3-kin2, hou7 i phoa3-lih8, ia7 m7-thang kiaN5 kian3-siau3 hoan7-choe7 e5 su7.
Hi-pek-lai5 13:4 “Hun-in lang5-lang5 tioh8 chun-tiong7, chhng5 bo5 la5-sam5; in-ui7 su-thong kiaN5-im5 e5 lang5, Siong7-te3 beh sim2-phoaN3 i.”
2.  M7-si7 kong2 moa2-chhui3 kong2 “Ai3”（愛) ; hian3 li2 e5 cheng5-chho, lang5 kiam2 chiu chin-chiaN3 e7 ai3--li2?  Che bo5 tek-khak.  Kiam2-chhai2 lang5 si7 tui3 hoe-sim(花心) ka7 li2 chhai2-khi3, jian5-au7 kui-lui2 hoe long2 ka7-li2 hiat-kak8.  Li2 khi3 thak8 2 Sat-bo2-ni2 13:7-29.  khoaN3-mai7.  Am3-lun3 teh loan5 Ap-sa-liong5 e5 sio2-moai7 ThaN-ma2, eng7 chhian hong pek-ke3 ai3 kah be7-tit tit-tioh8.  It-tan3 tit-tioh8, moa2-chiok i e5 sim-goan7, chiu7 ka7 i hiat-kak8.  Chit-khoan2 su7 ti7 sia5-im5 e5 hian7-se3 bo5 hi-han2.
3.  Lu2-seng3 eng3-kai tioh8 hian2-beng5 li2 e5 cheng-kiat8, toan3-jian5 ku3-choat8.  Tui3 an2-ni tui3-hong e5 lam5-seng3 e7 it-hoat keng3-bou7 li2 e5 phin2-tek.  Siat-su2 ui7-tioh8 li2 e5 ku2-choat8 chiu7 siu7-khi3, beh hoe3 chhin, goa2 siuN7 leng7-khou2, hoe3-chhin khah ho2.  In-ui7 hit khoan2 lam5-seng3 si7 bo5 chu7-che3, bo5 beng5-long2, tham-iok8 e5 lang5.  Kin-tu2 li2 ke3--i ia7 bo5 toa7 lou7-eng7.
C.  “Tang5-pang5”
Ti7 Ma2-thai3 1:25 u7 chit-ku3 “tang5-pang5” e5 oe7.  Chit-ku3 tui3 cha2 kau3-taN hoan-ek8 seng3-keng e5 lang5 liah choe3 chin oh ek8 e5 khoan2.  In-ui7 u7 ek8-choe3 chin che3 khoan2 e5 ji7.
1.	Ku7 lo5-ma2-ji7 ek8; ek8 choe3 “Seng5-chhin”.  
2.	Peh8-oe7 bun5 kok-gu2; ek8-choe3 “tang5-pang5”（同房).  
3.	Han3-bun5 bun5-li2; ek8-choe “tong5-sek”（同室） （男以女為室，女以男為家） 
4.	Ku7 jit8-pun2-bun5; ek8-choe3 “床(??)?=同 (??) =” “tang5 chhng5”.  
5.	Sin jit8-pun2-bun2; ek8-choe3 “相知 ?”(sio-bat, sio chai-iaN2).  
6.	Eng-gu2 khim-teng7 ek8; ek8-choe3 “Knew her”(bat i).  
“Tang5-pang5” Chiu7-si7 lam5-lu2 chiaN5-choe3 chit8-the2.  
Ti7 1 Lim5 6:16-18.  

“A3-si7 lin2 m7-chai kap chhiong-ki lian5-hap8 e5, si7 kap i choe3 chit8-the2?  In-ui7 kong2, Nng7-e5 beh chiaN2-choe3 chit8-the2.  Tok8-tok8 kap Chu2 lian5-hap8 e5 si7 chit8 e5 sin5.     Tioh8 siam2-pi7 im5-heng7.  Lang5 sou2 hoan7 tak8-hang7 e5 choe3 long2 si7 seng-khu goa7 e5; na7-si7 kiaN5 kan-im5 e5 si7 hoan7-choe7 kau3 ti7 ka-ki7 e5 seng-ku.”
Ang-bou2 e5 koan-he7 Chhong3-se3-ki3 2:24-25
“Sou2-i2 lang5 beh li7-khui i e5 pe7-bu2, kiat-lian5 i e5 bou2, in chiu7 chiaN5-choe3 chit8-the2.  Ang-bou2 nng7-lang5 piN5-piN5 thng3-pak-theh (kok-gu2 ek8-choe3 “chhiah-sin lou7-the2”) ia7 bo5 kian3-siau3.”
Ti7 chia sou2-i2 ek8-choe3 “Sio-bat, Sio chai-iaN2” sit8-chai7 e5 lian5-hap8 sio-bat.  Tui3 chia tit-tioh8 hu-hu7-kan chin e5 sio li2-kai2, saN an-ui3, sio-lo7 e5 thiaN3 cheng5.  Ti7 hia u7 hoaN-hi2, u7 thiaN3-cheng5, u7 ui3 siau2-le2, u7 an-ui3, chit e5 thiaN3 o3-biau2 ah!  Che chiu7-si7 jok8-the2-tek8 ka-teng5 thiaN3 e5 liu2-toa3.  Tui3 an-ni hu-hu7 saN kiat-lian5, seN kiaN2 seN sun lai5 ke-thiN “Jin5-seng e5 heng7-hok.”  Oan5-chiaN5 Sin5 e5 chiok-hok.  Chiong chit8 e5 choe3 chhou-siok8, choe3 gek8-seng3, im5-loan7, sia5-ok, hih-hiauh lai5 kun2-chhio3.  Pho3-hoai7 ka-teng5, hu2-hoa3 sia7-hoe7, gui5-hai7 kok-ka, chit e5 choe7 m7-si7 sio2-khoa2.  Sou2-i2 Seng3-keng kong2 lang5-lang5 e5 “chhng5 tioh8 chheng-khi3, bo5 la5-sam5”.
Thang kiaN e5 keng2-ko3!!
“Sou2-i2 chiau3 in sim-lai7 e5 su-iok8, Siong7-te3 kau-hu3 in ti7 bo5 chheng-khi3, hou7 in e5 seng-khu saN leng5-jiok8; in-ui7 an-ni Siong7-te3 kau-hu in ti7 kian3-siau3 e5 cheng5; in e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 eng7 sun7-seng3 e5 lou7-eng7 piN3 choe3 gek8-seng3 e5 lou7-eng7, saN i3-ai3, iok8-hoe2 tong7-sim, ta-pou kap ta-pou kiaN5 bo5 cheng3-keng e5 su7; ti7 in pun2-sin siu7 in e5 chha-biu7 sou2 eng3-kai tu2-tioh8 e5 po3-eng3,”(Lo5-ma2 1:24-27).

“Na7-si7 hiah8 e5 ... ... ... im5-loan7 e5, ... ... ... in e5 hun7-giah8 si7 ti7 hit e5 eng7 he2 kap jiu-ng5 teh sio e5 Ou5; chit e5 chiu7-si7 te7 ji7 pai2 e5 si2”(khe2-si7-liok8 21:8).
HiaN-ti7, chi2-moai7, chheng-lian5 lam5-lu2, lan2 tioh8 se3-ji7 m7-thang siu7 be5-hak8.  Chit8-e7 sit-chiok e7 tu2-tioh8 chhian-kou2-hin7, hoan2-hoe2 put-kip8 e5 kan-khou2.  Im5-loan7, kou2-hap8 (    ; bo5 chek-jim7, chhin3-chhai2 e5 choe3-hoe2) , su-thong, che m7-na7 sin-the2, chiu7 sim-sin5, phin2-tek, leng5-seng3 long2 siu7-siong.  M7-na7 jin5-keh tui7-loh8, si7 e7 hou7 Siong7-te3 chiu3-chou2, tioh8 siu7 sim2-phoaN3.  Lan2 tioh8 chun5-siu2 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7.  Siok8-gu2 kong2 “Ban7-ok im5 ui5 siu2”, chit hang7 tai7-chi3 loan7, ban7-su7 long2 loan7 liau2-liau2.
Tui3 ka-ti7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, tui3 ka-ti7 e5 tiong7-hu kiu5 seng3 e5 an-ui3, boan2-chiok u7 choe7 a2 bo5?  Bo5.  Chong2-si7 ia7 m7-thang koe3-thau5, Koe3-thau5 ia7-si7 e7 hai7 tioh8 sin-the2, su7-giap8.  Kiam2-chhai2 soa3 be7 seng-iok8 chu2-lu2, sou2-i2 sui-jian5 bo5 choe7, iau2-ku2 tioh8 chun2-chat.  Sian-siN li2 tek-khak m7-thang hou7 ian-chi, phang-chui2 tiu5 toan7, koan5-kia7-a2 e5, Sou2 ui7-chi jiok8-the2 e5 khiok-soaN3-bi2, io5-io5 pai2-pai2 a-na2 to-chu e5 mi7-thai3 sou2 be5.
Sio2-chia2 li2 tek-khak m7-thang hou7 chai5, se3, lek8 e5 lat8 sou2 khip-in2.  Tioh8 khia7-khi2-chai7 choe3 sin3-giong2 e5 tai7-tiong7-hu.  Ti7 sin3, ng3-bang7, jin5-ai3 lai5 keng2 li2 e5 phit-phoe3.  Seng3-iok8 si7 lang5 sou2 ai3, chong2-si7 m7-thang liah8 hit hang7 choe3 tui3-siong7, choe3 kiat-hun i5-it e5 bok8-tek8.  kiat-hun na7 chiu7 theng5-chi2 ti7 hia, li2 kho2-leng5 e7 ia3-sian7, au7-lai5 hek8-chia2 e7 phoa3-lih8.  A-si7 ai3 oaN7 sin bi7, sin e5 hoaN-hi2, sin e5 thit-tho5, liah8 seng3(性) choe3 chit8 khoan2 e5 iu5-hi3.  Kai-si2, chit e5 chho3-gou7 toa7 ah?  Ang-bou2 e5 kiat-hap8 tu5 jiok8-the2 seng5 e5 kiat-hap8 iau2 u7 khah iau2-kin2 e5 liu2-toa3 chiu7 si7 tang5 sin3, tang5 ng3-bang7, tang5 jin5-ai3.  Tui3 chiah-e5 chiah-e7 hou7 Ki-tok-tou5 e5 ka-teng5 tit-tioh8 chin e5 bi2-moa2.  Se3-siok8 lang5 e5 ka-teng5 chiu7-si7 chi2-u7 ti7 jiok8-the2 e5 cheng5-iok8, kap keng-che3 e5 long5-poe7 siong-i, a2-si7 tui3 ji5-lu2 ti7 hit tiong-kan lai5 choe3 lian5-he5 e5 liu2-toa3, chong2-kong2 long2 si7 siok8 se3-kan su7 e5 lian5-he5.  Bo5 siok8 sin5, siok8 teng2-bin7 e5 lian5-he5.  Sou2-i2 siok8-se3 e5 lian5-he5 na7 tng7-khi3, ka-teng5 ang-bou2 e5 koan-he7 chiu7 oa2-kai2 pheng-lih8 khi3.
Na7 chin-chiaN3 ti7 Sin3-giong2, ng3-bang7, jin5-ai3 lai5 kiat-hap8 e5 hu-hu7.  Sui5-jian5 hu-hu7 kan u7 chit8 e5 sin-the2 loan2-jiok8, ti3-kau3 be7 boan2-chiok siong-hong seng3 (性) e5 khoai3-lok8, a2-si7 kim-chiN5 pho3-san2, san3-chhiah, koh nng7-lang5 e5 tiong-kan bo5 kiaN2-ji5.  Seng3 e5 khoai3-lok8 bo5, chiN5, seng-oah8 e5 sou2-kho3 ia7 bo5, ia7 bo5 kiaN2, chiau3-khoaN3 in nng7-e5 e7 li7-khui.  Bo5 tek-khak, na7 ti7 Sin3-giong2, u7 tang5 pou7-tiau e5 ng3-bang7, koh u7 ti7 Chu2 e5 thiaN3 lai5 ak-chhiu2, hit tui3 hu-hu7 beh hoaN-hi2 ti7 teng2-bin7 e5 hoaN-hi2, jim2-siu7 it-chhe3 e5 thong3-khou2, khou2-tou3 lai5 chin7 in hu-hu7 bi2-moa2 e5 seng-oah8.  Sou2-i2 chin e5 hu-hu7 ai3-cheng5 e5 eng2-kou3, na7 m7-si7 ti7 Sin3-giong2 it-ti3 si7 put-kho2-leng5, m7-si7 kong2 hoe7-goa7 e5 lang5 chiu7 bo5 hu-hu7 pek-lian5 kai-lo2 e5 lang5, ia7-si7 u7, chong2-si7 hit e5 lai7-bin7-tek8 e5 sim-cheng5, thiaN3 e5 lip8-khiok-tiam2 bo5 sio-tang5.  Na7-si7 Ki-tok-tou5 kiat-hun e5 si5 sin-long5, sin-hu7, nng7 e5 khan-chhiu2, ia7 bok8-su hoaN7-chhiu2 ti7 hit teng2-bin7 lai5 ki5-to2 chiok-hok, hit e5 o3-biau7, i3-gi7 toa7 ah!  

9
V.  Sim2-mih8 si5 khi2 chiah thang tam7 ai3(談愛).
A.  Tam7 ai3 kho2-i2, tam7 loan7-ai3 put-kho2-i2.（談亂愛) 
Chong2-si7 lan2 tioh8 e7 ki3-tit, loan5-ai3 ai7 hu-hu7-kan sin5-seng3 e5 thiaN3 cheng5.  M7-si7 hu-hu7 e5 lam5-lu2 iN7-seng3 choe3-hoe2 tam7 loan5-ai3 si7 choe7-ok.  Koh tioh8 e7 ki3-tit m7-si7 chheng-lian5 lam5-lu2 chit8-ban7-lang5, chit8-ban7-lang5 long2 tek-khak tioh8 keng-koe3 se3-kan sou2 kong2 ho7 choe3 loan5-ai3 e5 kau-poe5 chiah si7 lang5, chiah u7 ho2 e5 kiat-hun, na7 kiat-hun cheng5 bo5 seng tam7 loan5-ai3 chiu7 be7 choe3-chiaN5 ho2 e5 kiat-hun, che ia7 si7 chho3-gou7.

Lan2 thak8 Ku7-iok I2-sat kap Li7-pek-ka boe7 ke3, boe7 chhoa7 e5 i2-cheng5 long2 m7 saN-bat.  Chong2-si7 in u7 choe3 ho2 e5 hu-hu7 seng-oah8.  Hek8-chia2 lan2 e5 lo2-poe3 e5 sian-siN ia7 u7 che7-che7 chit khoan2 e5 keng-giam7.  Sou2-i2 lan2 m7-bian2 be5-sin3 na7 bo5 sneg loan5-ai3 (Chit ku3 ki5-sit8 be7 kong2-tit, thang kong2 tam7-ai3, a2-si7 ai3 e5 kau-poe5) , chiu7 be7 tit ke3 chhoa7.  Na7-si7 hian7-tai7 che7-che7 chheng-lian5 chin be5-sin3 chit e5 su7.  Koh sui-jian5 kiat-hun cheng5 toa7 kong2 loan5-ai3 e5 lang5, kau3 si5 ka-teng5 phoa3-lih8 e5 lang5 ia7 be7 chhio2.
Chheng-lian5 kho2-i2 tam7-ai3, chong2-si7 tioh8 
1.  Bat ka-ti7 ia7 tioh8 bat tui3-hong.
2.  Li2 na7-si7 iau2 hak8-seng si5-tai7, sit8-chai7 m7-thang, si5-ki iau2 siuN cha2.  E7 hai7-tioh8 li2 e5 kong-kho3.
3.  Boe7 u7 keng-che3 tok8-lip8, an2-ni chhi7 lang5 be7 iaN5.
4.  Ni5-ki2 siuN-chio2.  Tou7-chai5-sai2 boe7 lak, kong2 oe7 iau2 chhau3-leng-tai.  Se3-su7 m7 bat, e7 chu3-seng5 toa7 chho3.
Lu2-seng3 18-22.  Lam5-seng3 ia7 tioh8 u7 it-ki poan3-ge7, ka-ti7 keng-che3 khia7 e7 tiau5 e5 si5 chiah lai5 kong2.  Tioh8 kho3 pe7-bo2 chhoa7 hou7 i, koh tioh8 kho3 pe7-bo2 chhi7 i e5 bou2, i e5 kiaN2, an2-ni chin kian3-siau3.  Goan7 ke3 an2-ni e5 tiong7-hu e5 lu2-seng3 ia7-si7 chin bo5 chu7-kak e5 lang5.  Lu2-seng3 beh ke3 tioh8 than3 cha2.  M7-thang li2-siong2 siuN koan5, au7-lai5 koe3-si5 chiah chu7-than3 poh8-mia7, chiah kin2 loh8 ke3, taN2 chiat, chhin3-chhai2 ke3 tian-to m7-ho2.  Kau3 30 hoe3 i2-siong7 chiah beh chhou-san2, an2-ni ia7 u7 khah bo5 li7-pian7.  Na7 ai3 thak8 Tai7-hak8 to bo5 kong2, na7 bo5 Ko-lu2, a2-si7 chhou-lu2 pit8-giap8 tioh8 kin2 oh8 ke-lai7 e5 kang, kin2 pi-pan7 u-kui（于歸).  Na7 bo5 chiong-lai5 chiu7 piN3 bo5 sou2-kui.  Lu2-seng3 chhut hong-thau5, kap lam5-seng3 peng7-kian hun3-tou3 ti7 sia7-hoe7 chin ho2, chong2-si7 to3-khi3 chau3-kha, io5 io-na5 iau2 khah ho2!  Choe3 Bok8-lan5 chiong5-kun chin thang o-lo2, choe3 Beng7-chu2 e5 lau7-bo2, liong5-chhe, hian5-bo2 goa2 siuN7 chiah si7 lu2-seng3 e5 pun2-sek.  Bo5 sou2 kui chiu7 tok8-lip8 choe3 kou-niu5 hok8-sai7 Chu2 chin ho2!  M7-thang hou7-hoe2 bo5 chheng.  
B.  “Chhou-loan5” tioh8 chu3-i3.
Ai3-cheng5 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 tiau-phi5 e5 gin2-na2, bo5 tiuN-ti5-a2 put-ti put-kak e5 tiong-kan e7 chau2-jip8 li2 e5 sim-pang5-lai7, au7-lai5 hoat-kak chiah beh kio3 i chhut-khi3, chin khun3-lan5.  Ia7 chhin-chhiuN7 chhiu7-tin5-a2 teh tiN5 chiuN7 toa7-chhiu7, put-ti put-kak hou7 i tiN5 tioh8 chin oh pak.
Koat-toan3 m7-thang sui5-sui5 pian7-pian7 tui3 chit8 e5 lam5-seng3, a2-si7 tui3 chit8 e5 lu2-seng3 kong2 “Goa2 thiaN3--li2.”  Ia7 m7-thang sui5-sui5 pian7-pian7 chiu7 khui sim-mng5 lai5 chiap-siu7.
1.  Tioh8 seng liau2-kai2 tui3-hong e5 ko5-seng3, chhu-bi7, phiah-phiN7 si7 e7 hah8 a2-be7?
2.  M7-thang pin5 chit8-si5 chheng-chhun e5 cheng5-jiat8, chit8 e7 choe3-hoe2 chiu7 be7 li7-tit.  Tioh8 sin7-tiong7, chhim siuN7, chu7-che3.
3.  M7-thang chu7-sun2, sun2 lang5 e5 chu7-chun sim.  M7-thang kiN3 tioh8 iN7-seng3 chiu7 piN3 chhiN-mi5, bong5-bok8 e5 saN-thiaN3.  Chit8--e7 teng3--i3 leh, sim2-mih8 to sui2, to ho2!
4.  Tioh8 leng2-cheng7, m7-bian2 sim-kip, khui siuN-kin2 e7 peng2-chhia.  Kin2-thin5 koh chiap8-lim e7 poah8-to2.
5.  Tioh8 chhun5 pe7-bo2, tioh8 mng7 su-tiong2 tai7-ke chham-kho2.
6.  Tioh8 ki5-to2. (Kap Bok8-su chim-chiok).

7.  Tioh8 chu3-i3 khau2-gian5 leng7-sek, toa7-lou7 khong2-khai3 e5 lam5-seng3, tioh8 chu3-i3 sai-nai kiau-thai3 bo5 tek tiaN7 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2.
8.  Ai3-cheng5 chhin-chhiuN7 hoe2.  Si7 be7 pau bat8-tit, lang5 liam-piN e7 chai, na7 bo5 se3-ji7 e7 hou7 i sio-tioh8.  Hit e5 jiat8 pi2 te7-gek8 e5 hoe2-iam7 khah jiat8, e7 sio-hui2 li2 e5 kim-chiN5, jin5-keh, oah8-mia7.
9.  Na7 chu7-kam2 u7 gui5-hiam2 tioh8 kin2 theng5-pou7, tioh8 kin2 pang2-khi3.  Koat-toan3 m7-thang to5-chui3 ti7 kong5-loan5, bong5-loan5(狂戀盲戀).
10.  Na7 chai li2 be7 tit chhoa7 i, be7 tit ke3 i, chiu7 m7-thang nge7-loan5, khang-loan5, si2-loan5.  Che si7 chin chho3-gou7, chin tai.  Na7 ui7 an2-ni lai5 si2 si7 gong7-si2.  Kah beh si2, chu7 hit e5 si2 e5 koat-sim lai5 cheng-chin3 pat8 hong-bin7 iau2 khah sui2.  Ui7 loan5-ai3 lai5 si2 hou7 lang5 khoaN3 e5 lang5 si7 chin put-tiong3-iong7.
C.  Sou2 kio3 choe3 Loan5-ai3 e5, si7 tiN-bit8 e5 hak8-kho3 a2 m7-si7?
Si7, chin tiN-bit8.  Bo5 tek-khak, u7 e5 si7 koe3 tit chin sng, siap, chin khou2-thang3(苦痛).  U7 e5 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 lim tioh8 tok8-ioh8, soa3 si2-loan5, ui7 an2-ni soa3 si2.
1.  Li2 na7 sin7-tiong7, eng7 sin3-giong2 choe3 lip8-khiok-tiam2.  Si7 sun5-kiat e5 thiaN3 kho2-leng5 hiong2-siu7 khoai3-lok8, kek-le7 li2 e5 chi3-khi3.  SaN bian2-le7 ng3 seng5-kong e5 lou7 khi3 chin3-pou7.
2.  Li2 na7 loan7-lai5, khia7 ti7 sia5-im5, houN3-sek hih-hiauh, long7-ban7 hong3-su3, li2 kho2-leng5 e7 ti3-kau3 hoe3 hak8, hong3-tong7, sit-pai7.
3.  Hek8-chia2 loan7-ai3.  SaN-kak loan5-ai3, e7 ti3-kau3 chiah8-chhou3 kau5 ka7-kau5, chit-tou3, chu7-pi-kam2, phoa3-piN7, chu7-sat, sat-jin5, hui2-iong5, sim-tiong (Jit8-pun2 oe7 chiu7-si7 nng7 e5 sio-chhoa7 khi3 si2=心中).

D.  ChaiN2-iuN7 chiah e7 tit-tioh8 li2 sim-ai3 e5 lang5?
1.  Seng jia2-khi2 lang5 e5 chu3-i3.
Tioh8 chheng7 liu5-heng5-saN, koan5 kiah8-a2 e5, tian7 ki5-heng5 e5 thau5-chang.  Bin7 boah ang5, oe7 ou, chhat-peh8.  KiaN5-lou7 bo5 tek-tiaN7 e5 io5-pai2, hian2-beng5 li2 e5 kiau-thai3.  An2-ni e7 hou7 lang5 chu3-i3 a2-be7?  E7 chu3-i3 li2 e5 lang5 chiu7-si7 hou-sin5.  Hou-sin5 ai3 cham chhau3-bah, ai3 cham sai2-phi2.
Hou7 lang5 chu3-i3 m7-bian2 eng7 an2-ni.  Tioh8 ti7 Chu2 u7 ho2 phin2-heng7, ho2 sin3-giong2.  Ho2 e5 hak8-lek8, u7 ho2 e5 ki-ge7.  Keng3-khian5, le2-gi5 toan-chong.  Kian7-khong, hoat8-phoat, tai7-hong7, gau5 hong7-su7 kau3-hoe7.  Ti7 ka-teng5 iu2-hau3, ti7 chhu3-piN, kau3-hoe7 u7 ho2 mia5-siaN.  An3-ni lai5 chhoe7 li2 e5 lang5 goa2 siuN7 un2-tang3 si7 khah chiaN5-mih8 e5 lang5.
2.  Ai3 e5 si, siu7(施受).
Li2 teh ai3 lang5, tui3-hong bo5 tek-khak ia7 teh ai3 li2, an2-ni li2 e7 piN3 choe3 phian3-loan5(片戀).  Bo5 siuN7 ka-ti7 e5 te7-ui7 jiat8-loan5, kong5-loan5 khiok u7-si5 hiau-heng7 e7 seng5-kong, chong2-si7 u7-si5 e7 sit-pai7.  Mng5-hong put-phoe3 e5 loan5 chhin-chhiuN7 Sih Jin5-kui3, Lu7 Bong5-cheng3 ia7 u7 seng5-kong.  Chong2-si7 he si7 hiau-heng7 lai5 tit-tioh8--e5.  Khah-siong5 bo5 li2 e5 mou7-hiam2 kap chhia-bong7(奢望) e7 sit-pai7.  “ThiaN3,” sui-jian5 si7 bo5 cheng2-chok8, kok-keng2 e5 hun-piat8, na7-si7 m7-si7 chhut tui3 sin3-giong2 choe3 te7-ki, ti7 Chu2 bo5 tiau5-kiaN7 e5 ak-chhiu2 si7 chin gui5-hiam2.  U7 si5 e7 chu7-gou7, gou7 lang5.  Sou2-i2 beh thiaN3--lang5, beh hou7 lang5 thiaN3, seng5-siu7 lang5 e5 thiaN3 long2 tioh8 chu3-i3.
3.  Tioh8 sin7-tiong7 m7-bian2 tioh8-kip, m7-bian2 loe2-chi3.  Hun-in m7-bian2 tioh8-kip, m7-bian2 chu7-pi.  Hoe bo5 chho3-khui, ian5 bo5 chho3 tui3.  Sui2-bai2 bo5 ti2-chi2, kah-i3 khah chham2 si2.  Na7 u7 ian5 chhian-li2 to e7 lai5 sio tu2.  Bo5 ian5 tui3-bin7 to be7 tit sio tui3.  Siu-tek, lip8-chi3 che si7 choe3 kin-pun2.  Eng7 ki5-to2 koh tan2-hau7.

VI.  TiN-bit8 e5 ka-teng5 beh chai2-iuN7 kian3-cho7?
A.  Tui3 thiaN3-cheng5 e5 kiat-chiN lai5 kian chiaN5.
ThiaN3-cheng5 tauh-ti2 si7 sim2-mih8?
“Ui7-tioh8 siu7 lang5 thiaN3（被愛) chiah thiaN3 lang5 e5 si7 lang5.  Ui7-tioh8 thiaN3 lai5 thiaN3 lang5 e5 si7 Sin5.”(Lou7-ka 6:32-36).
“ThiaN3-cheng5 chhin-chhiuN7 ka-sau3, si7 lun2 be7 tiau5, be7-tit un2-moa5 e5 su7”
(????kong2).
“Ai3-cheng5 e5 si7-kak m7-si7 bak8-chiu, si7 sim-leng5”    (??????kong2).
“Chin e5 ai3-cheng5 si7 khak-lip8 ti7 chin e5 chun-keng3 e5 teng2-bin7”
(?─??kong2).
Nga2-ko sou2 heng5-iong5 e5 “thiaN3.”
1.  “Ui7 thiaN3-cheng5 lai5 ti3 peN7.” 2:5.
2.  “Tu2-tioh8 goa2 e5 sim sou2-thiaN3 e5, goa2 chiu7 khiN5 i, m7 hou7 i khi3.” 3:4.
3.  “Goa2 ui7-tioh8 i e5 oe7, sin5 put-hu7-the2.” 5:6.
4.  “Goa2 beh chiong ai3-cheng5 hou7 li2” 7:12.

5.  “Ai3-cheng5 u7 toa7-lat8 chhin-chhiuN7 si2” 8:6.
6.  “Che7-che7 chui2 boe7-oe7 biat8 ai3-cheng5…….  Na7 u7 lang5 beh eng7 ke-lai7 choan5-giap8 oaN7 ai3-cheng5, tek-khak hou7 lang5 biau2-si7.” 8:7.
Li2 na7-khi3 hoa-ke liu2-hang7, m7-bian2 che7 loh8 lim 3 poe chiu2, li2 ia7 e7 thiaN-kiN3 ai3-cheng5 e5 oe7.  Ti7 hia u7 chhin-chhiuN7 chhau3 bah, noa7 pin5-ko2 e5 ai3-cheng5 siok8-be7 u7 chhau3-bi7 thang phiN7, thang thiaN.  Ke2 u7 sim ke2 u7 i3, theh8 kiuN-bo2 chhe3 bak8-kiN5, phian3 li2 chit-chiah gong7 toa7-ti, bo5 seN chhng pian7-si7 li2 cho7-hoa3-si7.  Chit khoan2 e5 thiaN3-cheng5 si7 chhoa7 li2 kau3 ti7 si2-biat8 e5 chhim-ian.
“ThiaN3-cheng5 chhut tui3 ti3-sek e5 choe3 kho2-kui3, chiu7-si7 saN li2-kai2 kian3-sek, chhu3-bi7 it-ti3, chu7-jian5 ji5-jian5 lai5 seN-chhut e5 ai3-cheng5.”  	???─ ?.
“Ai3-bou7 Sin5 chhin-chhiuN7 lok8 him-bou7 khe-chui2, tui3 khat-bou7 lai5 toh8 khi2 thiaN3 e5 hoe2-iam7, ti3-kau3 sim-thiaN3 piak-lih8 e5 thiaN3 choe3 jiat8-liat8”(Si-phian 42: 1-3. 63. 1-8). 		???????.
“Lin2 tioh8 saN-thiaN3, chhin-chhiuN7 goa2 u7 thiaN3 lin2, che-si7 goa2 beng7-leng7.  Lang5 ui7-tioh8 peng5-iu2 hian3 siN3-mia7, thiaN3 bo5 u7 pi2 chit e5 khah toa7 e5.”(Iok-han7 15: 12-13) Ia5-sou.
“Goa2 siat-su2 oe7 kong2 lang5 kap thiN-sai3 e5 im-gu2, na7 bo5 jin5-ai3, goa2 chiu7 chiaN5-choe3 hiang2 e5 tang5-khi3, tan5 e5 la5-poah8.  Goa2 siat-su2 choe3 sian-ti, beng5-pek8 long2-chong2 e5 o3-biau7 kap long2-chong2 e5 chai-bat, koh siat-su2 u7 chiau5-pi7 e5 sin3, kau3-giah8 lai5 i5-soaN, na7 bo5 jin5-ai3, goa2 chiu7 boe7 sng3 choe3 si7 sim2-mih8.  Goa2 siat-su2 chin7 sou2 u7 e5 lai5 chin2-che3, koh hian3 goa2 e5 seng-khu hou7 hoe2 sio, na7 bo5 jin5-ai3, chiu7 goa2 bo5 tit-tioh8 li7-ek.”(I.  Lim5 13:1-3) Po2-lo5.

“Jin5-ai3 eng2-oan2 boe7 bo5 khi3, na7-si7 sian-ti e5 chit beh hoe3 bo5, hiah e5 im-gu2 beh soah, chai-bat beh hoe3-bo5.”(I. Lim5 13:8) Po2-lo5.
“Hian7-kim sou2 chun5 e5, chiu7-si7 sin3, ng3-bang7, jin5-ai3, chi2 saN-hang7, ki5-tiong te7-it toa7 e5 si7 jin5-ai3. (I. Lim5 13:13) Po2-lo5.
Jin5-ai3 si7 Seng3 Sin5 sou2 kiat thau5-liap8 e5 koe2-chi2. (Ka-liap8-thai3 5:22).  Jin5-ai3 si7 sin3-tou5 phin2-tek e5 choe3 ko-hong (II. Pi2-tek 1:5-8).  ThiaN3 si7 tui3 Siong7-te3 chhut (I.  Iok-han7 4:).  Si7 Chu2 e5 beng7-leng7 (Iok-han7 15:).  Chu2 iau3-kiu5 thiaN3-sim(Iok-han7 21:15).
Chong2-si7 i2-siong7 sou2 kong2 chit e thiaN3 m7-si7 chi2 siok8-cheng5 e5 thiaN3.  Si7 chi2 “Seng3-kiat tui3 Sin5 lai5 e5 thiaN3.”  Chiau3 Seng3-keng e5 goan5-bun5 si7 sia2 “Agape” m7-si7 siok8-cheng5 e5 “Eros.” An2-ni thiaN3-cheng5 m7-si7 khang-gian5 si7 heng5-ui5.
ThiaN3 m7-si7 kam2-cheng5, si7 hi-seng.  ThiaN3-cheng5 m7-thang sit-khi3 li2-ti3, na7 sit-khi3 li2-ti3 e7 piN3-choe3 bong5-bok8 e5 thiaN3-cheng5.  ThiaN3-cheng5 m7-thang sit-khi3 chun-keng3.  Sit-khi3 chun-keng3 e7 liah8 tui3-siong7 choe3 thit-tho5-mih8.  KhoaN3 lu2-seng3 choe3 chhiu2-tiong chu.  Choe3 lang5-a2 lai7 e5 chiau2-a2, choe3 po5-le5 kheh-a2 lai7 e5 ang-a2, long2 si7 tui3 bo5 chun-keng3 lu2-seng3 e5 jin5-keh sou2-ti3.  ThiaN3-cheng5 tioh8 tui3 siok8-tek e5 thiaN5-cheng5 chin3-pou7, a2-si7 hiat-kak8 siok8-tek e5 ai3-cheng5, kau3 ti7 sun5-kiat khia7 ti7 sin3-giong2, tui3 Siong7-te3 chhut.  Than3 Chu2 e5 beng7-leng7 lai5 sit8-heng5.  Seng3-leng5 sou2 kiat e5 koe2-chi2 e5 ai3-cheng5 chiah u7 sui2, chiah u7 chin, chiah e7 eng2-chun5.  Eng7 chit khoan2 e5 ai3-cheng5 lai5 kiat-chiaN5 e5 hu-hu7 seng-oah8 chiah e7 tat8 kau3 chin-chiaN3 bi2-moa2 tiN-bit8 e5 ka-teng5.  Chiu7-si7 tioh8 tui3 Chu2 siu7, Siong7-te3 hia lai5 “Agape” “Seng3-kiat sin5-leng5-tek e5 thiaN3” lai5 un7-heng5 ti7 hu-hu7 e5 tiong-kan, thiaN3 chiah e7 eng2-oan2 kian-kou3.  Koh teng-leng5 chit8 pai2 “Loan5-ai3” si7 ti7 hu-hu7-kan chiah u7.  M7-si7 hu-hu7-kan si7 iu2-gi5-ai3, na7-si7 tek-khak tioh8 chi2-i5-le2, bu5-sia5.  
  

10
B.  Heng7-hok si7 kong-ke che7 e5.
Tioh8 e7 ki3-tit bi2-moa2 tiN-bit8 e5 ka-teng5 m7-si7 seN-chiaN5 u7 e5.  Si7 nng7 lang5 kong-ke che7 e5.
1.  Li2 khoaN3 ??— e5 boan2-cheng.
Kha khia7 ti7 tai7-te7 eng7 seng-san2 choe3 in seng-oah8 e5 ki-chhou2.  Eng7 pai3-tng5 e5 boan2-cheng choe3 in e5 seng-oah8 e5 poe3-keng2.  Nng7 ang-bou2 bin7 tui3 bin7 eng7 khiam-pi aN3-thau5 saN chun-keng3, saN-kap tang5-sin3, tang5-sim, tang5-siaN lai5 kam2-sia7 Siong7-te3.  Chit khoan2 kam2-sia7, lo5-tong7, saN-keng3, saN-chhin.  Seng-san2, chong-kau3, hu-hu7 saN-ho5 e5 seng-oah8, chu7-jian5 ka-teng5 beng5-long2-hoa3, piN3 choe3 lok8-hng5.
2.  Li2 thak8 Thoan5-to7 4:9-11.
Li2 e7 hoat-kian3 hu-hu7 e5 seng-oah8 e5 saN e5 iau3-tiam2.
(1) “SaN-kap tioh8-boa5 tit-tioh8 ho2 e5 hau7-ko2”  4:9.
(2) “Na7-si7 poah8-to2, chit8 e5 thang hu5 i e5 tang5-phoaN7 khi2-lai5, na7-si7 toaN-sin poah8-to2 bo5 pat8-lang5 hu5 i khi2-lai5” 4:10. (Che chiaN3 si7 chin e5 khan-chhiu2).
(3) “Nng7 lang5 saN-kap khun3 chiah e7 sio-lo7, na7-ai7 ka-ki7 chit8 lang5 thai2-tho2 e7 sio ah” 4:11.
I2-siong7 saN-hang7, choe3-hoe2 cho3 kang, saN hu5-chou7, choe3-hoe2 khun3, chit saN-hang7 na7 khiam3 chit8 hang7 bi2-moa2 e5 ka-teng5 chiu7 choe3 be7 lai5.  U7 e5 hu-jin5-lang5 si7 si2 che7 oah8 chiah8.  Chhiu2 put-tang7 sam-po2, ji5-chhiaN2 tho2 ai3 khoaN3 tian7-iaN2, thiau3-bu2, sng2 pai5-a2, poah8 ma5-chhiok.  Bo5 koan2-kou3 kiaN2-ji5, bo5 iau3-kin2 tiong7-hu.  Tak8-hang7 to eng7 leng-bo2, eng7 chu2-chiah8 e5, eng7 piaN3 lai7-bin7 e5 lu2-kang.  I tui3 tiong7-hu si7 iau-kiu5 koan5-li7, peng5-teng2, khoai3-lok8 e5 hiong2-siu7.  Am3-si5 ia7 bo5 tek-khak kap tiong7-hu khun3.  Ki5-siong2 thian-khai.  Put-lun7 lam5, lu2 na7 hoan7-tioh8 chit ho7 peN7 ka-teng5 si7 oah8 te7-gek8.（東食西寢，可能成美滿 之家庭，古今未之有也) 
3.  Sio-lo7 e5 ai3-cheng5 e5 lek8-liong7.
(1) Thang pou2-kiu3 han5-leng2, song3-sit, hong-hoe3 e5 sim-cheng5.
(2) Thang ban2-kiu3 toe5-hoe3, liu5-loh8 hong3-tong7 e5 sim-keng2.
(3) Thang chhit-khi3 choat8-bang7, pi-chham2 iu-siong e5 bak8-sai2.
(4) Thang chio3-kng kio3-chheN2 ou-am3 be5-lou7 e5 sim-leng5.
(5) Thang hou7 thai5-lang5 pang3-hoe2 e5 hiong-hoan7 kui-cheng3.
Sio-lo7 e5 thiaN3-cheng5 chhin-chhiuN7 lun7-kut8-iu5 tih ti7 beh hoe2-sio-sim e5 ki-khi3, thang m7-bian2 hoat-hoe2.  Chhin-chhiuN7 liat8-jit8 e7-tit siau-soaN3 kiat-oan3 chan5-jim2 e5 sim-tng5.  Ka-teng5 hu-hu7 sio-lo7 e5 thiaN3.  Pe7 kiaN2, bo2 kiaN2 sio-lo7 e5 thiaN3.  HiaN-ti7 chi2-moai7 sio-lo7 e5 thiaN3 chin-chiaN3 po2-kui3 ah!
4.  Tui3 sio-chim lai5 piau2-si7 ai3-cheng5.
Sio-chim, tek8-piat8 hu-hu7 e5 saN-chim si7 chit8-hang7 thiaN3 e5 piau2-hian7.  Ti7 Seng3-keng u7 ka3-si7 lan2 cheng2-cheng2 e5 saN-chim.
(1) A-hiaN Iok-sek kap sio2-ti7 saN-chim (Chhong3 45:5).

(2) Ta-ke Na2-o-bi2 kap sim-pu7 Lou7-tek saN-chim (Lou7-tek 1:9).
(3) Sian-siN Po2-lo5 kap I2-hut-sou2 e5 hoe7-iu2 saN-chim
(4) Tai7-pit8 kap peng5-iu2 Iok-na2-tan saN-chim(Bo2 siong7 20:41).
(5) Lau7-pe7 Tai7-pit8 chim kiaN2 Ap-sa-liong5 (Bo2 ha7 14:63).
(6) Choe7-jin5 chim Chu2 Ia5-sou, lau5 bak8-sai2 hoan2-hoe2 (Lou7-ka 7:38).
(7) Kan-hiam2 e5 saN-chim.  Iok-ap chim A-ma2-sat, ti7 A-ma2-sat bo5 the5-hong5 e5 si5 eng7 to tuh8 si2 i(Bo2 ha7 20:4).  Iu5-tai7 eng7 chim-chhui3 be7 Ia5-sou (Thai3 26:48-49.  Kho2 14:45-46.  Lou7-ka 22:47-48).
(8) “Lin2 tioh8 eng7 seng3(聖) e5 saN-chim lai5 saN chheng2-an.”(I Lim5 16:20).
Lam5-lu2 e5 saN-chim:
1.  Na7 u7 chit8 e5 lam5-seng3 e7-hiau2 siuN7 ai3 ╳ chit8 e5 lu2-seng3, an2-ni si7 hian2-beng5 hit e5 lam5-seng3 i2-keng si7 seng5-sek8 piN3 toa7-lang5 lah.  Na7 u7 chit8 e5 lu2-seng3 chu7-hoat-tek ╳ ╳ ╳ lai5 chim, hit e5 lu2-seng3 i2-keng lau7 lah. (Chim-kiaN2, chim-sun).
2.  Hu-hu7 e5 saN-chim, bok8-hui si7 beh piau2-si7 thiaN3-cheng5, ke-thiN thiaN3-cheng5.  Na7-si7 an2-ni ti7 su-ha7 nng7 lang5 ka-ti7 tiam3 e5 si5 lai5 choe3, pi2-kau3 khah hap8-li2, bo5 su-iau3 tng cheng5-lai5 kong-jian5 lai5 piau2-ian2.  Lang5 khoaN3 liau2 m7-na7 bo5 sim-sek, u7-si5 soa3 e7 hou7 lang5 gin7-bak8.

3.  Hu-hu7 saN-chhim, beh chhut-khi3 saN-chim, m7-tat8 tioh8 chhut-goa7 to3--lai5 e5 saN-chim iau2 khah tiN.  Li2 na7 ai3 tiong7-hu siong5-siong5 khoaN3 li2 si7 pi2 pat8 e5 lu2-seng3 keng3 kho2-ai3 chiah e7.  Lu2-seng3 chin e5 kho2-ai3, m7-si7 tui3 khiok-soaN3 e5 sui2, phang-chui2 e5 phang, hoe-hun2 e5 peh8.  Khiok chiah e5 ko2-chin kui2-hun e7 pang-chan7 hou7 tiong7-hu ai3 chhin-kin7--li2.  Chong2-si7 lam5-seng3 sim-te2 sou2 hoaN-hi2, sou2-ai3 e5 si7 lu2-seng3 un-cheng5 (溫情) e5 chiau3-kou3, tiN-bit8 e5 an-ui3 kap kou2-le7.
Ti7 chia u7 chit8-hang7 chin ki5-koai3 e5 su7, chiu7-si7 seng3-chheh u7 ki3 cheng2-cheng2 e5 saN-chim na7 si7 m7-bat ki3 ang-bou2 e5 saN-chim.  Sit8-chai7 chin chhu3-bi7, i3-gi7 bu5-kiong5.  An2-ni tui3 i2-siong7 sou2 kong2 e5 lai5 khoaN3, saN-chim si7 jin5 cheng5 thiaN3-sim e5 chu7-jian5 liu5-lou7, sou2-i2 tek-khak tioh8 chhut tui3 chin-seng5 sun5-kiat, tek-khak m7-thang loan7-iong7, keng3-ka m7-thang ok-iong7 chiah ho2.  Seng3-keng kong2 “Siong7-te3 m7-si7 hun-loan7 e5, si7 ho5-peng5 e5.……  Hoan7-su7 tioh8 bun5-nga2 ia7 chiau3 kui-ki2 lai5 kiaN5.” Na7-si7 an2-ni kiam2-chhai2 u7 lang5 mng7 se-iuN5 chin seng7-heng5 saN-chim, an2-ni si7 ho2 a2 m7-ho2?  Chiau3 khoaN3 che kap te7-li2, bun5-hoa3, jin5-cheng5, hong-siok8 u7 toa7 koan-he7.  U7-si5 tang-iuN5 e5 le2-gi7 theh8 khi3 se-iuN5 be7 thong, chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni se-iuN5 e5 le2-gi7 theh8 lai5 lan2 tang-iuN5, u7 e5 ia7 be7 thong.  Na7 be7 thong e5 su7, lang5 thi2-chhio3, kong-kek.  Ho2, m7-ho2 si7 te7 ji7 bun7-te5.  Sou2-i2 tui3 chit chan5 su7 tak8 lang5 thang ka-ti7 siuN7.
C.  ThiaN3 e5 kek8-ti3 (愛的極致) chiu7-si7 bu5-ngou2 hi-seng (無我犧牲).
Lan2 na7 chu3-i3 thak8 Nga2-ko e5 seng3-keng e7 hoat-kian3 e7-bin7 sou2 ki3 e5 su7.
1.  Nga2-ko 2:16.  “Goa2 (chi2 sin-niu5) sou2 loan5-ai3 e5 siok8 goa2, goa2 ia7 siok8 i”(i chi2 tiong7-hu).

Ti7 chia sin-niu5 chiong pun2-sin choe3 pun2-ui7 lai5 kong2 i e5 tiong7-hu.  Che si7 put-hian5 chu7-ki2 pun2-ui7 e5 lu2-seng3.
2.  Nga2-ko 6:3 “Goa2 siok8 goa2 sou2 loan5-ai3 e5, goa2(chi2 sin-niu5) sou2 loan5-ai3 e5 ia7 siok8 goa2”
Ti7 chia seng kong2 pun2-sin si7 siok8 i e5 tiong7-hu, jian5-au7 kong2 tiong7-hu ia7-si7 siok8 ti7 i.  Ti3 chia u7 khah chin3-pou7, chiong tiong7-hu choe3 Chu2, pun2-sin choe3 pin lai5 kong2.
3.  Nga2-ko 7:10.  “Goa2(chi2 sin-niu5) siok8 goa2 sou2 loan5-ai3, I ia7 him-bou7 goa2.”
Ti7 chia sin-niu5 oan5-choan5 m7-kaN2 kong2 ka-ki7, oan5-choan5 eng7 tiong7-hu lai5 kong2.  Kong2 i si7 siok8 ti7 tiong7-hu.  M7-kaN2 kong2 tiong7-hu ia7-si7 siok8 ti7 i.  Si7 kong2 tiong7-hu ia7 him-bou7 i, ji5-chhiaN2 I(chi2 tiong7-hu) si7 eng7 toa7-ho7-ji7 lai5 sia2.  Chiu7-si7 tiong7-hu tiong-sim, i pun2-sin kam-goan7 oan5-choan5 but8-ngou2(沒我).  Chiu7-si7 khoaN3 bo5 ka-ki7 lai5 ko-ku2 i e5 tiong7-hu.  U7 iaN2, hu7-jin5-lang5 ti7 ka-teng5 chhin-chhiuN7 iam5 e5 po2-poe3.  Iam5 e7 tiau-ho5 it-chhe3 hou7 long2-chong2 e5 mih8 hian2-chhut ho2 e5 bi7-sou3, koh m7-bian2 tu2-tioh8 hu2-pai7.  Hu7-jin5-lang5 ia7-si7 an2-ni, hu7-jin5-lang5 ti7 ke-lai7 tiau-ho5, hou7 ka-teng5 tit-tioh8 iu-nga2, ho5-peng5, sio-lo7 e5 seng-oah8.  Hou7 ka-teng5 u7 beng5-long2 e5 chhio3-siaN, hoan-lok8 e5 si-koa, hoat-phoat e oah-khi.  A-i ku-k?m sio-lo iu-nga e kau-poe.  Tiong-hu tit-tioh pang-chan an-ui, se-kia° tit-tioh poe-iu° ka-s?.  Ch…t ke toan-toan-i°.  Hu-jin-lang lu-seng e kong-lck toa ah!  Chong-s? ?-thang chu-ko sai-phoat, ang-lang koai°-phiah.  Na-chun iam chham t? thng e lai-b?n ? soa°, ch…t-liap ch…t-liap h3 lang p3--tioh, chhui-khi un-un loh khi, put-tek-i tioh ka i phui-tiau.  Hu-jin-lang ia-s? an-ni, ho-kan-ho, sui to-sui, na-s? ko-seng thai-kiong, kap ke-lai ta-ke-koa° toa-peh sio-chek, hia°-so sio-k be-ho, chhiah te-te lian tiong-hu to koan thau-koe.  Ho-to-ho, gau-to-gau, kho-sioh ui i ch…t lang thong-ke e chhui-khi long khu-khu loh khi, u-si k-put-chiong e h3 lang phui chhut--lai.  Iam e po-poe chiu-s? bu-ng¯, oan-choan khoa° bo ka-t? goan iong-hoa(溶化) ti7 thng e5 lai7-bin7.  Hou7 choan5-the2 tit-tioh8 bi2-bi7, i ka-ti7 oan5-choan5 hi-seng, che chiu7-si7 iam5 e5 po2-kui3, kap ui2-tai7 e5 sou2-chai7.  Hu7-jin5-lang5 lu2-seng3 e5 ui2-tai7 po2-kui3 ia7-si7 chai7 ti7 chia.
Koh hu-hu7 e5 kiat-hap8 ia7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 chui2 kap thou5.  Chui2 hoan7 chui2, thou5 hoan7 thou5, chit8 hang7 ka7 i khng3 chit8-ui7 be7 choe3 sim2-mih8.  Chong2-si7 thou5, chui2 ka7 i chhiau choe3-hoe2, au7-lai5 e7 choe3 chiaN5 khi3-khu7, oaN2, poaN5, ang3 tang7.  Chiong hiah e5 jip8 io5 khi3 sio, ka7 i thng7-sek choe3 iu3-hui5.  U7 e5 chin sui2 hou7 lang5 tui3-tiong7.  Ti7 hia lan2 chi2-u7 khoaN3 tioh8 thou5 sio e5 hui5, long2 bo5 khoaN3 tioh8 chhiau thou5 e5 chui2.  Chui2 chiu7-si7 lu2-seng3 hu7-jin5-lang5.  I e7 pang-chan7 tiong7-hu seng5-ke ti3-hoe2, tiam2-peng chhut-chiong3, koaN ki ong5-hou7.  Lang5 chi2-u7 khoaN3 i e5 tiong7-hu, ki5-sit8 chiu7-si7 u7 liong5-chhe ti7 au7-bin7.  Io5 io-na5 e5 chhiu2, e7 io5-tang7 se3-kai3.  Chiu7-si7 i sou2 io5 e5 kiaN2 chiong-lai5 khia7 ti7 thek-tha3 sam-kun, giu5-ni2 se3-kai3, ti7 koan5 e5 te7-ui7 hou7 lang5 o-lo2, na7-si7 i choe3 hian5-bo2 bih ti7 au7-bin7.  Hoe2-chhia chin gau5 chau2, chun2-si5 lai5 un7-su hoe3, kheh hou7 lang5 toa7 l-lo2 li7-pian7.  Ki5-sit8 na7 bo5 hiah e5 tiam7-tiam7 hou7 lang5 tai5 ti7 thou5-kha-te2, siu7 tam5 siu7 sip, jim2 hou7 peh8-hia7 chhia e5 kan-khou2, kau3-boe2 noa7-tiau7 ti7 thou5-lai7, eng2 bo5 khoaN3 tioh8 thian-jit8 e5 chim2-bok8-a2, chiu7 chhia chit8 pou7 to be7 chau2.  Hiah e5 chim2-bok8-a2 chiu7-si7 lu2-seng3, hu7-jin5-lang5.  Ah!  Lu2-seng3, hu7-jin5-lang5 ah, lin2 sit8-chai7 chin hi-seng, lin2 tui3 ka-teng5, sia7-hoe7, kok-ka, se3-kai3 e5 kong3-hian3 sit8-chai7 ui2-tai7 ah!
Lan2 m7 thang siuN7 lu2-seng3 si7 chin loan2-jiok8, u7 iaN2, i chin nng2-chiaN2.  Chong2-si7 koh chit8-bin7 i si7 chin kiong5.  I pi2 lam5-seng3 peng5-kin khah nai7-mia7, khah gau5 jim2 thiaN3, jim2 koaN5, khah gau5 jim2 khou2.  Sui-si7 eng-hiong5 ia7 lan5-koe3 bi2-jin5-koan.  Ui7 chit8 e5 lu2-seng3 kok-ui7 hiat-kak8, chit8 kok e5 heng-soe, siaN5-ti5 e5 siu2, sit(守,失) siong5-siong5 hou7 chit8 e5 lu2-seng3 cho2-iu7.  Lu2-seng3 e5 ki-ti3, mou7-hiam2 sit8-chai7 thang kiaN, li2 khoaN3 se3-kai3 e5 kan2-tiap8(se3-choh) -thoan5 lu2-seng3 e5 oah8-tang7.  U7 iaN2, lu2-seng3 si7 chin ui2-tai7, chong2-si7 it-chhe3 e5 ui2-tai7 choe3-au7 iu5-goan5 si7 chai7 ti7 lu2-seng3 e5 bu5-ngou2 hi-seng e5 sneg-oah8.  An2-ni choe3 tiong7-hu e5 lam5-seng3 li2 beh eng7 chaiN2-iuN7 lai5 khoan2-thai7 li2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5.  I2-hut-sou2 5:25.  “Choe3 tiong7-hu e5, lin2 tioh8 thiaN3 hu7-jin5-lang5, chhin-chhiuN7 Ki-tok thiaN3 kau3-hoe7, ia7 thoe3 i hian3 ka-ke7.”  Tioh8 hian3-chhut li2 ka-ki7, chhin-chhiuN7 Ki-tok thiaN3 kau3-hoe7, ui7-tioh8 beh kiu3-siok8 kau3-hoe7 chiu7 kam-goan7 jim2-kho2 kau3 si2.  Lam5-seng3 li2 iau-kiu5 lu2-seng3 ui7-tioh8 li2, ui7-tioh8 li2 chit8-ke lai5 hi-seng, lai5 si2, Li2 bat siuN7 li2 ia7 tioh8 ui7 lu2-seng3 lai5 hi-seng lai5 si2 a2-bo5?  Eng3-kai u7, an2-ni chiah e7 peng5-heng5 peN5-pang7.  Lam5-seng3 chiam3-iaN5, u7 chiN5 thang lim-chiu2, chiah8-hun hong-so, bo5 chiN5 thang thiah-ioh8 hou7 hu7-jin5-lang5 chiah8--e5 chin che7.  Hu7-jin5-lang5 tai3 hu7-jin5-lang5-peN7 kong2 bo5 chiN5 thang ka7 i i, na7-si7 u7 chiN5 thang khi3 hoa-ke liu2-hang7 be2 chhio3 e5 chio2.  Cha-pou-lang5 ah!  Bong-bong li2 e5 liong5-sim, ti7 chit-khoan2 e5 seng-oah8 beh ng3-bang7 kian3-chiaN5 tiN-bit8 bi2-moa2 e5 ka-teng5 choat8-tui3 bo5 ng3-bang7.
Koh kong2 chit8 pai2, bi2-moa2 tiN-bit8 e5 ka-teng5 m7-si7 chu7-jian5 u7--e5, si7 nng7-lang5 kiong7-tong5 kian3-cho7 e5.  Chit8 e5 beh khiN5-ke, chit8 e5 m7, chu-chu siuN7 beh phoa3 ke, an2-ni bo5 hoat-tou7.  Cha-pou than3, tioh8 ai3 cha-bou2 hoaN7, chit8 e5 chai, chit8 e5 ak-chui2, an2-ni chiah e7 chiah8 tioh8 heng7-hok ai3-cheng5 e5 koe2-chi2.  Tioh8 e7 ki3-tit hou7--lang5 pi2 theh8--lang5 khah u7 hok-khi3.  ThiaN3-cheng5 ia7-si7 an2-ni.  Lan2 u7 liong7 thang thiaN3 lang5, pi2 tiaN7 siuN7 beh tit lang5 thiaN3 e5 khah ho2.  Tak8-lang5 to chu7-jian5 u5 thiaN3 lang5 e5 sim, siang7-si5 tak8 lang5 to ng3-bang7 lang5 thiaN3.  Lang5 ti7 se3-kan sim-lai7 na7 bo5 thiaN3 poaN3 lang5, siang7-si5 ia7 kam2-kak bo5 poaN3-lang5 thiaN3 i, an2-ni hit e5 lang5 e7 kam2-kak chin pi-chham2, kou-tok8, bo5 liau5, u7 si5 e7 khi2-siau2, hek8-chia2 e7 kau3 chu7-sat.  Tui3 lang5 si-ai3(施愛) , na7 u7 lang5 seng5-siu7, kam2-kak chin hoaN-hi2.  Na7 u7 chit8 e5 lang5 chiong i e5 ai3-cheng5 beh hou7 lang5, ia7 bo5 lang5 ai3 ka7 i seng5-siu7, i e7 chin loe2-chi3, u7 si5 e7 chu7-po7 chu7-khi3, u7 si5 e7 seN ki2 sat-jin5, chu7-sat e5 kheng-ki2 bong5-tong7.  Hit e5 lang5 na7 chiong 5 hun thiaN3 beh hou7 i e5 tui3-siong7, i e5 tui3-siong7 m7-tihN8.  An2-ni e7 hoan2-to3-tng2 oan3 i 5 hun, m7-si7, u7 si5 soa3 piN3 oan3 i 8 hun.  Na7 chiong 10 hun thiaN3 beh hou7 i e5 tui3-siong7.  I e5 tui3-siong7 khi2-thau5 na2-chun2 boeh, au7-lai5 ui7 …… soa3 hoan2 khi3-khiok, soa3 biau2-si7, ku3-choat8 hit e5 thiaN3.  Hit-si5 e5 hoan2-eng3 m7-si7 sio2-khoa2.  U7-si5 e7 eng7 si2 phoe3 …… i3, lai5 pai5-siat ai3 siu7 ku3-choat8 e5 hin7.  Na7 lu2--e5 bo5 hoat-tit lam5--e5 ta-oa5, khah siong5 e7 khi2-siau2, chu7-sat, a2-si7 iau3-kiu5 choe3-hoe2 si2.  Na7 lam5--e5 e7 jia2 chhut hui2-iong5,(eng7 ioh8-chui2 phoah lu2 e5 bin7 hou7 i noa7, a2-si7 hou7 i chhiN-mi5) a2-si7 sat-jin5 e5 su7-kiaN7.  U7 si5 m7-na7 thai5 tui3-siong7 e5 lu2-seng3, lian5 chou2-tong3 e5 pe7-bo2 to e7 chiah8-khui.  Hit-si5 e5 sim-li2 pi2 ia2-gu5, pi2 khip-hiat-kui2 koh khah li7-hai7.  Sou2-i2 lam5-lu2 iN7-seng3-kan choat8-tui3 m7-thang sui5-pian7 iok-sok ai3-cheng5, jian5-au7 sui5-pian7 koh saN poe7, u7-si5 e7 jia2-chhut liau7 be7 tioh8 e5 chai-ho7.
Ai3-cheng5 m7-si7 eng7 chiN5 e7-tit boe2--lai5 e5, ia7 m7-si7 e7-tit hou7 li2 eng7 tiN-gian5 bit8-gu2 phian3--lai5, koai2--lai5 e5.  Ai3-cheng5 si7 ai3 tui3 seng5-sim seng5-i3, lau5-koaN7, piaN3-mia7 eng7 sim keh-kau3, liu5-sim hoe7-sin5(留心會神) lai5 choe3, it-seng e5 kiat-chok.  Si7 sim-leng5-tek ge7-sut8 e5 piau2-hian7.  Hu-hu7 na2-lau7 si7 na2-sui2, lau7-bou2 e5 bin7 na2-jiau5 khiok-soaN3 kng-am3 na2 hun-beng5, che chiah si7 bi2-sut8 e5 piau2-hian7.  M7-si7 lau7 tioh8 bo5 ho2 siaN-khui3, ku7-khim5 chai-seng3 na2 ti-im chiah e7 na2 chhut ho5-hai5 e5 siaN.
Na7 kong2 lau7 chiu7 hiam5 chhau3-lau7-hian3.  SeN chit8 e5 kiaN2 loh8 kau2 ki-hoe, lau7 lah piN3 ou-hi5-khak lah chiu7 m7-tihN8, chiu7 siuN7 beh oaN7-sin.  Che si7 chin kai-si2 e5 hu-hu7.
Hu7-jin5-lang5 ti7 ka-teng5 tiong si7 khia7 ti7 sim2-mih8 te7-ui7?  Goa2 chioh chit8 e5 kou3-su7 lai5 kong2.  Kong2 u7 chit8 e5 bou2-lang5, i e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 pang3 se3-kiaN2 lai5 piat8-se3.  I kam2-kak ia7 beh lai7, ia7 beh goa7 chap8-ji7-hun e5 khun3-lan5.  Chiu7 siuN7 ai3 chhiaN3 chit8 e5 Ka-cheng3-hu7(家政婦) lai5 pang-chan7 ke-lai7.  I chiu7 chhut kong2-ko3 ai3 teng-kiu5 an2-ni e5 lang5. (1) Chit8-jit8 choe3 24 tiam2 cheng. (2) Chit8-le2-pai3 choe3 7 jit8. (3) Chit8-ni5 choe3 365 jit8, bo5 hiu-khin5. (4) Oe7 hiau2 chu2-chiah8, chu2 liau2 seng2 koh hah8 chhui3. (5) Oe7-hiau2 ki3-siau3 bo5 tham-sim. (6) Oe7-hiau2 io gin2-na2 ka3-si7 kiaN2-ji5. (7) Gau5 cheng2-tun3 ke-lai7, lai7-goa7 cheng2-che5, chheng-khi3-siuN3. (8) Oe7-hiau2 se2-saN pou2-thiN7, choe3-saN. (9) Am3-si5 m7-na7 io se3-kiaN2 khun3, ia7 gau5 an-ui3 chu2-lang5. (10) Tioh8 u7 i2-siong7 e5 tiau5-kiaN7; Lai5 hoaN-hi2 chhut hou7 i chiah8, chheng7, kap toa3, na7-si7 bo5 kang-chiN5, kau3-boe2 chaiN2-iuN7?  Long2 bo5 lang5 lai5 eng3-bou7, na7 u7 chiu7-si7 goan7 hi-seng e5 gong7-lang5.  Bo5 pat8 lang5 na7 u7 chiu7-si7 ka-ti7 e5 bou2.  Ah!  Hu7-jin5-lang5 ui2-tai7 ah!  Si7 ka-teng5-tiong choe3 hi-seng e5 gong7-lang5.
Ti7 sia7-hoe7 e5 kau-poe5 iu2-ai3 khi2-thau5 lou7 khah khoah, chin khoai3 kau, li2 hiaN goa2 ti7, chiu2-chneg-a2 saN-cheN tu, na7-si7 chiong-lai5 bo5 boe2.  Hu-hu7 e5 thiaN3 khi2-thau5 lou7 eh8-eh8, chin oh sio tu2, mng5 eh8-eh8 chin oh chin3-jip8.  Chong2-si7 it-tan3 saN tu2-tioh8, kam2-kak si7 sim-sim siong-in3, cheng5-tau i3-hap8, na2 kiaN5 na2 khoai3-lok8.  Sim na2 khui-khoah, bo5 keh-moh8, na2 lau7 na2 saN-thiaN3, na2 sio po2-poe3.  Kau3-boe2 pek8-siu2 kai-lo2, ng3-bang7 tang5 kui thian-hiong, an2-ni chiah hap8-sek.  Chiah8 lau7 chiah oan-ke, u7 kiaN2, u7 sun chiah hoah li5-ian5, chiah tho2 kheh-hiaN, chiah tho2 cha-bou2.  ThiN-kha-e7 bo5 pi2 chit khoan2 e5 lang5 khah poe7 thian-liong5, hiau sim-heng7.  Siok8-gu2 kong2 ang-bou2 oan-ke kau2 to bo5 ai3 phiN7.  Sit8-chai7 kian3-siau3, ho5-hong2 ni5-lau7 chiah lai5 oan-ke li5-ian5 saN pun-khui.  

11
VII.  Ai3 long7-phoa3 ka-teng5 a2-bo5?
Na7-ai3 khi3 an-ni choe3 chiu7 long7 e7 phoa3.
1.  Chhong2-se2 ki3 16:1-7.  21:8-21.
Khi3 oh8 Sat-lai7 ka7 i ang A-pek-lan5 tau3 soan2 se3-i5.  Hit-si5 i si7 chiong lu2-pi7 Ha7-kah, hou7 i kap i e5 tiong7-hu thong-pang5, kau3-boe2 loan7 kau3 tioh8 koaN2 chhut-khi3.  M7-na7 koaN2 se3-i5-a2, lian7 kiaN2 ia7 m7-tihN8, koh hit e5 koaN2-hoat si7 chin chan5-jim2.  A-pek-lan5 ke-hoe2 hiah toa7, be7 chhut-tit chit8 chiah iuN5, chit8 chiah lu5 hou7 in.  Chiau3 Chhong3-se3-ki3 21:I sou2-ki3.
“A-pek-liap8-han2 cha2-cha2 khi2-lai5, theh8 piaN2 kap chit8 phoe5-te7 e5 chui2 hou7 Ha7-kah; he7 ti7 i e5 keng-thau5 teng2; lian5 gin2-na2 soa3 kah i khi3; i chiu7 khi3, kau3 Piat8-si7-pa e5 khong3-ia2 chiu7 kiaN5 bo5 lou7.” Chui2 chiah8 liau2 Ha7-kah chiong kiaN2 khng3 tiam3 chhiu7 kha, put-jim2 khoaN3 kiaN2 go7 si2, chhui3-ta si2, sou2-i2 li7 hng7-hng7 pang3-siaN thi5-khau3 i e5 phaiN2-mia7.  Tng I2-sit8-ma2-li7 boe7 chhut-si3 e5 si5 chiu7 hou7 chu2-bo2 phaiN2 khoan2-thai7.  Chhong3 16:6. sia2 kong2
“Sat-lai7 khou2-chhou2 i, i chiu7 tui3 Sat-lai7 e5 bin7-cheng5 to5-chau2.” Ui7 chit e5 su7 A-pek-lan5 kap Sat-lai7 ti7 ka-teng5 u7 put-tng7 e5 hong-pho, thak8 Chhong3 16:4-6.  chiu7 chai.  Ha7-kah se3-i5-a2 u7 sin chiu7 siu7 tek-thiong2 khoaN3-khin chu2-bu2, oan-ke kau3 ke-kau2 to bo5 peng5-an.  Sat-lai7 khau3-loa7 A-pek-lan5.  A-pek-lan5 be7 jim2 tit ka-teng5 put-si5 loan7, chiah tui3 Sat-lai7 kong2 “Lu2-pi7 ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2, li2 thang sui5-i3 khoan2-thai7 i”.  In-ui7 Sat-lai7 gia5 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 hiap8-che3 pek i e5 tiong7-hu, Sat-lai7 kong2 “Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 li2 goa2 e5 tiong-kan phoaN3-toan3”.  Sat-lai7 chin-chiaN3 theng2 i e5 toa7-bou2 e5 chhu5-ui(雌威).  Toa7 khou2-tok8 ji5 tek8 khou2-tok8.  Kau3-boe2 Ha7-kah khoaN3-phoa3, ang-sai3 kah be7 choe3 chu2, theng2 toa7-bou2 khou2-tok8--i.  Put-tek-i2 tioh8 chau2, siuN7 beh si2, heng7-gu7 thiN-sai3 chhut-hian7 kio3 i to3 lai5.  Chong2-si7 kau3-boe2 kiaN2 chhut-si3 to chap8-goa7 hoe3 lah, ia7-si7 nge7-nge7 koh koaN2 chhut-khi3.  Bo5 pun kau3 chit8-te3 oaN2, chit8-siang ti7, khang-chhiu2 koaN2 chhut-khi3.  An-ni lang5 na7 ai3 long7-phoa3 ka-teng5 e5 te7 it hong-hoat tioh8 chhui-chian3 se3-i5 hou7 ang-sai3.
Tui3-ti7 A-pek-lan5 kap Ha7-kah thong-pang5 e5 su7 Seng3-keng ka7 lan2 kong2 saN-hang7 tai7-chi3.
1.  Kap Ha7-kah thong-pang5 hit-si5 si7 boe7 siu7 kat-le2 cheng5 “ku7-lang5 A-pek-lan5” e5 si5, m7-si7 oaN7-sin choe3 “A-pek-liap8-han2” e5 si5.
2.  Ui7-tioh8 chit-chan5 su7, m7-na7 im5-loan7, si7 eng7 lang5 e5 ti3-sek beh lai5 tai7-the3 Siong7-te3 e5 ke3-oe7.  Sou2-i2 ka-teng5 seN-khi2 toa7-hong-pho, tioh8 kau3 tu5-khi3 chiah e7 soah.
3.  Peng5-si5 hou7 Siong7-te3 soan2--i, khoaN3 choe3 peng5-iu2 khoan2-thai7 choe3-hoe2 kiaN5, choe3-hoe2 kong2-oe7 e5 A-pek-lan5.  Tui3 chhoa7 se3-i5 Ha7-kah hou7 Siong7-te3 chek-pi7.  ChhiaN2 thak8 Chhong3-se3-ki3 17:1.
“A-pek-lan5 kau2-chap8-kau2 he3 e5 si5, Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 A-pek-lan5 hian2-hian7, ka7 i kong2, Goa2 si7 choan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3, li2 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 kiaN5-choe3 tioh8 oan5-choan5” chit-ku3 u7 ham5-khng3 chek-pi7 e5 i3-su3.  Koh lan2 khoaN3 Chhong3-se3-ki3 16:16.  Ha7-kah seN I2-sit8-ma2-li7 e5 si5 A-pek-lan5 si7 86 hoe3.  Kau3 17:1 A-pek-lan5 koh thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siaN e5 si5 si7 99 hoe3, an-ni thau5 boe2 iok 13-14 ni5 ku2, Siong7-te3 bo5 kap A-pek-lan5 kong2-oe7.  Che si7 goa7-nih thang kiaN e5 su7 ah!  Ui7 chhoa7 se3-i5 hou7 Siong7-te3 bo5 hoaN-hi2 kau3 an-ni.
2.  Chhong3 25:28.  27:1-8.
Oh8 I2-sat kap Li7-pek-ka in ang-a2-bou2.  SeN nng7 e5 kiaN2 chit8 e5 I2-so3, chit8 e5 Nga2-kok.  Lau7-pe7 thiaN3 toa7-kiaN2 I2-so3; in-ui7 i siuN7 kong2 chit e5 e7 khi3 phah-lah8 choe3 ho2 chhai3 thang hou7 i phoe3 sio-chiu2.  Lau7-bo2 thiaN3 Nga2-kok, in-ui7 i siuN7 chit e5 khah koai, khah u7 oe7 kong2, e7 pang-chan7 i choe3 ke-lai7 e5 kang tiaN5.  An-ni chit8 lang5 phian-ai3 chit8 e5.  Lan7-pe7 kap toa7-kiaN2 su-iok beh ka7 i chiok-hok.  Lau7-bo2 ka3 kiaN2 kong2 peh8-chhat8, pang-chan7 i phian3 lau7-pe7.  Hai7 tit ke-lai7 loan7 chhau-chhau, hiam2-hiam2 chiu7 jia2-chhut kut-jiok8 hiaN-ti7 sio chan5-sat.  Ka-chai3 Nga2-kok chau2 tit li7.  Na7-ai3 ke-teng5 loan7, chiu7 ang-bou2 toa7-se3-sim koh phian-ai3 kiaN2-ji5, long7 kiaN2-ji5 sio-cheN ke-hoe2, an-ni iu5-goan5 chin khoai3-phoa3.  Ia7 m7-si7 bo5 po3, Nga2-kok phian3 in lau7-pe7, kau3 ni5-lau7 ia7-si7 hou7 in kiaN2 phian3.  I e5 kiaN2 ia7-si7 hiaN-ti7-a2 sio hai7.
3.  Su7-su-ki3 16:19-21.
Oh8 chham-sun hong3-tong7, chiong chhiong-ki Tai7-li7-lah e5 toa7-thui2 choe3 chim2-thau5.  Liu5-liu5 khi3, na7 an-ni choe3 ka-teng5 m7-na7 e7 loan7, ia7 kho2-leng5 chhin-chhiuN7 Chham-sun e7 lok8-phek.
4.  Sat-bi2-ni2 siong7 2:12-17.  3:10-18.

Oh8 I2-li7 bo5 tiau-tok kiaN2.  KiaN2 Ho5-hut-ni5, Hui-ni5-khap bu5 ok put-chok, biau2-si7 Siong7-te3.  Kau3-boe2 m7-na7 ka-phoa3 jin5-bong5; lian5 Iok-kui7 to7 soa3 sit-loh8.
5.  Sat-bo2-ni2 ha7 11:2-27.
Oh8 Tai7-pit8 e5 sia5-loan5, tham Ou-li7-a e5 bou2 Poat8-si7-pa.  Tai7-pit8 kiaN5-iu5 ti7 ong5-kiong e5 liang5-tai5-teng2, bo5 tiuN-ti5 khoaN3 tioh8 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 teh se2-ek8, iong5-mau7 chin sui2.  An-ni u7 choe7 a2-bo5?  Goa2 siuN7 bo5.  Bo5 tiuN-ti5 khoaN3 kui2-na7 e5 hu7-jin5 lang5 long2 chin-sui2, long2 chhiah-sin lou7-the2 teh se2-ek8, un2-tang3 chin ho2 khoaN3.  Thang khia7 hia khoaN3 a2-bo5?  Tu5 khoaN3 ka7-ti7 e5 ╳ ╳ ╳ i2-goa7, goa2 siuN7 choat8-tui3 m7-thang.  Siat-su2 bo5 tiuN-ti5 hou7 li2 khoaN3 tioh8; goa2 siuN7 lan2 tioh8 kin2 oat-chau2 m7-thang koh khoaN3.  In-ui7 lang5 loan2-jiok8 kiaN liau2 tiaN7 tiam3 hia khoaN3 sim-lai7 e7 seN-khi2 sia5-liam7.  Tai7-pit8 khoaN3 liau2 be7 soah tit, soa3 chhe-lang5 tham3-thiaN hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 si7 chi7-chui7?  Ti7-chia i2-keng chho3-gou7.  Hit e5 lang5 si7 chi7-chui7 eng3-kai kap Tai7-pit8 bo5 kan-siap8.  Ho5-pit tham3-thiaN?  Ki3-jian5 chai si7 Ou-li7-a e5 bou2, an2-ni si7 iu2 hu chi hu7(有夫之婦).  Si7 u7 ang e5 cha-bou2-lang5, koh si7 ka-ti7 e5 pou7-ha7 e5 bou2, chai liau2 ka7 Ou-li7-a tau3 hoaN-hi2 chiu7 ho2.  M7-bian2 chhe lang5 khi3 chiong hu7-jin5-lang5 chiap lai5.  Hu7-jin5-lang5 siu7 tiau3 iat-kian3 tai7-ong5 che si7 chin eng5-kng.  Chu7-jian5 m7-kaN2 gek8-chi2 chiu7 lai5.  Lai5, su3-iat ka7 i bian2-le7, in-ui7 si7 ka-ti7 e5 pou7-ha7 e5 chhe-chu2.  An2-choaN2 tioh8 chai i e5 ╳ ╳ tu2-a2 chheng-khi3.  Ti7 chia Tai7-pit8 chin kai-si2.  Chhia loh8-kia7 se3-bin7 oh tong3 lah, kau3-boe2 chu7-jian5 peng2-chhia.  Tang5-pang5 lah, u7 sin-in7 lah.  Kau3-chia hoan2-hoe2 iau2 si7 tai7-tiong7-hu.  Ho5-pit ka-ti7 thau-chiah8, ou-kau2 thau-chiah8, chiah kio3 peh8-kau2 to3 lai5 siu7 choe7.  Tu2-tioh8 Ou-li7-a iu7 gong7-tiong, m7 to3-khi3 ti3 Ou-soan-bou7.  Goan7 tiam3 ong5-kiong ku jim5-chiN5-kha.  Che-iuN7 e5 chin7-tiong eng3-kai tioh8 ki3 tai7-kong chit8-chhu3, toa7-toa7 ka-chiong2.  Sim2-mih8 Tai7-pit8 chiah soa3 it-put-chok ji7-put-hiu.  Chiam3-bou2 toat8-chhe, soa3 eng7 leng2-to sat-jin5 ke3, pek Ou-li7-a ham7-tin7 cho7-si7 put-kiu3.

Chit khoan2-su7 u7 po3 a2-bo5?  U7.  I e5 kiaN2 Am3-lun3 kan-im5 sio2-moai7 ThaN-ma2.  Ap-sa-liong5 ia7-si7 i e5 kiaN2 po3-oan thai5-si2 hiaN-ti7 Am3-lun3 liau2-au7 chiu7 to5-chau2.  Au7-lai5 bou5-hoan2, hiam2-hiam2 pek-si2 lau7-pe7 Tai7-pit8.  Pek-tit Tai7-pit8 chau2-thau5 bo5 lou7 thau3-me5 koe3 Khip-lun5-khe, siam2-pi7 ti7 soaN-kan khong3-ia2 lai5 chau2-mia7.  Kai-chai3 Tai7-pit8 chiong-lai5 u7 toa7-toa7 chham3-hoe2, tit-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 sia3-bian2.
6.  Ong5 siong7 11:1-14.
Oh8 So2-lo5-bun5 lau7 hoan-tian.  Thiong3-ai3 goa7-kok e5 bi2-lu2, u7 hou7 hui 700 e5 long2-si7 kui3-chok8 e5, koh u7 pin3-hui 300 e5, chiaN3-keng, hou7-hui, pin3-hui sng3 kui chheng e5 bou2.  Chin-si7 kai-si2.  Seng3-chheh sia2 “Chiah e5 lu2-chu2 iu2-hek8 i e5 sim …… khi3 pai3 pat8 e5 Siong7-te3, i e5 sim bo5 sun5-choan5 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa i e5 Siong7-te3.” Au7-lai5 ui7-tioh8 hiah e5 bo7, khi2-bio7 kap Seng3-tian7 saN ng3.  Kap hiah e5 bou2 khi3 sio-hiuN ti7 ngou2-siong7 e5 che3-toaN5.
Seng3-keng ki3-kong2 “Lun7 kau3 chiah e5 liat8-kok, Ia5-ho5-hoa bat hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2, Lin2 m7-thang khi3 in hia, in ia7 m7-thang lai5 lin2 chia, in-ui7 in oe7 hou7 lin2 e5 sim phian-oai, khi3 toe3 in e5 siong7-te3; chong2-si7 So3-lo5-bun5 loan5-ai3 hiah e5 cha-bou2-gin2-na2, kap in kiat-hun.”(I Liat-ong5 11:2).  Khi2 seng3-tian7 toa7 jiat8-sim, sia2 Si-phian e5 chit8-pou7-hun7, sia2 Chim-gian5, sia2 Nga2-ko, sia2 Thoan5-to7, tu3-su lip8-soat, khong-chian5 choat8-hou7 e5 toa7 ti3-hui7 e5 beng5-kun So3-lo5-bun5 sit-pai7 kok phoa3 ti7 chiah e5 pai3 ngou2-siong7 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-na2.  Ah!  Chham-sun, Tai7-pit8, So3-lo5-bun5 sui si7 eng-hiong5, tai7-ti3 ia7 lan5-koe3 bi2-jin5-koan.  Chin-chiaN3 tioh8 keng2-kai3-ah lu2-sek.
7.  Liat8-ong5 siong7 16:29. 22:40.  Liat8-ong5 ha7 9:29-37.
KhoaN3 I2-sek-liat8 ong5 A-khap chhoa7 Se-tun3 ong5 pai3-put8 lang5 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 Ia5-sian2-piat.  Jia2-chhut Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siu7-khi3 3 ni5 poaN3 bo5 loh8-hou7 toa7 ki-hng.  Goan5-in chiu7-si7 choan5-kok pian3-te7 khi2 put8-bio7.  Tui3 Se-tun3 tit8 su-jip8 Ang5-i5, Sai-kong, peh-siN3 thang kong2 choan5-kok ngou2-siong7-kau3 hoa3.  Chhut Sian-ti I2-li7-a kap hiah e5 Sai-kong, Aan5-i5 tau3-hoat.  Siong7-te3 khah iaN5, chiah koh sin3-giong2 hok8-heng.  Ui7 an2-ni Ia5-sian2-piat tai7-theng2 chhu5-ui, ke-bo2 e7 thi5, beng7-leng7 tui sat I2-li7-a.  I2-li7-a chit8-si5 toa7-kiaN, chau2-kau3 bo5 iong5-sin chi te7, soa3 ti7 lo5-tin5 chhiu7-e7 kiu5 si2.  Au7-lai5 siat-ke3 hou7 Ong5 chiam3 Na2-pok8 e5 pho-to5-hng5, eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3 si2 bu5-kou3 e5 Na2-pok8, choe7-chek teng5-teng5 thah8-thah8, kau3-boe2 A-khap kap A-lan5 ong5 chian3-cheng tin7-bong5.  Au7-lai5 Ia5-sian2-piat ti7 se-chng-lau5 siu7 Ia5-hou7 kio3 thai3-kam3 tui3 lau5-teng2 e5 thang-a2 ka7 i chhia loh8 khi3; i e5 huih choaN7 tioh8 chhiuN5-piah, sin-si hou7 lang5 thun2-tah8.  Kau3 beh ka7 i tai5 e5 si5 chiah kan-ta chhoe7 tioh8 i e5 thau5-khak, kap kha-te5, kap chhiu2-chiuN2.  Ki-u5 e5 long2 hou7 kau2 thoa khi3 chiah8.  I2-sek-liat8 kok tui3 an2-ni toa7 soe-bi5, kau3-boe2 bong5-kok.
Teng2-bin7 chit chhit e5 kou3-su7 sit8-chai7 hou7 lan2 chin thang kiaN.  Lang5 na7 ai3 chhoe7 si2-lou7, ai3 ka-teng5 phoa3, kok-ka bong5 tioh8 khi3 oh8.  Ok iu2 ok-po3, sian7 iu2 sian7-po3, m7-si7 bo5 po3, si7 jit8-chi2 boe7 to3.  Lan2 e5 sin3-giong2 kiam2 e7 tat8-tioh8 A-peh-liap8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok.  Lan2 e5 eng-hiong5 ti3-sek kiam2 e7 tat8-tioh8 Chham-sun, Tai7-pit8, So3-lo5-bun5; choe3 m7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 to iu5-goan5 khian3-chek bo5 sia3-bian2.  Ho5-hong3 li2, kap goa2.  Tioh8 sio2-sim keng2-seng2.
Chi2-moai7 ah, li2 ai3 koh oh8 a2-bo5?  Na7-ai3, khi3 oh8 Na2-pho-lun5 e5 kiau-chhe, chha2-loan7 Na2-pho-lun5 kou3 pan7 cheng3-su7, m7 kap i tam7 ai3-cheng5.  Kou3 chian3-cheng, tang-chau2 se-phun, lam5-chun5 pak-be2(南船北馬) , m7-kap i san3-pou7 thiau3-bu2.  Loan7 kau3 Na2-pho-lun5 bo5 hoat i ta-oa5.  Oh8 Thok-ni2-su-thai3 e5 bou2 tiaN7 loan7 in ang be7 hiau2 ai3-chiN5.  Loan7 kau3 Thok-ni2-su-thai3 (?????) chau2 bo5 lou7, au7-lai5 khi3 si2 tiam3 ti7 beh khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 seng3-te7 sun5-le2 e5 chit8-e5 sio2 iah8-thau5.  Oh8 Lim5-kheng2 in bou2 chhiah-te-te, keh8-keh8-jiang2, khi3--tioh8 teh lim te5 lian5 te5-poe to tim3-khi3.  Pek tit Lim5-kheng2 tioh8 chhut-khi3 liu5.  Oh8 Sou-kek-ti2 e5 bou2 ka7 tiong7-hu lam5 chui2.  Oh8 Iok-han7 oe7-su-le2 e5 bou2 bu5-ko3 tiong7-hu tho2 cha-bou2 thau seN-kiaN2.  Be7-bai2 ou3; poh-kaN2 si7 chhoa7 tioh8 chhiah cha-bou2, in ang chiah e7 long2 choe3 se3-kai3 e5 ui2-jin5 ia7 bo5 tek-khak.  Li2 khoaN3 i2-siong7 e5 le7 kiam2 m7-si7 long2 an2-ni?  Lang5 kong2 hou7 chhiah bou2 ka3 chit8-pai2, pi2 hou7 pat8 lang5 ka3 saN-pai2 khah u7 kong-hau7.  An2-ni chhoa7 tioh8 chhiah bou2 e5 lang5 bo5 tek-khak si7 bai2.  Tan3-si7, mai3-tit khah ho2.
TaN chhin-ai3 e5 chi2-moai7, lau2-sit8 kong2 i2-siong7 chiah e5 bo5 ko3 tiong7-hu e5 keng-che3, bin7-phoe5, kiuh-kiuh-jiong2 ngauh8-ngauh8-liam7 bo5 soah e5 su7, un2-tang3 e7 chiong tiN-bit8 e5 ka-teng5 long7 kau3 na2-chun2 oah8-te7-gek8 e5 khou2-chham2.
Ia7 hiaN-ti7, lang5 ti7 se3-kan na7 be7-tit chiong i e5 ka-teng5 choe3 i cheng-sin5-tek un-loan2 in-ai3 an-hioh e5 sou2-chai7.  Tioh8 koh-khi3 chin5-lau5 chhou2-koan2(秦樓楚館) ang5-teng lek8-chiu2, hoa-ke liu2-hang7 lai5 chhoe7 hoan-lok8 an-ui3 e5 lang5 sit8-chai7 chhi-chham2 ah!
But8-lun7 ti7 chong-kau3 sim-leng5-siong7 e5 an-ui3 si7 tui3 Siong7-te3 lai5 tit-tioh8.  Na7-si7 Jiok8-the2-siong7 cheng-sin5 e5 an-ui3, hiat-kak8 ka-teng5, kong2 ti7 pat8-ui7 iau2 u7 pi2 ka-teng5 khah ho2 e5 sou2-chai7.  Ti7 se3-kan iau2 u7 pi2 pe7 bu2 iau2 khah u7 thang chun-keng3, iau2 u7 lang5 pi2 kut-jiok8 e5 hiaN-ti7 khah chhin, iau2 u7 lang5 pi2 ka-ti7 e5 ang-bou2 khah saN-thiaN3, chit e5 lang5 e5 seng-oah8 un2-tang3 chin bo5 chu7-jian5.  Eng3-kai si7 seng hau3-keng3 pe7-bo2, seng kui-jiok8 hiaN-ti7 saN-chhin, seng ang-bou2 saN-thiaN3, au7-lai5 tui3 kin7 kau3-hng7, thiaN3 chhu3-piN soa3 kau3 thiaN3 cheng3-lang5, an2-ni chiah be7 si7 hui, thau5-boe2 tian-to2.  
  
12
VIII Ai3 hak8-sip8 hu-hu7 e5 ai3-cheng5 hou7 i eng2-kou3(永固) a2-bo5?
Goa2 siuN7 tak8 lang5 to ai3.  Na7-si7 an2-ni tioh8 lai5 seng teng3-cheng3 2 hang7 su-siuN2.
1.  Tioh8 hun-piat “Loan5-ai3 chu7-iu5” kap “Chu7-iu5 loan5-ai3” e5 su-siuN2.

“Loan5-ai3 chu7-iu5;” i3-su3 si7 chhut-chai7 li2 beh loan5-ai3, a2-si7 m7 loan5-ai.  A2-si7 kong2 li2 tui3 chit chan5 su7 phau7 hoan2-tui3 e5 su-siuN2, li2 m7 ai3 kap iN7-seng3 kong2 loan5-ai3 e5 su7.  Kong2 khah kin2 li2 beh ke3, m7-ke3, beh chhoa7, m7-chhoa7, lu2 u7 chu7-iu5.  A2-si7 kong2 li2 u7 chu7-iu5 thang keng2 li2 sou2 ai3 e5 lang5, lai5 saN phit-phoe3.  Na7 an2-ni e5 theng5-tou7 e5 ke2-soeh, ko2-chin tak8 lang5 to u7 chu7-iu5-koan5.  Tian-te3 eng7 kiong5-koan5 lai5 pek hun, a2-si7 eng7 kim-chiN5 lai5 be2 e5 kiat-hun si7 chho3-gou7.  Lang5 chiau3 li2-khi3, lu2-seng3 eng3-kai u7 chu7-iu5 thang ke3 i sou2 ai3 ke3, loan5 i sou2 ai3 loan5 e5 lang5.  Lam5-seng3 eng3-kai u7 chu7-iu5 thang chhoa7 i sou2 ai3 chhoa7, thiaN3 i sou2 ai3 thiaN3 e5 lang5.
Chong2-si7 “Chu7-iu5 loan5-ai3” chiu7 m7-thang.  Chiau3 khah che7 lang5 e5 ke2-soeh kong2 chit ku3 si7 piN3 choe3 bo5 teng7-seng3.  A2-si7 chiong loan5-ai3 choe3 iu5-hi3, thit-tho5, kun2-chhio3.  Bo5 chu7-che3, bo5 liam5-thi2.  Ou-ang5-tah, loan7-loan7 kau, loan7-loan7 chhap, saN-kak, si3-kak e5 to-kak im5-loan7.  Lang5 na7 kong2 “Lang5 kho2-i2 chu7-iu5 loan5-ai3” chiu7 seng7 chit e5 “chu7-iu5” lai5 loan7-loan7 choe3, che si7 chin kian3-siau3.  Se3-kan bo5 pi2 chit hang7 koh-khah kian3-siau3.  M7-na7 kian3-siau3, un2-tang3 beh tu2-tioh8 toa7 chhi-chham2.  Sou2-i2 thau5 chit8-tiam2 lam5-lu2 iN7-seng3 e5 tiong-kan tek-khak tioh8 po2-siok sui-lang5 e5 jin5-keh.  Koh tioh8 po2-siu2 ka-teng5 hu-hu7 e5 seng3-kiat.  M7-thang phau7 sim2-mih8 “Loan5-ai3 chu7-iu5,” “Chu7-iu5 loan5-ai3” e5 khau2-ho7, bo5 chun-tiong7 hu-hu7 e5 to7-li2, an2-ni lai5 ka-teng5 chin oh ho5.  Sou2-i2 na7 ai3 hu-hu7 ai3-cheng5 eng2-kou3, te7-it tioh8 teng3-cheng3 chit e5 su-siuN2.
2.  Tioh8 teng3-cheng3 “Kiat-hun si7 loan5-ai3 e5 bong7.”  Chit8 ku3 oe7 ia7-si7 m7-tioh8.  Goa2 i2-keng kong2 liau2 lah, na7 m7-si7 ang-bou2 ki5-sit8 si7 bo5 “loan5-ai3” thang kong2.  Ang-bou2 iN7-seng3 e5 tiong-kan, chiah u7 li2 loan5, goa2 ai3 e5 thiaN3-cheng5 thang kong2.  Na7 m7-si7 ang-bou2, bo5-lun7 kau-poe5 goa7 chhim to-si7 iu2-gi5.  Na7 boe7 choe3 ang-bou2 chiu7 seng seN-khi2 loan5-ai3, an2-ni si7 sia5-loan5.  Na7 i2-keng hu2-hun(許婚) e5 lam5-lu2, teng7-hun liau2 lah, sou2-i2 e7-tit cheng-sin5-tek e5 saN loan5-bou7, saN i3-ai3, an2-ni iu2-ki chek-kho2.  Chin e5 loan5-ai3 si7 tui3 kiat-hun hit-jit8 khi2, cheng-sin5, jiok8-the2 oan5-choan5 it-ti3, sou2 ui7-chi nng7-e5 chiaN5-choe3 chit8-the2.  Hit-si5 sou2 hoat-chhut siang-hong tiN-bit8 e5 kam2-cheng5 chiah thang kong2 si7 chin e5 loan5-ai3.  An2-ni “Kiat-hun m7-si7 loan5-ai3 e5 bong7, tian-tou3 ai3 kong2 kiat-hun si7 loan5-ai3 e5 sit8-hian7,” a7-si7 “tan3-seng” chiah tioh8.  In-ui7 “Loan5-ai3” na7 bo5 “kiat-hun” chiu7 loan5-ai3 bo5 thang sit8-hian7.  Si7 choa2-bin7, toh-teng2 e5 khang-tam5 na7-tiaN7.  Bo5 kiat-hun lai5 sit8-hian7 e5 loan5-ai3, kio3 choe3 khang-loan5, a2-si7 sit-loan5 chiu7-si7 an2-ni.  Chong2-si7 che7-che7 lang5 tian-to3 kong2 si7 loan5-ai3 e5 si5 khah tiN-bit8, cheng3-keng kiat-hun e5 si5 si7 hoat-kian3 tioh8 che7-che7 mau5-tun2, khi-phian3, kna-khou2.  Tng loan5-ai3 e5 si5 chin siang-ho2, li2-siong2 chin koan5, san-beng5 hai2-se7[se3], lim5-thng tah8-hoe2 to goan7 pek8-siu2 kai-lo2.  Cheng3-keng kiat-hun liau2 hiah e5 li2-siong2, hiah e5 kau-poe5 kho2-kian3 si7 bong5-bok8, bo5 li2-seng3.  Kou3 khoaN3 bin7 siu2, kou3 khoaN3 kim-chiN5.  Bo5 teh siuN7 jin5-keh, bo5 the siuN7 sin3-giong2.  Kau3-si5 chham2 lah, kiat-hun liau2 li2 bat goa2, goa2 bat li2 lah.  Ku-cha so5-so5 chhut-lai5 lah.  Ka2-bian7-ku7  hian khi2-lai5 lah.  Sou2-i2 loan5-ai3 tong-si5 e5 tiN-bit8 long2 bo5 khi3 lah.  Sou2 lau5-teh e5 chiu7-si7 seng-oah8-khou2, cheng-sin5-khou2, khou2-khou2-khou2.  Sou2-i2 kong2 loan5-ai3 si7 tiN-bit8 e5 lok8-hng5, in-ui7 hit-si5 long2 si7 ti3 ka2-bian7-ku7 tai7-ke chiong ho2 theh8 lai5 kong2, theh8 lai5 khoaN3.  Goa2 phian3 li2, li2 phian3 goa2, choe3 chheN-me5 hi3, ka2-chong hi3.  Kau3 kiat-hun liau2 si2 lah, tai7-ke chiah lo7-lo7, ku-koa3 hian-khui, ku-kha so5 chhut-lai5, ang3-te2 e5 tau7-chhai3, kha-te2 u7 hoat-mng5 a2-bo5 long2 chai lah.  Siang-hong toa7 oan3-hin7, toa7 loe2-chi3, chiu3-chham3 kiat-hun.  Sou2-i2 kong2 “Loan5-ai3 si7 tiN-bit8 e5 lok8-hng5, ia7 kiat-hun si7 loan5-ai3 e5 bong7” chiu7-si7 an2-ni.  Chit e5 su-siuN2 tioh8 teng3-cheng3, na7 bo5 hu-hu7 e5 ai3-cheng5 be7 eng2-kou3.
3.  Tioh8 hou7-siong7 chu3-i3 seng-oah8 e5 sio2-su7
(1) Sio li2-kai2, saN tong5-cheng5, saN the2-thiap, saN le2-jiong7.  Chhin-chhiuN7 chhut-jip8 e5 si5 sio chioh mng7.  Tiong7-hu ka7 hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2 “Goa2 beh lai5 khi3 lah.”  Hu7-jin5-lang5 tui3 tiong7-hu kong2 “Li2 to3--lai5 lah.” Tai7-ke eng7 chhio3-chhio3 lai5 saN-mng7 chin ho2.
(2) Sio-sang3 chit8 tiam2-a2 tau2-lou7.  Tiong7-hu chhut-goa7 to3-lai5, be2 hu7-jin5-lang5 sou2 ai3 e5 hoe, hun2 sio2-khoa2-mih8.  Hu7-jin5-lang5 chhut-goa7 to3--lai5 be2 chit8-tiam2-a2 koe2-chi2.
(3) Chu3-i3 tiong7-hu sim-piN e5 seng-oah8.  U7 toa3 chhiu2-kin a2-bo5?  Lai7-saN lau5-koaN7 kin2 oaN7, u7 toa3 jin5-tan a2-bo5?  Ke chheng7 chit8 nia2 saN, koaN5-koaN5.
(4) U7-si5-a2 chu2 tam7-poh8 tiong7-hu khah hah8-chhui3 e5 chhai3.  Lan2 sui-bong2 si7 san3-san3 ah.  U7 ki-hoe7 chit8 poaN3 pai2-a2 khek-liam2, chiu7 chu2 chit8 oaN2 hou7 tiong7-hu hoaN-hi2.
(5) Gau5 an-ui3, gau5 pang-chan7.  Sio2-khoa2 su7 to ho2.  Tiong7-hu beh kia3 che7-che7 phoe, lai5 tau3 kou5 iu5-phio3, a2-si7 giah8 ka-to lai5 tau3 ka phoe-long5 e5 kak.  Sui-si7 sio2-khoa2, kha-lai5 chhiu2-lai5 hou7 tiong7-hu u7 phoaN7.  Choe3 li2 khi3 khun3, pang3 chit8 e5 bong kau3 sian7 m7-ho2.  Li2 na7 e7 tit, u7 si5 pang-chan7 hu7-jin5-lang5 chhiuN7-chui2, sau3 thou5-kha, chih phoe7 chin ho2.
(6) Sio ki3-liam7 seN-jit8, ki3-liam7 kiat-hun-jit8.  Tai7-ke siau3-liam7 chhoa7 liau2 chin tioh8, ke3 liau2 chin ho2.  An2-ni chiah e7 na2 ho2.
(7) U7 ki-hoe7 ham5-ha5 tioh8 choe3-hoe2 san3-pou7 choe3-hoe2 kiaN5-kiaN5, choe3-hoe2 tam7-lun7 cha2 siau3-lian5 saN-thiaN3 e5 kou3-su7.  ThiaN3 e5 kou3-su7, si7 ku7 iau2-ku2 eng2-sin.  Kiat-hun siong7 khoaN3-khoaN3 leh tong-si5 e5 phoe thak8-thak8 chhio3-chhio3 leh chin ho2.
4.  Chit kui2-tiam2 mai3 hoan7 tioh8 khah ho2.
(1) M7-thang eng7 tong5-cheng5-sim khi3 chhoa7 sin-the2 bo5 tau3-tah, ti3-lek8 kam2-cheng5 u7 koh-iuN7 e5 lang5, kau3-boe2 tong5-cheng5-sim na7 tng7-cham7 hou7-hoe2 chiu7 hai7.
(2) Keng-che3, te7-ui7 li7 siuN hng7 e5 lang5 chin-sou2-e7 tioh8 se3-ji7.  In-ui7 kiaN liau2 poe5-toe3 be7 kau3 e7 seN bun7-te5.

(3) I3-chi3, chhu3-bi7, seng-oah8 khoan5-keng2 put-ho5 e5 lang5 khah oh tit tiau-ho5.
(4) Sin3-giong2 put-tong5 e5 lang5 siang7 gui5-hiam2.  E7 seN chhut tong5-chhong5 iN7-bong7.  Chit8 e5 kau3 boe2 ng3-bang7 beh khi3 Thian-tong5, chit8 e5 siuN7 beh khi3 se-thian.  Na2 lau7 na2 kiaN5 e7 na2 li7-khui, pou7-tiau e7 na2-be7 ho5.
(5) Jin5-cheng2, kok-chek8 bo5 tang5 ia7 u7 khun3-lan5.  Chong2-si7 ti7 sin3-giong2 kap thiaN3-cheng5 na7 it-ti3 u7-si5 kho2-leng5 choe3 bi2-moa2 e5 ka-teng5.
I2-siong7 e5 su7 si7 khah ho2 tioh8 chu3-i3.  M7-si7 kong2 choat8-tui3 m7-thang ke3-chhoa7.  Na7 e7 bian2-tit si7 khah tho3-tong3 ia7 bo5 tek-khak.
5.  Chit kui2-tiam2 tioh8 tek8-piat8 chu3-i3.
(1) M7-thang sio-me7.  Sio-phah koh khah m7-thang.  Liu5-seng-ki e5 khek-phoaN5 bo5 lun7 goa7 ho2 thiaN, na7 u7 khi5, chhiuN3 lai5 kau3 hia e7 chhiat8-chhiat8-hau2 ia7 si7 phaiN2 thiaN.
Phah-sng3 ki5-u5 e5 ho2 thiaN.  Hu-hu7 e5 kam2-cheng5-siong7, sim-pang5 tiong tek-khak m7-thang hou7 i u7 khi5, m7-thang hou7 i u7 lih8-hun5 chiah ho2.  I3-kian3 na7 be7 ho5, tioh8 sio-niu7, m7-thang chit8 e5 chiam3 teh kong2, m7-thang toa7-siaN jiang2, un-un-a2 kong2.  Siang7-ho2 long2 mai3 kong2 hou7 ang phiN kau3 to2-ui7?  Hou7 bou2 phiN kau3 to2-ui7?  Nng7 e5 chhek8-kau3-tit8 u7 saN2-mih8 ho2.  IaN5 e7 khah toa7-han3, su e7 khah se3-han3 a2 m7-si7?  Kin-tu2 m7-si7 siang7 chit8-the2.  M7-bian2 cheN3, lun2-khi3 hit e5 siang7-gau5.  Chio choe3-hoe2 kui7-loh8 ki5-to2 hit e5 koh khah gau5.  ChiN5 bo5 nng7 e5 poah8-be7-tan5.  Nng7 e5 peN5-peN5 put-seng7-soan3 chiah e7 oan-ke.  Jit8-pun2 siok8-gu2 kong2 ang-bou2 oan-ke kau2 to bo5 ai3 phiN7.
(2) M7-bian2 kiong5-kiong5 kio3 li2 e5 tang5-phoaN7, tioh8 khut-hok8 kap li2 siang7-khoan2 chhu3-bi7, siang7-khoan2 sim-seng3.  Si7 eng7 thiaN3 e5 kam2-hoa3, tong5-hoa3.  Ti seng3 chiu7 kho2-i2 tong5-ki.  Kiong5-kiong5 beh kiau-cheng3 gu5-kak e7 hai7-si2 gu5.  Chhou, peN5, tit8-a2 chiu7 ho2.  Khiau-khiau-a2 tit8, tit8-tit8-a2 khiau.  M7-thang su7-su7 tioh8 giah8 chhioh lai5 pi2.  Bo5 kau3 chhun3-chhioh chiu7 be7 ent7-tit.  An2-ni e7 put-si5 thui5 kong3 phah.
(3) M7-thang loan7-loan7 hiam5.  O-lo2 khah ho2, saN chun-keng3, saN o-lo2, saN seh-sia7.  Jit8-pun2-oe7 kong2 “???????. ????” e5 oe7 khah che7 e5 ka-teng5 si7 te7-gek8.  “??????. ?????” e5 siaN khah che7 e5 ka-teng5 si7 lok8-hng5.  Lan2 na7 ai3 ka-teng5 bo5 tioh8 siong5-siong5 saN chun-chhun5, saN seh-sia7.
(4) Put-lun7 ti7 to2-ui7 tioh8 ko-ki2 lan2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, tioh8 chun-keng3 lan2 e5 tiong7-hu.  Choat8-tui3 m7-thang tui3 pat8-lang5 phoe-pheng5 ka-ti7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 loat-tiam2.  M7-thang ti7 pat8-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 khoaN3-khin ka-ti7 e5 tiong7-hu.  Ia7 ti7 ka-ti7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 lai5 o-lo2 pat8-lang5 e5 bou2 sui2, gau5 ia7-si7 gong7-su7.  Na7 e7 li2-kai2 khiok bo5 iau3-kin2.  Hu7-jin5-lang5 che7-che7 chin gau5 chiah8-chhou3, chit-tou3 sim chin chhim, sou2-i2 siam2-pi7 chit khoan2 gong7-su7 khah ho2.
(5) Tioh8 choat8-tui3 sio sin3-iong7.  M7-thang gi5 sim tang7, nng7-lang5 tiaN7 sio tng, sio chhoe7 phang7.  Chin kai-si2, long7-ke2 seng5 chin chiu7 chham2.
(6) Li2 ai3 li2 e5 tiong7-hu thiaN3 li2, hit e5 hong-hoat chiu7-si7 li2 seng thiaN3 i.  Li2 ai3 li2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 thiaN3 li2, hit e5 hong-hoat chiu7-si7 li2 seng thiaN3 i.  Tu5 chit e5 hong-hoat i2-goa7 bo5 pan7-hoat.  Li2 e5 tiong7-hu u7 sim2-mih8 phaiN2 sip8-koan3 oh ke2.  M7-si7 eng7 oan-ke, a2-si7 khi3 ka7 i thau tng, eng7 li2 chhut-tui3 sim-te2 seng5-i3 thiaN3-thang3 e5 bak8-sai2 ui7-tioh8 i ki5-to2 siang7-ho2.  Goa7 ok, goa7 nge7-sim, ai3 phah lang5 e5 cha-pou-lang5, thiau3 be7 chhut hu7-jin5-lang5 thiaN3-sim e5 bak8-sai2, kap tui3 sim-te2 chhut thiaN3-thang3 e5 ba5-bun2-chhio3.  Chhio3, khau3 si7 lu2-seng3 choe3 kiong5 e5 bu2-khi3.

I2-siong7 e5 hong-hoat khi3 kiaN5 khoaN3-mai7.  Che7-chio2 un2-tang3 e7 chin3-pou7 hu-hu7 e5 thiaN3-cheng5.
Kiat-boe2 lai5 kong2 “tiN-bit8 e5 ka-teng5” choe3-au7 e5 pi3-koat si7 ti7 to2-ui7?
ChhiaN2 tai7-ke thak8 
I Lim5 13 chiuN, I2-hut-sou2 5:22-33.  I Pi2-tek 3: 1-9.  The5-to 2:4-6.  Ko-lo5-se 3:18-19.
Bo5 chit8 lang5 sou2 kong2 e7 pi2 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7 khah ho2.
1.  Eng7 sin3-giong2 choe3 te7-ki.  Eng7 ng3-bang7 choe3 thang, mng5.  Eng7 thiaN3 choe3 chhu3-teng2 lai5 kham3.  An2-ni e5 ka-teng5 choe3 an-choan5.
2.  Tai7-ke sio chun-keng3 ti7 ThiN-pe7 saN kap choe3 I e5 kiaN2, cha-bou2-kiaN2 peng5-teng2.  Ti7 Chu2 Ia5-sou e5 thiaN3 sim-lai7 saN-lian5, na2 chhia-lian2 saN kap koan3-chhoan3 ti7 1 ki chhia-sim.  Ti7 Seng3 Sin5 e5 leng2-to7 tang5 pou7-tiau ng3 kng-beng5, eng2 oah8 e5 thian-hiong lai5 chian5-chin3, choe3 kng-beng5.
3.  Eng7 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7 chhut-hoat.  Eng7 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7 lai5 kiaN5, lai5 seng5-tiong2.  Eng7 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7 lai5 choe3 kiat-kiok8.  Si5-si5 ki5-to2 siong5-chou7 hit e5 ka-teng5 siang7 kian-kou3.
Choe3-au7 chhiaN2 thak8 chit8-chat seng3-keng.
Ia5-li7-bi2 2:2.  “Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 li2 siau3-lian5 e5 un-ai3, hun-in e5 ai3-cheng5, li2 chaiN2-iuN7-a2 ti7 khong3-ia2, ti7 boe7-bat cheng3-choh e5 te7, kun-te3 Goa2; Goa2 long2 ka7 li2 ki3-tit” chit e5 i3-su3 si7 
1.  Lang5 choe3 se3-kiaN2 ti7 lau7-bu2 e5 hoai5-phau7, teh chiah8 lau7-bu2 e5 leng, si7 ho5-teng2 e5 su-bou7 lau7-bu2.

2.  Lang5 tu2-a2 kiat-hun e5 bit8-goeh8, ang-chhin bou2-chhin e5 hoaN-hi2, hit e5 saN-thiaN3 chhin-chhiuN7 hi5 tit-tioh8 chui2.
3.  I2-sek-liat8 peh-si3 chhut Ai-kip8 ti7 khong3-ia2, boe7 cheng3-choh e5 te7, tan2 Siong7-te3 loh8 Ma2-na2, bang7 Siong7-te3 iuN2-chhi7.  Hit-si5 e5 kho3 Siong7-te3, him-bou7 Siong7-te3, kam2-sia7 Siong7-te3 e5 sim, hit e5 chi3-seng5 jiat8-chhiat.
I2-siong7 saN khoan2 e5 sim-cheng5 long2 si7 chin chi3-seng5, chin sui2.  Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 “Goa2 long2 ka7 li2 ki3-tit.”  Chong2-si7 lang5 chin kian3-siau3.
1.  Toa7-han3 tiong2-seng5 lah.  Siok8-gu2 kong2 sit8-kou2-boe2-a2 ta lah.  M7-bat pe7-bo2 lah, bong5-un poe7-gi7 lah.
2.  Bou2 chhoa7 liau2 ku2 chhau3-phu2 lah.  SeN kiaN2, phoa3-piN7 bai2 lah.  San3-hiong lah.  Ai3-cheng5 chiam7-se.
3.  Ho2-giah8 than3 u7 chiah8, ngou2-kok hong-siu, chhek toa7-pun7, chiu2 toa7 ang3, gu5, lu5 cheng-siN toa7 kun5 lah.  Siong7-te3 na2 Siong7-te3.  Bo5 kam2-sia7 lah, m7-bian2 Siong7-te3 lah.
Chin kian3-siau3.  HiaN-che2 hian7-si5 lan2 kok-lang5 e5 hu-hu7 seng-oah8 iau2 u7 chhin-chhiuN7 kiat-hun tong-si5, bit8-goeh8 hit chun7 hiah siong-ho2 a2-bo5?  Na7 bo5 tioh8 oat8 to3-tng2 lai5 teng5 un-sip8 chiah ho2.  Li2 poh-kaN2 be7 ki3-tit tong-si5 e5 ai3-cheng5 lah ia7 bo5 tek-khak.  Lan2 e5 ThiN-pe7 “long2 ka7 li2 ki3-tit.”
ChhiaN2 lan2 sui5-lang5 oat-to3-tng2 lai5 hoe5-kou3 tong-si5 e5 ai3-cheng5.  Ai3-cheng5 si7 ku7 iau2-ku2 eng2-sin.  Koh chit8 pai2 khoaN3 lan2 kap sui2-sui2 e5 ai3-kheng.  Chheng-chong3 e5 hu-kun tong-si5 kiat-hun e5 siong7.  Siau3-liam7 tong-si5 e5 un-ai3(溫愛).  Phah-sng2 kaN2 m7-thang oan-ke, m7-thang siuN7 beh pun-khui.  Na7 an2-ni siuN7 si7 chin kian3-siau3.  Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 tek-khak tang7-tang7 khian3-chek.  Goan7 Chu2 chiok-hok liat8-ui7 hiaN-che2 e7-tit kian3-siat tiN-bit8 e5 ka-teng5.  Hu-hu7 e5 ai3-cheng5 e7 eng2-kou3 lai5 eng5-kng Siong7-te3 e5 seng3-mia5.  Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chiok-hok.
“Chiong-lai5 Nga2-kok beh teng3 i e5 kun, I2-sek-liat8 beh hoat-ge5 khui-hoe; in e5 koe2-chi2 beh chhiong-moa2 se3-kai3”(Sai3 27:6).  A3-beng7.
An2-ni J. S. bok8-su e5 kang2-ian2; “TiN-bit8 e5 ka-teng5” oan5-pit.  Choe3-au7 toa7-toa7 kiong5-tiau sin3-tou5 m7-thang chhoa7 hoe7-goa7 e5 bi7-sin3-chia2.  Ia7 m7-thang ke3 hoe7-goa7 e5 bi7-sin3-chia2.  Toa7 hi-bong7 sin3-tou5 tioh8 chhoa7 tong5-sin3, ke3 tong5-sin3 e5 lang5.  Sin3, che chiah si7 hap8 ThiN-pe7 e5 seng3 chi2-i3.  Tui3 an2-ni chiah e7 siu7 chiok-hok, chiah e7 po2-siu2 kap cheng-chin3 sin3-tek.  Tai7-ke thiaN liau2 toa7 kam2-kek.  Che7-che7 chheng-lian5 tui3 an2-ni lip8-chi3 piau2-si7 chit e5 koat-sim.  Soa3 ui7-tioh8 koe3-khi3 chong-kau3-siong7 chap8-hun(雜婚) e5 hiaN-che2 e5 put-heng7 e5 su7-sit8 lai5 m7-kam.
Hui7-bi2 tui3 thiaN chiah e5, koh hoe5-ek chiah e5, koh siuN7 tioh8 i ka-ti7 kap Khun-hong e5 su7 chiu7 it-hoat kiaN-sim.  Chiu7 koh khah koat-sim m7 ai3 ke3 hoe7-goa7 e5 lang5.  
13
Kong2 u7 chit8 jit8 Khun-hong in bo2-ku7 TiuN chiong-kun hut-jian5 lai5 chhoe7 Khun-hong, ka7 i kong2 tui3 hit-chan5 chhin-su7 taN ju5-chhu2 ju5-chhu2 ho2 lai5 chin3-heng5 lah.  Bo2-ku7 kio3 Khun-hong khi3 pin5-au7 chhui3 aN3 i e5 hiN7-a2 piN chhi-bu2 chhi7-chhu7 m7-chai ka7 i kong2 sim2-mih8.  Khun-hong chhut-lai5 moa2-bin7 chhun-hong chhio3 gi7-gi7, thau5-khak khok8-khok8 tim3 lian5 siaN hoah “Hau5-hau5”(ho2-ho2).  PiN-a2 e5 lang5 kong2 bok8-beng5 ki5-biau7.  Keh-jit8 tu2-si7 long5-lek8 e5 5 goeh8 13.  SiaN5-lai7 teh ngia5 Seng5-hong5-ia5, ke-ke hou7-hou7 chin nau7-jiat8.  ThiN-kng-cha2 Khun-hong chiu7 beng7-leng7 ka-teng thai5-ti to2-iuN5, chioh-toh pan7 chhiN-chhau, pang3-thiap.  Lai7-bin7 tiam2-teng kat-chhai2, lian5 in lau7-bu2 kap Siu3-chhun to m7-chai i3-su3.  Long2 si7 liah8 choe3 5 goeh8 13 ngia5 Seng5-hong5, ia7 Khun-hong beh tek8-piat8 chhiaN2 lang5-kheh kap lang5 eng3-siu5, iu7 m7-koh ho5-pit8 tioh8 thai5-ti to2-iuN5 leh?  Chin ki5-koai3, tang-si5-a2 12 am3 in bo2-ku7 chiu7 tui3 Khun-hong chioh ka-teng chiaN5-chap8 e5 kap kio3 i e5 sim-pak e5 su7-koaN toa3 it-ji7-chap8 e5 peng-a2 tau3 choe3-hoe2 beh oa2 2, 30 e5, thau3-mi5 seng7 goeh8-iaN2 ha5-hun5 e5 si5 pang3-kio7 lai5 Su-liong5.
Kau3-ui7 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2-niu5 kap Hui7-bi2, sim-pu7 Soat-mui5 saN e5 long2 tu2 teh choe3 am3-si5 e5 ka-teng5 le2-pai3, 112  nng7 e5 sun-a2 long2 teh khun3 lah.  Na7-si7 in lai7-bin7 u7 chit8 e5 tng5-kang thau5 kio3 choe3 Siu2-jin5 tu2 chhut-khi3 bo5 ti7-teh.  Hut-jian5 hit ji7-saN-chap8 lang5 tui3 toa7-mng5 jip8--lai5.  Bo5-hun bo5-hoe7 tit8-tit8 long3 kau3 toa7-thiaN, toa7-siaN chiu7 jiang2 kong2 u7 lang5 ti7-teh a2-bo5?  Hui7-bi2 chhut-lai5 khoaN3, chai si7 chit8 e5 kun-jin5 su7-koaN, au7-bin7 khoaN3 chit8-tui lang5.  Mng7 kong2 chiah am3 si7 beh chhong3 sim2-mih8?  Hit e5 lang5 in3 kong2 “Thoan5-tiuN2 TiuN chiong-kun u7 su7 ai3 chhiaN2 Hui7-bi2 sio2-chia2 khi3 hoe7-bian7.” TiuN2-lo2-niu5 kap Soat-mui5 ti7 pin5-au7 thiaN chit8-e7 toa7 kiaN chhut-lai5 khoaN3.  KhoaN3 tioh8 hiah che7 lang5, koh si7 am3-si5 Siu2-jin5 ia7 bo5 ti7-teh.  Na7-si7 Hui7-bi2 chin ho2-taN2 toa7-siaN kap i kong2.  “Goa2 si7 chit8 e5 lu2-chu2 na2-li2 kap Thoan5-tiuN2 chiong-kun u7 koan-he7?  I ho5-pit8 tioh8 kap goa2 hoe7-bian7.  Goa2 ia7 bo5 pit-iau3 kap i hoe7-bian7.  Goa2 peng7-bo5 sim2-mih8 tai7-chi3.” Lau7-bu2 tiuN2-lo2-niu5 kiaN kau3 khu7-khu7 chun3, chhui3-e7-tau2 khok8-khok8 hou3, chin kho2-lin5 kui7 loh8 kiu5 Siong7-te3 po2-hou7.  Chit8-bin7 kiu5 hit e5 su7-koaN chhiu2 giah8-koan5, tauh-ti2 si7 sim2-mih8 su7?  Hit e5 su7-koaN chin siu7-khi3 toa7 siaN hoah kong2, “Kio3 li2 lai5 khi3 chiu7 lai5 khi3,” hoah lang5 chhah chiuN7 kio7.  Lang5 chiu7 tui3 Hui7-bi2 tit8-tit8 chhah chhut-khi3.  Su7-koaN tui3 io-nih8 thiu-chhut te2-chheng3 hoah kong2 “Tiam7-tiam7 m7-chun2 khui-siaN soan-jiang2 hoah-kiu3.  Na7 khui-siaN jiang2 chiu7 beh khui-chheng3 phah-si2.” Lim5 tiuN2-lo2-niu5 khui-siaN khau3, “KiaN2 ah!  Kiu5 Siong7-te3 po2-hou7 kap li2 khi3.” Hui7-bi2 thiaN lau7-bu2 ai-kio3 thi5-khau3 e5 siaN, oat8-thau5 kong2, “A-bu2 m7-bian2 hona5-lo2 choe3 li2 pang3-sim, goa2 tek-khak kau3-si2 siu2 Chu2 e5 to7-li2.” Hui7-bi2 hou7 lang5 chhah jip8 kio7, kio7-mng5 kio7-thang long2 koaiN-khi3 ka-teng kng teh long7.  Lau7-bu2 chu7 an2-ni be7 kou3-tit to2-to2 loh8 khi3.  Ah!  Chham2-ah!  Tiong7-hu si2, kiaN2 si2, cha-bou2-kiaN2 hou7 lang5 liah8 khi3.  Soat-mui5 khoaN3 ta-ke to2-to2 loh8 khi3, pang5-nih8 nng7 e5 gin2-na2 thiaN-kiN3 hiah che7 lang5 ti7 lai7-bin7 kiuh-kiuh jiang2, kiaN cheng-sin5 ia7 khau3 be-be.  Sio2-kou iu7 hou7 lang5 nge7 kng-khi3, sim loan7 chhau-chhau, iu7 m7-kaN2 jiang2.  Kau3 lang5 long2 chhut-khi3 liau2 chiah hoah kiu3 lang5.  Chhu3-piN tai7-ke ia7 chin kiaN, sui5-lang5 kou3 ka-ti7, bo5 su7 te7-it ho2.  Si5-kan ia7 oa2 chiaN5 poaN3 mi5 lah, kai-chai3 chhu3-au7 u7 chit8 hou7 hoe7-iu2 tai7-ke khah tang5-sim, kin2 chau2 lai5 khoaN3, khoaN3 tioh8 an2-ni chit8-bin7 tau3-kiu3 tiuN2-lo2-niu5.  Chit8-bin7 kin2 kio3 lang5 khi3 po3 Bok8-su chai.  Bok8-su ti7 bin5-chhng5 chhia khi2--lai5 kin2 thong-ti si3-ui5 e5 hoe7-iu2 long2 giah8 thui5-a2 jiok chhut-khi3.
Tu2-gu7 Siu2-jin5 chhut-khi3, au7-lai5 chiah chai si7 khi3 sun5 chhan5-chui2, giah8 chit8 ki ti-thau5 tui3 hng7-hng7 teh lai5, tai7-khai3 si7 siuN7 kong2 chhan5-chui2 long2 sun5-liau2 beh koah tiu7-a2 e5 si5 chit8 e5 lang5 choe3 chit8 pian3 eng7 chhiam-taN taN tit 4 taN3 chhek.  Si3-pah goa7 kin, oa2 500 kin lat8.  Kui2 e5 lang5-a2 oa2 lai5 i bo5 lun2--tioh8, koh u7 oh8 kun-thau5, kha-chhiu chin ho2.  Goeh8 hou7 hun5 kham3-leh, goeh8-kng hoaN2-ou hoaN2-ou.  KhoaN3 thau5-cheng5 chit8-tin7 lang5 kng chit8-teng2 kio7, kng-teh-chhek8, poaN3-kau2-chau2.  In m7-kaN2 kng tui3 toa7-be2-lou7, si7 chau2 tui3 sio2-lou7-a2, chiah e7 hiah tu2-ho2 kap Siu2-jin5 sio cheng-thau5.  Siu2-jin5 ia7 put-kai2 ki5-i3 ian5-lou7 gim5-si choe3 phoaN7 bo5-lam7 bo5-lam7 kin2 gim5 kin2-kiaN5.  Kio7-lai7 Hui7-bi2 jin7-tit si7 Siu2-jin5 e5 siaN am3-am3 hoaN-hi2, ki5-to2 Chu2 pang-chan7, ng3-bang7 u7 kiu3.  Tiam7-tiam7 m7-kaN2 chhut-siaN.  ThiaN gim5-si e5 siaN na2-kin7, chiu7 chai Siu2-jin5 i2-keng oa2 lai5 kau3 sin-piN, hut-jian5 tui3 kio7-lai7 toa7-siaN kio3.  “Siu2-jin5 kin2 lai5 kiu3 goa2.”  Siu2-jin5 jin7-tit si7 Hui7-bi2 e5 siaN koh khoaN3 su7-koaN choe3 cheng5 kiaN5, chit8 pou7 hun7 e5 lang5 i2-keng chau2 chin3-cheng5.  In-ui7 Hui7-bi2 chin gau5, Siong7-te3 hou7 i u7 ti3-sek, tui3 thiaN Siu2-jin5 gim5-si e5 siaN hit-si5, i ti7 kio7-lai7 thiau-ti5 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-tang7, kio7 io5-lai5, io5-khi3, u7 si5 giong7-giong7 beh peng2-kio7, kng kio7 e5 si7 ka-teng koh m7-si7 kio7-hu, bo5 koan3-si3, kio3-khou2 lian5-thian.  Sou2-i2 su7-koaN kap chit8 pou7-hun7 e5 peng long2 chau2 chin3-cheng5 khi3.  Chhun chit8 pou7-hun7 ka-teng kou3 kio7 chau2 ban7 sui5 ti7 kio7-au7.  Siu2-jin5 thiaN Hui7-bi2 sio2-chia2 teh kio3 i, chek-si5 kam2-kak si7 pang2-hui2 liah8 lang5, i si7 m7-chai Khun-hong kap in bo2-ku7 teh piN3-kui2.  Siu2-jin5 e5 tit8-kam2 si7 pang2-hui2 liah8 lang5 beh kong3 hoan-thau5.  Che ia7-si7 TiuN chiong-kun cha2 choe3 lek8-lim5 pang2-siu2 (綠林綁首) e5 ku7-thng-thau5.  Siu2-jin5 chek-si5 chau2-oa2 siong3 cheng-cheng tui3 thau5 cheng5 hit-e5 kng-kio7--e5 e5 kha-kut, eng7 ti-thau5-kheng hou3 chit8-e7 kha tng7 li7-li7, kui sian lang5 chu7 an2-ni un loh8 khi3.  Kui teng2 kio7 chhuh tui3 thau5-cheng5 loh8 khi3.  In-ui7 si7 bo5 tiuN-ti5 au7-bin7 hit e5 kng-kio7 e5 chu7 an2-ni hou7 kio7 thoa phak loh8-khi3.  Thau5-khak hou7 chioh8-thau5 kong3 chit8 khang.  Tit8-tit8 hoah kiu3 lang5.  Hui7-bi2 seng7 hit e5 se3 cham3-khui kio7-mng5 tui3 chit8 tiau5 phian-lou7 tit8-tit8 chau2.  Au7-bin7 e5 ka-teng khang-chhiu2 bo5 ke-si, Siu2-jin5 u7 ti-thau5 sui e5 oa2--lai5 but8 kau3 tang-to2 sai-oai, khau3-pe7 kiam khau3-bo2.  Thau5-cheng5 e5 peng-a2 jih8 to3-tng2 lai5, tu5 su7-koaN u7 te2-chheng3 i2-goa7 bo5 chheng3, peng-a2 u7 to.  Su7-koaN chek-si5 khui chheng3 thau5-mng5 phah bo5 tioh8, in-ui7 goeh8 bo5 siaN2 kng.  Te7 ji7 mng5 koh phah--lai5, Siu2-jin5 siam2-koe3 phah tioh8 chhiu2-kou2-thau5, sio2-khoa2 siong.  Siu2-jin5 chin beng2-iong2 chhin-chhiuN7 ia2-gu5, chhin-chhiuN7 hiong5-sai khoaN3 tioh8 chiah8-mih8.  Hoah-siaN ta3-oa2-khi3 eng7 ti-thau5 khan-thian-bun5 tui3 thau5-khak ka7 i bo7 loh8-khi3.  Aih8 chit8 e5 in3-siaN chu7 an2-ni to2 loh8-khi3.  Su7-koaN e5 thau5-khak chhui3-chhui3, jih8 oa2-khi3 tui3 te2-chheng3 chhiuN2 khi2-lai5.  Peng-a2 long2 poeh8 to beh oa2--lai5, Siu2-jin5 chiong te2-chheng3 giah8 ti7 chhiu2-nih ka7 in kong2 mai3 lai5 khah ho2.  Tai7-ke khoaN3 m7-si7 Siu2-jin5 e5 tui3-chhiu2 chiu7 the3-chui2 lau3-chau2.  Tu2 hit si5 Bok8-su kap chit8 kun5 chheng-lian5 ia7 jiok kau3, khoaN3 Hui7-bi2 teh chau2.  Ia7 thiaN cheng5-bin7 u7 chheng3-siaN kap hiam3 sat e5 siaN.  ThiaN Hui7-bi2 kong2, chiah chai Siu2-jin5 lai5 kiu3.  Bok8-su kin2 chhoa7 Hui7-bi2 bih ti7 chit8 e5 tu2-ho2 e5 sou2-chai7.  Ki5-u5 e5 chheng-lian5 jiok kau3, khoaN3 lang5 to long2 the3 khi3 lah sou2-i2 bo5 koh jiok.  Tai7-ke chiu7 long2 to3-lai5 Hui7-bi2 kap Bok8-su bih e5 ui7.  Tai7-ke siuN7 chit chan5 su7 m7-si7 sio2-khoa2.  Kong2 si7 TiuN chiong-kun lai5 liah8, chiah siuN7 kiN3 cheng5-jit8 Khun-hong kap in bo2-ku7 lai5, kai3-siau7 kong2 si7 bou2 Peng-thoan5-tiuN2 TiuN chiong-kun, an2-ni si7 beh lai5 eng7 kiong5-toat8 e5 seng5-hun.
