TaN ki3-jian5 jia2-chhut jin5-beng7, tek-khak m7-si7 sio2-khoa2.  Sou2-i2 tai7-ke siong-liong5 koat-teng7, chiong Su7-liong5 e5 chhu3 so2 khi2--lai5, chiong lau7-bu2 kap hiaN-so2 sun-a2 long2 poaN khi3 pai3-tng5.  Ti7 hia ng3-bang7 tit-tioh8 po2-hou7.  Soat-mui5 to3-khi3 ia7 khi3 choe3 kau3-hoe7 hu3-siat i-koan2 e5 hou7-su7.
Chiah kong2 Siu2-jin5 chhoa7 Hui7-bi2 chu7 an2-ni thau3-mi5 chau2.  Jit8--si5 bih, am3-si5 chau2, tit8-tit8 chau2-kau3 Hun5-lam5 seng2-siaN5.  Khi3 bih ti7 Siu2-jin5 chhin-chhek e5 tau.  In si7 choe3-sit lang5, si7 jiat8-sim e5 Ki-tok-tou5.  Toa3 ti7 li7 siaN5 chiaN5 phou3-lou7 chit8 e5 phian-phiah e5 hiuN-chng e5 sio2 tek-ui5-a2 lai7.  Sou2-i2 bo5 hiah khoai3 hoat-kian3 tioh8.
TaN hiah e5 peng-a2 chu7 an2-ni thoa sin-si, kap kng tng7-kha, tng7-chhiu2 tioh8-siong--e5 to3-khi3.  Peng-a2 chau2 khi3 peng-iaN5 po3 si2.  Ka-teng to3-khi3 soa3 m7-kaN2 jip8-khi3.  Chhu3-nih8 lang5-kheh kong7-kong7-kun2.  Khun-hong le2-hok chheng7 pian7-pian7, kau3 beh tau3 lah tai7-ke chiah chai si7 beh chhoa7 sin-niu5.  Tit8-tit8 tan2, khoaN3-si5 beh chin3-pang5, si5 ia7 koe3 lah, sin-niu5 kau3-taN iau2-boe7 lai5.  Tai7-ke am7-kun2 chhun tng5-tng5, long2 hong-siaN Tan5--ka3 e5 siau3-ia5 beh chhoa7-chhin.  Chiah che7-hoe3 chiah beh chhoa7, chit-pai2 siu3-kiu5 si7 chhin chhiu2 pha--e5.  Liah8 in bo2-ku7 TiuN chiong-kun choe3 moai5-lang5--e5.  Un2-tang3 chin-sui2, na7 m7-si7 u7 Goat2-li2 Siong5-gou5 e5 pan7, ia7 tioh8 u7 Sai3 Se-si e5 khoan2.  Na7 bo5 “Siu-hoa pi3-goat8 e5 sui2, ma7 u7 tim5-hi5 lok8-gan7 e5 sui2”（＝Na7 bo5 hoe khoaN3 i lai5 kian3-siau3 chiu7 hap8 khi3, goeh8-niu5 khoaN3 i lai5 chiu7 ng-bin7 e5 sui2, ia7 tek-khak u7 li2-hi5 khoaN3 i lai5 e5 sui2 chiu7 chhang3 loh8 chui2, gan7 teh poe khoaN3 i lai5 e5 sui2 chiu7 hioh loh8--lai5 e5 sui2).  Ji5-chhiaN2 ke3-chng m7-chai beh kah goa7 che7 lai5 leh.  Sou2-i2 jin5-san jin5-hai2 e5 lang5 ai3 lai5 khoaN3.  Iu7-koh si7 5 goeh8 13 jit8, siaN5-lai7 ngia5 Seng5-hong5, hong-siaN pong3-iaN2 pi2 beh lai5 khoaN3 toa7-hi3 e5 lang5 iau2 khah che7.  Khun-hong ia7 iong5-iong5 tek-i3 chhun-hong moa2-bin7, chit8 tiam2 tan2 koe3 chit8 tiam2 tan2 bo5.  Tan2 kau3 bak8-chiu seN bi2-lo5-a2, sim-lai7 chian tiN-koe2.  Chit8-choa7 chhut, chit8-choa7 jip8, mng5-teng7 tah8 kau3 beh ui-khi3.  Lang5-kheh tan2 kau3 toa7-tng5 ko3 sio2-tng5.  Kou-put-chiong in bo2-ku7 hoah khui-toh.  In bo2-ku7 sim-te2 am3-am3 teh siuN7 poh-kaN2 e7 chhut-su7.  Bo5, an2-choaN2 e7 bu2 kau3 chiah oaN3.  Chit8-sim siuN7 kong2 sim-pak e5 su7-koaN kap iaN5-lai7 e5 oe7-peng khi3, che si7 siang7 tho3-tong3 un2-tang3 e7 sun7-su7 chiah tioh8.  M7-ku2 eng3-kai boe7 tau3, m7-si7, si7 ai3 koh khah-cha2 tioh8 kau3-ui7 chiah tioh8.  M7, kiam2-si7 siuN-oaN3 he7 chhiu2, m7, kiam2-si7 lou7-tiong u7 lang5 lai5 kiap.  SiuN7 liau2 chin put-tek khai-khiau.  Koh theng5 chit8-e7-a2 lang5 hoa7-hoa7 kio3 teh lai5.  Khun-hong siuN7 kong2 tai7-khai3 sin-niu5 kau3 lah.  Kin2 chiN3 choe3 cheng5 lai5 khoaN3, khoaN3 chit e7 nou7-khi3 chhiong-thian.  KhoaN3 kng-kio7 e5 ka-teng Han-chi5-a7 tng7-kha hou7 lang5 aiN7.” Koh chit8 e5 ka-teng kng kio7-au7 hit e5 phak loh8-khi3, chin tu2-chhian-chhian siang3 tui3 chioh-thau5 loh8-khi3 thau5-hiah8 kong3 chit8 khang, phiN7 ia7 hiam2-hiam2-a2 kong3 peN5-khi3 phiN7-hoeh chhia teh to3.  U7 e5 chhiu2 lut-khu7, tng7-khi3 e5 ia7 u7, khau3-khou2 lian5-thian.  Tai7-ke kiu-kiu lun-lun m7-kaN2 chin3-cheng5.  U7 chit8 e5 lau7 ka-teng ho7 choe3 Chhau3-thau5-a2-chek, tai7-ke tu i choe3 cheng5 lai5 kong2.  Chhau3-thau5-a2 chin3-cheng5 khok8-lok8 kui7 loh8-khi3, siang-chhiu2 kiok-kiong khok8-khok8 hou3, kiu5 Siau3-ia5 jiau5-mia7, “Sin-niu5 kng …… kng kau3 …… kau3 poaN3-lou7.” “PoaN3-lou7 an2-choaN2?” “To …… to hou7 hou7 lang5 …… lang5 …… lang5” koh loh8-khi3 hit ku3 m7-kaN2 kong2, kan-ta tiam3-hia lang7-lang7-lang7.  Khun-hong hui-siong5 khi3, chau2 oa2 khi3 pa-sian-chiuN2 chhut-lat8 siuN2 chit8 e5 hou7 i, “kan-ta lang7, poaN3-lou7 kiam2 u7 lang5 teh lang7 sin-niu5 tioh8 bo5?”  “M7 …… m7 …… si7” “M7-si7, bo5 an2-choaN2 lang7” “Hou7 lang5 chhiuN2 khi3 lah.” ThiaN chit8 siaN hou7 lang5 chhiuN2-khi3, khi3 chit8 e7 huih hiam2-a2 pun5 chhut--lai5.  Kha-chiN chu7 an2-ni ka7 cham3-khi3.  Lang5-kheh kong7-kong7 kun2 bo5 koh chiah8, tai7-ke long2 li7-sek8.  Peng ia7 lai5 po3 chiong-kun e5 phaiN2 siau-sit.  In bo2-ku7 hoah tai7-ke an-cheng7 teN3 chhin3-chhio3, kong2 che sio2-su7, che si7 gin2-na2 su7 na7-tiaN7.  U7 lang5 toe3 chhui3 in3 kong2, kah si7 TiuN chiong-kun teh choe3-su7, na2-li2 kiaN i m7-lai5, u7 e5 sim-te2 siuN7 kong2 sin-niu5 eng7 ka7 lang5 chhiuN2--e5 bo5 cheng5-li2, chong2-si7 bo5 lang5 kaN2 khui-chhui3.  Tai7-ke chin bo5 i3-su3 chu7 an2-ni pai7-heng3 soaN3-sek8.  
14
Lim5 tiuN2-lo2-niu5 thiaN Bok8-su to3-khi3 sou2 kong2 e5 siau-sit, chai Hui7-bi2 siu7 Siu2-jin5 kiu3 khi3 chiu7 kui2-hun khah an-sim.  Tai7-ke kiu5 Chu2 pang-chan7 in2-chhoa7, ng3-bang7 e7 sun7-su7.  Chong2-si7 phah-si2 lang5 chit8 tiau5 beng7-an3 tek-khak e7 u7-su7, tui3 chit-chan5 tai7-ke chin khoa3-lu7.  TiuN chiong-kun theng3-hau7 tai7-ke soaN3-sek8 au7, chin siu7-khi3 kio3 hiah8 e5 ka-teng lai5, seng3 hoat tin5-tiau5 giah8 khi2--lai5 tit8 but8.  Chiok-chham2 tioh8 siong bo5 lang5 kho2-lin5 koh hou7 lang5 but8.  Chiong-tiong khah lau7-poe3 e5 chhau3-thau5-a2-chek hou7 lang5 but8 siong7 thiam2.  I siau3-lian5 ia7-si7 chit8 e5 lou5-moa5.  TiuN chiong-kun me7 i an2-ni si7 chin “sit-hong”（=Iu2--e5 choe3-su7 sit-loh8 hong-thau5, bo5 the2-bian7).  An-choaN2 iam2-ki5 sit-kou2, na2 iap-boe2 kau2 boe2-a2 iap-leh, bin7 ti3 kah-hah8, an2-ni soe-soe-a to3-lai5.  Sit-liau2 goa2 pun2 chiong-kun e5 ui-hong.  Khi3 kau3 bo5 ho2 kho2-jim2, chiong chiaN5 chap8 e5 ka-teng tiap8 tit chit8 tiuN5 lok8-hoa liu5-sui2 chhi-chham2 lok8-phek.  Khau3-khou2 lian5-thian, oan3-siaN su3-khi2.  Chhoa7 sin-niu5 e5 jit8 soa3 piN3 choe3 loan7 chhau-chhau thi5-khau3 e5 jit8.  Chiong-kun but8 lang5 chhiu2 kaN2-si7 sng lah, tin5-tiau5 pang3-leh, jip8--lai5 chhiu2 tui3 toh-teng2 toa7-e7 chiu7 tng3 loh8 khi3, toa7-siaN hoah-kong2 na7 bo5 liah8 chit e5 loh8-kau3-a2-kui2 lai5 chek-kut tek-khak bo5 beh pang3 i kan-hiu.  Keh jit8 chek-si5 chhe lang5 lai5 Su7-liong5 tiau-cha.  Lai5 bo5 poaN3 lang5, chai tiuN2-lo2-niu5 kap sim-pu7 iau2 ti7--teh, hian7-si5 khi3 ti7 pai3-tng5.  U7 soan-kau3-su po2-hou7, si7 cha-bou2 lang5, kap che su7 ia7 bo5 siang-kan.  Iau3-kin2 si7 ai3 liah8 Siu2-jin5 kap Hui7-bi2.  Tui3 an2-ni chiu7 si3-ke3 am3-hong2.  Goan5-in ui7-tioh8 si7 su-su7, lam7-iong7 kun-ui, chit-koan5 lai5 jia2-su7, sou2-i2 m7-kaN2 hian2-jian5 tui-chhip.  M7-na7 phai3-lang5 si3-koe3 am3-hong2, chiu7 Khun-hong ia7 si5-khi3 Chioh-iu5 kong-si e5 thau5-lou7 si3-ke3 lok8-lok8 kiaN5, be7 su sit-khi3 ka-ti7 chhui3-nih beh chiah8 e5 bah lai5 si3-ke3 tui-chhoe7 e5 kong5 kau2 chit8-iuN7.
Si5-jit5 chin khoai3-koe3 liam-piN koe3 poaN3-ni5 khah ke, ni5-te2 kau3 lah chin kin7 chiok Seng3-tan3 e5 si5, Siu2-jin5 jit8--si5 m7-kaN2 chhut-khi3.  Am3-si5 chiu7 khi3 chit8-keng hun2-chhiuN2 choe3 kang.  Hui7-bi2 ia7 m7-bat chhut-khi3, siong5-siong5 si7 ti7 lai7-bin7 pang-bang5 ke-lai7 su7.  U7 chit8-jit8 thau3-cha2 Hui7-bi2 beh chhut-khi3 se2-saN.  Chhiu2 phang5 chit8 bin7-thang2 saN tui3 au7-boe2-mng5 chhut-khi3, beh khi3 au7-piah khe-a2.  Hut-jian5 taN thau5 chit8 khoaN3 toa7 tioh8-kiaN.  Che si7 bin5-bang7 a2-si7 chin-chiaN3, chiu7-si7 Khun-hong chhiu2 hiahN chit8-nia2 toa7 hiu5, bin7 chin siau-san2 khia7 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5.  Hui7-bi2 kiaN chit8 e7 sin5-put-hu7 the2, saN piaN tiam3 thou5-kha oat8-thau5 chu7 an2-ni piaN3 teh chau2.
Khun-hong khoaN3 chit8-e7 ia7 na2-chun2 tui3 bang7-tiong kiaN-chhiN2, toa7-hiu5 hiat-kak8 khui-po7 tit8-jiok.  Bian2 kui2 pou7 chiu7 hou7 i jiok tioh8.  Hia si7 phian-phiah e5 hiuN-chng thau3-cha2 lang5 chin-chio2, si3-piN long2 bo5 lang5.  Ki3-jian5 hou7 i jiok-tioh8, Hui-bi2 chiu7 tong3-tiam7, thau5-khak chhih-chhih kiong2-chhiu2, bak8-chiu kheh-kheh ki5-to2.  I e5 sim-lai7 siuN7 kong2 chham2-lah, hai2 sui-bong2 khoah-khoah, chun5-thau5 eh8-eh8, ku2 ia7 e7 sio-tng7.  TaN ti7 chia iu7-koh tng7 tioh8 i.  Lau2-sit8 kong2 i tui3 Khun-hong peng7 m7-si7 phaiN2-i3.  Si7 m7-ke3 bo5 siang7 sin3-giong2 e5 lang5, koat-sim ai3 siu2 lau7-pe7 e5 ui5-gian5.  Chit8 sim ia7 si7 chin thiaN3--i, m7-ku2 na7 siuN7 tioh8 i na2 pang2-hui2 eng7 nge7-liah8--e5 sit8-chai7 chin m7-goan7.  Ia7 siuN7 ui7 chit chan5 su7 jia2-khi2 mia7-an3, taN chit pai2 hou7 i tu2-tioh8 m7-chai beh chaiN2-iuN7?  Sim-lai7 ia7 siu7-khi3, ia7 kiaN-hiaN5, ia7 thiaN3--i.  Sit8-chai7 si7 chit8 e5 kho2-ai3 e5 tek8-jin5, be7-hiau2 kong2 e5 sim-cheng5.  Chi2-u7 bak8-chiu pang3-kheh ki5-to2 kau-tai3 Chu2.  Phah-sng3 kau3 chia chit tiau5 beng7-an3 phoa3 lah.  Tai7-khai3 Khun-hong e7 chin siu7-khi3, e7 thoa i khi3 kiN3-koaN.  Bo5 phah-sng3 u7 sio-lo7 e5 chui2 tih ti7 i e5 kha-poaN5.  Koh u7 teh hau2 chheh-khui3 e5 siaN.  Hui7-bi2 bak8-chiu thau thi2-khui ka7 i khoaN3-mai7, chiah chai Khun-hong e5 chiaN3-kha chit8-kha kui7 ti7 thou5-kha, chhiu2 ng-bin7 teh hau2, tih ti7 i e5 kha-poaN5 sio-sio e5 chui2 m7-si7 chui2, si7 Khun-hong e5 bak8-sai2, chin ku2 nng7 e5 lang5 bo5 kong2-oe7.  Au7-lai5 Hui7-bi2 tui3 chhiu2 ka7 i khan khi2-lai5.  Khun-hong taN-thau5 khoaN3 Hui7-bi2 kam5-bak8-sai2 e5 bin7.  Khun-hong lian5 siaN kiu5 “Hui7-bi2 sio2-chia2 chhiaN2 li2 sia3-bian2, hou7 li2 siu7 kiaN, hou7 li2 phun-pho, goan7 li2 sia3-bian2.” Hui7-‘ bi2 khoaN3 Khun-hong e5 thai3-tou7 m7-si7 beh lai5 tui-chhip i, si7 ho2-i3 lai5 chhoe7 i, sim chiah siu7 an-ui3.  Tui3 an2-ni bin7 tng2-chhio3.  Khun-hong khoaN3 Hui7-bi2 tng2-chhio3 chiah khi2--lai5, khan Hui7-bi2 e5 chhiu2 lai5 chim.  Tui3 an2-ni nng7-lang5 choe3-hoe2 kiaN5 jip8 sou2 bih e5 chhu3.  Tu2 jip8-khi3 che7-loh8 u7 chit8-e7-a2 Siu2-jin5 tui3 che3-hun2 kang-tiuN5 to3-lai5.  In-ui7 i si7 choe3 me5-kang, thau3-cha2 lang5 iau2 chio2-chio2 bo5 siaN2 lang5 teh kiaN5 lou7 e5 si5 i chiu7 to3--lai5.  Jip8-mng5 khoaN3 tioh8 Khun-hong, chit8 si5 hoe2 toh8, khi3-tit nou7-hoat chhiong-thian.  Tui3 chit-kioh hoai7-tong-si hai7-tit chhit-khap peh-chhio3.  Long2 bo5 poe2-hoe7 oa2--lai5, na2 teh koaN7 chhau2-chang2 an2-ni, chit8 chhiu2 tui3 heng-khau2 giu2 leh, chit8-chhiu2 tui3 e7-io ka7 i chhah khi2--lai5, kui-sian lang5 ka7 i haiN3 kau3 khong-tiong, chhek chit8 e7 be2-se3 beh ka7 i siak tui3 chhiuN5-piah loh8-khi3, chit e7 hou7 i siak khi3, thau5-khak khi3 tong7 chhiuN5-piah, chiu7 phah-sng3 i teh siau3-ia5 thak8 tai7-hak8 pit8-giap8 e5 hak8-su7.  In lau7-bo2 chiu7-khi3 khau3 bo5 kiaN2.  Khun-hong kiaN chit8 e5 bin7 chheN sun2-sun2, kin2 kio3 kiu3 lang5.  Hui7-bi2 khoaN3 chit8 e7 ia7 ho2 khi3, ia2 ho2 chhio3, ia7 kho2-lin5, siuN7 kong2 eng3-kai, chong2-si7 ia7 m7-kam.  Kin2 hoah “Siu2-jin5, Siu2-jin5 lan2 m7-thang eng7 phaiN2 po3 phaiN2.  Lan2 tioh8 thiaN3 tui3-tek8, kin2 ka7 i pang3 loh8-lai5.”  Siu2-jin5 thiaN Sio2-chia2 teh kio3, hit e5 siaN u7 kaN5 thiaN3-thang3 ai-kiu5 e5 siaN, chu7 an2-ni tng2-chhio3 un-un-a2 ka7 i hoe5 loh8 lai5, ka7 i khng3 tiam3 thou5-kha.  Peng5-si5 Khun-hong si7 bun5-sin, tui3 chit chan5 su7 liau2-au7 be7 chiah8, cheng5-sin5 na7 chun2 iN7-chong7 e5 leh.  Chit8-bin7 liong-sim chu7-chek, chit8-bin7 ai3-bou7 i sim-ai3 e5 Hui7-bi2.  I tiaN7 ka7 i pi2-pheng7 choe3 kho2-ai3 e5 moai5-kui3.  Sou2-i2 piN3 chin-chiaN3 san2, si3-ke3 liu5-long5 kin-a2-jit8 chhoe7 lai5 kau3-chia.  Tu2 khi3 kap Hui7-bi2 sio-tu2, ki5-sit8 lian5 cha2-khi2 to iau2-boe7 chiah8.  In-ui7 i chai Hui7-bi2 si7 teh keng-koe3 bih e5 seng-oah8, sou2-i2 i ia7-si7 eng7 am3-si5 kap thau3-cha2 teh chhoe7 i.  Chiah e7 ti7 thau3-cha2 hou7 i tu2-tioh8.  Lau2-sit8 kong2 u7 khou2-sim, go7 liau2 khin-khin to bo5 80 kin leh.  Na2-li2 tu3 oa2 500 kin lat8 e5 chong3-su7 ia2-gu5 e7 tiau5.  Tui3 heng-kham2 giu2 oa2-lai5 am7-nia2 sok-an5 hiam2-hiam2 bo5 khui3.  Tui3 e7-io hou7 Siu2-jin5 lak8 chit8 e7 thiaN3 chit8 peng5.  Koh ka7 i haiN3 hiah koan5, liah8 tian-to3-thau5-chai pi2 beh ka7 i siak tui3 chhiuN5-piah loh8 khi3, kiaN chit8 e7 sin5 long2 chau2 khi3 heng5-siong7 goa7.  Ka7 i pang3 loh8 lai5 chiu7 an2-ni un tiam3 thou5-kha, bak8-chiu theh8-theng5 theh8-theng5 liah8 Siu2-jin5 kim-kim siong3, chhiu2 khu7-khu7 chun, khok8-khok8 pai3, be7 chhut siaN.  Hui7-bi2 khoaN3 liau2 soa3 sim-sng, m7-kam, kin2 ka7 i khan khi2-lai5, chhiau5 i2-a2 hou7 i che7, khi3 phang5 chit8 poe sio-te5 hou7 i lim, ka7 i teh-kiaN, jian5-au7 chiah khui-chhui3 kong2-oe7.  Siu2-jin5 khoaN3-liau2 ia7 chin-chiaN3 ho2 khi3, ia7 ho2-chhio3, ia7 kho2-lin5 i e5 sit-thai3.  Kong2 “Kin-a2-jit8 na7 m7-si7 goan2 sio2-chia2 kio3 goa2 ka7 li2 pang3-khi3, li2 bo5 mia7 lah li2.  Li2 koh kaN2 eng7 chit ho7 pou7, eng7 lang5 lai5 nge7-liah8, be7 su pang2-hui2, bo5-le2 thai3-sim7.” Khun-hong tit8-tit8 hoe7 sit-le2, chhe7 put-si7.  Hui7-bi2 khoaN3 an2-ni, khou2-khng3 Siu2-jin5 mai3 koh the5-khi2 koe3-khi3 e5 phaiN2 lai5 chek-pi7 i.  Ia7 chai i iau2-boe7 chiah8 cha2-khi2, chiu7 tai7-ke chun2-pi7 cha2-tng3 choe3 hoe2 chiah8.  Khun-hong hit cha2-khi2 ia7 kiaN, ia7 koaN5 tioh8 soa3 hoat-jiat8, chu7 an2-ni ti7 hia tiam3 kui2 na7 jit8.  Hui7-bi2 chiau3-ku7 ho2 khoan2-thai7 i.  Ia7 tui3 Khun-hong e5 thou3-lou7, chiah chai in bu2-ku7 tui3 hit-si5 liau2-au7 chit-si5 chin siu7 khi3, si3-ke3 phai3-lang5 tui-chhoe7, koe3 kui2 goeh8 jit8 au7 chiu7 na2 leng.  U7 chit8-pai2 ti7 toa7 chiu2-ian3 tiong po7 im2 (暴飲) , chhut-chiu2 ti7 ian3-sek8-tiong chu7 an2-ni to2 tui3 toh-kha loh8 khi3.  Thau5-khak khok8 tioh8 toh-koaiN, nau2-kin chhut-huih soa3 poan7-sui7, koh bo5 loa7 ku2 chiu7 si2-khi3.  Hit-am3 si7 8 goeh8 15 jit8 Tiong-chhiu lo5-kun e5 si5.  Tui3 an2-ni chit chan5-su7 oan5-choan5 soah khi3 lah.
Chiah e5 tai7-chi3 Khun-hong in tau thong ke bo5 lang5 hoaN-hi2.  Chi2-u7 Siu3-chhun siong7 hoaN-hi2.  Tak8-hang7 i to phah chhiu2 kong2 eng3-kai.  Ui7 tioh8 an2-ni Khun-hong it-hoat chiah8-khi3 beh kiu5 kau3 Hui7-bi2 tioh8.  Chong2-si7 Hui7-bi2 chai Khun-hong u7 lau7-bu2, i long2 m7-chai iau2 u7 chit8 e5 cheng5-tek8 Siu3-chhun, chit8 e5 pi2 lau7-bu2 khah li7-hai7, i long2 m7-chai2, in-ui7 Khun-hong long2 m7 bat kong2.  Khun-hong ti7-hia phoa3-piN7 siu7 Hui7-bi2 un-jiu5 thiaN3-thang3 e5 chiau3-kou3.  Hui7-bi2 kin7 chiok-seng3-tan3 ai3 kiN3 lau7-bu2 e5 sim chhiat.  Khun-hong ti7 hia ia7 chu7-kak na7 m7-si7 kap i loh8-kau3, beh ban2 chit8-lui2 sui2 e5 moai5-kui3 bo5 hong-hoat, chiu7 ia7 chin7 sou2 e7 oh8 ki5-to2.  Seng3-keng chu7-jian5 thak8 kok-gu2--e5 bo5 bun7-te5, chhiaN2 Hui7-bi2 ka3 i gim5-si.  Bian2 kui2-jit8 giam5-jian5 Ki-tok-to5.
U7 chit8-jit8 i chiu7 koh tui3 Hui7-bi2 kiu5-chhin, Hui7-bi2 lai5 kau3 chia khoaN3 i e5 seng5-i3 hou7 cheng5 sou2 tiN5 ia7 sim-nng2, kap i kong2 kui2-na7 hang7 tiau5 kiaN7.
1.  Li2 tioh8 kap goa2 pai3 Siong7-te3 sin3 Chu2 Ia5-sou.
2.  Li2 tioh8 po2 goa2 peng5-an, to3 lai5 khi3 kiN3 lau7-bu2.
3.  Li2 tioh8 po2 Siu2-jin5 bu5 su7.  I si7 chin7-tiong e5 lou5-pok8.  Li2 ia7 tioh8 thiaN3--i.
Tak8-hang7 to in3 ho2.  Tui3 an2-ni kap Siu2-jin5 chham-siong5 keh-jit8 chiu7 khoan2 heng5-li2 chhut-hoat to3 lai5 Su7-liong5.  Bian2 keng-koe3 kui2-jit chiu7 kau3-chhu3.  Lang5 khi3 po3 TiuN2-lo2-niu5 chai, tai7-ke bo2 kiaN2 sa-kiN3 lam2 teh khau3.  Khun-hong ia7 kui7 loh8 jin7-chho3 kio3 m7-kaN2.  Lau7 lang5 khoaN3 tioh8 an2-ni ia7 sia3-bian2--i.  Soa3 thiaN Khun-hong kiu5-chhin, Hui7-bi2 kap i iok-sok e5 su7.  Bok8-su kong2 su7 kau3-chia, i na7 choe3 chin-sit8 e5 ki-tok-to5 ia7-si7 kho2-i2 lah.  Tui3 an2-ni Khun-hong chiu7 koh kap in ti7 hia kui2-na7-jit8, tai7-ke koh poaN-poaN to3 lai5 ka-ti7 e5 chhu3.  Tai7-ke hoaN-hi2 koe3 Seng3-tan3-cheh.
Khun-hong chiu7 to3 khi3, koh chheng2 hok8-chit phai3 lai5 Su7-liong5 choe3 cham7-tiuN2.  In-ui7 chioh8-iu5 kong-si iau2 u7 ti7 chia chiap-siok8 teh khai-chhai2 chioh8-iu5.  Tui3 koh lai5 Su7-liong5 liau2-au7 Khun-hong chiu7 jiat8-sim khi3 siu2 le2-pai3.  Put-ko3 kio3 i nia2 se2-le2, i mui2-mui2 kong2 theng3-hau7 lau7-bu2 ni5-lau7 chiah lai5.  Kong2 in lau7-bu2 si7 seng5-sim e5 chhai3-kou chu7 siau3-lian5 chiuN2 chheng-koaN2, chiuN2 i chit8 e5, m7-ai3 hou7 i hoan5-lo2, siu7-khi3.  An2-ni thiaN liau2 chin u7 li2-iu5, ki-sit8 sim-lai7 si7 bo5 hiah khoai3 chiap-lap8 Chu2 Ia5-sou, put-ko3 goa7-mau7 tek-khak si7 Ki-tok-tou5.  Chiau3 ku7 khi3 kia3 siok ti7 TiuN2-lo2-niu2 in tau.  U7 chit8-jit8 chit-tui3 chheng-lian5 chiu7 ti7 Ong5 Bok8-su e5 su-sek-ha7 i-chiau3 ki-tok-kau3-sek kiaN5 kiat-hun tian2-le2.  Bo5 loa7 ku2 ia7 ka7 Siu2-jin5 chhoa7 bou2.  Ia7 chiong ke-lai7 it-chhe3 e5 su7 kau-tai3 Siu2-jin5 chiang2-li2.  Si5-jit5 chin khoai3-koe3 bian2 loa7 ku2 iu koe3 chiaN5 poaN3 ni5 lah.  TiuN2-lo2-niu5 ni5 lau7 lah, u7 chit8 pai2 tui3 chiah8 liau2 bo5 tu2-ho2 soa3 lau3 chin ku2, soa3 piN3 ban7-seng3 chin oh i-ti7.  San2 kau3 chit8-teng5 phoe5 ne5 chit8 ki kut, chong2-si7 i e5 sim u7 peng5-an.  In-ui7 Hui2-bi2 e5 chhin-chiaN5 ia7 cho3-liau2 ke3 liau2.  Sun-a2 ia7 koai-koai toa7-han3 long2 e7 kiaN5 lah.  Siu2-jin5 ia7 chhoa7 lah, chit8-ke chin nau7-jiat8.  U7 chit8-me5 hut-jian5 khi2 sim-chong7 bo5 lat8, long2 bo5 kong2 sim2-mih8 ui5-gian5 chu7 an2-ni tiam7-khi3.  Tai7-ke chin iu-bun7. 
15
Khun-hong kap Hui7-bi2 liau7-li2 lau7-bu2 e5 chong3-sek liau2-au7 it-toaN7-lok8, ia2 tu2-ho2 kong-si beh ka7 i choan2-khin5, chiu7 tho2 khi3 ka-ti7 e5 kou3-hiong Chiang-chiu koan7-siaN5.  Hui7-bi2 ia7 hoaN-hi2, siuN7 kong2 chu7 ke3 Khun-hong to iau2-boe7 u7 ki-hoe7 thang to3-khi3 pai3-tham3 ta-ke.  Koh ka-ti7 ia7 chai pak-tou2 i2-keng u7 sin iok gou7, lak8 goeh8-jit8 lah.  Sou2-i2 ia7 chin hoaN-hi2 kap tai7-ke saN-si5 poaN-poaN to3-khi3 koan7-siaN5.  Jip8-mng5 chiu7 chai-si2 lah.
Kap ta-ke sio-chioh mng7, ta-ke chin bo5 chheng3-i3, chhui3 tu7-tu7 bo5 in3, liah8-chun2 si7 bo5 thiaN-kiN3, lian5 mng7 kui2-na7-siaN, bin7 oat8-tui3 piN-a chiah hng3 chit8--e5.  Chai khou2 lah!  Siu3-chhun siam2 m7 kiN3 i e5 bin7, kin-pun2 i ia7 m-chai lai7-bin7 iau2 u7 chit8 e5 lang5 ho7 choe3 Siu3-chhun.  Ta-ke bo5 chheng3-i3 sim2-mih8?  Te7 1, loh8 kau3--e5 si2 liau2 bo5 lang5 khau3, i tit8-kam2 i na7 si2, bo5 chhai2 i chiah8 chheng chhai3 beh chiuN7 Se-thian, ng3-bang7 kiaN2-ji5 sim-pu7 e7 ka7 i sio-hiuN, liam7-keng, hau3 png7.  TaN bian2 ng3-bang7 lah.  I eng2-oan2 tioh8 choe3 go7-kui2.  Sou2-i2 bo5 pi2 chit-hang7 khah chheh.  Te 2, bo5 sun7-hok8 i e5 chu2-i3.  Siu3-chhun kin-ni5 ia7 oa2 30 lah.  M7-ke3 chiu7-si7 m7-ke3.  I an3-sng3 beh tit ke-hoe2, an3-sng3 beh kap Hui7-bi2 piaN3 seN-si2, cheN kau3 tauh-te2.  Ta-ke-a2 ia7-si7 be7 li7-tit Siu3-chhun.  Siu3-chhun si7 chit8 e5 hui-siong5 li7-hai7 e5 lu2-seng3.  Liam7-keng le2-hut8, goa7-kau chiap kheh ku3 li2 lai5.  Sit-chai7 bo5 kian3-siau3 choe3 chit8 e5 koan7-siaN5 e5 kau-che3-hoa, kin7 lai5 oh8 kau3 poah8 ma5-chhiok, sng2 pai5-a2, chiah8-hun, thiau3-bu2 tak8-hang7 to e7.  ChiN5 theh8 e7 tioh8, tui3 iuN2-bu2(Khun-hong e5 lau7-bu2) ia7 sun7 cheng5, chhut-chai7 i eng7, chng kau3 chit8-sian na2 ang-a2 leh.  To3 lai5 3 jit8 tu2 si7 Khun-hong lau7-pe7 e5 ki7-jit8.  Hit-jit8 pan7 chin chhiN-chhau kou i5, ku7 kim7 chek peh, chim2 m2, chhu3-piN lin5-iu7 che7-che7 lang5 long2 lai5 saN tham3.  Koh thiaN Khun-hong chhoa7 sin-niu5 to3-lai5 koh-khah che7 lang5 lai5.  Chiok chiok khui iok 10 te3 toh.  Long2 si7 toa7 hi5 toa7 bah, san-tin hai2-bi7.  Tai7-ke hoah-kun5 thiong3 im2, toa7 nau7 ji5 tek8-nau7.  Khun-hong chit8 chhiu2 theh8-hun, chit8-chhiu2 theh8 chiu2 poe, chit8-toh kiaN5 koe3 chit8 toh chhiaN2 lang5 lim-chiu2.  Ka-ti7 ia7 hoah kun5, khoaN3 sim2-mih8 kun5 to e7-hiau2 hoah.  Chit khoan2 su7 Hui7-bi2 it-seng long2 m7-bat khoaN3 tioh8, ia7 m7-bat siuN7 tioh8, an2-choaN2 ki7-jit8 si7 tui3 kou3-jin5 e5 tui-to7 si7 iu-bun7, choe3-sek le2-pai3 kong2 khi2 kou3-jin5 e5 li2-lek8 lai5 bian2-le7 hou7-poe3.  SaN kap ki5-to2, hiaN-ti7, chi2-moai7 koh chu7-chip8 saN kap siau3-liam7 cha2-si5 pe7 bo2 e5 thiaN3.  Na7-u7 kam2-cheng5 m7-tu2-ho2 sun7 chit-jit8 ti7 kou3-jin5 pe7 bo2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tai7-ke na2-chun2 khoaN3 pe7 bo2 e5 bin7 koh lai5 ak-chhiu2.  Siong5-siong5 si7 tai7-ke kam2-kek kau3 lau5 bak8-sai2.  Na2-li2 u7 chit heng5--e5.  Toa7 chiah8 toa7 lim, chit8 sut-a2 to bo5 pi-ai, to bo5 siau3-liam7 kou3-jin5.  Si7 tit8-tit8 hoa7, bo5-kou3 si7 chia3 chit8 e5 ki-hoe7 lai5 ian3-lok8.  Sou2-i2 Hui7-bi2 khoaN3 liau2 chin m7-koan3-si3.  Sim siang7 thiaN3 e5, chiu7-si7 Khun-hong oan5-choan5 kap ti7 Su7-liong5 e5 si5 koh piN3 chit8 khoan2 lang5.  I long2 m7-chai Khun-hong e7 chiah8-hun, chiah8-chiu2, hoah-kun5, ji5-chhiaN2 chiu2-liong7 hiah-kiong5.  I e5 sim e7 thiaN3, long2 choat8-bang7 lah.  Thau5-khak tiaN7 chhih-chhih, sui-jian5 che7 ti7 toh-nih tiaN7-tiaN7 theh8 chhiu2-kin-a2 thau chhit bak8-sai2.  Ia7 be7 hiau2 ka7 lang5 thin5 chiu2, kin-pun2 i bo5 koan3-si3 chit ho7 su7.  U7 lang5 kong2 i toa7-te3 kek-sai2, u7 e5 kong2 i iau2 sin-niu5 phaiN2-se3, u7 e5 kong2 i khah u7 cheng5 kaN2-si7 teh siuN7 tioh8 Ta-koaN.  Long2 bo5 lang5 chai i si7 ui7 sin3-giong2 e5 lip8-tiuN5 lai5 kan-khou.  Khun-hong chai, thiau-ti5 teN3 chhin3-chhio3.  Chong2-si7 ti7 toh-nih u7 chit8 e5 na2-chun2 boe2-iah8 e5 sui2, kap Khun-hong ho2 chit8-tui3, iu-goan5 chit8 chhiu2 giah8 hun, chit8-chhiu2 koaN7 pan5 si3-ke3 keng3-chiu2, chhui3 chhio3 gi7-gi7, kek-ki5 u7 le2-mau7, kou-i5 ku7-kim7, chek-peh chim2-m2 long2 chin sek8-sai7, le2-le2 chia2-chia2, hu5-kha sang2-chhiu2 e5 khoan2-thai7 lang5 kheh.  Siong5-siong5 eng7 bak8-boe2 khoaN3 Khun-hong, piau2-si7 ho2-i3 e5 bi5-chhio3.  Ho2 li7-hai7 ah?  Sim chin m7-goan7, chong2-si7 it-chhe3 khng3 ti7 sim lai7.  Si2 to chiu3-choa7 beh cheN kau3 iaN5.  Chhin-chhek che7-che7 ti7 toh-nih ian5-siah tiong soa3 phoe-pheng5 chhoa7 m7-tioh8 e5, phoe5 chiuN7 kut-chiuN7, na7 chhoa7 Siu3-chhun m7-chiu7 chin ho2.  Ho2 chit8-tui3 ang-seng bou2-toaN3, khoaN3 khi3 chhoa7 tioh8 chit8 e5 hau3-lam5-sin5, ia7 be7 khi2-chhiaN2 khi2-kheh.  Tai7-ke tit8 hoe7 tit8 kong-jian5, Hui7-bi2 chiah chai lang5 si7 teh kong2--i, chiah chai hit e5 na2 boe2-iah8-po5 hit e5 si7 kio3 choe3 “Siu3-chhun”.  Chong2-si m7-chai hit e5 lang5 kap chit e5 ka-teng5 si7 sim2-mih8 koan-he7.  In-ui7 chiau3 i sou2 chai Ta-ke si7 chiuN2-koaN2, chi2 u7 seN tiong7-hu Khun-hong chit e5.  TaN che si7 an2-choaN2?  Khah theng5 ta-ke chhut lai5 Siu3-chhun chit8 e7 chiu7 khi2--lai5 kio3 “A-nia2” tui3 chhiu2 ka7 i khan leh.  Niu7 ui7 hou7 i che7.  Chiah hoaN-hi2 ka7 a-nia2 thin5 chit8-poe chiu2.  Hui7-bi2 chin gong5-ngiah8, an2-choaN2 chit e5 lang5 thai2 kio3 Ta-ke A-nia2.  Kiam2-si7 sio2-kou?  I ia7 bo5 i3-sek khia7 khi2-lai5 chheng2-an ta-ke.  Ta-ke m7 chhiu3--i, kou3 kap pat8-lang5 kong2-oe7.  I ka-ti7 bo5-i3-sin5, bo5-i3-sin5 che7 toh loh8 khi3.  Khan-theng5 cha-bou2 lang5 kheh chiu7 u7 lang5 ng3 in ta-ke kong2 lin2 Khun-hong e5 bak8-chiu chin-chiaN3 hou7 leng5-geng2-hut8 oaN7 khi3.  U7 e5 ka7 i poe2-chhiu2 bih-chhui3 kong2 m7-thang kong2, phaiN2-se3.  U7 e5 kong2 boe7-ban7 ou3, siau3-lian5 siau3-tak nng7 e5 long2 siu khi2-lai5, chit8 e5 li2 lai7, chit8 e5 li2 goa7.  Lan2 to7 u7 leh to7 m7-si7 choe3 be7 kau3, koh pian7-pian7 ti7 lai7-bin7.  Siu3-chhun thiaN liau2 chin hoaN-hi2.  Thiau-ti5 ng3 Khun-hong bun2-chhio3, hian2-beng5 kiau-thai3, kong2 “Goan ia7 e7 kham tit, lang5 soa3 boeh, kah hiah ho2-mia7”.  Khun-hong chin phaiN2-se3, eng7 bak8-boe2 khoaN3 Hui7-bi2, Hui7-bi2 thau5-khak chhih chhih, theh8 chhiu2 kin-a2 chhit bak8-sai2 sim chai khou2 lah.  Tang-si5-a2 ke-lai7 iau2 u7 chit8 e5 ai3-cheng5 e5 tui3-tek8.  Siu3-chhun thiau-ti5 kong2 “A-m2 mai3 koh kong2 noh!  Khah-theng5-a2 hai7 lang5 hou7 lang5 me7, lang5 teh hau2 lah”.  Lau2-sit8-kong2 Hui7-bi2 tiam3 hiah che7 be7 tiau5, i e5 ui7 be7 su chiam teh chhak8.  Chong2-si7 m7-kaN2 li7-sek8, koh bo5 loa7 ku2 tai7-ke chiah8 pa2.  Toa7 e5 chhi-chham2 kau3 lah.
Ta-ke pi7-pan7 hit-jit8 ai3 hau3 kong-ma2.  Ia7 tioh8 pai3 thiN-te7, in-ui7 tioh8 pai3 lai5 pou2 choe3 sin-niu5 e5 si5 bo5 pai3.  Ti-thau5 ngou2-seng long2 pai5 ho2, hiuN sio khi2--lai5 Ta-ke seng pai3.  Pai3 kin-a2-jit8 e5 ki7-sin5, au7 lai5 pai3 kong-ma2.  Pai3 toh-teng2 e5 koan-im hut8-chou2, sim2-mih8 ong5-ia5-kong ma2-chou2-po5, kui toh-teng2.  Ia7 u7 ou-bin7--e5, ia7 u7 ang5-bin7 e5, ia7 u7 peh8-bin7--e5.  Ia7 u7 hui5--e5, ia7 u7 chha5--e5, tiong-ng hit sian si7 gek8--e5.  Sin5-chu2-a2 kui toh teng2.  Ia7 u7 toa7-chek, hiuN-lou5, kim-tiaN2, kui7-tiam7, khiang khok, siuN7-poe long2 u7.  Si2 lah, Ta-ke pai3 ho2 chiu7 tu hou7 Khun-hong, Khun-hong khi2 thau5 m7-pai3.  Lau7-bu2 le2, khut, me7 kong2 phah-sng3 chi2-u7 thoan5 chit e5 hiuN-lou5-hiN7, beh lai5 lau5 ban7-se3 hiuN-ian, bo5 phah-sng3 khi3 hou7 loh8-kau3-po5 chhek-soe tioh8.  PiN3 bou2 seN--e5 bu5-sou2-put e5 phai2-oe7.  Koh hiah e5 kou-i5 ku7-kim ia7 me7 ia7 khou2-khng3 chiu7 chiap hiuN ia7 pai3.  Pai3-liau2 chiap hou7 Siu3-chhun.  Siu3-chhun khok8-lok8 chiu7 kui7 loh8 khi3, pai3 tit chin ho2-se3, sam-kui7 kau2 khau3-thau5, mui2 chit8-kui7, sam khau3-thau5, chiu7 koh peh khi2-lai5, hiuN siang-chhiu2 chhiaN2 koan5, bin7 ng3 kong-ma2 kong2-oe7, kiok-kiong ha7-pai3, chiu7 kui7 loh8 koh-chai3 sam khau3-thau5.  Na2-chun2 teh poaN-hi3 leh.  Kha-pou7 chhiu2-lou7 chin ho2-khoaN3.  Pai3 liau2 tioh8 Hui7-bi2.  Hui7-bi2 si2 to m7 chiap hiuN, kan-ta lau5 bak8-sai2.  In ta-ke khi3 kau3 bo5 ho2 kho2 jim2, kio3 Siu3-chhun khi3 giah8 tin-tiau5 lai5.  Tng cheng3-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, kong-ma2, sin5-hut8 e5 bin7-cheng5 tioh8 ka3 hou7 lang5 khoaN3, ut ho loh8 seng3.  Hui7-bi2 hou7 lang5 phah bo5 khui-siaN hau2, bin7 ng3-piah kui7 lok8 ki5-to2, ku3 in ta-ke phah.  U7 e5 kong2 ho2 lah noh8, seng-khu u7 sin leh.  Siu3-chhun tiam3 piN-a2 kong2 “Ho2-cheng2 m7-thng5, phaiN2-cheng2 m7-tng7, seN hit ho7 loh8-kau3-a2 kiaN2, goa7 sui2-ah!” Chit-ku3 oe7 Khun-hong thiaN-liau2 bo5 hoaN-hi2.  Khun-hong khoaN3-liau2 ia7 chin m7-kam, kui7 loh8 khi3 thoe3 Hui7-bi2 hou7 lau7-bu2 phah kui2-na7-e7.  Lau7-bu2 chiah pang3-chhiu2, koh tu hiuN lai5.  Khun-hong chiu7 an2-ni chin3-cheng5 ka7 i chiap8 hiuN lai5 the3-pai3.  Tui3 an2-ni chit8-tiuN5 e5 hong-pho chiah soah.
Hit-am3 Hui7-bi2 kui-mi5 bo5 khun3 kan-ta hau2, mng7 Khun-hong chiah-chai Siu3-chhun chiu7-si7 Khun-hong e5 bo5-ian5 sim-pu7-a2 bou2!  Kau3-taN iau2-boe7 ke3-chhut, chiu7-si7 koat-si2 beh kap i cheN Khun-hong e5 cheng5-tek8.  Kau3 chia chiah chai-khou2, siuN-ban7 lah.  Khun-hong tui3 to3 lai5 hou7 lau7-bu2 me7 chu7 an2-ni m7-bat koh khi3 le2-pai3.  Lang5 na7 mng7, Hui7-bi2 na7 kong2, i long2-si7 chhio3-chhio3 kong2, “Kham2--e5, chit8-si5-hong, eng3-kai sai2 chit8-si5 chun5.  Chit-si5 beh an2-choaN2 pi2 hit-si5.  Goa2 ia7 bo5 kap lin2 jip8-kau3 nia2 se2-le2 lah.” Ah!  Hui7-bi2 chai si2 lah.  Chiu7-si7 ti7 chia, siuN-ban7 lah.  Thong3-hoe2 tong-si5 bo5 thiaN lau7-pe7 e5 ui5-gian5, chit8 si3-lang5 si7 choe3 “Chhi3-a2-lai7 e5 pek-hap8-hoe” lah.
Pek-hap8-hoe, pek-hap8-hoe!
Li2 si7 peh8 koh sui2, phang koh toa7 lui2.
U7 soaN-teng2, u7 kheN-kok, u7 peN5-iuN5.  
Tak8-ui7 khui-khui khoah-khoah.  
U7 iong5-kong, u7 lou3-chui2.
Li2 thai2-m7 tiam3 hia khui, tiam3 hia sui2.
Thai2 kho2-sioh, li2 thai2 e7 chiah phaiN2-un7.
Phian-phian lai5 khui tiam3 che chhi3-a2-lai7.
Li2 kiam2 m7-chai si3-piN long2 si7 chhi3.  
Li2 loan2-jiok8 hou7 hong chhoe, 
Cheng5 ia7 chhi3, au7 ia7 chhi3.
Kau3-boe2 tioh8 kak-ngou7 oan5-choan5 hun2-chhui3.
Po2-siu2 li2 e5 kiat-pek8, kap phang-bi7.
Goan7 koat-sim hun3-tou3, bu5-ngou2, hi-seng.
Kau3-boe2 e5 seng3-li7 chiu7 kui ti7 li2.  
Ah!  Pek-hap8-hoe, kho2-lian5!  
Chhi3-a2-lai7 e5 pek-hap8-hoe!
Hui7-bi2 bak8-sai2 chhit-chhit leh, giah8 pit khi2 lai5 sia2 chit siu2 chek-kam2 e5 sin-sek chu7-iu5 si, chu7 an2-ni khia7 khi2-lai5, khi3 se2-bin7, oaN7-saN, tui3 chia-khi2 ban7-su7 chhui3-khi2-kin ka7-leh, chi2 u7 ki5-to2 i2-goa7 bo5-lou7.  Pa-kiat thun bak8-sai2, piau2-chhut un-sun5 chhio3-iong5 lai5 chiap ta-ke, chiap Siu3-chhun.  Ta-ke si7 bu5-sou2-put e5 khe2-cheh8.  Siu3-chhun chit8-bin7 chau-that Hui7-bi2, chit8-bin7 pa-kiat Khun-hong.  Hui7-bi2 seng-san2 e5 ki5 kau3 lah, kam2-sia7 Chu2 khoai3 pian7 chiu7 seN cha-bou2-kiaN2.  Na7-chhun2 gek8 e5 sui2, chin seng5 lau7-bu2 e5 bin7.  In a-ma2 chit8-ku3 chiu7 me7 kong2 seN kau3 hit ho7 cha-bou2 gin2-na2-kui2 bo5 lou7 eng7, chiu7 ka7 i ho7-mia5 choe3 “M7-tihN8-a2”.  Kho2-lian5 phah-sng2 Hui7-bi2 un-a2 siuN7 chit8 e5 ho2-mia5 beh ho7 soa3 bo5 chhai2-kang.  SeN hit kui2-jit8 tu2 Khun-hong ui7 kong-si bo2 lang5 m7-tihN8, lian5 kiaN2 bo5 choe7 tu2 chhut-si3 lang5 ia7 m7-tihN8.  Khun-hong to3--lai5 chai Hui7-bi2 khioh cha-bou2-kiaN2 ia7-si7 bo5 kau3-goa7 hoaN-hi2.  In-ui7 ni5-ki2 30 lah chiah kiN3 tioh8 chit e5 thau5-chiuN-a2 koh si7 cha-bou2--e5.  Chin loe2-chi3, ia7 chiu7 bo5 siuN7 beh ka7 i oaN7 mia5.  Na7-si7 Hui7-bi2 su-khia ka7 i ho7 choe3 “Hui7-chu5”（惠慈).  Am3-si5, bo5 lang5 ti7 sin-piN e5 si5 chiah ka7 i thau-kio3 “Hui7-chu5”.  Na7 ti7 A-nia2 e5 bin7-cheng5 chiu7 kio3 “M7-tihN8-a2”, ah!  Kho2-lian5, ka-ti7 seN-kiaN2, bo5 chai5-tiau7 kio3 kiaN2 eng7 sou2 ai3 ho7 e5 mia5.  Siu3-chhun seng7 chit8 e5 ki-hoe toa7 hian3 bi2-jin5-ke3.  Tu2-gu7 Khun-hong khi3 hou7 i leng2 tioh8.  Hui7-bi2 iu7 goeh8-lai7, eN-a2 hau2, chha2 be7 khun3-tit, Khun-hong chiu7 leng7-goa7 khi3 khun3 ti7 keh-piah pang5.  Hui7-bi2 goeh8-lai7 bo5 khi2-lai5, su7-su7 Siu3-chhun thoe3 su-hau7 Khun-hong.  Siu3-chhun pia3-miaN7 khoan2-thai7.  Kau3-boe2 lian5 am3-si5 to lai5 kap Khun-hong choe3-phoaN7, put-ti put-kak nng7-lang5 i2-keng seN-chhut ai2-mai7 e5 koan-he7 lah.  
16
Kau3 chia chham2-siong7 ka-chham2 lah.  Khun-hong phoa3-piN7 ho2, nng7 e5 hian2-jian5 chhoa7-chhut chhoa7-jip8.  Thiau3-bu2 thiaN, moa5-chhiok-tiuN5, tian7-iaN2-iN7, chhu3-chhu3 to u7 in nng7-e7 e5 kha-jiah.  Tui3-lang5 kai3-siau7 ia7-si7 Tan5 thai3-thai3.  Hui7-bi2 kap Siu3-chhun lai saN-pi2 Hui7-bi2 si7 sun5-liong5 chhin-chhiuN7 Kap.  Sui2 chhin-chhiuN7 Pek-hap8-hoe.  Siu3-chhun si7 iau-kiau to-thai3.  Seng-khu liu2-liah8, hu3-iu2 liu5-soaN3-heng5 e5 khiok-soaN3-bi2.  Bu2-i, ia7-le2-hok8 chheng7 khi2--lai5, chit8 e7 thiau3 oan2-jian5 Sian-lu2 ha7-hoan7 oan2-ju5 Tiap8-bu2 hoa-kan e5 khin-sang.  A-na2 to chu, chheng7 koan5-kia7-a e5 kiaN5-lou7 ngiu2-lai5 ngiu2-khi3, kap Khun-hong chhiu2 kau chhiu2 san3-pou7 ti7 kong-hng5 e5 chhiu7-kha.  Che7 loh8, kha khiau-khi2-lai5 chit8 chhiu2 pok-hun, chit8 chhiu2 khan Khun-hong, chit-khoan2 e5 the2-thai3 Hui7-bi2 si2 to2 choe3-be7 lai5.  An2-ni Siu3-chhun e5 khoan2 thang kong2 na2 siok8-gu2 kong2 “Than2-ki2, hou5-li5-chiaN” sui2 na2-chun2 Ia2-chhun-a2 hoe.  Hit e5 the2-thai3 phin2-chit, it-seng e5 sou3-iong2, sim-seng3, cheng-sin5, sou2-ai3 long2 bo5 sio-tang5.  Koe3-khi3 Khun-hong chiap Hui7-bi2 si7 cheng7, si7 ka-teng5-tek8, na2-chun2 siu-to7-iN7 e5 seng3-lu2.  Tai7-hong, keng3-khian5, thiam5-cheng7.  Chiap tioh8 Siu3-chhun si7 goa7-kau-heng5, thiau3-bu2, thiam2-mi7, sng2, chhio3 eng3 sia7-hoe7 e5 tiau5-liu5.  Khun-hong pan7-li2 su7-bu7 iu2-hong chiu7 seng-chin3 choe3 koan7-siaN5 hun kong-si e5 keng-li2.  Tu2-gu7 lau7-bu2 60 hoe3 e5 hi2-siu7, chiu7 siat-hoat beh ka7 lau7-bu2 choe3 seN-jit8.
Kong-jian5 hoat-piau2 ti7 hit-jit8 beh soa3 chiap Siu3-chhun khi2-lai5 choe3 se3-i5.  Siu3-chhun put-hok8 choe3 se3-i5.  I kong2 chu7-se3 chiu7 jip8-mng5, koh pi2 Hui7-bi2 khah che7 hoe3.  Tek-khak ai3 cheN Toa7-bou2 e5 beng5-hun7.  Hit-jit8 kau3, thai5-ti to2-iuN5, in-ui7 cheng5-pai2 chhiaN2 sin-niu5-chiu2 chhiaN2 bo5 seng5.  Chhoa7 Hui7-bi2 ti7 Su7-liong5 kiat-hun, bo5 to3-lai5 chhu3-nih chhiaN2 lang5-kheh.  Chit-pai2 lau7-bu2 60 hi2-siu7, ka-ti7 seng choe3 keng-li2.  Koh chhoa7 Siu3-chhun.  Lau7-bu2 hui-siong5 hoaN-hi2, chu2-tiuN toa7 chhiaN2 chit8--e5.  Tng chhiaN2 lang5-kheh e5 si5 kou-i5 ku7-kim7, chek-peh, chim2-m2 to long2 o-lo2 thin7 Siu3-chhun chin ho2, an2-ni chiah hap8-sek.
Sek8 au7 pai3 siu7 chit8-tui3 Sin-niu5 kiaN2-sai3 seng lai5 pai3.  Khun-hong, Siu3-chhun khok-lok8 chiu7 pai3 loh8 khi3.  Sit8-chai7 m7-si7 sin-niu5, tui3 Hui7-bi2 goeh8-lai7 in nng5 e5 chiu7 choe3 kian3-siau3 su7.  Koh ho2 kha-chhiu2 i2-keng u7 sin nng7 goeh8-jit8 lah.  Se3-siok8 tui3 che si7 chin peng5-siong5.  Au7-lai5 kio3 Hui7-bi2 pai3.  Hui7-bi2 tu5-khi3 kui7-loh8 ki5-to2 i2-goa7 m7-bat pai3 lang5, ia7 m7-bat pai3 ngou2-siong7.  I oa2-khi3 ia7 be7-hiau2 liam7 ho2-oe7, chi2-u7 kiaN5 keng3-le2, an2-ni kong2 be7 eng7-tit, ai3 kui7 loh8-khi3 chhiu2 kiok-kiong liam7 ho2-oe7 chiah e7 eng7-tit.  Thu5 chin ku2 cheng3-lang5 chin bian2-kiong2 i, kau3 au7-lai5 put-tek-i2 chiu7 pho7 se3-kiaN2 kui7 oai-oai bak8-chiu pang3-kheh ki5-to2.  Tai7-ke khoaN3 i u7 kui7 chiu7 ho2 lah.  Na7-si7 in ta-ke kau3 sek-au7, tai7-ke to3-khi3 liau2 chiu7 kio3 i lai5 mng7 kong2 tha-tu2-a2 an2-choaN2 m7-bian2 kui7 chiaN3-chiaN3?  An2-choaN2 kui7 oai-oai?  An2-choaN2 bo5 liam7 ho2-oe7?  An2-choaN2 liam7 Ia5-sou?  Oa2 lai5 gou7-kin-ke5 khiak8 kui2-na7 e7.  Bak8-chiu phoe5 koaN7 khi2 lai5 hiu3, toa7 thui2 choan7 kui2-na7-e7, le2 koh khut8.  Hit am3 Hui7-bi2 bo5 hau2 lah, ka-ti7 eng7 ioh8-iu5 ou-chheN e5 ui7 so-so leh.  Thau5-khak tiaN7 hou7 ta-ke khiak8, u7 si5 cheng2-cheng2 se-thau5 e7 thiaN3 chiu7 thau5-chang chhin3-chhai2 se-se leh, bak8-chiu phoe5, chhui3-phoe2 tiaN7 ou-chhiN, chhut-khi3 chin phaiN2 khoaN3, sou2-i2 ia7 han2-tit chhut-khi3.  Goeh8-lai7 lang5 ia7 bo5 chhiu3-chhai2--i, bo5 sim2-mih8 leng, gin2-na2 chhi7-liau2 siau-hoa3 put-liong5.  Thou2-oe7 kong2 tioh8-kau5, chin bai2, san2-san2, phoe5 leng7-leng7.  Ta-ke bo5 hoaN-hi2, lau7-pe7 ia7 m7-bat pho7.  U7 chit8-jit8 ta-ke kap Siu3-chhun chin ok, tng-tan2 Khun-hong bo5 ti7-teh.  Kong2 Hut8-chou2 kang3-chhiam, in khi3 thiu-chhiam, poah8-poe kong2 Siu3-chhun kai-chiam3 toa7-pang5, kio3 Hui7-bi2 tioh8 soa2 pang5 -keng, chiong toa7-pang5 niu7 i, kio3 i tioh8 poaN-khi phian-pang5.  Hui7-bi2 bo5 hiah khoai3 beh poaN, Khun-hong to3-lai5 kong2 hou7 Khun-hong thiaN, Khun-hong ia7 m7-kaN2 choe3 chu2, teN3 tiam7-tiam7.  Tui3 an2-ni Siu3-chhun na2 long7-koan5.  Khun-hong choe3 keng-li2 liau2-au7 chiu7 siong5-siong5 chhut-chhai khi3 Lam5-kiaN, Siong7-hai2, Hiong-kang2, Siu3-chhun tak8-ui7 toe3 kau3-tioh8.  Na7 to3-lai5 chiu7 be2 tan2-lou7 to3-lai5 hou7 lau7 ta-ke-a2.  Hui7-bi2 gin2-na2 na2 chhi7 na2 bai2, tu5-khi3 thak8 Seng3-keng ki5-to2 i2-goa7 bo5 sim2-mih8 thang siu7 an-ui3.  Khi2-thau5 lai5 bat khi3 le2-pai3, au7-lai5 ta-ke kim3 chin an5, m7-chun2 i chhut mng5 soa3 bo5 ki-hoe7 thang khi3 le2-pai3.  U7-si5 Kou-niu5, a2-si7 Bok8-su-niu5 lai5 sio-tham3, tng-bin7 hou7 in ta-ke siau-tok8.  Sit8-chai7 chin kho2-lin5.  Bo5 loa7-ku2 Siu3-chhun khioh gin2-na2 seN cha-pou-e5, choe3 chit8 e7 ang5 khi2--lai5, chiu7 ho7-choe3 Eng5-chong(榮宗).  Moa2-goeh8 chiu7 koaN2 Hui7-bi2 khi3 phian-pang5.  Tui3 hit-jit8 khi2 Hui7-bi2 chiu7 siu7 khoaN3 choe3 se3-i5 taN2-pan7.
Put-lun7 sim2-mih8 to su--lang5.  Ni5-cheh chhoe-koe2, pak8-chang3, pi7-pan7 seng-le2.  Liam7-keng kong3-khok, sio-hiuN poah8-poe.  Pan7 chho-toh, pan7 chhai3-toh, bo5 chit-hang7 e7 iaN5 Siu3-chhun.  Lang5-bin7 sek8, hong-liu5, poah8 moa5-chhiok i chit8-kha, thiau3-bu2 i chit8-kioh.  Kong2 kou2, tam7 hi3-bun5 ku3 li2 lai5, chiah8 hun lim-chiu2 tak8-hang7 e7.  Hui7-bi2 ne3, chi2-u7 liam7 Ia5-sou, e7 hiau2 toaN5-khim5, e7 hiau2 chhai5-hong5, ho2 phin2-heng7.  Su7-su7 to choe3 hong-boe2, chu7 an2-ni hou7 lang5 kim3 loh8 leng2-keng, khia7 choe3 chheN-chha5, chiuN2 seN-koaN2.  I e5 pang5-keng tiong7-hu chit8 kha-pou7 to m7-bat jip8-khi3.  Cheng5-au7, si3-piN chau2 bo5 lou7, kai-chai3 teng2-bin7 iau2 chit8-lou7, chi2-u7 bang7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 po2-iu7.  Kho2-lian5 ho7 put tan-heng5, sou2 thiaN3 e5 kiaN2 Hui7-chu5, m7-si7, sit8-chai7 si7 M7-tihN8-a2 tioh8-kau5 be7 ho2 tit8-tit8 hoa-khi3.  Lau7-pe7 u7 Eng5-chong hau7-siN pui5 kun3-kun3 chhio3 gi7-gi7 thang pho7.  Sim2-mih8 lang5 beh khoaN3 tioh8-kau5 e5 M7-tihN8-a2.  Na7-si7 Hui7-bi2 ui7 bo2-seng3-ai3, na2 kam-tit pang3 hou7 i si2.  Me5-jit8 chiau3-kou3 bak8-sai2 chun2 png7 thun.

I3-goa7 e5 ho2 siau-sit chiu7-si7 Khun-hong siu7 theh8-poat8 choe3 chong2 kong-si e5 Siong-li2(襄理).  Chu7 an2-ni kap Siu3-chhun kap se3-kiaN2 Eng5-chong chiu7 poaN-khi3 chong2 kong-si e5 sou2-chai7 te7 Hiong-kang2.  Lau7-bu2, Hui7-bi2 kap M7-tihN8-a2 hou7 lang5 pang3 tiam3 chhu3-nih.  Bo5 phah-sng3 in khi3 liau2 bo5 loa7-ku2 lau7-bu2 tioh8 thoa-sai2-lian5 e5 peN7.  Ti7 hia khun3, ti7 hia chiah8, ti7 hia pang3, pian3-sui7 be7-tin2 be7-tang7.  Hui7-bi2 chin7-sim chiau3-kou3, khin-siaN se3-soeh, tak8-hang7 un-jiu5 siong5-se3.  Khiok u7 kio3-chhui3 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 Sou3-lan5 ah, Bok8-ni7-ah, chong2-si7 in long2 tang2-hiaN2.  Khah kong2 ia7-si7 Hui7-bi2 lai5 pang-chan7 siang7 ho2.  Hu5-khi2, hu5-to2, oaN7-saN, oaN7 kha-peh8, pak8-kha, cheng2-thau5-a2 phang7-un5-un5-a2 chhit-hou7-ta sam2-hoan5, tng3-hun2, kha-peh8 chhiN-chhiN un5-un5-a2 pak8, sai2, jio7 un5-un5-a2 se2, un5-un5-a2 chhit.  Tak8 saN tng3 chhi7 png7 na2-chun2 teh chhi7 se3-kiaN2.  Siong5-siong5 chiah8 be7 tiau5-pak.  Gu5-leng hiam5 chhau3-hian3, Hui7-bi2 siong5-siong5 khek-liam2 hou7 se3-kiaN2 chiah8 e5 leng teN7 hou7 ta-ke-a2 chiah8.  Sia2 phoe hou7 Khun-hong, keh chin ku2 chiah to3-lai5 khoaN3.  Na2 un3 tau7-iu5 bo5 ke3-me5 choe3 i khi3.  Hoan-hu3 Siu3-chhun to3--lai5, Siu3-chhun bo5 siau3-siuN7.  I tiam3 hia thiau3-bu2, tian7-iaN2, moa5-chhiok, chhap li2 teh thoa-sai2-lian5, teh pak8-kha sam2-hoan2, tng3-hun2 chhau3 kiaN5-kiaN5.  Kau3 hit-si5 Ta-ke chiah chai ho2 phaiN2 lang5.  Hui7-bi2 siong5-siong5 kui7-loh8 ti7 bin5-chhng5 cheng5 chhut-siaN thoe3 ta-ke ki5-to2, thak8 Seng3-keng, kong2 to7-li2 hou7 i thiaN.  Chiah8 sim-pu7 e5 leng koan3-si3, Hui7-bi2 soa3 siong5-siong5 aN3 ti7 ta-ke e5 sin-piN eng7 leng hou7 ta-ke suh.  60 goa7 hoe3 lah, chit8 e7 loan2-jiok8 na2 gin2-na2 leh.  Siong5-siong5 tui3 Hui7-bi2 jin7 chho3.  Kong2 i eng2-koe3 m7-bat lang5, be5-sin3 ngou2-siong7.  U7 si5 Hui7-bi2 ia7 ho2-le2-a2 ka7 i pho7 chhut lai5 thiaN mng5-khau2 ni-chiN5 e5 an-lok8-i2 hou7 i chio3 jit8-thau5 khoaN3 hoe-bak8.  An2-ni chiok-chiok ni5 goa7 ku2 Siu3-chhun m7-bat tah8-kha kau3, Khun-hong to3-lai5 khoaN3 nng7-choa7 long2 bo5 keh-me5.  Sit8-chai7 chin liau2-jian5.
U7 chit8 jit8 ta-ke hut-jian5 ka7 Hui7-bi2 kong2 cha-hng goa2 khun3-khi3 e5 si5 u7 nng7 e5 lang5 chheng7 peh8-saN hoat-sit8 lai5 chhoa7 goa2 khi3.  Kau3 chit8 cho7 siaN5, siaN5-mng5 chin-chu, siaN5-chhiuN5 phek-gek8, lai7-bin7 chin kng.  Goa2 chin ai3 jip8-khi3, na7-si7 u7 chit8 e5 lau7 a-peh chhui3-chhiu3 tng5-tng5 ti7 hia kou3-mng5.  M7 hou7 goa2 jip8-khi3, kong2 goa2 e5 saN che7-che7 kiaN-lang5, bo5 siu7 IuN5-ko e5 po2-huih se2-chheng, koh bo5 sin3-giong2 e5 bun5-pin5, ka7 goa2 koaN2 to3 chhut--lai5, chin phah-sng2.  Tu2 teh tiu-tu5 e5 si5 u7 chit8-ui7 chin chu5-siong5, bin7 chhio3-iong5, thau5 ti3 chhi3-a2 e5 bian2-liu5, chhiu2 u7 teng-jiah e5 lang5, hit lang5 chheng7 peh8-saN kui-sin hoat-kng.  Goa2 ti7 se3-kan m7-bat khoaN3 an2-ni e5 lang5, ka7 goa2 kong2 “Cha-bou2 kiaN2 ah, li2 thang an-sim to3-tng2-khi3, chin7 it-chhe3 e5 gi7 chiah koh lai5, Goa2 chiu7 chiap-lap8 li2 chiu7-kin7 Goa2.  Ho7 Goa2 sou2 ti7-teh e5 ui7 li2 ia7 beh ti7 hia, thang kap Goa2 saN-kap tit eng5-kng.” Chin hoaN-hi2, ia7 chin phah-sng2, m7-bat i3-su3 chiu7 chhiN2 khi2-lai5.  Hui7-bi2 thiaN liau2 toa7 hoaN-hi2.  Ka7 i kong2 kap li2 kong2 oe7 e5 lang5 chiu7-si7 Kiu3-chu2 Ia5-sou.  Ta-ke kong2 taN goa2 tioh8 chaiN2-iuN7?  Hui7-bi2 ka7 i kong2 li2 tioh8 sin3, ia7 beh thoe3 i chhiaN2 Bok8-su lai5 ka7 i kiaN5 se2-le2.  Ta-ke chin hoaN-hi2 sin3 Ia5-sou, ia7 kiu5 Chu2 sia3-bian2 i it-chhe3 koe3-khi3 e5 choe7, chiu7 tui3 Ng5 Bok8-su nia2 se2-le2.  Ng5 Bok8-su kau3 i e5 tau, hit-jit8 u7 Kou-niu5, Bok8-su, che7-che7 chi2-moai7 lai5 le2-pai3, ti7 ka-teng5 choe3-hoe2 siu2 Chu2 e5 seng3-chhan.  Chhu3-piN lin5-iu7 tai7-ke chin ki5-koai3.  Ia7 tong-tiuN5 ui5-gian5 i na7 si2 tioh8 choe3 Ki-tok-kau3 sek.  Ia7 thiaN-nih e5 ngou2-siong7 tioh8 chin7 tu5.  Koa3-khi2 chap8-tiau5-kai3 piau2-beng5 choe3 sin3 Siong7-te3 Ki-tok-kau3 e5 ka-teng5.  An2-ni liau2-au7 koh oah8 chiaN5 le2-pai3 chiah si2.  Ti7 hit le2-pai3-lai7 i chin peng5-an, put-lun7 sim2-mih8 lang5 lai5 khoaN3 i, kou-i5, ku7-kim7, chek-peh, chim2-m2 lai5 i to kong2 Ia5-sou hou7 lang5 thiaN.  Tai7-ke chin ki5-koai3, chong2-si7 thiaN i e5 sou2 kong2 chin sit8, ia7 khoaN3 Hui7-bi2 e5 iu2-hau3 tai7-ke chin kam2-kek.  Ki5-tiong ia7 u7 lang5 siuN7 kong2 tioh8 lai5 thiaN to7-li2 khah ho2.  ChiaN5 le2-pai3 au7 chiu7 koe3-sin.  Kong3-tian7 hou7 Khun-hong, Khun-hong tu2 khi3 chhut-chhai, kau3 in to3-lai5 to i2-keng chiau3 Ki-tok-kau3 sek jip8-bok8 liau2.  Chu7 an2-ni chhiaN2 ka7 i taN2-thang2 lai5 tan2 Khun-hong in to3-lai5.  To3--lai5 chiu7 siat-hoat beh chong3-sek.  Hui7-bi2 chu2-tiuN Ki-tok-kau3-sek, Siu3-chhun chu2-tiuN Hut8-kau3-sek, koh tioh8 kio3 chhai3-kou, hoe5-siuN7 lai5 liam7-keng.  Chit8 e5 chu2-tiuN chit8 khoan2.  Au7-lai5 tai7-ke chun-tiong7 i pun2-lang5 e5 ui5-gian5, chiu7 chiau3 Ki-tok-kau3 sek, hit-jit8 che7-che7 hoe7-iu2, kap Thoan5-kau3-chia2, Soan-kau3-su lai5 sang3-chong3.  Hui7-bi2 in chhu3 Siu2-jin5, A-so2, Ong5 Bok8-su ia7 long2 lai5.  Chu7 Hui7-bi2 lai5 Khun-hong in tau kin-a2-jit8 siang7 seng3-li7, siang7 eng5-kng, chong2-si7 Siu3-chhun ia7 m7-jin7 su.  ChiN5 u7, i ia7 khi3 kat-toaN5 ti7 piN-ah, tiam3 hia liam7-keng lai5 kap Hui7-bi2 nau7.  Pan2 kng chhut--lai5 Hui7-bi2 be7 hiau2-khau3, chi2-u7 siong-sim lau5 bak8-sai2.  Siu3-chhun khau3 kau3 i-i o-o, li-li lo-lo, “Sim-koaN-a2 goa2 bo2 o-oe3!  Kin-a2-jit8 kui-sim choe3 li2 khi3, ia7 bo5 thang hou7 goa2 kiN3 chit8 bin7, goa2 sim-koaN goa2 bo2 o-oe3!” Chiok peh8-chhat8, peN7 ni5 goa7 ku2, thoa-sai2-lian5 to2 ti7 chhng5-nih, phoe tian7-po3 tit8 tui, lian5 tham3-thau5 to m7-kaN2.  TaN khau3 kau3 toa7-siaN ia2-au5, phiN7 chhui3-noa7 khok8-khok8 tih.  Sim2-mih8 thau5-chhit, sam-chhit, chu7-jian5 choe3 cha-bou2 kiaN2 ia7 lang7-lau5.  Tai7-ke kong2 Siu3-chhun khah iu2-hau3.  
17
Chong3-sek liau2 it-toaN7-lok8 Khun-hong kap Siu3-chhun in chiu7 koh khi3 Hiong-kang2.  Chit8-cho7 chhu3 hiah toa7, cha2 ta-koaN choe3 koaN, A-kong si7 ki2-jin5, thau5-cheng5 ki5-koaN au7-piah hoe-hng5.  Ti5-teng5 chui2-koh koe2-chi2-hng5 chin khui-khoah.  Chi2-u7 tiam3 Hui7-bi2 kap se3-kiaN2 M7-tihN8-a2, ki5-u5 kio3-chhui3 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 Sou3-lan5 ah, Bak8-ni7-ah, kap chit8 e5 tng5-kang-a2 peh8-tit8 peh8-tit8, lang5 long2 kio3-i “Toa7-tai.” Sou3-lan5-ah si7 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2 in hia kah lai5 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2, u7 sin3 Ia5-sou.  Kai-chai3 chit e5 chin thang choe3 Hui7-bi2 e5 an-ui3.  Siong5-siong5 choe3-hoe2 gim5-si, thak8 Seng3-keng, choe3-hoe2 ki5-to2 saN an-ui3.  Khun-hong in khi3 bo5 loa7 ku2 M7-tihN8-a2 chiu7 tng2 koh-khah m7-ho2, in-ui7 sin-the2 loan2-jiok8 koh hou7 lang5 oe3 tioh8 chhut-phiah8, koh hou7 leng2 tioh8 soa3 piN3 kip-seng3 hi3-iam7, nng7-saN jit8 chiu7 si2-khi3.  Kong3-tian7 hou7 Khun-hong, Khun-hong ia7 bo5 to3--lai5.  Tai7-khai3 si7 siuN7 kong2 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 kin-tu2 to M7-tihN8-a2 chu7 an2-ni si2-si2-tiau7 khah tit8.  Na7-si7 tui3 ti7 Hui7-bi2 si7 i5-it e5 ng-bang7.  Tiong7-hu hou7 lang5 chiam3-khi3, chiuN2 seN-koaN2 u7 ang na2 bo5 ang.  Lang5 u7 hau7-siN ang5 tiam2-tiam2, lan2 lian5 chit e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 to ki be7 tiau5.  SiuN7 liau2 chin chham2-chheh, u7 si5 chin loe2-chi3 soa3 giau5-gi5 Siong7-te3 hiat-kak i.
U7 chit8 cha2-khi2 kap Sou3-lan5-ah thau3-cha2 khi3-lai5 choe3-hoe2 thak8 Seng3-keng ki5-to2.  Thak8 tioh8 kui2 na7 ui7 Seng3-keng put-chi2 siu7 an-ui3.  Thak8 kong2 
“KhoaN3 ah!  Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 m7-si7 te2, boe7-oe7 chin2-kiu3, hi7-khang m7-si7 tang7, boe7-oe7 thiaN”(I2-sai3-a 59:1).

“U7 Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-te3 choe3 i e5 pang-chan7.  Ng3-bang7 i e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5, chit ho7 lang5 u7 hok-khi3.” (Si-phian 146:5).
“Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bak8-chiu khoaN3 keng3-ui3 I e5 lang5, khoaN3 ng3-bang7 I e5 chu5-ai3 e5 lang5.  Beh kiu3 in e5 seN3-mia7 thoat-li7 si2-bo5.  Po2-chun5 in e5 oah8-mia7 ti7 ki-hng e5 si5.” (Si-phian 33:18-19).
“Goa2 koat-toan3 bo5 pang3-sak li2, koat-toan3 bo5 li7-khui li2.  Sou2-i2 lan2 thang ho2-taN2 kong2 “Chu2 chiu7-si7 pang-chan7 goa2 e5, goa2 bo5 beh kiaN-hiaN5, Lang5 beh siaN2 hoat-tit goa2 ta-oa5”(Hi-pek-lai5 13:5-6).
“Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 goa2 e5 khui3-lat8, iah8-si7 goa2 e5 tin5-pai5.  Goa2 e5 sim oa2-kho3 I, goa2 chiu7 tit-tioh8 pang-chan7.  Sou2-i2 goa2 e5 sim toa7 hoaN-hi2; goa2 beh eng7 goa2 e5 si2-koa o-lo2 I.”(Si-phian 28:7).
“In-ui7 Li2 beh su3-hok hou7 gi7-lang5; Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 beh eng7 un-hui7, chhin-chhiuN7 tin5-pai5, si3-bin7 ui5-i”(Si-phian 5:12).
“I bo5 beh hou7 li2 e5 kha io5-choah; Po2-siu2 li2-e5 tek-khak bo5 tuh-bin5.  KhoaN3 ah!  po2-siu2 I2-sek-liat8 e5, ia7 bo5 tuh-bin5, ia7 bo5 khun3-khi3.  Po2-siu2 li2--e5 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 li2 e5 chiaN3-peng5 choe3 li2 e5 im3-ng2.  Ia5-ho5-hoa beh po2-siu2 li2, bian2-siu7 it-chhe3 e5 chai-hai7; I beh po2-siu2 li2 e5 seN3-mia7.  Li2 chhut, li2 jip8, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh po2-siu2 li2, tui3 chit si5 tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2.”(Si-phian 121:3-5, 7-8).

“Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa si7 kou3-siu2 phu5-to5-hng5--e5, Goa2 si5-khek koan3-ak i, me5-jit8 kou3-siu2 i, bian2-tit lang5 sun2-hai7 i.  Chiong-lai5 Nga2-kok beh teng3 i e5 kun, I2-sek-liat8 beh hoat-ge5 khui-hoe; in e5 ke2-chi2 beh chhiong-moa2 se3-kai3”(I2-sai3-a 27:3,6).
“Chu2 beh kiu3 goa2 thoa-li7 long2-chong2 e5 phaiN2-tai7, ia7 beh kiu3 goa2 jip8 ti7 I thiN-nih e5 kok, goan7 eng5-kng kui I kau3 tai7-tai7 bo5 chin7.  A3-beng7”(2 The5-mou5-thai3 3:18).
Hui7-bi2 kap Sou3-lan5 thak8 chiah e5 seng3-keng tit-tioh8 toa7 an-ui3.  Moa2-sim hoaN-hi2 kau3 lau5 bak8-sai2 kam2-sia7 Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 e5 thiaN3-thang3 chiau3-kou3.  Koh hoe5-ek i kiu3 i e5 ta-ke, khah iaN5 Mou5-kui2 lai5 eng5-kng Siong7-te3 e5 keng-giam7, chiu7 na2 chong3-taN2.  Nng7 e5 khi2-lai5 bak8-sai2 chhit-chhit leh, koh chit8-pai2 sin e5 koat-sim beh kap Mou5-kui2 choe7-ok chian3 kau3 tauh-ti2.  Siu3-chhun i ia7 chiu3-choa7 beh kap Hui7-bi2 chian3 kau3 tauh-ti2.  Chiau3-khoaN3 i i2-keng khah-iaN5, ang hou7 i chiam-khi3, seN hau7-siN chin ang5-tiam2, siong-li2 e5 thai3-thai3.  Hui7-bi2 khah-su ang hou7 lang5 chiam3-khi3, chiuN2 seN-koaN2, kiaN2 si2-khi3.  Chi2 u7 kiu3 ta-ke e5 leng5-hun5, che Siu3-chhun chin khoaN3-khin, cheN chit8 e5 thoa-sai2-lian5, ka7 lang5 se2-kha, pak8-kha chhau3 kia5-kia5--e5 khi3 hok8-sai7, cheN chit8 e5 si2 lang5 bo5 gau5.  It-khai3 long2 Siu3-chhun chhong3, tai7-ke ma7-si7 kong2 Siu3-chhun khah iu2-hau3.  Sou2-i2 tui3 Siu3-chhun e5 bak8-chiu lai5 khoaN3 Hui7-bi2 si7 put-tiong3-iong7 kin2-si2 kin2 ho2.
U7 chit8-jit8 m7-chai khi3 hou7 sim2-mih8 sin5 kam2-tioh8, Khun-hong siuN7 kong2 chhu3-nih kang-san hiah-toa7 kan-ta pang3-hou7 Hui7-bi2 chit8 e5 lang5 ti7 chhu3-nih bo5 i3-su3, chiu7 koat-jian5 si5-the3 siong-li2 to3--lai5.  Tui3 an2-ni Siu3-chhun kap Eng5-chong ia7 long2 to3-lai5.  An2-ni Hui7-bi2 iu7-si7 Siu3-chhun e5 gan2-tiong-teng.  Khun-hong to3--lai5 bo5 sou2 su7-su7, chia hia thit-tho5, lim hoa7, put-ti put-kak soa3 khi3 Sai3-hoa-lau5 chhap tioh8 chit8 e5 hoe-ki  kio3-choe3 Bi2-chu.  Sit8-chai7 u7 sui2 kin-ni5 19 hoe3.  Na2-chun2 hoe ham5-m5 tu2-a2 khui.  Liu2-hioh8-bai5, eng-ko phiN7, tai7-hi5 chhui3, sia7-liu5 khi2, bak8-chiu teng5-sun5, bak8-chiah mng5 tng5-tng5.  Bin7-bah hun2-peh8, chhio3 tioh8 siang-peng5 chiu2-khut-a2 chin sui2.  Heng koan5, io se3, kha-chhng-tau2 toa7 e5.  Chheng7 khi2 koan5-kiah8-a2-e5 kiaN5-lou7 e5 khoan2, m7-si7 Hui7-bi2, Siu3-chhun sou2 toe3 e7 tioh8.  In nng7 e5 bat seN-kiaN2 lah, na2-li2 tu3 Bi2-chu e7 tiau5.  Khun-hong goan5-lai5 tui3 hong3-su3 i2-au7 chiu7 piN3 choe3 chhai2-hoe-phang chit8 e7 khoaN3 tioh8 noa7 lau5 sou3-chap8-tng7.  Chek-khek pau-chhi7, Bi2-chu ia7 tan2 bo5 chit ho7 khoeh, chiu7 phoe5-si2 thiam2-mi7 kau-tiN5.  Tu2-tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 ti-tu tiN5 hou-sin5 an2-ni.  Chit8 e7 toa3-me5 lian5-lian5 kui2 na7 me5 ia7 m7-chai thang to3-khi3.  Siu3-chhun e7 si2 e7 oah8, thong siaN5 jiok thau3-thau3.  Chu3-si2 khi3 hou7 i chhoe7 tioh8 ti7 Sai3-hoa-lau5.  Tai7-nau7 Sai3-hoa-lau5 be7 tit i seN-si2, ian2 chhut chit8-tiuN5 m7-si7 kau5 ka7-kau5, si7 hoa-tou3-hoa e5 hi3-kek.  Chu5-jian5 lau5-chu2 ui7 Bi2-chu, sou2-i2 Siu3-chhun ke-soe bin7 hou7 Bi2-chu jiau3 kui2-na7 khang.  Tng loan7 e5 si5 Khun-hong choe3 i ho2-lang5-a2 bo5 ti7-tai7 liu tui3 au7 boe2 mng5 chhut-khi3.  Siu3-chhun chiok m7-goan7, sui2-bin7 khi3 hou7 Bi2-chu jiau3 kui2-na7 khang tek-khak siuN7 beh po3-siu5.  Kau3-chia Siu3-chhun chha Khun-hong chit8-hoe3 i2-keng 31 lah, khah gau5 chng to m7-tat8-tioh8 Bi2-chu 19 hoe3 e5 sui2.  Hui7-bi2 to bian2 kong2 kin-ni5 ia7 26 hoe3 lah, kiaN2 si2, sim chhau-hoan5, saN e5 tiong-kan khoaN3 liau2 i siang7 lau7, koh keng3-khian5, ti-chiok, siu2-ki2, bo5 siuN7 beh kap lang5 cheN.  Chit pai2 khah u7 ki-hoe7 thang khi3 le2-pai3, kap Sou3-lan5 khi3 tau3 pang-chan7 kau3-hoe7.  ToaN5-khim5, ka3 Chu2-jit8-oh8, tau3 sun5 chi2-moai7, choe3 hu7-jin5-hoe7 chu2-li2.  Tui3 an2-ni Hui7-bi2 sim na2 khiN5-tiau5 ti7 Chu2.  Ta-ke si2 lah, Khun-hong kou3 hong lu2-sek, bo5 koan2--i.  I jiat8-sim keng3-pai3 Siong7-te3, ui7 Chu2 choe3 kang hong7-su7 kau3-hoe7.  Sou2 khoa3-lu7 e5 chiu7-si7 me5-jit8 ui7 tiong7-hu ki5-to2 ng3-bang7 tiong7-hu u7 hoan2-hoe2 e5 jit8-chi2.  Na7-si7 Khun-hong taN si7 chap8-lou7 chng5, chiu2, sek, ma5-chhiok, tit8-tit8 tui7-loh8, thiau3-bu2, hi3-iN7 si7 i e5 khi3-chhu3, kau3-hoe7, Siong7-te3 taN I m7-bat lah.
Siu3-chhun khoaN3 Khun-hong be5 Bi2-chu, phoat-hu7 ok-tok8 sim, ke3 chiu7 seN-chhut--lai5.  SiuN7 chhut “Hap8-kong pho3 Cho5”(Chiu7-si7 chiong-ke3 chiu7-ke3, Se Siok Khong-beng5 sang3 Lau5-pi7 khi3 kap Tong Gou5 Sun-khoan5 e5 sio2-moai7 seng5-chhin, an2-ni kap Sun-khoan5 lian5-beng5 lai5 phoa3 Pak Gui7 Cho5 Chho3.  Ke3 i2-keng tiaN7-tioh8, chiu7 khng3 Khun-hong chhoa7 Bi2-chu choe3 te7 2 ho7 i5-thai3-thai3, Khun-hong chiok hoaN-hi2, o-lo2 Siu3-chhun bat-su7, sit8-chai7 bat su7.  TiaN7 chhut-khi3 chhai3-tiam3 loan7 bo5 the2-thong2 kian3-siau3, koh long7-hui3, na7 oe3 tok8 to3--lai5 tian-to3 si2, m7-tat8-tioh8 chhoa7 jip8--lai5 iau2 khah ho2-mia5.  Hoe7-goa7 e5 lang5 4 ho7, 5 ho7 i5-thai3-thai3 ma7 u7, te7 2 ho7, te7 3 ho7 bo5 hi-han2, chiu7 chhoa7 jip8--lai5.  Chhoa7--lai5 Siu3-chhun chiu7 ka3 Bi2-chu ju5-chhu2 ju5-chhu2 eng7 ke3-chhek lai5 hai7 Hui7-bi2.  Khun-hong, Siu3-chhun, Bi2-chu saN e5 siang7 pang5 siang7 chhng5 chin chhin.  Hui7-bi2 kio3 Sou3-lan5-e5 lai5 choe3 phoaN7, chin che7 ni5 to si7 an2-ni ka-ti7 jin7-hun7.  Chit8 pai2 khe2-cheh8 kau3 m7-chun2 i siang7-toh chiah8 png7.  In saN e5 kun2 hoa7-hoa7 lim-chiu2, toa7-hi5 toa7-bah chiah8 lim.  Chhai3-boe2-a2 Hui7-bi2, Sou3-lan5, kap iau2 chit8 e5 kio3-chhui3 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 Bak8-ni7-ah choe3-hoe2 chiah8.  Bak8-ni7-ah bo5 sin3 Chu2, khoaN3 Siu3-chhun khah ang5, i oa2 Siu3-chhun.  TiaN7-tiaN7 tui3 Siu3-chhun, Bi2-chu oh8 oe7.  Khi3 sun5 chi2-moai7, tau3 choe3 kau3-hoe7 e5 kang, kong2 si7 lou5-moa5 cha-bou2 la7-kha, gau5 koe3-ke khi3 thop8-oe7.  Siu3-chhun, Bi2-chu chiu7 giah8 chau3-pan2 tit8 chau3.  Khun-hong chiu7 siau2-sin5-khi3 khi2 chiu7 phah.  U7 si5 saN e5 chiah8-png7 kio3 i tiam3 toh piN hia hoat8 kui7, kong2 i la7-kha gau5 koe3-ke.  Siu3-chhun ka7 i tim3 bah-kut.  Kho2-lian5 ah!  Hui7-bi2 sim-lai7 chu7-hin7 chin-chiaN3 si7 Chhi3-a2-lai7 e5 pek-hap8-hoe.  Ta-ke khou2-tok8, se3-i5 ia7 bou5-hai7, tiong7-hu ia7 bo5 khoaN3-kou3, kiaN2 ia7 si2.  Tui3 hia khi2 m7-chun2 i koh chhut-khi3, kong2 i si7 khi3 koaN7-oe7, koe3-ke, bo5 cheng3-keng.  U7-si5 lian5 le2-pai3-jit8 to be7-tit chhut-sek8.
U7 chit8 am3 goeh8 am3-mi5, in saN e5 chhoa7 chhut-khi3 Sai3-hoa-lau5, khi3 kap lang5 chheng-siau3 sng3 hoa-tai7(花 代) , chiu7-si7 siok8 Bi2-chu e5 sin-ke3, ti7 hia soa3 hou7 lang5 chhiaN2.  Thau5-ke chhio3 gi7-gi7 pan7 chit8 toh khiau-khiau, kho2-sioh hit am3 Khun-hong lioh-a2 kam2-tioh8 bo5 sim2-mih8 kaN2 lim chiu2, chiah lim nng7 koan3 Beh8-a2-chiu2 na7-tiaN7.  Na7-si7 peng5-si5 chit8 taN2 bo5 lun2--i, Ui-suh-kih, but8-lan5-ti5 koan3-goa7 ia7-si7 boe7 chui3, chheng-chiu2 lim-tit kui2-na7 koan3.  Na7-si7 nng7 e5 bou2 ti7 sin-piN, koh si7 sng3 u7 tioh8 siaN5-lai7 e5 bi2-jin5, chiu7 kek an2-ni khong-khong hou7 nng7 e5 se3-i5-a2 chit8 e5 chhah chit8 peng5 ian7-lou7 san3-pou7 to3--lai5.  MoaN nng7 e5 se3-i5 teh kiaN5 iu5-goan5 tui3 toa7-lou7 phaiN2-se3, tui3 au7-boe2 lou7, tui3 in au7-hoe-hng5 jip8--lai5.  ThiaN lang5 ti7 au7-hoe-hng5 e5 lian5-hoe-ti5 piN teh khau3.  SaN e5 chiu7 houN3 ki5-sim kiaN5 tui3 hia khi3, koh si7 cha-bou2-lang5 siaN, Khun-hong sio2-khoa2 chui3-se3, chui3-se3, be7 jin7-tit siaN.  Siu3-chhun chit8 e7 chiu7 chai si7 Hui7-bi2 e5 siaN, chiu7 thoa in tui3 hia khi3.  Tu2-tu2 si7 Hui7-bi2 chio Sou3-lan5 khi3 lian5-hoe-ti5 piN ki5-to2.  Sou3-lan5 khoaN3 lang5 lai5 kin2 chau2 khi3 bih, in long2 m7-chai.  Chhun Hui7-bi2 ti7 hia, in kiaN5 oa2--lai5, Hui7-bi2 tui3 Khun-hong e5 kha ka7 i lam2-leh tit8-tit8 khau3.  In-ui7 siuN7 tioh8 chheng-lian5 tong-si5 e5 thiaN3-cheng5, kin-a2-jit8 hou7 tiong7-hu hiat-kak8 e5 chhi-chham2, khau3 kau3 be7 tng2 siaN.  Khun-hong toa7-siaN chhoh phaiN2-chhui3, soa3 kong2 hou7 i khau3-kau3 soe khi3.  Hui7-bi2 in kong2 “A hu ah!  Li2 kiam2 thang hiah8 nge7-sim kiam2 long2 be7 ki3-tit cha2-si5 e5 ai3-cheng5.” Khun-hong kong2 “Ai3-cheng5, na2 teh ai3-cheng5 leh, beh si2, si2 lou7-khi3, m7-bian2 teh koh kau-tiN5.” Me7 khah kin2, a2-si7 that-khi3 khah kin2, sun7 me7 e5 se3 chu7 an2-ni ka7 i that-khi3.  Hui7-bi2 chu7 an2-ni tiam7-tiam7.  Goan5-lai5 hit-si5 Hui7-bi2 si7 kui7 ti7 ti5-piN e5 chit8 liap8 toa7 chioh8-thau5 piN, phak ti7 chioh8-thau5 teh ki5-to2.  Hou7 i cham3 chit8 e7 tu2 tng3-lap-che7, koh chit8 e7 chu7 an2-ni lian3 loh8-khi3.  Ti5 chin chhim, chui2 m7-bat ta.  
18
Hui7-bi2 e5 it-seng sit8-chai7 chin kau3 kho2-lin5.  Bo5 thiaN lau7-pe7 e5 ui5-gian5, hou7 cheng5-si sou2 tiN5, kau3 chia sit8-chai7 hoan2-hoe2 chin ti5.  Thau5-khak tiaN7 chah8 gou7-kin-ke5, hun-chhoe-thau5.  Bak8-chiu-phoe5, chhui3-phoe2, toa7-thui2 tiaN7 hou7 lang5 liam3.  Tin5-tiau5, koaiN2-a2-thau5, ta-ke phah, tiong7-hu phah.  Se3-i5 tim3 bah-kut, bak8-he bak8-gin5, kiaN2 si2 tiong7-ku m7-tihN8.  Kin-tu2 oah8 leh ia7 si7 khou2.
Khun-hong thiaN chui2-siaN, thom5-lom5 chit-siaN aih8 chit8 e7 chu7 an2-ni tiam7-tiam7 chai phaiN2-tai7 lah.  Tioh8 kiaN kin2 hoah kiu3 lang5, si3-piN cheng7 chauh-chauh, am3-bin7-bong.  AN3 loh8 khi3 sa, sa bou5.  Siu3-chhun ke2 u7 sim, ke2 u7 i3, tit8-tit8 ka7 i kong2 “Mai3-noh, koaN5-koaN5--lang5, li2 koh lim-chiu2, ia7 hou7 kam2 tioh8 leh.  Mai3 bak-chui2 lah, na2 chun2 li2 kong2--e5, si2 lou7-khi3 mai3 teh kau-tiN5.  Ka7 i chun2 choe3 chu7-sat thiau3-chui2, kin-tu2 ia7 bo5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3.  Si2 to si2-lah, kin-tu2 bin5-a2-chai3 chiah lai5 kou ia7-si7 sio-siang7.” Chong2-si7 Khun-hong kui2-hun u7 liong5-sim, to3-khi3 kin2 hoah tng5-kang Toa7-tai, kap nng7 e5 kio3-chhui3 e chha-bou2 gin2-na2 beh khi3 tau3 kou.  Kau3 chhu3 mng5 iam2 leh bo5 poaN3 lang5 ti7-teh.  Bio7-khau2 teh choe3 toa7-hi3, tai7-ke khi3 khoaN3 hi3.  Khun-hong ka-ti7 giah8 chit8-ki tek-ko khi3 lian5-hoe-ti5 tit8 la7, tit8-tit8 kio3 Hui7-bi2.  Bo5 siaN bo5 soeh, Siu3-chhun kap Bi2-chu choe3 in khun3, m7 chhap i.  M7-na7 m7 chhap si7 tian-to3 hoaN-hi2.  Sim-lai7 siuN7 kong2 gan2-tiong-teng tu5 khi3 lah.
Hui7-bi2 na2-li2 tu3 lang5 e7 tiau5.  Chit8 e5 si7 na2-chun2 keng-koe3 ban7-li2 e5 chian3-tiuN5, leng5-cheng koan3-chian3 cheng5-tiuN5 e5 lau7 chian3-su7 hou5-li5-bu2 Siu3-chhun.  Chit8 e5 si7 Sai3-hoa-lau5 e5 iau-ki .  Sim2-mih8 khoan2 e5 thiam2-mi7 im5-loan7 e5 the2-thai3, si7 iu2 sou2 koan3-si3, si7 chit8-lui2 chhou-hong3 e5 tho5-hoa.  Hui7-bi2 hou7 lang5 me7 m7-kaN2 to3 me7 lang5, nng2-thou5 chhim kut8, kio3 hoat8-kui7 chiu7 hoat8-kui7, kui7-loh8 chong2-si7 ki5-to2, ki5-to2 bak8-chiu kheh-kheh, kiong2-chhiu2 aN3-thau5, tu2 hou7 lang5 tim3 ke-kut, bah-kut.  Na7 siat-su2 bat sio2-khoa2 in3--lang5, chiu7 nng7 e5 khiN5 oa2 lai5 phah chit8 e5, Khun-hong teN3 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3.  U7 si5 Sou3-lan5 khoaN3 liau2 be7 khat-tit oa2 lai5 ui7, kau3 boe2 Sou3-lan5 si7 tho2 phoe5-thiaN3.  Sou2-i2 su7-su7 niu7, na7 phah chiaN3-peng5, oat8 to3-peng5 soa3 hou7 lang5 phah khah tit8.
Siu3-chhun khoaN3 gan2-tiong-teng, chhau3 lang5, si2 lah, chin tek-i3.  Chu7-jian5 cheng3-sek toa7-bou2, Bi2-chu se3-i5.  Bi2-chu to3-boe2 lai5, ni5-hoe3 chio2, koan2 tit koe3-koe3.  Chhoe7 Hui7-bi2 kau3 keh-jit8 ia7 si7 chhoe7 bo5.  Tong5-si5 Sou3-lan5 ia7 sit-chong, put-tit khi3-hiong3.  Chit-chan5 su7 bo5 kha bo5 sit8, chu7-jian5 e7 chau2 e7 poe, keh nng7 jit8 sin-bun5 chin toa7 ji7.  Te5-bak8 si7 sia2 “Chiang-chiu koan7-siaN5 Lian5-hoe-ti5 su7-kiaN7.” Loe7-iong5 sou2 sia2 chin li7-ki5.  Sia2 kong2 “Tan5--ka e5 se3-chu2 Tan5 Khun-hong, chian5 chioh8-iu5 kong-si Hiong-kang2 Chong2-kong-si siong-li2 e5 thai3-thai3(hoat-chhe) chu7-sat.  Mia5 Lim5 Hui7-bi2, si7 chit8-ui7 jiat8-sim e5 Ki-tok-tou5.  KhoaN3 si7 thiau3-chui2 si2, m7-ku2 ki3-jian5 si7 jiat8-sim e5 Ki-tok-tou5, eng3-kai si7 bo5 chu7-sat e5 li2-khi3.  Kong2 si7 ui7 ka-teng5 ai3-cheng5 e5 kiu3-hun, chiah chhoe7 te2-lou7.  M7-ku2 na7 si7 jiat8-sim e5 lu2-tou5, kiam2 be7 thun-lun2, eng7 ho2 lai5 iaN5 phaiN2.  Ho5-pit chu7-sat, kiam2 m7-si7 tek-choe7 in e5 Siong7-te3.  Koh tang5-si5 i e5 chhe-eng7 Sou3-lan5 ia7 sit-chong, thiaN kong2 peN5-peN5 si7 Ki-tok-tou5.  Tui3 an2-ni ka7 i chhui-chhat khi2--lai5, kiam2-chhai2 poe3-au7 u7 bou5-sat ia7 bo5 tek-khak.  Sou2-i2 ia7 thang siuN7 choe3 si7 thaN-sat.  Chit e5 hiam5-gi5 lang5 chit-chun7 boe7 keng-koe3 siong5-se3 tiau-cha, sou2-i2 chhiaN2 m7 hoat-piau2.  Keng2-chhat-kiok8 khoaN3 chit chan5 su7 choe3 chin iau3-kin2.  Sou2-i2 chit-si5 i2-keng teh si3-ui5 cheng-chhat.  Phah-sng3 bo5-ku2 su7 chiu7 e7 beng5-pek8.”
Tong5-tong5 chhut ti7 Bin5-seng-po3 te7 saN iah8 chin toa7-ji7.  Khun-hong thak8 chit8 e7 bin7 long2 sit-sek, thau3-me5 chhoa7 Bi2-chu tit8-tit8 che7 kip-heng5 chau2 kau3 Siong7-hai2, khi3 bih tiam3 Hoat-kok chou-kai3.  Theng3-hau7 keng2-chhat e5 heng5-su7 kau3, lang5 to chau2-khi3 lah.  It-hoat kho2-gi5, chiu7 chiong Siu3-chhun khu khi3 keng2-chhat-kiok8 mng7.  Keh-jit8 e5 sin-bun5 koh chhut--lai5, sia2 kong2 “Choe3 ki5-koai3 e5 chiu7-si7 kau3 chit-si5 kou iau2-boe7 u7 sin-si.  Ia7 Tan5 Khun-hong kap Sai3-hoe-lau5 e5 Bi2-chu, ti7 ji7 ho7 i5-thai3-thai3 ia7 hut-jian5 sit-chong.  Hian7-si5 te7-it ho7 i5-thai3-thai3 Siu3-chhun pi7 keng2-chhat-kiok8 khu-liu5 tiong.  An2-ni khoaN3 tui3 cheng5-tek8 e5 tou3-khi bou7-sat e5 hiam5-gi5 chin beng5.”
Siu3-chhun khi2-thau5 long2 m7 kong2.  Khah kong2 to kong2 i m7-chai.  Keng-koe3 che7-che7 e5 hong-hoat lai5 mng7 chiah lau3-khau2 chhut--lai5 kong2 i u7 thiaN lang5 e5 siaN poah8 loh8-khi3.  Au7-lai5 chiah jin7 ti7 lian5-hoe-ti5, si5-jit8 si7 11 goeh8 chhe 2, si7 goeh8 am3-mi5.  Au7-lai5 chhoa7 khi3 sit8-te7 kiam2-cheng3.  Chin tu2-ho2, koh iau2 u7 chhiu2-kin-a2 nng7-tiau5 ka-lauh8 ti7 ti5-piN, chit8-tiau5 ti7 chioh8-thau5 kha, bak kau3 choan phiN7, bak8-sai2 e5 jiah, chit8-tiau5 ti7 hi5-ti5 piN e5 chhau2-a2 teng2, giong7-giong7 beh ka-lauh8 loh8-chui2 lah.  Hit tiau5 si7 tiu5--e5, hiu3 phang-chui2 chin phang, ia7 u7 chhit chhui3-tun5 ang5 ian-chi e5 jiah.
Hit nng7-tiau5 chhiu2-kin si7 chin ho2 e5 but8-cheng3.  Theh8 to3-khi3 kau Keng2-bu7-chhu3 hoat-i hoa3-giam7, ti7 hit nng7-tiau5 chhiu2-kin chhoe7 chhut lang5 e5 cheng2-thau5-a2 hun5.  Cheng2-thau5-a2 hun5 si7 pi2 in3-a2 khah ho2, che si7 be7 ke2-tit e5 in3-cheng3.  Hoa3-giam7 liau2 chit tiau5 u7 Hui7-bi2 sou2 iong7 e5 kho2-gi5.  In-ui7 u7 phiN7, bak8-sai2 tai7-khai3 si7 ti7 hia khau3, kin-a2 si7 chhou peh8-pou3.  Koh tui3 chhiu2-kin-a2 kah, eng7 soaN3 thiN7 chit8-ji7 Lo5-ma2-ji7 “Hui7.” An2-ni chin beng5 si7 kou3-jin5 e5 ui5-but8.  Ia7 u7 chhiu2-hun5 long2 hip khi2-lai5.  An2-ni Hui7-bi2 khak-sit8 ti7 Lian5-hoe-ti5 sit-su7 bo5-gi5.
Koh hoa3-giam7 iau2 chit8-tiau5 keN5 ti7 hi5-ti5-piN e5 chhau2-a2 boe2 e5 tiu5 chhiu2-kin.  Chit tiau5 chhiu2-kin e7 ui7-ti3 pi2 pou3-chhiu2-kin khah lip-kiN5 ti7 ti5 piN, an2-ni chit tiau5 chhiu2-kin e5 chu2-lang5 kho2-leng5 pi7 chhui-chhut kui2-na7 hang7. (1) Tiu5 chhiu2-kin e5 chu2 lang5 ia7 bat kau3 Lian5-hoe-ti5 piN. (2) Ji5-chhiaN2 bat khia7 chin oa2, chin lip-kiN5, e5 sou2-chai7. (3) Koh hek8-chia2 bat chin chhut-lat8 cho3 sim2-mih8 su7 ti3-kau3 i e5 kin-a2 ka-lauh8, pun2-lang5 soa3 m7-chai. (4) Ia7 hit e5 si5-kan kho2-leng5 si7 chin am3 e5 si5 sou2-i2 bo5 khoaN3 tioh8 thang khioh, kap 11 goeh8 chhe 2 bo5 goeh8-kng chin hu5-hap8.
Koh chit8-pai2 beng5-se3 e5 hoa3-giam7, chiu7 chai(1) Chhiu2-hun5 chin beng5, kio3 Siu3-chhun lai5 giam7 u7 tui3. (2) Chhit ti7 kin-a2 e5 ian-chi sek kap i chhui3-tun5 e5 ian-chi sek, phin2-chit long2 tui3.  Tui3 an2-ni chiu7 toan3-teng7 Siu3-chhun kap chit-chan5 sat-jin5 su7-kiaN7 iu7-koan.  Chong2-si7 iau2 m7 seng5-jin7.  Pek kau3-boe2 chiah seng5-jin7 in khi3 Sai3-hoa-lau5, saN e5 to3--lai5.  Kau3 hia thiaN Hui7-bi2 teh khau3, Hui7-bi2 lam2 Khun-hong e5 kha, Khun-hong ka7 i cham3 loh8-khi3.  An2-ni chu2-hoan7 si7 Khun-hong.  Tui3 an2-ni chiu7 chiam7-si5 kau-po2, pang3 i to3-khi3, chiau3 i siuN7 lai5 kau3 chia hoe2-sio-kha sui5-lang5 poe2.  I ka-ti7 na7 piaN3 e7 li7 ho2 bi7-si7, hoan-koan2 pat8-lang5 si2 liau2-liau2.  It-chhe3 long2 piaN3 hou7 Khun-hong.  Chit8-bin7 tui3 sin-bun5 chhut, cheng3 kau3-hoe7 bo5 m7 ui7 chit chan5 su7 ki5-to2.  Ng3-bang7 Siong7-te3 chu2-chhi5 kong-to7.  Lai5 siu bu5-kou e5 oan.
Khun-hong chau2 kau3 Siong7-hai2, khi3 bih tiam3 hoat chou-kai3 e5 “Te7-it lu2-sia7.” Hit am3 kau3 ui7 chin koaN5.  Lai7-bin7 e5 lau2-pan2 kap kang lang5, long2 khoaN3 choe3 Kim-gu5 lai5.  Hu5-kha sang2-chhiu2, chiu7 chhiaN2 i tiam3 tek8-teng2 pang5.  Tak8-hang7 si-siat iuN5-hoa3, piah-lo5, tang5 bin5-chhng5, phong3-i2 long2 chin sui2.  Kai-si2, chiN5 tong7 jin5-sim Khun-hong koaN7 chit8 phoe5-te7 e5 Bi2-chhau2-phio3.  Bi2-chu chheng7 chit8 seng-khu e5 tiu5-toan7.  Chin-chu, soan7-chioh8, kim-khoan5, am7-lian7, chhiu2-chi2 hiN7-kau, kim siam2-siam2 e7 toat8 lang5 e5 bak8-chiu.  Koan2 hit ho7 sek e5 lu2 chiau-thai7-seng nng7 e5 chiu7 iong7 hong-hoat lah, chiu7 theh8 Siau-sng kap iam5-sng ka7 i lam7 choe3-hoe2. (Chiu7-si7 lang5 si5-kiaN5 ka7 cha-bou2 lang5 phoah-bin7 hou7 i noa7 e5 ioh8-chui2).  Phau3 tiam3 ko-pi te5, sio kun2-kun2, koh phang5 chit8 e7 iu3-piaN2 lai5 chhiaN2 in chiah8.
Nng7 e5 m7-chai si2, m7-chai si2, chin hoaN-hi2 chiu7 chiap--lai5.  Khun-hong boe7 lim seng thng3-saN khi3 se2-ek8.  In-ui7 kam2-kak khah bo5 hiah chhui3-ta, chiu7 bo5 lim chhiaN2 tng3 leh.  Khi3 se2-seng-khu e5 si5 Bi2-chu lim.  Lim koe3-au5 ai chit8 siaN be7 kou3-tit un loh8-khi3.  Chu7 an2-ni si2 tiam3 i2-kha.  Khun-hong se2-ek8 ho2 lai5, khoaN3 Bi2-chu i2-keng koe3-khui3, kin2 khi3 po3 keng2-chhat.  Heng5-keng2 chit8 e7 lai5 liam5-piN chai-iaN2 si7 tok8-sat.  Chhun e5 ko-pi theh8 khi3 hoa3-giam7, liam5-piN chai si7 Siau-sng Iam5-sng phau3-che3 e5 Ong5-chui2(王水).  Chek-si5 toa7 sou-cha, liam5-piN bo5 koe3 kui2 tiam2-cheng chiu7 chai si7 lu2 chiau-thai7-seng e5 kiong7-bou5 e5 bou5-chai7 hai7-beng7.
Keh-jit8 sang3 loh8 hoat-teng5 kong-phoaN3.  Ai3 Khun-hong khi3 choe3 cheng3-jin5.  I ti7 chia kai2-choe3 Tan5 Hok-choan5(陳福全).  Ia7 Bi2-chu kai2-choe3 Po2-chu.  I si7 i5-it e5 cheng5-jin5, bo5 chhut-teng5 choat8-tui3 be7 eng7-tit.  Chin put-tek-i2 chiu7 chhut-teng5.  Chu7-jian5 cheng3-ku3 chhiong-hun, hit nng7 e5 lu2 chiau-thai7-seng chiu7 siu7 phoaN3-koat si2-heng5.  Liau2-au7 chiu7 soan-ko3 soaN3-teng5.  Tu2 hit-si5 u7 chit8 e5 lang5 tui3 tng5-au7 kiaN5 lai5 thau5-cheng5, pai3-thok Tan5 Hok-choan5 ban7-chiah li7-teng5.  Tan5 Hok-choan5 e5 bin7 chek-si5 sit-sek.  Chit e5 m7-si7 pat8-lang5, goan5-lai5 chiu7-si7 Siong7-hai2-chhi7 Keng2-bu7-chhu3 e5 Heng5-su7 kho-tiuN2.  Si7 chhut-mia5 e5 cheng-tham3 Chhoa3 Thian-pheng5(蔡天枰).  I e5 goan5-mia5 si7 “Thian-peng5”(天平), tai7-ke kong2 i kong-to7, na2-chun2 thian-pheng5.  It-tan3 su7-kiaN7 jip8 i e5 chhiu2 bo5 m7 chin beng5.
In-ui7 Lian5-hoe-ti5 su7-kiaN7 Hui7-bi2 e5 au7-thau5 A-so2 Soat-mui5 khoaN3 sin-bun5, kap Chiang-chiu koan7-siaN5 keng2-chhat-kiok8 e5 thong-ti.  I2-keng theh8 chhut siong7-ko3 ti7 Chiang-chiu te7-hng hoat-iN7.  Hoat-iN7 i2-keng hoat-chhut thong-chhip-leng7.  Kin-a2-jit8 ti7 chia tu2-tioh8 Chhoa3 sian-siN chhah-sit8 to lan5 poe.  Chhoa3 sian-siN theh8 sin-hun7-cheng3 hou7 i khoaN3.  Si7 Siong7-hai2 Tek8-piat8-chhi7 e5 keng2-bu7-chhu3 heng5-su7 kho-tiuN2.  Cheng-tham3 chu2-jim7 Chhoa3 Thian-peng5.  Soa3 chiong thong-chhip-leng7 hou7 i khoaN3.  Ti7 hia u7 i e5 siong7, chek-si5 chi2-chek i e5 goan5-mia5 si7 Tan5 Khun-hong.  Long2 bo5 oe7 thang in3, thau5-khak kau loh8-khi3, bak8-sai2 lian3 chhut-lai5.  Bo5 se3-ji7 e5 Chhoa3 sian-siN theh8 chhiu2-khau3 khi2--lai5 siang-chhiu2 ka7 i khau3 choe3-hoe2.  Hoan-hu3 koaiN-loh8 u5-sim2 kaN-pang5.  Ah!  Kau3 chia ia7 liau2-jian5, cheng5-chin7.  Ai3 Hui7-bi2 ai3 kau3 be7 tit-tioh8, chhian-hong pah-ke3.  Kou-chiaN5, kiong5-toat8.  Tui-chhoe7, kui7-loh8 kio3 m7-kaN2, hoe7 sit-le2, chiu3-choa7 beh loh8 kau3.  PiN3 chit8-pah lian5-peh piN3, kau3 chia tui7-loh8.  ChiN5 u7, chiu2, sek, kiau2, thiau3-bu2.  In3 Hui7-bi2 “Chit-si5 pi2 hit si5, chit8-si5 hong sai2 chit8-si5 chun5.  To bo5 teh gong7, chit-si5 sim2-mih8 lang5 beh koh kap li2 loh8 kau3 ah.” U7 iaN2 lah, chhoa7 koe3 chhiu2 lah.  Hoe to chhai2 liau2 lah, oaN7 sin khah sim-sek.  Na7-si7 choe7-ok teh tui-jiok.  Kau3 chia tioh8 chhi3-chhi3 thih-thang e5 chu-bi7. 
19
Tui3 siu7 khu-jip8 u5-sim2 kaN-pang5 hit am3, Khun-hong khi2 jiat8 kong5.  In-ui7 i khoaN3-kiN3 Hui7-bi2 chit8-thau5 chit8-bin7 long2 si7 lou7-kou-moai5, seng-khu tam5 lok-lok.  Soa3 kam2-kak san2 khok8-khok8, chih8-a2 thou2 tng5-tng5.  Khah-theng5 ti7 bin5-chhng5-cheng5, i bin7 na7 oat8 ng3-piah chiu7 chau2-khi3 bin5-chhng5 au7.  Phoe7 thoa lai5 kham3-bin7, soa3 kam2-kak teh ka7 i jih8.  Kou put-chiong i chiu7 toa7-siaN jiang2, hoah kiu3 lang5.  Kou3-kaN e5 lai5 khoaN3, i soa3 kui7 loh8 khi3 kio3 m7-kaN2.  Khah-theng5 gim5 Ki-tok-kau3 e5 si “Goa2 choe7 kek8-tang7 be7 tit the-si5, chiau3 thiN lut8-hoat eng3-kai tioh8 si2, chai bo5 hoat-tou7 thang-kiu3 ka-ti7, Ia5-sou goa2 lai5 chiu7-li2” chiu7 kui7-loh8 lau5 bak8-sai2.  Khah-theng5 chiu7 chhiuN3 “Chai3-lai5 chit8-poe, ho5-pit kheh-khi3, chit-si5 hoe tng phang, chiu2 tng ang5, m7-lim m7-phiau5, chheng-chhun put-chai3 lai5.” chiu7 hah8-hah8 toa7-chhio3.  Khah-theng5 kio3 Ia5-sou Siong7-te3, khah-theng5 kio3 Hut8-chou2, Ong5-ia5-kong, khah-theng5 kio3 Hui7-bi2, khah-theng5 hoah kong2 Bi2-chu to2 toh8 khi3-lah.  Khah-theng5 jiang2-kong2 long2 si7 Siu3-chhun hai7 i, chiu7 chin siu7 khi3, chhiu2 teN7 kun thau5-bu2 beh phah, cham3-te5 chiu7 koh toa7-khau3.  Au7-lai5 chiu7 kui7 leh se3-a2 siaN kong2 Hui7-bi2 li2 oan-hun5 mai3 lai5 tiN5 lah.  Goa2 chiah ka7 li2 choe3 Sai-kong, chhiau-tou7 lah.  Khah-theng5 chiu7 kong2 “Chu2 e7-kiu3 Chu2 e7 kiu3”.  Chong2-kong2 kui me5 bo5 khun3, u7 si5 ka-ti7 kong2 kai-si2, chiu7 ka-ti7 sai chhui3-phoe2.  Kou3-kaN e5 khoaN3 liau2 chin kiaN chiu7 khi3 po3 tian2-gak8-tiuN2 chai.  Bin5-a2-chai3 chiu7 siat-hoat hou7 i chiam7-si5 chhut-gak8 khi3 jip8-iN7.  Chiu7 hou7 i jip8-ti7 Siong7-hai2 Seng3 Iok-han7 tai7-hak8 e5 hu3-siok8 peN7-iN7, chun2 i cheng7-iong2 chit8-le2-pai3, au7 lai5 chiah sim2-mng7.  Ah!  Chin-chiaN3 si7 choe7 teh lang5, boe7 sim2-mng7 seng ka-ti7 kiaN.  Jip8-iN7 te7 4 jit8, jiat8 long2 the3 khah e7 khun3 tit.  U7 chit8-am3 goeh8 hoaN2-ou hoaN2-ou khi2 lai5 kui7 loh8 ti7 thou5-kha, bin7 phak ti7 i2-a2, liong5-sim chhut-hian7, koh siuN7 tioh8 Siong7-te3 lah.
Chiu7 ki5-to2 kong2 “Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 lin5-bin2 sia3-bian2 goa2 koe3-khi3 e5 choe7.  Goa2 sit8-chai7 u7 tek-choe7 Li2.  Goa2 eng7 kau-kui2 e5 sim lai5 phian3 lang5, ia7 phian3 Siong7-te3.  TaN kau3-chia it-chhe3 choe7 e5 kang-chiN5 long2 kau3-chhiu2 lah.  Ah3!  Choe7 e5 kang-chiN5 chiu7-si7 Si2.  TaN goa2 chai tu5 si2 i2-goa7, goa2 ka-ti7 bo5 lou7 thang thoat-li7.” Ki5-to2 kau3-chia chiu7 koh khui-siaN hau2 kau3 chheh khui3.  Theng5 ho2-ku2 chiu7 koh chiap-soa3 ki5-to2.  “Cha2 ah!  Li2 si7 lin5-bin2 e5 Chu2, Li2 kiam2 m7 kheng2 lin5-bin2 chin2-kiu3 goa2?  Goa2 na7-tioh8 siu7 teng7 si2-heng5, ThiN-pe7 Li2 kiam2 bo5 beh tai3-liam7 Chu2 e5 bin7, khoaN3 goa2 chit-tiap8 chin-sit8 e5 thong3-hoe2 lai5 kiu3 goa2 e5 leng5-hun5?” Chiu7 koh khui-siaN hau2, na2-hau2 soa3 na2 chin chhi-chham2 kiu5 kio3 kong2 “Chu2 ah!  Chu2 ah!  Kiu5 li2 sia3-bian2 goa2.” Khan3-hou7-hu7 che7-che7 si7 Ki-tok-tou5, in-ui7 Seng3 Iok-han7 tai7-hak8 si7 Kau3-hoe7 siat e5 tai7-hak8.  Khau3-hou7-hu7 thiaN i teh hau2 teh ki5-to2, chiu7 chai i ia7 u7 thiaN to7-li2, chiu7 lai5 mng7 lai5 an-ui3 i.  Kio3 i kin2-khun3, m7-thang sui7-bin5 put-chiok kho2-leng5 e7 koh hoat-jiat8.  Au7-lai5 sin-the2 e7 koh phah-phaiN2.  Teh kong2 chiah e5 oe7, a2-si7 i teh ki5-to2 e5 si5, ti7 peN7-sek au7-bin7 e5 thang-a2 goa7 u7 chit8 e5 lang5 khia7 ti7 hia teh thau-khoaN3, thau-thiaN, i long2 m7-chai.  Siu7 lang5 khou2-khng3 chiu7 an-cheng7 to2 loh8 khi3-khun3.  Na7-si7 khun3 be7-khi3, chiu7 koh peh khi2 lai5, tui3 kou3-me5 lai5 sun5 peN7-pang5 e5 hou7-su7 tho2 choa2-pit.  I e5 i3-su3 si7 ai3 sia2 ui5-gian5-chng7 hou7 Hui7-bi2.
In-ui7 kau3 chit e5 si5 i e5 sim iau2 u7 chit8 e5 chin-toa7 e5 gi5-hek8. (1) Chiu7-si7 i siuN7 Hui7-bi2 un2-tang3 si2 lah.  Si2 ti7 lian5-hoe-ti5 te2.  Tai7-khai3 si7 thau5-khak tian-to3 thau5-chai, chhap-jip8 ti7 lou7-kou-moai5 te2, chui2-chhim m7-bat ta, chin-che7 lom3-lom3 e5 thou5.  Chu7 an2-ni bo5 khui3, kou-bo5, si7 si2 ti7 lou7-kou-moai5 e5 lom3-thou5 lai7. (2) Hui7-bi2 bo5 si2.  In-ui7 i kam2-kak that bo5 kau3 goa7 toa7 e7, kek8-ke si7 tng3-lap-che7, an2-choaN2 e7 poah8 loh8 ti5.  Loh8 ti5 an2-choaN2 e7 soa3 bo5 sin-si, chin-chiaN3 si7 ki5-koai3.  Sou2-i2 chiu7 koat-sim beh sia2 ui5-gian5-chng7 hou7 Hui7-bi2.
Hou7-su7 theh8 choa2 pit lai5 hou7 i, i chiu7-sia2.  “Sou2 thiaN3 e5 Hui7-bi2.  Kiu5-li2 sia3-bian2 goa2 e5 choe7.  Goa2 tui3-li2 chin put-chu7.  Goan7-li2 ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5 thoe3 goa2 ai-kiu5, in-ui7 goa2 i2-keng u7 chhim-chhim hoan2-hoe2 chai-choe7.  Cheng5 goa2 chun5 kan-kui2 e5 sim phian3-li2, phian3 Siong7-te3.  Sit8-chai7 chin kai-si2, taN chit-si5 goa2 tui3 sim-te2 chhim-chhim thong3-hoe2, hoat-sim sin3 Chu2 Ia5-sou.  Kiu5 I un-tian2 chin2-kiu3 goa2 e5 leng5-hun5.  Goa2 ng3-bang7 e7-tit kap li2 saN-kiN3 ti7 thiN.  Chong2-si7 goa2 iau2 u7 chit8-tiam2 e5 ng3-bang7, chiu7-si7 bang7 li2 kho2-leng5 iau2 ti7 se3-kan.  Na7-si7 chit e5 ng3-bang7 si7 chin poh8, kiam2-chhai2 si7 goa2 e5 gong7-siuN7.  Chong2-si7 goa2 i2-keng chai, goa2 e7 siu7 hoat-lut8 e5 chhai5-phoaN3.  Goa2 bo5 lou7 thang ka-ti7 se2-chheng.  Ah!  Sou2 thiaN3--e5.  Siat-su2 li2 na7 iau2-oah8, li2 kiam2 be7 tai3-liam7 tioh8 chhou-hoe7 ti7 soaN-teng2 ban2 Pek-hap8-hoe e5 si5.  Kiam2 be7 siuN7 tioh8 choe3-hoe2 kou3 A-pa ti7 peN7-chhng5.  Kiam2 be7 siuN7 tioh8 goa2 tui-chhoe7 li2, chhoe7 li2 ti7 Hun5-lam5-siaN5-goa7 e5 chit8 e5 hiuN-chng e5 sio2-tek-ui5 e5 cheng5-keng2.  Ah!  Na7 koh siuN7 hiah e5 tiN-bit8 e5 ai3-cheng5, goa2 e5 sim sit8-chai7 beh piak-lih8.” Sia2 kau3 chia bak8-sai2 hou3 m7-khui tit8-tit8 hau2 chhut--lai5, chiu7 khi2-lai5 kiaN5-oa2 au7-piah thang-a2-kiN beh theh8 bin7-kin chhit bak8-sai2.  Hut-jian5 taN-thau5 khoaN3 thang-a2-goa7 u7 chit8 e5 lang5, hit e5 lang5-iaN2 chhin-chhiuN7 Hui7-bi2!  I bo5 i3-sek kio3 chin toa7-siaN “Hui7-bi2” chong2-si7 hit e5 lang5-iaN2 chu7 an2-ni bo5 khi3.  I chin m7-goan7 chu7 chheng7 khun3-saN khui-mng5 jiok chhut--lai5.  Ko2-jian5 u7 chit8 e5 lang5 teh chau2, ji5-chhiaN2 si7 cha-bou2-lang5 e5 khoan2.  In-ui7 goeh8 bo5 kng, tak tioh8 chioh8-thau5 soa3 phak-loh8-khi3, khi2 nau2 pin5-hiat, kou3 me5 e5 hou7-su7 kin2-lai5, ia7 kap hit e5 teh chau2 e5 lang5 ia7 oat to3-tng2--lai5.  Ka7 i kng jip8 peN7-pang5.  Theng5 oa2 chiaN5-khek ku2 chia cheng-sin5.  Sim chin giau5-gi5, siong7-se3 mng7 chia u7 lang5 ho7 choe3 “Lim5 Hui7-bi2” a2-bo5?  Tai7-ke long2 ka7 i kong2 bo5.  Chu7 an2-ni chiu7 ka-ti7 siuN7 si7 siuN khoa3-sim chit8 si5 e5 hoan3-kak(幻覺) sou2 ti3.
Kau3 chit8-le2-pai3 au7 chiu7 koh siu7 tiau3 kau3 hoat-iN7 siu7 u5-sim2.  U5-sim2 koaN tai7-seng mng7 i e5 se3-mia5, ni5-hoe3, chu7-chi2.  Khak-jin7 chit-e5 lang5 ko2-jian5 si7 Tan5 Khun-hong, Tan5 Hok-choan5 si7 ke2-mia5, it-it chu7-jin7.  Ia7 ka-ti7 chu7-jin7 si7 ui7 kiaN choe7, sou2-i2 chiah to5-choe7 lai5 Siong7-hai2.  Thang-kong2 10 hun e5 8.9 i ka-ti7 seng-jin7 Hui7-bi2 e5 si2 si7 i ka7 i that loh8 khi3 e5.  Put-ko3 u7 kui2-na7 tiam2 thang koh tiau-cha chiu7-si7. (1) Si7 ok-i3, a2-si7 bu5-i3. (2) Si7 i chit8 e5 ka7 i thak lai5 ti3-si2, a2-si7 iau2 u7 pang-chhiu2.  Na7 siat-su2 u7 pang-chhiu2, chiu7 piN3-choe3 ok-i3, kiong7-bou5. (3) ChaiN2-iuN7 e7 biat8-si.  An2-ni si7 poah8 loh8-chui2 si2, a2-si7 ti7 pat8-ui7 i2-keng ka7 i chhong3-si2, chiah kng lai5 thiam7 ti7 Lian5-hoe-ti5, ke2 choe3 poah8-loh8-chui2 si2.  In-ui7 si7 biat8-si, sou2-i2 lang5 poah8-loh8-chui2 ka-ti7 kou-bo5, ia7 bo5 lang5 lai5 po3 keng2-chhat.  Tui3 chit 3 tiam2 iau2 boe7 beng5.
Ui7 beh phoaN3-koat si2-heng5 tek-khak ai3 u7 jin5-cheng3(人證) , but8-cheng3(物證) , khong-kan, si5-kan, tong7-chok it-chhe3 iu2-lek8 e5 cheng3-ku3, m7-si7 sui-sui pian7-pian7, chiu7 koat-teng7 chiong chit kiaN7 an3 i5 to3-khi3 pun2 te7-hng e5 Te7-hng-hoat-iN7.  Soa3 thang sit8-te7 kiam2-cheng3.  Keh jit8 chiu7 lian5-jin5 tai3-an3, ah-sang3 loh8 lai5 Chiang-chiu-siaN5 Te7-hng hoat-iN7.  Chit-khi2 an3 Keng2-bu7-chhu3 phoe hou7 Chhoa3 Thian-peng5 sian-siN choan-an3 cheng-cha.  Sou2-i2 Chhoa3 sian-siN chhin-sin ah i loh8-lai5 Chiang-chiu.  Kau3-chia Khun-hong chin-chiaN3 si7 bo5 bin7 thang kiN3 lang5.  Loh8 hoe2-chhia khoaN3-kiN3 e5 lang5 u7 e5 bih-chhui3, u7 e5 phui3-noa7.  Tai7-ke kong2 i si7 liau2-boe2-a2-kiaN2, hong-im5 chiu2-sek bo5 theng5-tou7.  Kau3-ui7 keh-jit8 kap chin-che7 hoat-keng2, hoat-i(法醫) , Chhoa3 Sian-siN chhin-sin khan, thau5-khak ka7 i ti3 chhau2-lap-a2, kan-ta chhun bak8-chiu khang hou7 i khoaN3-lou7, chhiu2, khau3 chhiu2-khau3 pak8 iap-au7.  Khan lai5 kau3 Lian5-hoe-ti5 piN, jin5-san, jin5-hai2 e5 lang5 ui5 lai5 khoaN3.  Sit8-chai7 chiok kian3-siau3.  Kio3 i ka-ti7 siong7-se3 soat-beng5, Hui7-bi2 ti7 to2-ui7 lam2 li2 e5 kha, lin2 saN e5 an2-choaN2 moa?  Lam2-kha lam2 sim2-mih8 se3-bin7?  Lam2-kha chu7 an2-ni theng5 kha khia7 leh, a2-si7 u7 lam2 teh kiaN5?  KiaN5 kui2-pou7?  M7-chai iaN2 kau3 ti5-piN lah a2 m7-si7?  That goa7 toa7 e7, pi2 khoaN3-mai7?  That chit8-e7 sui-si5 poah8 loh8 khi3, a2-si7 theng5 chit8 e7-a2 chiah poah8 loh8 khi3?  Bo5 sui-si5 in3-siaN poah8-loh8 khi3, si7 iau2 u7 lang5 tau3 that loh8 khi3 a2 m7-si7?  Kau3-chia chit-ku3 i siuN7 chin ku2 be7-hiau2 in3, Kak-tek m7-si7 i that-khi3 chek-si5 poah8 loh8-khi3.  Na2-chun2 u7 ………, m7-ku2 am3-am3, ka-ti7 u7 lim-chiu2 sio2-khoa2 chui3-chui3, sou2-i2 ki3-ek put-chheng-chho2 m7-kaN2 in3.  Li2 u7 hoah kiu3 lang5 a2-bo5?  U7.  Li2 u7 loh8 khi3 kou a2-bo5?  Goa2 chek-si5 loh8 khi3 hoe5.  U7 thng3-e5 a2-bo5?  Bo5 thng3-e5, kan-ta ti7 hoaN7-teng2 aN3 loh8 khi3 bong.  An2-choaN2 koan-he7 jin5-beng7 hiah lo2-chho2, m7-bian2 thng3 e5, kin2 giah8 hoe2 lai5 bong?  Siu3-chhun kio3 goa2 mai3, kong2 chin-koaN5, goa2 u7 lim-chiu2, ia7 sio2-khoa2 kam2-tioh8.  Kong2 si2 to si2 lah, bin5-a2-chai3 chiah lai5 kou.  Au7-lai5 chu7 an2-ni tan2 kau3 bin5-a2-chai3 a2 m7-si7?  M7-si7, goa2 u7 giah8 tek-ko lai5 la7.  Hit-si5 Siu3-chhun ti7 to2-ui7?  I m7-chhap goa2 choe3 i to2-teh khun3.
Chhoa3 sian-siN te7 6 kam2 si7 kam2-kak Siu3-chhun tui3 chit-chan5 su7 ia7-si7 chit8 e5 Chu2-kak, chek-si5 kio3 chit8 e5 heng5-keng2 khi3 kio3 Siu3-chhun lai5.  Kio3 i lai5 Lian5-hoe-ti5-piN kiam2-cheng3.  Heng5-keng2 khi3 e5 si5 chhoe7 bo5.  To3-tng2 lai5 po3-ko3, kong2 lai7-bin7 chhoe7 bo5 lang5, pang5-keng chi2 u7 chit8 e5 eN-a2 teh-hau2, chin ki5-koai3, it-hoat kho2-gi5 chit e5 lang5 u7 choe7-hiam5(罪嫌).  Sou2-i2 beng7-leng7 choan5-chhu3-theh8 lai7-goa7 chong2 sou-cha.  Tauh ti2 Siu3-chhun tui3 to2-ui7 khi3?  Kau3-boe2 chiah hoat-kian3 i si2 ti7 au7 hoe-hng5 e5 kou2-chiN2-te2.  In-ui7 lang5 thoa Khun-hong beh lai5 kiam2-cheng3 e5 si5, i iaN2 tioh8 Khun-hong bin7 ti3 chhau2-lap-a2, chhiu2 hou7 lang5 pak8 iap-au7, eng7 chhiu2-khau3 khau3 leh.  Siu3-chhun toa7-kiaN, chai si2 lah.  Koh-si7 choan5-kok ti5-mia5 e5 Chhoa3 cheng-tham3 choan-an3 cheng-pan7.  Chai hoat-bong2 lan5-to5.  I ka-ti7 chai, chha5 kau3-boe2 chu2-hoan7(主犯) m7-si7 Khun-hong.  Chu2-hoan7 si7 i pun2-sin, Khun-hong si7 bu5-i3, na7-si7 iu2-i3 chun5 sat-jin5, koh tit8-chiap e5 ti3-si2(致死) si7 tui3 i e5 heng5-tong7.  Sou2-i2 kau3-chia i siuN7 khi2 hoat-teng5 hian7-si3, m7-tat8-tioh8 si2 tiam3 chhu3-nih khah tit8.  Sou2-i2 chiong Eng5-chong(eN-a2) ka7 i hiat tiam3 bin5-chhng5, than3 lang5 bo5 chu3-i3 chu7 an2-ni khi3 thiau3 kou2-chiN2.  I m7-si7 eng7 thiau3, i si7 eng7 tian-to3-thau5-chai chai loh8 khi3.  Sou2-i2 kou khi2--lai5 i2-keng koe3-khui3 nge7-nge7, si5-kan ia7 i2-keng koe3 30 hun khah ke.  Thau5-khak chai ti7 chiN2-te2 e5 lou5-kou-moai5, sou2-i2 chit8 chhui3 chit8 phiN7, si3-ke3 long2 si7 lou5-kou-moai5 that tiN7-tiN7.  Tui3 u7 chui2-to7, chit e5 cheN2 han2 tit eng7 chin chhim, chui2 ia7 u7 chhau3-bi7, kau3-boe2 kiu3 be7 oah8.  Na7-si7 tong5-si5 sou-cha, ti7 Hui7-bi2 e5 pang5-keng u7 hoat-kian3 tioh8 Hui7-bi2 chu7-sat e5 ui5-gian5-chng7, che-si7 chin ki5-koai3 e5 su7.
An2-ni chit e5 an3 chin tiN5.  Ho2 e5 cheng3-jin5 Bi2-chu2 ti7 Siong7-hai2 Te7-it li2-sia7 hou7 lang5 thau7-si2.  U7 chu2-hoan7 a2-si7 tong5-bou7-hoan7 kho2-gi5 e5 Siu3-chhun ui3-choe7 chu7-sat.  I5-it e5 but8-cheng3 si7 nng7-tiau5 e5 chhiu2-kin.  Chit8-tiau5 Hui7-bi2 e5.  Chit8-tiau5 Siu3-chhun e5 long2 i2-keng chai.  Choe3 hiam5-gi5 e5 Siu3-chhun ki3-jian5 be5 tit chhut-teng5.  Sou2-i2 taN chi2-u7 sim2-phoaN3 Khun-hong.  Koat-teng7 lai5 12 goeh8 14 jit8 beh ti7 Chiang-chiu siaN5 Te7-hng hoat-iN7 kong-phoaN3.  Hit-jit8 8 tiam2 beh khui-teng5.  Koe3-khi3 si7 chit8 e5 te7-hng e5 beng5-bong7-ka, koh sin-bun5 chhut chiah toa7 ji7, koh chit8-si5 saN e5 bou2, chiah hia-pai.  Hut-jian5 3 e5 bou2 ui7 i chit8 e5 choe3 tiong-sim long2 si2.  Ji5-chhiaN2 si2 tit chin li7-ki5.  Toa7-bou2 siu7 that loh8-ti5 si2, te7-ji7-ho7 i5-thai3-thai3 hou7 lang5 thau7-si2, te7-it-ho7 i5-thai3-thai3 thiau3 kou2-cheN2 si2.  Long2 si2 ti7 hui-beng7, an2-ni se3-siok8 lang5 long2 kong2 chit8 e5 Khun-hong tek-khak e7 hou7 cha-bou2-kui2 kau-tiN5 lai5 liah8-khi3.  Oan-hun5 tek-khak m7-soaN3, e7 lai5 kau-tiN5.  Kong-phoaN3 hit-jit8 chiok-che7 lang5, tioh8 theh8 pai5-a2-ho7 chiah e7 tit jip8 khi3.  
20
12 goeh8 14 jit8 chiau3 sou2 u5-teng7 chiu7 ti7 Chiang-chiu siaN5 Te7-hng hoat-iN7 khai-teng5 lai5 kong-phoaN3.  Chiau3-si5 siong7-ngou2 8 tiam2 khai-teng5.  Thau5 chit8-teng5 si7 sim2 chit8 kiaN7 thong-kan hai7-hu e5 an3-kiaN7.  Chiu7-si7 sim2 chit8 e5 cha-bou2-lang5 hiam5 i tiong7-hu phoa3-peN7 phoa3-peN7, chiu7 kap siang7 chng e5 bou2 chheng-lian5 thong-kan.  Au7-lai5 tong5-bou5 thai5-si2 tiong7-hu.  Thau5-si2 liau2-au7 chiah ka7 i kng chhut-khi3 hiat tiam3 au7-piah kau.  Theng3-hau7 kan-hu chau2 liau2, chiah ka-ti7 eng7 pin-hng5-to thai5 to3-chhiu e5 hou2-khau2, koh thiah phoa3 saN.  Jian5-au7 chiah khi3 po3 keng2-chhat, ke2-iaN3 chau2 kau3 pheN7-pheN7 chhoan2.  Kong2 si7 chhat8-a2 lai5, tiong7-hu hou7 chhat8 thai5-si2, i pun2-sin ia7 siu7 siong.  Chong2-si7 chit e5 tai7-chi3 tui3 i kap kan-hu e5 thong-phoe lai5 chhut-phoa3.  Cheng3-ku3 tak8-hang7 chhiong-hun, chiu7 siu7 phoaN3-koat si2-heng5.  Choe7-mia5 si7 thong-kan hai7-hu, kiong7-bou5 ok-i3-tek e5 sat-jin5.
Te7-ji7-tng5 sim2 chit8 e5 Lu2-chu2 ko-tiong e5 im-gak8 sina-siN im5-loan7 ka-ti7 sou2 ka3 e5 hak8-seng, i2-keng u7 sin-in7 4 goeh8 jit8 lah.  Sim-i3 ai3 chhoa7--i, na7-si7 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 e5 pe7-bo2 m7-kheng2.  ThiaN3 soa3 hoan2-oan3, am3-si5 chio hit e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 chhut-khi3 te5-sek chiah8 te5.  Phian3 i kong2 beh chhut-khi3 be2 koe2-chi2-a2, kio3 i chhiaN2 tan2 chit8--e7.  Ke2-iaN3 khi2--lai5 kiaN5 tui3 lu2-chu2 e5 au7-bin7 khi3.  Chiu7 chiong sou2 pi7-pan7 chah ti7 seng-khu e5 tok8-ioh8-chui2 tui3 thau5-khak ka7 i lam5 loh8 khi3.  Ioh8-chui2 lau5 tui3 bin7-nih, ti3-kau3 chit8 peng5 e5 bin7, bak8-chiu, hiN7-a2, thau5-khak-phoe3 chu7 an2-ni sek8-sek8.  Sui-jian5 jip8-iN7 ti7-liau5 chong2-si7 bak8-chiu iu5-goan5 chit8-lui2 sit-beng5.  HiN7-a2 chit8 peng5 bo5 thiaN-kiN3, thau5-mng5 lut chit8 peng5.  Bin7 piN3 choe3 chin phaiN2 khoaN3.  Ah sit8-chai7 u7 kau3 chan5-jim2.  Sian-siN si7 thak8 koe3 Su-hoan7 hak8-iN7, siu7 koe3 ko-teng2 kau3-iok8 e5 lang5.  Choe3 lang5 e5 lau7-su, keng3-jian5 im5-loan7 ka-ti7 e5 hak8-seng, kau3 boe2 ji5-chhiaN2 eng7 chiah chan5-jim2 e5 hong-hoat lai5 hui2-hoai7 tui3 hong e5 iong5-mau7.  Cheng3-ku3 chhiong-hun chiu7 phoaN3-koat, chhu2 iu2-ki5 tou5-heng5 10 ni5.  Pak-toat8 kong-koan5 5 ni5.
Te7 3 tng5 si7 beh phoaN3 “Chiang-chiu siaN5 e5 Lian5-hoe-ti5 su7-kiaN7.” Tui3 chit-chan5 su7 iu2-koan e5 cheng3-jin5 Sai3-hoa-lau5 e5 Bi2-chu i2-keng si2.  Choe3 thang giau5-gi5 e5 chu2-hoan7, hek8-chia2 si7 pang-hiong e5 chiong5-hoan7 Siu3-chhun ia7 si2.  Siu3-chhun si7 chin tiong7-iau3 e5 chu2-kak u7 3 hang7 e5 kho2-gi5.
1.  Ti5-piN e5 tiu5 chhiu2-kin. (1) Ti7 chin lip-kiN5 e5 sou2-chai7 khah tioh8. (2) Chhiu2-kin e5 chhiu2-hun5. (3) Ian-chi e5 sek-ti3 kap phin2-chit, oan5-choan5 si7 Siu3-chhun e5.
