2.  Ui3-choe7 chiu7 chu7-sat?  I e5 chu7-sat m7 khah cha2 m7 khah ban7.  Tng kio3 i lai5 hian7-tiuN5 tui3 cheng3 e5 si5 chiah thiau3-cheN2.  Sou2-i2 u7 ui3-choe7 e5 kho2-gi5.
3.  Ka-theh8 sou-cha e5 si5 u7 hoat-kian3 tioh8 Hui7-bi2 chu7-sat e5 ui5-gian5-su.  Keng-koe3 hoat-i kiam2-giam7 au7, chiu7 chai pit-chek kap Hui7-bi2 chai7-seN sou2 sia2 e5 ji7 e5 pit-chek8 bo5 tui3.  Koh giam7 bak8-chui2 e5 sek-ti3 chiu7 chai m7-si7 Hui7-bi2 si2 e5 i2-cheng5 sia2--e5.  Si7 Hui7-bi2 si2 liau2 sim2-mih8 lang5 sia2, lai5 mou7-chhiong choe3 Hui7-bi2 chu7-sat e5 ui5-gian5.  In-ui7 hit e5 pit-jiah, bak8-chui2 e5 sek-ti3 iau2 chin sin.  Koh hoa3-giam7 choa2-bin7 e5 chhiu2-hun5, kap ti5-piN e5 tiu5 chhiu2-kin u7 tui3.  An2-ni thang toan3-teng7 chit tiuN ui5-gian5 si7 Siu3-chhun sia2--e5, chiu7-si7 beh ian-biat8 thaN-sat e5 hiam5-gi5.
Tui3 i2-siong7 saN-tiam2 ka7 i chhui Hui7-bi2 e5 si2 kap Siu3-chhun toa7 koan-he7.  Chong2-si7 lang5 i2-keng si2 bo5 hoat-tou7 thang koh tui-kiu3.  I5-it e5 oah8 lang5 chiu7-si7 Khun-hong.  Khun-hong chhin-sin ka7 i that.  Ji5-chhiaN2 ka7 i that e5 si5, i5-chiau3 Siu3-chhun e5 khau2-keng kong2, Khun-hong u7 chhoh phaiN2-chhui3, ji5-chhiaN2 me7 kong2 “Beh si2 si2-lo7-khi3, m7-bian2 tiaN7 teh kau-tiN5.” Me7 an2-ni chiah chhut-lat8 ka7 i that-khi3.  Sou2-i2 ia7 be7-tit kong2 m7-si7 ok-i3.  Koh tui3 koe3-khi3 e5 kiu3-hun, kap su7-su7 phaiN2 khoan2-thai7 Hui7-bi2 e5 su7-sit8 long2 cha-chhut.  Kau3 kin-a2-jit8 ui7-tioh8 beh chiok nng7 e5 se3-i5 e5 sim-goan7, ai3 hou7 nng7 e5 se3-i5 hoaN-hi2.  Seng7 chiu2-chui3 e5 heng-hun3 lai5 that Hui7-bi2.  Tui3 i that lai5 ti3 si2.  Sui-jian5 m7-bian2 si2-heng5, ia7 tioh8 Bu5-ki5 tou5-heng5.  Che-si7 tong-si5 kiam2-chhat e5 lun7-ko3.  Chiau3 khoaN3 Bu5-ki5 tou5-heng5 si7 chin lan5 bian2 tit, hek8-chia2 tioh8 si2-heng5.
Khun-hong u7 chhiaN2 chit8 e5 pian7-hou7-su7 mia5 Tan5 Chi3-hun.  I chin chin7-lat8 chu2-tiuN kui2-na7 tiam2.
(1) Chiah8-chiu2, u7 chui3, sim bo5 i3-sek.
(2) Chiau3 i that e5 lek8-liong7, kap i khia7 e5 ui7-ti3 iau2-boe7 e7 ti3-kau3 hou7 Hui7-bi2 poah8 loh8 ti3 si2 e5 theng5-tou7.
(3) Sui-jian5 beh that e5 si5 u7 chhoh.  M7-ku2 i u7 hoah kiu3 lang5.  Pun2-sin ia7 u7 khi3 kou, giah8 tke-ko khi3 la7.  Tui3 an2-ni thang chai hui ok-i3.  Eng3-kai tioh8 kiam2-heng5.
Kiam2-chhat kong2 an2-ni be7 kong2-tit.  Kiam2-chhat e5 lun7-ko3:
(1) Na7 kong2 chiah8-chiu2 u7 chui3, thang kio3 Sai3-hoa-= lau5 e5 thau5-ke lai5 choe3-cheng3 hit-jit8 e5 sit8-cheng5.  Koh chhiaN2 Hoat-i lai5 kiam2-giam7 i e5 the2-chit, khoaN3 u7-iaN2 nng7-koan3 beh8-chiu2 e7 chui3 a2-be7?  Ia7 chhiaN2 cheng-sin5 peN7-kho e5 choan-ka lai5 kam3-teng7 kong2 chiah8 nng7-koan3 beh8-chiu2 e5 chui3, kho2-leng5 chiong lang5 that-loh8 ti5-te2 si2 ia7 m7-chai thang ka7 i giu2 khi2--lai5.  Soa3 biat8-si e5 theng5-tou7 a2-bo5?  Sui5-si5 khi3 chhiaN2 Sai3-hoa-lau5 e5 lau2-pan2, kap Hoat-i, kap cheng-sin5 peN7-kho e5 choan-ka lai5.
Lau5-chu2 jip8--lai5.  Po3 seN3-mia5, chu7-chi2, chit-giap8, ni5-leng5, kau chhut sin-hun7-cheng3, khak-jin7 bo5 chho3.  Kio3 i chiu3-choa7 bo5 kong2 peh8-chhat8.  Chiu3-choa7 liau2 chiu7 kong2.

“Khun-hong siong5-siong5 ti7 goa2 hia chhut-jip8, i si7 goa2 hia e5 kou3-kheh.  I e5 chiu2-liong7 chin toa7.  Kho2-leng5 lim Beh8-a2-chiu2 chit8-taN2.  Lim nng7-koan3 tui3 i si7 bo5 chui3 chiah tioh8.  Chiau3 goa2 sou2 chai si7 an2-ni.” Kong2 liau2 chiu7 che7 loh8-khi3.  Pian7-hou7-su7 chin siu7-khi3.  Toa7 me7 Sai3-hoa-lau5 e5 lau2-pan2.  Kong2 “Lim nng7-koan3 tui3 i si7 bo5 chui3 chiah tioh8” chit ku3 li2 put eng3-kai kong2.  Li2 m7-si7 i pun2 lang5, li2 na2-e7 chai i pun2 lang5 tong-si5 e5 sit8-cheng5.  Li2 m7-si7 kam3-teng7-jin5.  Put eng3-kai an2-ni lun7-toan3.
Chiu7 chhiaN2 Hoat-i lai5 giam7 hiat-chit, kap chu3-sia7 hou7 i hoan2-eng3.  Chai-iaN2 ko2-jian5 nng7-koan3 beh8-chiu2 Khun-hong si7 be7 chui3.  Na7 e7 si7 kek8 kheng-bi5.
Chiu7 chhiaN2 Cheng-sin5-kho e5 choan-ka lai5 kam3-teng7 nng7-koan3 beh8-chiu2 e5 chiu2-cheng-hun jip8 an2-ni e5 the2-chit e5 lang5 i e5 cheng-sin5 chok-iong7 e7 eng2-hiong2 kau3 chaiN2-iuN7?  ChhiaN2 i theh8 sit8-le7 lai5 kong2.  Cheng-sin5-kho e5 choan-ka ia7 cheng3-beng5 bo5 kong2 an2-ni e5 chiu2-cheng-hun e7 ti3-kau3 hou7 Khun-hong chit khoan2 the2-chit e5 lang5 e7 ti3-kau3 be7 ki3-tit cheng5-au7 e5 su7.
(2) Sui-jian5 i that e5 lat8, kap khia7 e5 ui7-ti3 bo5 chap8-hun e7 ti3-kau3 hou7 Hui7-bi2 poah8-loh8 ti5 e5 khoan2.  Chong2-si7 che si7 li2-lun7.  Na7-si7 sit8-chai7 to u7 poah8 loh8-khi3, li2-lun7 bo5 lou7-eng7, ai3 an3-chiau3 sit8-che3.
(3) I sui-jian5 u7 hoah kiu3 lang5.  A2-si7 u7 lai5 chhoe7, na7-si7 an2-choaN2 chhoe7 bo5 e5 si5 m7-bian2 po3 phai3-chhut-sou2.  KhoaN3 tioh8 sin-bun5 e5 si5 bo5 lai5 chu7-siu2, koh ui3-choe7 chau2 khi3 Siong7-hai2 un2-lek.  Ji5-chhiaN2 oaN7-mia5 choe3 Tan5 Hok-choan5.  Koh u7 gui7-cho7 Hui7-bi2 chu7-sat e5 ui5-gian5-su.  Hit-tiuN giam7-liau2 si7 Siu3-chhun e5 chhiu2-pit, m7-si7 Khun-hong gui7-cho7 e5.  M7-ku2 ia7 thang kong2 i hek8-chia2 u7 tong5-i3.
Pian7-hou7-su7 kong2 eng7 chhui-siong2 kong2 “Hek8-chia2 i u7 tong5-i3” chit ku3 m7-thang kong2.  Chhui-su7 chhiaN2 PhoaN3-koaN mng7 Khun-hong pun2-lang5.  Kong2 tui3 Hui7-bi2 chu7-sat e5 ui5-gian5-su e5 su7 i chai a2-m7-chai?  Khun-hong kong2 i m7-chai.  Kong2 ui5-gian5-su e5 su7, i chiah siuN7 tioh8 hian3 chit8 tiuN ui5-gian5-su chhut-lai5.  Chiu7-si7 i ti7 Siong7-hai2 e5 Seng3 Iok-han7 tai7-hak8 peN7-iN7 sia2 beh hou7 Hui7-bi2 e5 ui5-gian5-su.  Khiok i 10 hun 9.9 m7-kaN2 kong2 Hui7-bi2 iau2 ti7 se3-kan.  Chong2-si7 iau2 u7 chit8-si-si e5 hi-bang7.  U7, bo5, put-koan2, i si7 ai3 pai3-thok hoat-iN7 chiong hit-tiuN kia3 hou7 in au7-thau5, lai5 piau2-pek8 i hoan2-hoe2 kap thiaN3 Hui7-bi2 e5 sim-cheng5.  Chiu7 theh8 kia3 teng5-tiuN2.
Ki5-u5 long2 bo5 sim2-mih8 thang kong2, han7 10 hun-cheng koh hou7 Khun-hong siuN7.  Na7 bo5 chiu7 beh phoaN3-koat Bu5-ki5 tou5-heng5.  Chhun 10 hun, chhun 5 hun, si5-kan tit8-tit8 koe3.  Pian7-hou7-su7 chin ai3 kiu3 Khun-hong.  Ng3-bang7 e7-tit bo5 choe7, a2-si7 e7-tit kiam2-heng5.  Chhun 4 hun-cheng, 3 hun-cheng.  PhoaN3-koaN mng7 i kiam2 bo5 sim2-mih8 thang kong2, chhun 2 hun-cheng.  Hut-jian5 au7-bin7 chit8 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 chheng7 chit8 nia2 ku7 hoe-a2-saN ti7 cheng3-lang5 e5 tiong-kan hoah kong2 “Chit chan5 su7 oan-ong2, goa2 chai-iaN2.” Kiam2-chhat hoah kong2 beng7-leng7 ka7 i koaN2 chhut-khi3.  Chek-si5 teng5-tiuN2 beng7-leng7 teng5-teng ka7 i koaN2 chhut-khi3.  Pian7-hou7-su7 tit8-tit8 kong2 put kong-peng5.  Che si7 Khun-hong i5-it e5 kiu3-chheN.  Tioh8 iong5-un2 i khi3 chhoe7 chiah eng3-kai.  In-ui7 Bu5-ki5-tou5, kap Si2-heng5, peN5-peN5 chit8-si3-lang5 si7 bo5 lou7-eng7 khi3.  Chiah iu-siu3 e5 chheng-lian5 kin-ni5 32 hoe3 chiu7 soan-ko3 Bu5-ki5-tou5, be7-bian2 thai3 phah-sng2.  Iau-kiu5 ian5-ki5 phoaN3-koat.  PhoaN3-koaN chiu7 kap Poe5-sim2-koaN chham-siong5.  Chiu7 chun2 choe3-ban7 ian5-tiong5 kau3 bin5-a2-jit8 chit e5 si5.  Ia7 kio3 chit e5 pian7-hou7-su7 khi3 chhoe7 hit e5 jiang2 oan-ong2 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 lai5 choe3 kan-cheng3.  Na7 chhoe7 bo5, chiu7 beh i5-chiau3 sou2 lun7-ko3 lai5 pan7-li2.  Tui3 an2-ni chiu7 soan-ko3 pi3-teng5.
Kau3 bin5-a2-chai3 iau2 khah che7 lang5.  Chit e5 siau-sit chit8 e7 thoan5 chhut, kui siaN5 e5 lang5 long2 chin chhiong2-tong7.  Kau3-si5 boan2-teng5, ji5-chhiaN2 teng5-goa7 e5 lang5 jin5-san jin5-hai2 ai3 khoaN3 chit e5 phoaN3-koat, kap lai5 choe3-cheng3 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 tau3-ti2 si7 siaN2 lang5?  Kau3-si5 chhoe7 bo5.  Sui-jian5 pian7-hou7-su7 liam5-piN jiok chhut-khi3, mng7 thoa-chhia--e5, mng7 be7 pai5-thoaN--e5, kong2 u7 khoaN3 chit8 e5 chheng7 ou-hoe-a2 saN e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 koaN7 chhai3-na5-a2 tui3 hoat-iN7 chhut-lai5.  TaN tui3 to2-ui7 khi3 ia7-si7 chhoe7 bo5?  Pian7-hou7-su7 chin put-peng5 kiam2-chhat e5 bo5-li2.  Na7-si7 kiam2-chhat kong2 hit e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 kho2-leng5 si7 siau2--e5.  In-ui7 lang5 beh choe3 cheng3-jin5 eng3-kai ai3 u7 siong-tong e5 chhiu2-siok8.  Hoat-teng5 si7 sin5-seng3, be7 eng7-tit soan-jiong2, che si7 siong5-sek, an2-choaN2 sui5-pian7 jiang2.  Ia7 kho2-leng5 si7 pian7-hou7-su7 chhiaN3--e5.  Thiau-ti5 beh loan7-teng5 lai5 thoa-ian5 phoaN3-koat.  Put-koan2-thaN chhoe7 bo5 chiu7 pa7-lun7.  TaN eng3-kai tioh8 phoaN3-koat.
Tu2 beh phoaN3-koat e5 si5 Chhoa3 Thian-peng5 Heng5-su7 kho-tiuN2.  Cheng-tham Chu2-jim7 chhoa7 nng7 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 jip8--lai5.  Chit8 e5 chap8-goa7-hoe3, chit8 e5 20 goa7 hoe3.  Phoa3-koaN tu2 beh phoaN3-koat, Chhoa3 sian-siN kin2 chau2-oa2 khi3 i e5 sin-piN phak tiam3 i e5 hiN7-a2 piN ka7 i kong2 se3-siaN oe7.  PhoaN3-koaN chit8-si5 chin kiaN.  Che si7 an2-choaN2?  Na2-li2 u7 chit ho7 tai7-chi3?  Choan5-teng5 e5 lang5 ia7 long2 toa7 ki5-koai3, hoa7-hoa7 kio3 khia7 khi2-lai5 khoaN3.  Teng5-tiuN2 hoah tai7-ke an-cheng7, che7 loh8-khi3.  Tai7-ke chiu7 che7 loh8-khi3, tai7-ke chhi7-bu2 chhi7-chhu7 kong2 taN che tauh-ti2 si7 an2-choaN2?  
21
Heng5-su7 kho-tiuN2 Chhoa3 sian-siN sou2 chhoa7 jip8--lai5 hit nng7 e5 lu2-chu2 goan5-lai5 m7-si7 pat8-lang5, chit8 e5 chiu7-si7 Hui7-bi2, chit8 e5 chiu7-si7 tui3 in au7-thau5 kah--lai5 e5 chhe-eng7 Sou3-lan5.  Khun-hong khoaN3 chit8--e7 toa7-kiaN, tui3 i hut-jian5 e5 chho3-kak, kap cheng-sin5 e5 heng-hun3, e7 kam2-kak si7 Hui7-bi2 e5 iu-leng5 chhut-hian7.  Chit8-si5 tui3 khan i jip8--lai5 e5 teng5-teng lam2 tiau5 tiau5 chin-kiaN, tit8-tit8 hoah kiu3-lang5, beh piaN3 chhut-khi3.  Hit e5 khoan2-sit sit8-chai7 khoaN3 liau2 chin kho2-lin5.  Goan5-lai5 Khun-hong si7 chit8 e5 bin7 peh8-peh8 e7-kok chiam-chiam sin5-keng chit8 e5 lang5.  Sou2-i2 chin to-cheng5, ji5-chhiaN2 chin khoai3 heng-hun3 e5 lang5.  Hui7-bi2 khoaN3 i an2-ni sim ia7-si7 m7-kam, chiah kiaN5 oa2-khi3.  Ka7-i kio3 “A-hu-ah!  M7-bian2-kiaN chin-chiaN3 si7 goa2 ne7.  Hui7-bi2 iau2 oah8 teh ne7.” Khun-hong jin7 kiN3 si7 Hui7-bi2 e5 siaN, sim thau5 chiah tiaN7, oat8 to3--tng2 lai5 kui7 loh8 khi3 lam2 Hui7-bi2 e5 kha tit8-tit8 kiu5 Hui7-bi2 sia3-bian2.  Hui7-bi2 ia7 hau2, Sou3-lan5 ia7 hau2, chiu7 aN3-loh8 khi3 siang-chhiu2 ka7 i hu5 khi2--lai5, m7-bian2 kiaN, m7-bian2 hoan5-lo2, goan2 long2 iong2-iong2 ti7-teh.” chiu7 ka7 i tau3 chhah khi2--lai5.  PhoaN3-koaN kio3 i chhiaN2 khia7 tiam3 piN-ah, chiu7-kio3 Hui7-bi2 lai5 mng7.
Seng mng7 lang5-mia5, chu7-sou2 ni5-leng5, chit-giap8, au7-lai5 theh8 sin-hun7-cheng3 khi2 lai5 tui3 long2 bo5 chho3.  Chiu7 kio3 i chiu3-choa7 bo5 kong2 peh8-chhat8 oe7, chiu7 chiu3-choa7.  PhoaN3-koaN beng7-leng7 su-ki3 siong5-se3 sia2 i e5 khau2-keng khoaN3 tauh-ti2 si7 chaiN2-iuN7?  Hui7-bi2 chiu7 kong2.
“12 goeh8 chhe 2 am3, Khun-hong kap Siu3-chhun, Bi2-chu khi3 sai3-hoa-lau5.  Goa2 seng7 in bo5 ti7 teh e5 ki5-hoe7 chiu7 chhoa7 Sou3-lan5 khi3 Lian5-hoe ti5-piN ki5-to2.  In-ui7 goa2 peng5-jit8 siong5-siu7 gek8-thai7.” kong2 kau3 chia chiu7 lek8 i e5 chhiu2-ng2, kap khou3-kha hou7 phoaN3-koaN, khoaN3 seng-khu chat-chat ou.  Chiu7 koh ke3-siok8 kong2.  “Hit-am3 tng in bo5 ti7-teh chiu7 khi3 ti5-piN ki5-to2.  Cha2 goa2 ia7 bat khi3 hit ki5-to2.  Goa2 long2 bo5 chun5-sim beh chu7-sat.  Goa2 chhim-sin3 Siong7-te3 teh chiau3-kou3.  Goa2 toa7 ng3-bang7 Kiu3-chu2 beh kiu3 goa2 e5 ka-teng5, hou7 tiong7-hu e7 hoe5-thau5, hou7 ka-teng5 e7 ho5-peng5.  Goa2 m7-bat siuN7 beh po3 sim2-mih8 lang5 e5 oan.  Goa2 chu7-jin7 goa2-si7 pek-hap8-hoe khui ti7 chhi3-phe3-a2 e5 lai7-bin7.  Goa2 hit-si5 na2 ki5-to2 na2 hau2, In saN e5 kiaN5-oa2-lai5 goa2 e5 sim chin iu-bun7, lun2 be7 tiau5 tit8-tit8 hau2.  Tiong7-hu oa2 lai5 me7 goa2, goa2 chiu7 tui3 kha ka7 i lam2 teh.  Khi2-thau5 bo5 hiah oa2 ti5 piN, hou7 i thoa kiaN5 kui2-na7-pou7 chiu7 chin oa2 ti5-piN.  In-ui7 am3-am3, sou2-i2 goa2 m7-chai gui5-hiam2, tit8-tit8 hau2 ka7 i lam2 tiau5 leh.  Au7-lai5 i chiu7 chhoh phaiN2-chhui3 ka7 goa2 cham3-khi3, goa2 chu7 an2-ni tng3-lap8-che7, to3-siang-hiaN3, chit8 chhiu2 jih8 ti7 thou5-nih, chit8 chhiu2 jih8 tioh8 chui2.  Na7 ka7 goa2 thoa iau2 e7 khi2-lai5, chong2-si7 hit-si5 iau2 u7 chit8 e5 pat8 lang5 chan3 kha ka7 goa2 that-loh8 khi3.  Goa2 tu2 beh sian to3 khi2-lai5, i tu2 that--lai5.  Goa2 e5 chhiu2 khiu2 tioh8 i e5 e5-chiam-boe2.  Goa2 tioh8 chit8-hang7 mih8, tui3 i e5 e5 lut ti7 goa2 chhiu2-nih.  Goa2 chit8-si5 ia7 m7-chai si7 sim2-mih8 mih8.  Ai chit8 siaN goa2 chu7 an2-ni poah8 loh8-khi3.  Goa2 m7-chai Khun-hong u7 aN3 loh8 lai5 sa, ia7 bo5 thiaN lang5 kong2 sim2-mih8.  Goa2 tim5 loh8-khi3 chiah8 chui2.”
PhoaN3-koaN chiu7 oat8 koe3 lai5 mng7 Sou3-lan5, khoaN3 Sou3-lan5 hit chun7 chai-iaN2 bo5?  Sou3-lan5 chiu7 in3 kong2 “Hit e5 cheng5-heng5 goa2 long2 chai.  Goa2 khoaN3 in saN e5 lai5, goa2 kin2 chau2 khi3 bih ti7 toa7 chhiu7-au7.  Goan2 A-koaN Khun-hong beh ka7 i bong khi2--lai5.  Siu3-chhun tit8-tit8 chaN5-chhui3 kong2 m7-bian2.  Kong2 ‘koaN5-koaN5--lang5’ li2 ia7 lim chiu2 chui3-chui3, koh lioh8-a2 hou7 i leng2 tioh8--leh, mai3-nou3.  Kong2 si2 to si2 lah, kin-tu2 bin5-a2-chai3 chiah lai5 kou ma7-si7 sio-siang5.  Kong2 Khun-hong, li2 to me7 kong2 beh si2 chiu7 si2 lou7-khi3, bian2 tiaN7 teh kau-tiN5.  TaN ka7 i chun2 choe3 chu7-sat thiau3-chui2 ma7 bo5 lang5 chai, ia7 bo5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3, tit8-tit8 kio3 i m7-bian2 kou.  Tui3 an2-ni saN e5 chiu7 kiaN5 to3-khi3.”
Phoa3-koaN chiu7 koh mng7 Hui7-bi2 au7-lai5 an2-choaN2?  Hui7-bi2 chiu7 koh kong2.
“Poah8 loh8-khi3 chiah8-chui2, kai-chai3 kam2-sia7 Siong7-te3 hou7 goa2 koh liong3 khi2-lai5.  Kai-chai3 piN-a2 u7 chit8 chiah leng5-kak chun5-a2, in-ui7 hi5-ti5 te2 u7 lian5-hoe, ia7 u7 leng5-kak.  Sou2-i2 u7 cho3 chit8 chiah chun5-a2 ti7 hia, peng5-si5 thang ban2 leng5-kak, a2-si7 ban2 lian5-hoe, chhai2 lian5-chi2.  U7 si5 goeh8-kng thang ti7 hia che7 chun5-a2.  Goa2 to3 liong3 khi2--lai5 e5 si5 bo5 phah-sng3 hou7 goa2 khiN5 tioh8 leng5-kak chun5-a2, goa2 chiu7 khiN5 ti7 chun5 piN, bo5 lat8, bo5 se3-bin7 thang peh chiuN7 chun5.  Kan-ta khiN5 ti7 chun5 piN.  Au7-lai5 in saN e5 chiu7 to3-khi3 lah.”
PhoaN3-koaN mng7 kong2 “Hit-si5 li2 thai2 bo5 hoah kiu3 lang5?” Hui7-bi2 in3 kong2 “Hit-si5 goa2 e5 sim-keng2 si7 chin khoaN3 phoa3, chin liau2-jian5.  Me5-jit8 siu7 lang5 gek8-thai7, kau3 chia koh hou7 lang5 eng7 ok-i3 bou5-sat.  Goa2 siuN7 tiong7-hu i si7 bo5 ok-i3.  In-ui7 i m7-chai goa2 i2-keng beh poah8-loh8 ti5.  Si7 chan3 kha cham3 goa2 loh8 khi3 hit e5 cha-bou2-lang5 si7 ok-i3.”
PhoaN3-koaN: “Li2 na2 e7 chai chan3-kha cham3 li2 loh8 khi3 e5 lang5 si7 cha-bou2-lang5?”
Hui7-bi2: “Goa2 u7 giu2 tioh8 i e5 e5-chiam, tui3 e5-chiam u7 hou7 goa2 giu2 chit8 hang7 mih8, lut ti7 goa2 e5 chhiu2-nih.”
PhoaN3-koaN: “Hit-hang mih8 si7 sim2-mih8?  Chit si5 iau2 u7 ti7-teh a2-bo5?”

Hui7-bi2: “U7” chiu7 tui3 i e5 saN-a2-te7 jim5 chhut-lai5, kau hou7 chiang2-teng5 e5 lang5.  Theh8 hou7 phoaN3-koaN khoaN3.
PhoaN3-koaN: “Che-si7 sim2-mih8?”
Hui7-bi2: “Che-si7 Siu3-chhun peng5-si5 tio3 lian5 ti7 i e5 thiau3-bu2-e5 e5 e5-chiam, si7 ou-sek, te7-chau2-phoe5 e5 koan5-kiah8-a2-e5, si7 chit8 lui2 phoe5 choe3 e5 hoe.  Hoe-sim si7 kim--e5, u7 jip8 Khun-hong e5 siong7.  Che si7 hian7-si5 choe3 liu5-heng5 e5 e5.  Eng7 i e5 ai3-jin5 e5 siong7 jip8 ti7 hoe-nih, a2-si7 jip8 ti7 tho5-a2-heng5 (sim-heng5) e5 kim-a2 lai5 tio3 ti7 e5-chiam.  An2-ni i cham3--lai5, tu2 hou7 goa2 giu2 tioh8, lut ti7 goa2 chhiu2-nih.”
PhoaN3-koaN: “Koh khi3 li2 an2-choaN2 e7-tit khi2-lai5?”
Hui7-bi2: “In long2 chau2 liau2 e5 si5, Sou3-lan5 kin2 chau2 chhut--lai5, eng7 chun5 ko-a2 hou7 goa2 giu2.  Goa2 chit8-chhiu2 khi5 chun5-a2, chit8 chhiu2 giu2 chun5-ko-a2 (theN-chun5 e5 tek-ko-a2) , Sou3-lan5 chin7-lat8 ka7 goa2 thoa khi2--lai5.”
PhoaN3-koaN: “Sou3-lan5 li2 chit8 e5 an2-choaN2 thoa u7 hoat?”
Sou3-lan5: “Hit-si5 chin chhut-lat8.  In-ui7 si7 kiaN, chhun5-si2 e5 chhut-lat8.  Koh goa2 e5 kha keng ti7 toa7 chioh8-thau5, chun5-a2 kap lang5 long2 phu5-phu5, sou2-i2 kam2-kak khah khoai3 giu2 e5 khoan2.  Bian2 chit8-e7-a2 chiu7 hou7 goa2 giu2 chiuN7-hoaN7.”
PhoaN3-koaN: “ChiuN7-hoaN7 liau2 siaN2-su7 bo5 kin2 to3-khi3?”

Hui7-bi2: “Goa2 e5 sim i2-keng siuN7 to3-khi3 bo5 sim2-mih8 lou7-eng7.  In saN e5 ki3-jian5 tang5-sim beh gek8-thai7 goa2.  Sim7-chi3 ai3 goa2 si2, an2-ni goa2 siuN7 to3-khi3 bo5 i3-su3.  Sou2-i2 chiu7 koat-sim to5-chau2.”
PhoaN3-koaN: “Chau2 khi3 to2-ui7?”
Hui7-bi2: “Khun-hong to3-khi3 keh chin ku2 chiah giah8-hoe2 lai5 chhio7, eng7 chun5-ko-a2 la7.  Hit-si5 i boe7-lai5, Sou3-lan5 i2-keng to3-khi3 hiahN goa2 e5 saN kap theh8-chiN5 lai5, goan2 nng7 e5 chiu7 oaN7-saN bih ti7 ti5-piN e5 toa7 chhiu7-au7.  Kau3 i la7 bo5 to3-khi3.  Goan2 nng7 e5 chiu7 tui3 au7-boe2-mng5 liu chhut-khi3, chau2 khi3 bih ti7 chit8 e5 tu2-ho2 e5 sou2-chai7.  Keh thiN-kng thau3-cha2 saN-tiam2 e5 chhia chiu7 khi3 Siong7-hai2.”
PhoaN3-koaN: “Sou3-lan5 li2 to3-khi3 hiahN-saN theh8 chiN5 e5 si5, in saN e5 teh chhong3 sim2-mih8, an2-choaN2 bo5 kin2 lai5 kiu3?”
Sou3-lan5: “Khun-hong beh kin2 giah8 hoe2 lai5, in nng7 e5 ka7 i chou2-tong3.  Siu3-chhun ka7 i chhiuN2 teng, pun5-hoa hoe2.  Kap i oan-ke, m7 hou7 i lai5.  Nng7 e5 sio-me7, au7-lai5 Siu3-chhun hou7 Khun-hong sai chhui3-phoe2, khau3.  Chu7 an2-ni kap Bi2-chu tiuN khi3 khun3 m7 chhap Khun-hong.  Goa2 bo5 khoa3 ka7 in khoaN3 kau3-boe2, kin2 theh8-saN lai5 hou7 goan2 A-niu5 oaN7.”
PhoaN3-koaN: “Kau3 Siong7-hai2 khi3 tiam3 sim2-mih8 lang5 tau?”
Hui7-bi2: “Khi3 tiam3 goan2 e5 i5-piau2 hiaN-ko e5 tau.  I seN3 Khou2, si7 ti7 Siong7-hai2 Seng3 Iok-han7 tai7-hak8 e5 hu3-siok8 peN7-iN7 choe3 i-seng.”
PhoaN3-koaN: “Li2 chai Khun-hong ti7 Siong7-hai2 bat khi3 hit keng peN7-iN7 jip8-iN7 a2-bo5?”
Hui7-bi2: “Chai.”

PhoaN3-koaN: “An2-choaN2 li2 e7 chai?”
Hui7-bi2: “Goa2 e5 a-ko Khou2 sian-siN si7 lai7-kho-i, i lai5 hou7 goa2 e5 a-ko khoaN3.  Jip8-iN7 ti7 thau5-teng2 te7 2 ho7 sek.  Goa2 e5 a-ko tui3 peN7-iN7 to3-lai5 u7 teh ka7 goa2 kong2.  Goa2 ia7 poaN3-sin3 poaN3-gi5, hit am3 khi3 ka7 i khoaN3.”
PhoaN3-koaN: “Khi3 ka7 i khoaN3, an2-choaN2 i pun2-lang5 e7 m7-chai?”
Hui7-bi2: “I hit am3 teh khau3, kui7-loh8 ki5-to2 hoan2-hoe2, au7-lai5 beh oa2-lai5 thang-a2 mng5-kiN theh8 bin7-pou3 chhit bak8-sai2, hit-si5 i u7 khoaN3 goa2 e5 lang5-iaN2 ti7 goa7-bin7.  I khui-siaN kio3, khui-mng5 jiok chhut--lai5, goa2 chau2 ti7 am3-am3 e5 chhau2-pou-a2.  Hit me5 goeh8 am3-so, am3-so, i that tioh8 chioh8-thau5 phak loh8-khi3.  Khi2 nau2-pin5-hiat, goa2 oat8 to3-tng2--lai5 kap kou3-me5 tong-tit8 e5 hou7-su7 ka7 i kng jip8-khi3 peN7-pang5.  Hit-si5 i m7-chai lang5.”
Khun-hong thiaN kau3 chia bak8-sai2 si3 lam5-sui5, khau3 be7 chhut-siaN.
PhoaN3-koaN: “Khun-hong ko2-jian5 si7 an2-ni a2 m7-si7?”
Khun-hong: “Si7.  Goa2 ti7 hia ko2-jian5 hong2-hut u7 khoaN3 Hui7-bi2 ti7 peN7-pang5 e5 au7-bin7 thang-a2 goa7.  Goa2 jiok chhut--lai5 u7 khoaN3 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 teh chau2.  Chong2-si7 goa2 tioh8-tak poah8 loh8-khi3, liau2-au7 e5 su7-cheng5 goa2 m7-chai.”
PhoaN3-koaN: “Hui7-bi2, ki3-jian5 si7 an2-ni, li2 ti7 peN7-iN7 chaiN2-iuN7 m7 kap i sio-jin7?”
Hui7-bi2: “Hit-si5 goa2 e5 sim bo5 pian7.  In-ui7 goa2 m7-chai i tu2-tu2 hoan2-hoe2 kau3 sim2-mih8 khoan2, ia7 sio-jin7 au7, to3-khi3 koh kap hiah e5 se3-i5 choe3-hoe2 seng-oah8 ia7-si7 bo5 lou7-eng7.  Sou2-i2 sim theh8 lian3-tng2, koh tan2-hau7 koh lai5 e5 ki-hoe7.”

PhoaN3-koaN: “Chit-si5 li2 an2-choaN2 e7 lai5 ti7 chia?”
Hui7-bi2: “Goa2 tui3 Siong7-hai2 Tiong-iong-po3 khoaN3 tioh8 Bi2-chu e5 su7-kiaN7.  Ia7 khoaN3 tioh8 Khun-hong pi7 khau3-liu5, pi7 u5-sim2, sang3 loh8 lai5 Chiang-chiu koan7-siaN5 Te7-hng hoat-iN7 beh ti7 chia kiam2-cheng3 kong-phoaN3, ti7 sin-bun5 long2 chai-iaN2, sou2-i2 goa2 chiu7 to3-tng2 lai5 chia.”
PhoaN3-koaN: “Cha-hng lai5 hoat-teng5 jiang2 e5 lang5 si7 li2 a2 m7-si7?”
Hui7-bi2: “M7-si7, si7 Sou3-lan5.”
PhoaN3-koaN: “Sou3-lan5 li2 cha-hng u7 lai5 hoat-teng5 a2-bo5?”
Sou3-lan5: “U7.  Goa2 chhut-lai5 be2-chhai3, thiaN lang5 kong2 beh kong-phoaN3 ‘Lian5-hoe-ti5 su7-kiaN7’, goa2 chiu7 oat lai5 khoaN3.  Goa2 khoaN3 liau2 u7 oan-ong2 goa2 chiu7 jiang2 chhut-lai5.  Pun2 goa2 siuN7 beh kong2, to hou7 lang5 koaN2 chhut-khi3.”
PhoaN3-koaN: “Li2 an2-choaN2 bo5 lai5 chhiu2-siok8 choe3 cheng3-jin5.”
Sou3-lan5: “Goa2 be7 hiau2, m7-bat tioh8 chaiN2-iuN7.”
PhoaN3-koaN: “KoaN2 li2 chhut-khi3, li2 tui3 to2-ui7 khi3?”
Sou3-lan5: “Goa2 kin2 chau2 khi3 ka7 goan2 A-niu5 Hui7-bi2 kong2.”
PhoaN3-koaN: “Hui7-bi2 li2 thiaN liau2 thai2 bo5 kin2-lai5?”
Hui7-bi2: “Goa2 u7 lai5, to i2-keng soaN3-teng5 lah, sou2-i2 oat to3-tng2-khi3.  Kau3 cha2-khi2 tham3-thiaN Chhoa3 sian-siN iau2 ti7 chia, chiah lai5 chhoe7 Chhoa3 sian-siN.  In-ui7 tui3 sin-bun5 khoaN3 tioh8, chai chit e5 an3-kiaN7 si7 i choan-an3 cha-pan7, sou2-i2 chiah khi3 chhoe7 i, chhiaN2 i chhoa7 goan2 lai5.”

PhoaN3-koaN chiong Siu3-chhun gui7-cho3 e5 Hui7-bi2 chu7-sat e5 ui5-gian5-chng7, kap Siu3-chhun e5-chiam e5 hoe, kap Siu3-chhun e5 tiu5 chhiu2-kin long2 theh8 hou7 Khun-hong, kap Hui7-bi2, Sou3-lan5 in jin7.  Chiah chai chit e5 bou5-sat su7-kiaN7 e5 chu2-kak oan5-choan5 si7 chhut tui3 Siu3-chhun, Khun-hong long2 bo5 koan-he7.”
An2-ni kau3 chia.
An3-kiaN7 long2 sim2-li2 beng5-pek8 chiong-kiat.  Chiu7 soan-phoaN3 hit e5 Chu2-bun5 chhin-chhiuN7 e7-bin7:
“Lun7 Chhiang-chiu siaN5 lian5-hoe-ti5 su7-kiaN7.  Bou5-hai7 Lim5 Hui7-bi2 e5 su7, kap Tan5 Khun-hong bo5 koan-he7, i-hoat phoaN3-koat bo5 choe7.”
Su7-sit8: Lun7 chit-chan5 su7-kiaN7 e5 chu2-hoan7 si7 Li2 Siu3-chhun.  Na7-si7 heng7-tit Lim5 Hui7-bi2 gu7-kiu3 bo5 si2.  Chiu7 piN3 choe3 sat-jin5 bi7-sui5 choe7.  M7-ku2 Li2 Siu3-chhun ui3-choe7 i2-keng chu7-sat.  Sou2-i2 koat-teng7 pun2 an3-kiaN7 m7 koh tui-kiu3, chu7 an2-ni chiong-kiat.  
22
Ang-bou2 tui3 an2-ni koh thoan5-oan5.  Hit e5 hoaN-hi2 kong2 be7 chin7.  Soa3 be7 ki3-tit si7 ti7 hoat-teng5 nng7 e5 lam2-teh hau2 tit chin chhi-chham2, lu2-pi7 Sou3-lan5 ia7 khia7 ti7 sin-piN bak8-sai2 hou3 m7-khui.  Lai5 ti7 hoat-teng5 khoaN3 kong-phoaN3 e5 chhin-ke, chheN-m2 Ong5 Bok8-su, bok8-su-niu5, kap hiaN-so2 Soat-mui5 ia7 long2 ui5 oa2 lai5 tai7-ke hau2, chit8-si5 pi-hi2 ban7-kam2 kau-chip8, tek8-piat8 Soat-mui5 chau2 oa2-lai5 tui3 sio2-kou Hui7-bi2 e5 chhiu2 khan leh, kio3 chit8-siaN “A-kou” bak8-sai2 hou3 m7-khui, hau2 be7 chhut-siaN, sim-lai7 chit8-si5 siuN7 tioh8 ka-ti7 phaiN2 keng2-gu7 tiong7-hu si2, ta-ke koaN ia7-si2, sio2-kou ia7 chiah phaiN2 keng2-gu7, theng5 chin ku2 chiah hau2 chhut-siaN.  Chit8-si5 theng3 chiong3 khoaN3 tioh8 chit e5 cheng5-keng2, ia7 kap in saN-kap lau5 bak8-sai2, sim7-chi3 kap in saN-kap khui-siaN hau2 kau3 chhngh-chhngh-kio3 e5 lang5 ia7 be7 chio2.  Chit-si5 hoat-teng5 chin-loan7, teng5-tiuN2 hoah tai7-ke an-cheng7, beng7-leng7 teng5-teng kio3 tai7-ke the3 teng5.
Tui3 an2-ni Ong5 Bok8-su chiu7 chhoa7 in che7 sio2 pau-chhia seng to3-khi3 Pai3-tng5 hiah-khun3.  Tai7-ke jip8 pai3-tng5-thiaN ti7 hia saN-kap gim5-si, kam2-sia7 Siong7-te3 koe3-khi3 e5 chiau3-kou3.  Tek8-piat8 Khun-hong kap Hui7-bi2 nng7-e5 koh sio-khan kau3 kang2-tai5 cheng5 tai7-ke kui7 loh8 ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5, chai3 hoan2-seng2, koh chit8-pai2 siuN7-tioh8 kiat-hun tong-si5 e5 lip8-se7, hit tong-si5 lau7-bu2 Lim5 tiuN2-lo2-niu5 iau2 ti7 sin-piN, kap cha2-si5 boe7 kiat-hun cheng5 saN-thiaN3 e5 kau-poe5.  Be7 kim3-tit nng7 e5 kui7-loh8 saN-ng3 lai5 lau5 bak8-sai2, tui3 Siong7-te3 toa7-toa7 chham3-hoe2.  Tek8-piat8 Khun-hong hau2 kau3 phiN7-lau5 noa7-tih.  Tui3 Hui7-bi2 chhim-chhim jin7 i e5 koe3-sit, hit e5 thai3-tou7 chin-chiaN3 khiam-pi, su5 chin cheng5-chhiat.  Chit8-si5 Hui7-bi2 siu7 i chin-cheng5 hoan2-hoe2 e5 kam2-tong7, ia7 bo5 koh u7 te7-ji7 ku3 thang kong2.  Chi2-u7 kong2 “Goan7 Chu2 sia3-bian2, in-ui7 li2 m7-chai li2 e5 sou2 choe3.  Tui3 chia khi2 bang7 hu-kun chin-sim hoan2-hoe2, tang5-sim saN-kap hok8-sai7 Chu2, chiu7 goa2 sou2 siu7 e5 kan-khou2 si7 chin u7 ke3-tat8.” Khun-hong thiaN Hui7-bi2 e5 in3-tap it-hoat kam2-kak kian3-siau3.
Ong5 Bok8-su kap bok8-su-niu5 chiu7 eng7 tu2-ho2 e5 oe7 an-ui3 in.  Au7-lai5 Bok8-su eng7 chhiu2 hoaN7 in e5 thau5-khak thoe3 in ki5-to2.  Kiu5 Chu2 chiok-hok in e5 chian5-tou5.
Tui3 chia oan5-jian5 chai3 sin kiat-hut lai5 sin chhut-hoat.  Tai7-ke chiah siu7 an-ui3.  Tui3 hit-si5 i2-au7 sin seng-oah8 e5 hoaN-hi2 kong2 be7-chin7.  Chiu7 to3-khi3 chiong it-chhe3 cheng2-li2, jian5-au7 poaN khi3 tiam3 Su7-liong5.  Ti7 hia teng5-sin khi2-chhu3.  Khun-hong jiat8-sim sin3 Chu2 nia2 se2-le2 jip8 seng3-hoe7, chin-chiaN3 kai2-thau5 oaN7-bin7 choe3 sin e5 ka-teng5.  Hui7-bi2 bo5 khioh-hin7 chin7-sim thiaN3 Siu3-chhun sou2 lau5 e5 se3-kiaN2 Eng5-chong, an2-chun2 chhin-siN--e5.  I2-au7 chiu7 ti7 kau3-hoe7 e5 sin-piN, chit8-peng5 goan5 u7 hu7-siat e5 chin2-liau5-sou2, in ti7 koh chit8 peng5 chhong3-siat chit8-keng Iu3-ti7-hng5 ka7 i ho7 mia5 choe3 “Hui7-chu5 Iu3-ti7-hng5” lai5 ki3-liam7 si2-khi3 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 “M7-tihN8-a2.” Hui7-bi2 pun2-sin choe3 hng5-tiuN2.  Mui2-jit8 hu-hu7 hoaN-hoaN hi2-hi2 chin7-sim hok8-sai7 Siong7-te3, thiaN3 kau3-hoe7 lai5 hong7-su7 lang5.  Tui3 an2-ni ka-teng5 koh chit8-pai2 chhiong-moa2 si-koa, ki5-to2, thak8 Seng3-keng e5 siaN.
Ah!  Thang kho2-lin5 “Chhi3-a2-lai7 e5 Pek-hap8-hoe,” li2 e5 keng2-gu7 thai2 e7 khou2 kau3 an2-ni leh!  Kai-chai3 li2 u7 si2-siu2 ho2 e5 sin3-giong2, chin7-sim thiaN3 Chu2 kau3-boe2, chiu7 Siong7-te3 ui7-tioh8 li2 khui-lou7.  Kiu3-chu2 ko2-jian5 kiu3 li2.  TaN goan7 Chu2 chio-hok thiaN lin2 e5 ki5-to2, hou7 lin2 chhu2-khi3 e7-tit hiong2-siu7 hu-hu7 bi2-moa2 tiN-bit8 e5 ka-teng5 kau3 eng2-oan2.  A-so2 Soat-mui5 choe3 kau3-hoe7 i-koan2 e5 hou7-su7, se3-kiaN2 Ju5-liong5, Ju5-mui5 ia7 koai-koai chiam7-chiam7 toa7-han3.  Hui7-bi2 tit Chu2 un-tian2 ia7 koh siN kiaN2, cha-bou2-kiaN2 chit8-ke toa7 thoan5-oan5.
(Oan5)
A. D. 1954. 3. 15.
Sia2 ti7 Ji7-lim5 kau3-hoe7 
Bok8-su-koan2 su-chai e5 tang-chhong.  

CHOK-CHIA2 SU7-GIAN5

Ti7 kin-ni5 A.D. 1954 ni5 8 goeh8 kan ti7 Khe-ou5 kau3-hoe7 u7 khui Tiong-tiong chheng-lian5-pou7 chu2-chhui e5 Chheng-lian5 thoan5-khe3 ha7-leng7-hoe7.  Hit-si5 Chheng-lian5-pou7 u7 chhiaN2 sio2-ti7 kang2-ian2 chit8 e5 choan-te5 kio3-choe3 “TiN-bit8 e5 ka-teng5”.  Goa2 bo5 se3-ji7 u7 kang2-ian2 iok 4 tiam2-cheng-ku2.  Bo5 pha3[phah]-sng3 tit-tioh8 tai7-ke e5 hoan-geng5.  Au7-lai5 goa2 u7 chhut chit8 e5 choan-te5 hou7 in tho2-lun7 iok-u7 120 e5 hoe7-oan5 kap 30 e5 pong5-theng3 chia2 kiong7-iok 150 lang5, hun choe3 kui2-na7 chou2[chou] chin jiat8-sim lai5 tho2-lun7 hit e5 bun7-te5.  TaN u7 chiong hit e5 tho2-lun7 e5 kiat-ko2 lai5 khng3 ti7 au7-bin7 choe3 hu7-liok8.

Hit e5 tho2-lun7 e5 te5-bak8 si7 “Loan5-ai3”.  Hun choe3 kui2-na7 hang7 lai5 tho2-lun7.

1. Loan5-ai3 si7 sim2-mih8?

2. Loan5-ai3 si7 thang a2 m7 thang?

3. Tioh8 tui3 sim2-mih8 si5 khi2 chiah thang loan5-ai3?

4. Loan5-ai3 kap Loan7-ai3(亂愛）u7 sim2-mih8 hun-piat?

5. Loan5-ai3 kap kiat-hun u7 sim2-mih8 koan-iau3?

Tai7-ke chin jiat8-sim lai5 tho2-lun7.  ThiaN kang2-ian2 e5 si5 tai7-ke ia7 chin jiat8-sim.  Tit8-tit8 chhiaN2 kang2-su tioh8 koh chiap-soa3 kong2.  Tai7-ke liah8 choe3 chin iau3-kin2 e5 ka3-si7.  Kho2-sioh ui7-tioh8 si5-kan e5 che3-han7 be7 e7.  Tui3 an2-ni Chheng-lian5-pou7 kam2-kak u7 chiong Kau3-iok8-pou7 sou2 khan-chai3 ti7 Iu3-hioh8 e5 chong-kau3 siau2-soat “Chhi3-a2-lai7 e5 pek-hap8-hoe” lai5 chhut-pan2 e5 pit-iau3.  In-ui7 sou2-kong2 “TiN-bit8 e5 ka-teng5” si7 hit e5 siau2-soat e5 chit8 sio2 pou7-hun7.  Tui3 an2-ni Chheng-lian5-pou7, kap Kau3-iok8-pou7 chiu7 chham-siong5 eng7 nng7-pou7 e5 beng5-gi7 lai5 kiong7-tong5 chhut-pan2.

Chong2-si7 sio2-ti7 m7-si7 Siau2-soat-ka, ia7 m7-si7 bun5-hak8-ka.  Si7 chit8 e5 pai5 ti7 boe2-liu pi-bi5 e5 lou5-pok8.  Put-ko3 iu2 sou2-kam2, koh ti7 ki5-to2 tiong tit-tioh8 goa2 sou2 thiaN3 e5 ThiN-pe7 Siong7-te3 un-tian2.  Ia7-si7 in-ui7 I u7 chhim-chhim thiaN3 goa2 chiu7 in2-chhoa7 goa2 sia2 chiah e5.  Un2-tang3 u7 che7-che7 bo5 kau3-giah8 e5 sou2-chai7 che-si7 tui3 goa2 e5 gu5-gong7, bo5 lau2-lian7.  Sou2-i2 chhiaN2 lin2 bo5 se3-ji7 ka7 goa2 chi2-cheng3 pian-that.

Sia2 chit kui2-ku3 eng7 12 ban7-hun e5 keng3-i3 ka7 thiaN3 goa2, pang-chan7 goa2 chhut-pan2 chit pun2 chheh, kap sia2 su7-bun5 e5 sian-poe3 seh-sia7.  Soa3 ka7 liat8-ui7 thok8-chia2 chheng2-an.  Ng3-bang7 Chu2 chiok-hok lin2 khong-lok8.

Sio2-ti7 Loa7 Jin5-seng Chu7-su7.

Sia2-ti7 Ji7-lim5 Kau3-hoe7 bok8-su-koan2 e5 su-chai

A.D. 1954 ni5 11 goeh8 8 jit8.
